atha śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamī vāyavīya saṃhitā prārabhyate śrī gaṇeśāya namaḥ śrī gaurī śaṃkarābhyām namaḥ atha saptamī vāyavīya saṃhitā prārabhyate vyāsaḥ uvāca namaḥ śivāya somāya sa gaṇāya sa sūnave svāmi tvam ca vibhu tvam ca svabhāvam saṃpracakṣate tam ajam viśvakarmāṇam śāśvatam śivam avyayam mahādevam mahātmānam vrajāmi śaraṇam śivam dharmakṣetre mahā tīrthe gaṃgā kālindisaṃgame munayaḥ śaṃsita ātmānaḥ satya vrata parāyaṇāḥ tatra satram samākarṇya teṣām akliṣṭa karmaṇām sākṣāt satyavatī sūnoḥ vedavyāsasya dhīmataḥ śiṣyaḥ mahātmā medhāvī triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ madhuraḥ śravaṇānām ca manojña pada parvaṇām kathānām nipuṇaḥ vaktā kāla vid naya vid kaviḥ ājagāma sa tam deśam sūtaḥ paurāṇika uttamaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā sūtam āyāntam munayaḥ hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ tasmai sāma ca pūjām ca yathāvat pratyapādayan pratigṛhya satām pūjām munibhiḥ pratipāditām uddiṣṭa mānasam bheje niyuktaḥ yuktam ātmanaḥ tatas tad saṃgamāt eva munīnām bhāvitātmanām sa utkaṃṭham abhavat citam śrotum paurāṇikīm kathām tadā tam anukūlābhiḥ vāgbhiḥ pūjya mahā ṛṣayaḥ atīva abhimukham kṛtvā vacanam ca idam abruvan ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ saṃprāptā udya mahābhāga śaiva rāja mahāmate purāṇa vidyām akhilām vyāsāt pratyakṣam īyivān tasmāt āścarya bhūtānām kathānām tvam hi bhājanam ratnānām uru sārāṇām ratna ākaraḥ iva arṇavaḥ tvam adṛṣṭa vaśāt asmad darśana artham iha āgataḥ tasmāt śrāvyataram puṇyam sat kathā jñāna saṃhitam vedānta sāra sarvasvam purāṇam śrāvaya āśu naḥ ślakṣṇām ca nyāya saṃyuktām pratyuvāca śubhām giram sūtaḥ uvāca kasmāt samyak na vibrūyām purāṇam ṛṣi pūjitam abhivandya mahādevam devīm skandam vināyakam nandinam ca tathā vyāsam sākṣāt satyavatī sutam vakṣyāmi paramam puṇyam purāṇam veda saṃmitam śiva jñāna arṇavam sākṣāt bhakti mukti phala pradam śabda artha nyāya saṃyuktaiḥ rāgama arthaiḥ vibhūṣitam śvetakalpa prasaṃgena vāyunā kathitam purā vidyā sthānāni sarvāṇi purāṇa anukramam tathā aṃgāni vedāḥ catvāraḥ mīmāṃsā nyāya vistaraḥ purāṇam dharma śāstram ca vidyāḥ cetāḥ caturdaśa arthaśāstram param tasmāt vidyāḥ hi aṣṭādaśa smṛtāḥ aṣṭādaśānām vidyānām etāsām bhinna vartmanām ādikarttā kaviḥ sākṣāt śūlapāṇiḥ iti śrutiḥ brahmāṇam vidadhe sākṣāt putram agre sanātanam vidyāḥ ca imāḥ dadau pūrvam viśva sṛṣṭi artham īśvaraḥ pālanāya harim devam rakṣā śaktim dadau tatas madhyamam tanayam viṣṇum pātāram brahmaṇaḥ api hi labdha vidyena vidhinā prajā sṛṣṭim vitanvatā prathamam sarva śāstrāṇām purāṇam brahmaṇā smṛtam pravṛttiḥ sarva śāstrāṇām tad mukhāt abhavat tatas yadā asya vistaram śaktāḥ na adhigantum prajāḥ bhuvi tadā vidyā samāsa artham viśveśvara niyogataḥ dvāpara anteṣu viśvātmā viṣṇuḥ viśvaṃbharaḥ prabhuḥ evam vyastāḥ ca vedāḥ ca dvāpare dvāpare dvijāḥ nirmitāni purāṇāni anyāni ca tatas param sa punar dvāpare ca asmin kṛṣṇadvaipāyana ākhyayā araṇyām iva havya āśī satyavatyām ajāyata saṃkṣipya sa punar vedān caturddhā kṛtavān muniḥ purāṇānām ca saṃkṣiptam catur lakṣa pramāṇataḥ yaḥ vidyāt caturaḥ vedān sāṃga upaṇiṣadān dvijaḥ na ced purāṇam saṃvidyāt na eva sa syāt vicakṣaṇaḥ itihāsa purāṇābhyām vedam samupabṛṃhayet sargaḥ ca pratisargaḥ ca vaṃśaḥ manvantarāṇi ca vaṃśānucaritam ca eva purāṇam paṃca lakṣaṇam daśadhā ca aṣṭadhā ca etat purāṇam upadiśyate brāhmam pādmam vaiṣṇavam ca śaivam bhāgavatam tathā bhaviṣyam nāradīyam ca mārkaṃḍeyam atas param āgneyam brahmavaivartam laiṃgam vārāham eva ca skāndam ca vāmanam ca eva kaurmyam mātsyam ca gāruḍam brahmāṃḍam ca iti puṇyaḥ ayam purāṇānām anukramaḥ tatra śaivam turīyam yat śārvam sarva artha sādhakam granthaḥ lakṣa pramāṇam tat vyastam dvādaśa saṃhitam tad uktena eva dharmeṇa śaivāḥ traivarṇikāḥ narāḥ tam āśritya eva devānām api muktiḥ na ca anyathā yat idam śaivam ākhyātam purāṇam veda saṃmitam aumam mātṛpurāṇam ca rudraikādaśakam tathā kailāsam śatarudram ca śatarudrā ākhyam eva ca sahasra koṭi rudra ākhyam vāyavīyam tatas param dharma saṃjñam purāṇam ca iti evam dvādaśa saṃhitāḥ vidyeśam daśa sāhasram uditam grantha saṃkhyayā raudram vaināyakam caumam mātṛkā ākhyam tatas param raudraka adaśaka ākhyam yat kailāsam ṣaṣ sahasrakam śatarudram tri sāhasram koṭi rudram tatas param dharma saṃjñam purāṇam yat tat dvādaśa sahasrakam tat evam lakṣam uddiṣṭam śaivam śākhā vibhedataḥ vidyeśvara ākhyā tatra ādyā dvitīyā rudra saṃhitā tṛtīyā śatarudrā ākhyā koṭirudrā caturthikā paṃcamī kathitā ca umā ṣaṣṭhī kailāsa saṃhitā saptamī vāyavīya ākhyā saptā evam saṃhitāḥ iha vidyeśvaram dvi sāhasram raudram paṃcaśata ayutam triṃśat tathā dvi sāhasram sārddha ekaśatam īritam catvāriṃśat sa aṣṭaśatam kailāsam bhū sahasrakam catvāriṃśat ca dviśatam vāyavīyam atas param catur sāhasra saṃkhyākam evam saṃkhyā vibhedataḥ śrutam parama puṇyantu purāṇam śiva saṃjñakam catur sāhasrakam yat tu vāyavīyam udīritam na a veda viduṣe vācyam idam śāstram anuttamam na ca eva a śraddha dhānāya na a purāṇa vide tathā parīkṣitāya śiṣyāya dhārmikāya anasūyave pradeyam śiva bhaktāya śiva dharma anusāriṇe purāṇa saṃhitā yasya prasādāt mayi varttate iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe vidyāvatārakathanam nāma prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca purā kālena mahatā kalpeti ite punar punar pratiṣṭhitāyām vārtāyām prabuddhāsu prajāsu ca munīnām ṣaṭkulīyānām bruvatām itaretaram te abhijagmuḥ vidhātāram draṣṭum brahmāṇam avyayam yatra āste bhagavān brahmā stūyamānaḥ sura asuraiḥ meru śṛṃge śubhe ramye deva dānava saṃkule vihaṃga saṃgha saṃghuṣṭe maṇi vidruma bhūṣite tatra brahmavanam nāma nānā mṛga samākulam daśa yojana vistīrṇam śata yojanam āyatam taruṇa āditya saṃkāśam tatra cāru mahat puram durddharṣa bala dṛptānām daitya dānava rakṣasām tapta jāṃbūnada mayam prāṃśu prākāra toraṇam nirvyūha valabhī kūṭa pratolī śata maṃḍitam mahārha maṇi citrābhiḥ lelihānam iva aṃbaram mahā bhavana koṭībhiḥ anekābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam tatra gatvā mahātmānam sākṣāt lokapitāmaham śuddha cāmīkara prakhyam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam divya śukla aṃbara dharam divya mālā vibhūṣitam sarva lakṣaṇa yukta aṃgyā labdha cāmara hastayā tam dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ sarve prasanna vadana īkṣaṇāḥ śirasi aṃjalim ādhāya tuṣṭuvuḥ sura puṃgavam munayaḥ ūcuḥ puruṣāya purāṇāya brahmaṇe paramātmane namaḥ pradhāna dehāya pradhāna kṣobha kāriṇe trayoviṃśati bhedena vikṛtāya avikāriṇe namaḥ brahmāṇḍa dehāya brahmāṃḍa udara vartine tatra saṃsiddha kāryāya saṃsiddha karaṇāya ca tvayā eva nikhilam sṛṣṭam saṃhṛtam pālitam jagat tathā api māyayā nātha na vidmaḥ tvām pitāmaha sūtaḥ uvāca evam brahmā mahābhāgaiḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ abhiṣṭutaḥ prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā munīn prahlādayan iva ṛṣayaḥ he mahābhāgāḥ mahā sattvāḥ mahā ojasaḥ kimartham sahitāḥ sarve yūyam atra samāgatāḥ tam evam vādinam devam brahmāṇam brahma vittamāḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ bhagavan andhakāreṇa mahatā vayam āvṛtāḥ khinnāḥ vivadamānāḥ ca na paśyāmaḥ atra yat param tvam hi sarva jagat dhātā sarva kāraṇa kāraṇam kaḥ pumān sarva sattvebhyaḥ purāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ paraḥ viśuddhaḥ paripūrṇaḥ ca śāśvataḥ parameśvaraḥ tat tvam vada mahā prājña sva saṃdeha apanuttaye evam pṛṣṭaḥ tadā brahmā vismaya smera vīkṣaṇaḥ devānām dānavānām ca munīnām api sannidhau ānanda klinna sarva aṃgaḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ abhāṣata iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe muniprastāvavarṇanam nāma dvitīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ kāraṇānām ca yaḥ dhātā dhyātā parama kāraṇam sarva aiśvaryeṇa saṃpannaḥ nāmnā sarveśvaraḥ svayam sarvaiḥ mumukṣubhiḥ dhyeyaḥ śaṃbhuḥ ākāśa madhya gaḥ yaḥ agre mām vidadhe putram jñānam ca prahiṇoti me tad prasādāt mayā ālabdham prājāpatyam idam padam īśaḥ vṛkṣaḥ iva stabdhaḥ yaḥ ekaḥ divi tiṣṭhati yena idam akhilam pūrṇam puruṣeṇa mahātmanā ekaḥ bahūnām jantūnām niṣkriyāṇām ca sa kriyaḥ jīvaiḥ ebhiḥ imān lokān sarvān īśaḥ yaḥ īśate sadā janānām hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭaḥ api yaḥ paraiḥ alakṣyaḥ lakṣayan viśvam adhitiṣṭhati sarvadā yaḥ tu kālāt pramuktāni kāraṇāni akhilāni api svabhāvikī parāśaktiḥ nityā jñāna kriye api tau ubhau akṣara ātmānau ekaḥ devaḥ svayam haraḥ īśate tad abhidhyānāt yojana asattva bhāvanaḥ yasya bhāsā vibhāti idam iti eṣā śāśvatī śrutiḥ svatantraḥ paripūrṇaḥ ca sva icchā adhīnaḥ cara acaraḥ aprākṛta vapuḥ śrīmān lakṣya lakṣaṇa varjitaḥ ayam muktaḥ mocakaḥ ca hi akālaḥ kāla codakaḥ sarva uparikṛta āvāsaḥ sarva āvāsaḥ ca sarva vid akhaṃḍa jagat aṃḍānām piṃḍīkaraṇa paṃḍitaḥ audārya vīrya gāṃbhīrya mādhurya makara ālayaḥ na eva asya sadṛśam vastu na adhikam ca api kiṃcana atulaḥ sarva bhūtānām rājarājaḥ ca tiṣṭhati asya bhūtāni vaśyāni ayam sarva niyojakaḥ ayam tu parayā bhaktyā dṛśyate na anyathā kvacid vratāni sarva dānāni tapāṃsi niyamāḥ tathā kathitāni purā sadbhiḥ bhāva artham na atra saṃśayaḥ hariḥ ca aham ca rudraḥ ca tathā anye ca sura asurāḥ tapobhiḥ ugraiḥ adya api tasya darśana kāṃkṣiṇaḥ bhaktaiḥ antar bahis ca api pūjyaḥ saṃbhāṣyaḥ eva ca tat idam trividham rūpam sthūlam sūkṣmam tatas param asmat ādi amaraiḥ dṛśyam sthūlam sūkṣmam tu yogibhiḥ tad niṣṭhaiḥ tad paraiḥ bhaktaiḥ dṛśyam tad vratam āśritaiḥ prasādāt eva sā bhaktiḥ prasādaḥ bhakti saṃbhavaḥ yathā ca aṃkurataḥ bījam bījataḥ vā yathā aṃkuraḥ tad abhyāsa vaśāt sāmyam pūrvayoḥ puṇya pāpayoḥ sāmyāt prasāda saṃparkaḥ dharmasya atiśayaḥ tatas dharma atiśayam āsādya paśoḥ pāpa parikṣayaḥ evam prakṣīṇa pāpasya bahubhiḥ janmabhiḥ kramāt sa aṃbe sarveśvare bhaktiḥ jñāna pūrvā prajāyate bhāva anuguṇam īśasya prasādaḥ vyatiricyate prasādāt karma saṃtyāgaḥ phalataḥ na svarūpataḥ tasmāt karma phala tyāgāt śiva dharma anvayaḥ śubhaḥ tatra anapekṣāt sāpekṣaḥ mukhyaḥ śataguṇa adhikaḥ śiva dharma anvayasya asya śiva jñāna samanvayaḥ jñanā anvaya vaśāt puṃsaḥ saṃsāre doṣa darśanam tatas viṣaya vairāgyam vairāgyāt bhāva sādhanam yādṛśī yogyatā puṃsaḥ tasya tādṛś anugrahaḥ bālaḥ vā taruṇaḥ vā atha vṛddhaḥ vā mucyate paraḥ kaścid kṣīṇa padaḥ bhūtvā punar āvartya mucyate tasmāt nā eka prakāreṇa narāṇām muktiḥ iṣyate jñāna bhāva anurūpeṇa prasādena eva nirvṛtiḥ tasmāt asya prasāda artham vā ā manaḥ doṣa varjitāḥ dhyāyantaḥ śivam eva ekam sa dāra tanaya agnayaḥ tad niṣṭhāḥ tad parāḥ sarve tad yuktāḥ tad upāśrayāḥ sarva kriyāḥ prakurvāṇāḥ tam eva manasā āgatāḥ saḥ eva bhavataḥ śreyaḥ sa upāyam kathayiṣyati tatas vārāṇasī puṇyā purī parama śobhanā gantavyā yatra viśveśaḥ devyā saha pinākadhṛk sadā viharati śrīmān bhakta anugraha kāraṇāt tatra āścaryam mahat dṛṣṭvā mad samīpam gamiṣyatha tatas vaḥ kathayiṣyāmi mokṣa upāya dvijottamāḥ aneka janma saṃsāra bandha nirmokṣa kāriṇī etat manaḥ mayam cakram mayā sṛṣṭam visṛjyate yatra asya śīryate nemiḥ sa deśaḥ tapasaḥ śubhaḥ iti uktvā sūrya saṃkāśam cakram dṛṣṭvā manaḥ mayam te api hṛṣṭatarāḥ viprāḥ praṇamya jagatām prabhum cakram tat api saṃkṣiptam ślakṣṇam cāru śilā tale tat vanam tena vikhyātam naimiṣam muni pūjitam aṣṭādaśa samudrasya dvīpān aśnan purūravāḥ vilāsa vaśam urvaśyā yātaḥ daivena coditaḥ akrameṇa haran mohāt yajña vāṭam hiraṇmayam viśvam sisṛkṣamāṇāḥ vai yatra viśvasṛjaḥ purā satram ārebhire divyam brahma jñāḥ gārhapatya gāḥ ṛṣibhiḥ yatra vidvadbhiḥ śabda artha nyāya kovidaiḥ śakti prajñā kriyā yogaiḥ vidhiḥ āsīt anuṣṭhitaḥ sphaṭika maya mahībhṛt pāda jābhyaḥ śilābhyaḥ prasarat amṛta kalpaḥ svaccha pānīya ramyam ati rasa phala vṛkṣa prāyam avyāla sattvam tapasaḥ ucitam āsīt naimiṣam tat munīnām iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe naimiṣopākhyānam nāma tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca tasmin deśe mahābhāgāḥ munayaḥ śaṃsita vratāḥ tat ca satram pravavṛte sarva āścaryam mahā ṛṣiṇām viśvam sisṛkṣamāṇānām purā viśvasṛjām iva śiṣyaḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ devaḥ sarva pratyakṣa dṛś vaśī ājñāyām marutaḥ yasya saṃsthitāḥ saptasaptakāḥ prerayan śaśvat aṃgāni prāṇa ādyābhiḥ sva vṛttibhiḥ sarva bhūta śarīrāṇām kurute yaḥ ca dhāraṇam aṇima ādibhiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ aiśvaryaiḥ ca samanvitaḥ ākāśa yoniḥ dviguṇaḥ sparśa śabda samanvayāt tejasām prakṛtiḥ ca iti yam āhuḥ tattva cintakāḥ tam āśrama gatam dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ dīrgha satriṇaḥ pitāmaha vacaḥ smṛtvā praharṣam atulam yayuḥ cāmīkara mayam tasmai viṣṭaram samakalpayan vāyuḥ uvāca atra vaḥ kuśalam viprāḥ kaccit vṛtte mahā kratau prāyaścittam duriṣṭam vā na kaccit samajāyata kaccit abhyarcya yuṣmābhiḥ vidhiḥ āsīt su anuṣṭhitaḥ nivṛtte ca mahā satre paścāt kim vaḥ cikīrṣitam iti uktāḥ munayaḥ sarve vāyunā śiva bhāvinā prahṛṣṭa manasaḥ pūtāḥ pratyūcuḥ vinaya anvitāḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ śṛṇu ca idam purāvṛttam tamasā ākrānta mānasaiḥ upāsitaḥ purā asmābhiḥ vijñāna artham prajāpatiḥ saḥ upi asmān anugṛhya āha śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇa āgatān bhaktiḥ ca asya prasādena prasādāt eva nirvṛtiḥ iti ādiśya vayam sarve preṣitā parameṣṭhinā asmin deśe mahābhāga tava āgamana kāṃkṣiṇaḥ dīrgha satram samāsīnāḥ divya varṣa sahasrakam iti ākarṇya purāvṛttam ṛṣīṇām dīrgha satriṇām vāyuḥ prīta manāḥ bhūtvā tatra āsīt muni saṃvṛtaḥ tatas taiḥ munibhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ teṣām bhāva vivṛddhaye sarga ādi śārvam aiśvaryam samāsāda vadat vibhuḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe vāyusamāgamaḥ nāma caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca tatra pūrvam mahābhāgāḥ naimiṣa araṇya vāsinaḥ naimiṣīyāḥ ūcuḥ bhavān katham anuprāptaḥ jñānam īśvara gocaram vāyuḥ uvāca ekonaviṃśatiḥ kalpaḥ vijñeyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ tapasā tena tīvreṇa tuṣṭaḥ tasya pitā svayam divyam kaumāram āsthāya rūpam rūpavatām varaḥ śvetaḥ nāma muniḥ bhūtvā divyām vācam udīrayan tam dṛṣṭvā pitaram brahmā brahmaṇaḥ adhipatim patim praṇamya parama jñānam gāyatryā saha labdhavān asṛjat sarva bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca yatas śrutvā amṛtam labdham brahmaṇā parameśvarāt munayaḥ ūcuḥ kim tat jñānam tvayā labdham tathyāt tathī antaram śubham yatra kṛtvā parām niṣṭhām puruṣaḥ sukham ṛcchati paśu pāśa pati jñānam yat labdham tu mayā purā tatra niṣṭhā parā kāryā puruṣeṇa sukha arthinā ajñāna prabhavam duḥkham jñānena eva nivarttate paśuḥ pāśaḥ patiḥ ca iti kathyate tat trayam kramāt akṣaram ca kṣaram ca eva kṣara akṣara param tathā akṣaram paśuḥ iti uktaḥ kṣaram pāśaḥ udāhṛtaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ kim tat akṣaram iti uktam kim ca kṣaram udāhṛtam tayoḥ ca paramam kim vā tat etat brūhi māruta vāyuḥ uvāca prakṛtiḥ kṣaram iti uktam puruṣaḥ akṣaraḥ ucyate munayaḥ ūcuḥ kā eṣā prakṛtiḥ iti uktā kaḥ eṣa puruṣaḥ mataḥ anayoḥ kena sambandhaḥ kaḥ ayam prerakaḥ īśvaraḥ vāyuḥ uvāca māyā prakṛtiḥ uddiṣṭā puruṣaḥ māyayā vṛtaḥ saṃbandhaḥ mūlakarmabhyām śivaḥ prerakaḥ īśvaraḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ kā iyam māyā samā khyātā kiṃrūpaḥ māyayā vṛtaḥ mūlam kīdṛś kutas vā asya kim śiva tvam kutas śivaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca māyā māheśvarī śaktiḥ cit rūpaḥ māyayā vṛtaḥ malaḥ cicchādakaḥ naijaḥ viśuddhiḥ śivatā svatas munayaḥ ūcuḥ āvṛṇoti katham māyā vyāpinam kena hetunā kimartham ca āvṛtiḥ puṃsaḥ kena vā vinivartate vāyuḥ uvāca āvṛtiḥ vyapinaḥ syāt vyāpi yasmāt kalā ādi api munayaḥ ūcuḥ tat kimādi kim antam vā kim phalam vā kimāśrayam mala kṣayasya kaḥ hetuḥ kīdṛś kṣīṇa malaḥ pumān vāyuḥ uvāca kalā ādayaḥ samākhyātāḥ yaḥ bhoktā puruṣaḥ bhavet anādi mala bhoga antam ajñāna ātma samāśrayam bāhya antaḥkaraṇa dvāram śarīram bhoga sādhanam bhāva atiśaya labdhena prasādena mala kṣayaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ kalā ādi paṃcatattvānām kim karma pṛthak ucyate kimātmakam tat avyaktam kena ākāreṇa bhujyate kim tasya śaraṇam bhuktau śarīram ca kim ucyate vāyuḥ uvāca avyaktam kāraṇam yat tat triguṇam prabhava apyayam pradhānam prakṛtiḥ ca iti yat āhuḥ tattva cintakāḥ sukha duḥkha vimoha ātmā bhujyate guṇavān tridhā sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ iti guṇāḥ prakṛti saṃbhavāḥ prakṛtau sūkṣma rūpeṇa tile tailam iva sthitāḥ sukham ca sukha hetuḥ ca samāsāt sāttvikam smṛtam sāttvikī ūrdhva gatiḥ proktā tāmasī syāt adhas gatiḥ madhyamā tu gatiḥ yā sā rājasī paripaṭhyate tanmātra pañcakam ca eva bhūta paṃcakam eva ca jñāna indriyāṇi paṃca aikyam paṃca karmendriyāṇi ca pradhāna buddhi ahaṃkāra manāṃsi ca catuṣṭayam samāsāt evam avyaktam sa vikāram udāhṛtam vyaktam kārya daśā āpannam śarīra ādi ghaṭa ādi vat yathā ghaṭa ādikam kāryam mṛd ādeḥ na ati bhidyate śarīra ādi tathā vyaktam avyaktāt na ati bhidyate tasmāt avyaktam eva aikya kāraṇam karaṇāni ca śarīram ca tad ādhāram tat bhogyam ca api na itarat munayaḥ ūcuḥ vāyuḥ uvāca buddhīndriya śarīrāṇām na ātmatā sadbhiḥ iṣyate smṛteḥ aniyata jñānāt ayāvat deha vedanāt atas smartā anubhūtānām aśeṣa jñeya gocaraḥ antaryyāmī iti vedeṣu vedānteṣu ca gīyate sarvam tatra sa sarvatra vyāpya tiṣṭhati śāśvataḥ tathā api kvāpi kena api vyaktam eṣa na dṛśyate na eva ayam cakṣuṣā grāhyaḥ na aparaiḥ indriyaiḥ api na ca strī na pumān eṣa nā eva ca api napuṃsakaḥ aśarīram śarīreṣu caleṣu sthāṇum avyayam sadā paśyati tam dhīraḥ naraḥ pratyavamarśanāt vipadām vīja bhūtena puruṣaḥ tena saṃyutaḥ sukhī duḥkhī ca mūḍhaḥ ca bhavati svena karmaṇā adbhiḥ āplavitam kṣetram janayati aṃkuram yathā ājñānāt plāvitam karma deham janayate tathā atyantam asukha āvāsāḥ smṛtāḥ ca ekānta mṛtyavaḥ anāgatāḥ atītāḥ ca tanavaḥ asya sahasraśas āgatya āgatya śīrṇeṣu śarīreṣu śarīriṇaḥ chāditaḥ ca viyuktaḥ ca śarīraiḥ eṣu lakṣyate aṣṭāpada parikṣepe hi akṣa mudrā iva lakṣyate pathi saṃgamaḥ eva ayam dāraiḥ putraiḥ ca bandhubhiḥ yathā kāṣṭham ca kāṣṭham ca sameyātām mahā udadhau sametya ca vyapeyātām tadvat bhūta samāgamaḥ sa paśyati śarīram tat śarīram tat na paśyati tau paśyati paraḥ kaścid tau ubhau tam na paśyataḥ brahma ādyāḥ sthāvara antar ca paśavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ paśūnām eva sarveṣām proktam etat nidarśanam saḥ eṣa badhyate pāśaiḥ sukha duḥkha aśanaḥ paśuḥ līlā sādhana bhūtaḥ yaḥ īśvarasya iti sūrayaḥ ajñaḥ jantuḥ anīśaḥ ātmanaḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ sūtaḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya anila vacaḥ munayaḥ prīta mānasāḥ procuḥ praṇamya tam vāyum śaiva āgama vicakṣaṇam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe śivatattvajñānavarṇanam nāma paṃcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ yaḥ ayam paśuḥ iti proktaḥ yaḥ ca pāśaḥ udāhṛtaḥ abhyām vilakṣaṇaḥ kaścid koyam asti tayoḥ patiḥ vāyuḥ uvāca asti kaścid aparyanta ramaṇīya guṇa āśrayaḥ patiḥ viśvasya nirmātā paśu pāśa vimocanaḥ abhāve tasya viśvasya sṛṣṭiḥ eṣā katham bhavet acetana tvāt ajñānāt anayoḥ paśu pāśayoḥ pradhāna paramāṇu ādi yāvat kiṃcid acetanam tad kartṛkam svayam dṛṣṭam buddhimat kāraṇam vinā jagat ca kartṛ sāpekṣam kāryam sa avayavam yatas tasmāt kāryasya kartṛ tvam patyuḥ na paśu pāśayoḥ paśoḥ api ca kartṛ tvam patyuḥ preraṇa pūrvakam ayathā karaṇa jñānam andhasya gamanam yathā ātmānam ca pṛthak matvā preritāram tatas pṛthak vyakta avyaktam bibharti īśaḥ viśvam viśva vimocakaḥ na atas param vijānadbhiḥ veditavyam hi kiṃcanaḥ yathā āpaḥ srotasi vyāptāḥ yathā araṇyām hutāśanaḥ evam eva mahātmānam ātmani ātma vilakṣaṇam yaḥ ekaḥ jālavān īśaḥ īśānībhiḥ sva śaktibhiḥ sarvān lokān imān kṛtvā ekaḥ eva saḥ īśate saṃsṛjya viśva bhuvanam goptā te saṃcukoca yaḥ viśvatas cakṣuḥ eva ayam uta ayam viśvatomukhaḥ tathā eva viśvatobāhu viśvatas pāda saṃyutaḥ dyāvābhūmī ca janayan devaḥ ekaḥ maheśvaraḥ veda aham etam puruṣam mahāntam amṛtam dhruvam āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt saṃsthitam prabhum asmāt nā asti param kiṃcid aparam paramātmanaḥ na aṇīyaḥ asti na ca jyāyaḥ tena pūrṇam idam jagat sarva ānana śiraḥ grīvaḥ sarva bhūta guhā āśayaḥ sarvavyāpī ca bhagavān tasmāt sarva gataḥ śivaḥ sarvatas pāṇi pādaḥ ayam sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukhaḥ sarvatas śrutimān loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati sarvasya prabhuḥ īśānaḥ sarvasya śaraṇam suhṛd a cakṣuḥ api yaḥ paśyati a karṇaḥ api śṛṇoti yaḥ sarvam vetti na vettā asya tam āhuḥ puruṣam param aṇoḥ aṇīyān mahataḥ mahīyān ayam avyayaḥ guhāyām nihitaḥ ca api jantoḥ asya maheśvaraḥ tam akratum kratu prāyam mahima atiśaya anvitam dhātuḥ prasādāt īśānam vīta śokaḥ prapaśyati veda aham enam ajaram purāṇam sarvagam vibhum ekaḥ api trīn imān lokān bahudhā śakti yogataḥ viśvadhātrī iti ajā ākhyā ca śaivī citrā kṛtiḥ parā tām ajām lohitām śuklām kṛṣṇām ekām tu ajaḥ prajām janitrīm anuśete anyaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ svarūpiṇīm vṛkṣe ismin puruṣaḥ magnaḥ guhyamānaḥ ca śocati juṣṭam anyam yadā paśyet īśam parama kāraṇam tadā asya mahimānam ca vīta śokaḥ sukhī bhavet chandāṃsi yajñāḥ ṛtavaḥ yat bhūtam bhavyam eva ca māyī viśvam sṛjati asmin niviṣṭaḥ māyayā paraḥ māyām tu prakṛtim vidyāt māyinam tu maheśvaram sūkṣma ati sūkṣmam īśānam kalalasya api madhyatas sraṣṭāram api viśvasya veṣṭitāram ca tasya tu śivam eva īśvaram jñātvā śāntim atyantam ṛcchati saḥ eva kālaḥ goptā ca viśvasya adhipatiḥ prabhuḥ tam viśva adhipatim jñātvā mṛtyu pāśāt pramucyate ghṛtāt param maṃḍam iva sūkṣmam jñātvā sthitam prabhum sarva bhūteṣu gūḍham ca sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭam tam jñātvā eva amṛtam aśnute kevalaḥ śivaḥ eva ekaḥ yatas prajñā purātanī rudrasya asya prapadyante rakṣā artham dakṣiṇam sukham kṣaram tu avidyā hi amṛtam vidyā iti parigīyate sarva ādhipatyam kurute sṛṣṭvā sarvān pratāpavān svabhāva vācakān sarvān vācyān ca pariṇāmayan guṇān ca bhogya bhoktṛ tve tat viśvam adhitiṣṭhati te vai guhya upaṇiṣadi gūḍham brahma parātparam bhāva grāhyam anīha ākhyam bhāva abhāva karam śivam yena idam āvṛtam nityam kāla kāla ātmanā yatas tat karma bhūyaśas kṛtvā vinivṛtya ca bhūyaśas aṣṭābhiḥ ca tribhiḥ ca evam dvābhyām ca ekena vā punar kālena ātma guṇaiḥ ca api kṛtsnam eva jagat svayam guṇaiḥ ārabhya karmāṇi svabhāva ādīni yojayet teṣām abhāve nāśaḥ syāt kṛtasya api ca karmaṇaḥ tam viśvarūpam abhavam bhavam īḍyam prajāpatim kāla ādibhiḥ paraḥ yasmāt prapaṃcaḥ parivartate dharma āvaham pāpa nudam bhoga īśam viśva dhāma ca tam īśvarāṇām paramam maheśvaram tam devatānām paramam ca daivatam patim patīnām paramam parastāt vidāma devam bhuvaneśvara īśvaram parā asya vividhā śaktiḥ śrutau svābhāvikī śrutā jñānam balam kriyā ca eva yābhyaḥ viśvam idam kṛtam tasya asti patiḥ kaścid nā eva liṃgam na ca īśitā kāraṇam kāraṇānām ca sa teṣām adhipa adhipaḥ na janma hetavaḥ tadvat mala māyā ādi saṃjñakāḥ saḥ ekaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ vyāptaḥ ca viśvatas sarva bhūta adhivāsaḥ ca sākṣī cetā ca nirguṇaḥ ekaḥ vaśī niṣkriyāṇām bahūnām vivaśa ātmanām nityānām api asau nityaḥ cetanānām ca cetanaḥ ekaḥ bahūnām ca akāmaḥ kāmān īśaḥ prayacchati sāṃkhya yoga adhigamyam yatkāraṇam jagatām patim jñātvā devam paśuḥ pāśaiḥ sarvaiḥ eva vimucyate pradhānaḥ kṣetrajña patiḥ guṇa īśaḥ pāśa mocakaḥ brahmāṇam vidadhe pūrvam vedān ca upādiśat svayam mumukṣuḥ asmāt saṃsārāt prapadye śaraṇam śivam niṣphalam niṣkriyam śāntam niravadyam niraṃjanam yadā carma vat ākāśam veṣṭayiṣyanti mānavāḥ tadā śivam a vijñāya duḥkhasya antaḥ bhaviṣyati tapaḥ prabhāvāt devasya prasādāt ca mahā ṛṣayaḥ ati āśrama ucita jñānam pavitram pāpa nāśanam na apraśāntāya dātavyam etat jñānam anuttamam na putrāya āśu vṛttāya na a śiṣyāya ca sarvathā tasya ete kathitāḥ ahi arthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ atas ca saṃkṣepam idam śṛṇudhvam śivaḥ parastāt prakṛteḥ ca puṃsaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe śivatattvavarṇanam nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ yadā asya antargatam viśvam śaśvat saṃsāra maṇḍalam brahmā hariḥ ca rudraḥ ca tathā anye ca sura asurāḥ kaḥ eṣa bhagavān kālaḥ kasya vā vaśa vartī ayam vāyuḥ uvāca kāla kāṣṭhā nimeṣa ādi kalā kalita vigraham kāla ātmā iti samākhyātam tejaḥ māheśvaram param niyoga rūpam īśasya balam viśva niyāmakam tasya aṃśa aṃśa mayī muktiḥ kāla ātmani mahātmani tatas niṣkramya saṃkrāntā visṛṣṭa agreḥ iva āyasī tasmāt kāla vaśe viśvam na sa viśva vaśe sthitaḥ śivasya tu vaśe kālaḥ na kālasya vaśe śivaḥ yatas a pratihatam śārvam tejaḥ kāle pratiṣṭhitam kālam prajñā viśeṣeṇa kaḥ ativartitum arhati eka chatrām mahīm kṛtsnām ye parākramya śāsati āyurveda vidaḥ vaidyāḥ tu anuṣṭhita rasāyanāḥ śriyā rūpeṇa śīlena balena ca kulena ca durvijñeya svabhāvasya kāla asya aho vicitra tā yaḥ niḥśrīkaḥ kālaḥ citra gatiḥ dvijā na ābhijātyam na vai śīlam na balam na ca naipuṇam bhavet kāryāya paryāptam kālaḥ ca hi anirodhakaḥ ye sa nāthāḥ ca dātāraḥ gīta vādyaiḥ upasthitāḥ ye ca anāthāḥ para anna ādāḥ kālaḥ teṣu sama kriyaḥ tāni eva kālena samāhṛtāni siddhim prayānti āśu sukham diśanti na akālatas ayam mriyate jāyate vā na akālatas puṣṭim agryām upaiti na akālataḥ sukhitam duḥkhitam vā na akālikam vastu samasti kiṃcid kālena śītaḥ prativāti vātaḥ kālena vṛṣṭiḥ jaladān upaiti kālena ca ūṣmā praśamam prayāti kālena sarvam saphalatvam eti kālena sasyāni layam prayānti kālena saṃjīvati jīva lokaḥ ittham kāla ātmanaḥ tattvam yaḥ vijānāti tattvataḥ kāla ātmānam atikramya kāla atītam sa paśyati iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe kālamahimavarṇanam nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ saṃkhyā rūpasya kālasya kaḥ punar paramaḥ avadhiḥ vāyuḥ uvāca āyuṣaḥ saṃkhyā rūpasya kālasya śānttu atīta kalā avadhi akṣi pakṣma parikṣepaḥ nimeṣaḥ parikalpitaḥ tādṛśānām nimeṣāṇām kāṣṭhāḥ daśa ca paṃca ca kāṣṭhān triṃśatkalāḥ nāma kalān triṃśat muhūrtakaḥ muhūrttānām api triṃśat ahorātram pracakṣate triṃśat saṃkhyaiḥ ahorātraiḥ māsaḥ pakṣa dvaya ātmakaḥ jñeyam pitryam ahorātram māsaḥ kṛṣṇa sita ātmakaḥ māsaiḥ taiḥ ayanam ṣaḍbhiḥ varṣam dve ca ayanam matam laukikena eva mānena abdaḥ yaḥ mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ dakṣiṇam ca ayanam rātriḥ tathā udagayanam dinam māsaḥ triṃśat ahorātraiḥ divyaḥ mānuṣa vat smṛtaḥ devānām māsaiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ tathā trīṇi varṣa śatāni eva ṣaṣṭi varṣa yutāni api divyaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ jñeyaḥ mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitaḥ pūrvam kṛta yugam nāma tatas tretā vidhīyate dvāparam ca kaliḥ ca eva yugāni etāni kṛtsnaśas catvāri tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām tat kṛtam yugam tasya tāvacchatī sandhyā sandhyā aṃśaḥ ca tathāvidhaḥ itareṣu sa sandhyeṣu sa sandhyāṃśeṣu ca triṣu eka apāyena vartante sahasrāṇi śatāni ca etat dvādaśa sāhasram sa adhikam ca caturyugam kalpe caturdaśa ekasmin manūnām parivṛttayaḥ sa prajāni vyatītāni śataśas atha sahasraśas ajñeya tvāt ca sarveṣām asaṃkhyeya tayā punar śakyaḥ na eva ānupūrvyāt vai teṣām vaktum su vistaraḥ kalpānām vai sahasram ca brāhmam varṣam iha ucyate varṣāṇām aṣṭa sāhasram yat ca tat brahmaṇaḥ yugam savanānām sahasram ca triguṇam trivṛtam tathā kalpyate sakalaḥ kālaḥ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ śatāni māse catvāri viṃśatyā sahitāni ca abde paṃca sahasrāṇi catvāriṃśat yutāni ca catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi paṃca lakṣāṇi ca āyuṣi brahmā viṣṇoḥ dine ca ekaḥ viṣṇuḥ rudra dine tathā sākṣāt śivasya tad saṃkhyaḥ tathā saḥ api sadāśivaḥ catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi paṃca lakṣāṇi ca āyuṣi tasmin sākṣāt śivena eṣa kāla ātmā sampravartate yat tat sṛṣṭeḥ samākhyātam kāla antaram iha dvijāḥ etat kāla antaram jñeyam ahar vai pārameśvaram rātriḥ ca tāvatī jñeyā parameśasya kṛtsnaśas ahar tasya tu yā sṛṣṭī rātriḥ ca pralayaḥ smṛtaḥ eṣa upacāraḥ kriyate lokānām hita kāmyayā prajāḥ prajānām patayaḥ mūrttayaḥ ca sura asurāḥ indriyāṇi indriya arthāḥ ca mahābhūtāni paṃca ca tanmātrāṇi atha bhūtādiḥ buddhiḥ ca saha daivataḥ ahar tiṣṭhanti sarvāṇi pārameśasya dhīmataḥ yaḥ viśvātmā karma kāla svabhāva ādi arthe śaktiḥ yasya na ullaṃghanīyā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva bhāge kālaprabhāve tridevāyurvarṇanam nāma aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ katham jagat idam kṛtsnam vidhāya ca nidhāya ca ājñayā paramām krīḍām karoti parameśvaraḥ kena vā punar eva idam grasyate pṛthu kukṣiṇā vāyuḥ uvāca śaktiḥ prathama sambhūtā śānti atīta pada uttarā tatas māyā tatas avyaktam śivāt śaktimataḥ prabhoḥ śānti atīta padam śakteḥ tatas śānti pada kramāt tatas vidyā padam tasmāt pratiṣṭhā pada saṃbhavaḥ nivṛtti padam utpannam pratiṣṭhā padataḥ kramāt evam uktā samāsena sṛṣṭiḥ īśvara coditā ānulomyāt tathā eteṣām pratilomyena saṃhṛtiḥ asmāt pañca pada uddiṣṭāt paraḥ sraṣṭā samiṣyate kalābhiḥ paṃcabhiḥ vyāptam tasmāt viśvam idam jagat avyaktam kāraṇam yat tat ātmanā samanuṣṭhitam mahat ādi viśeṣa antam sṛjati iti api saṃmatam kim tu tatra api kartṛ tvam na avyaktasya na ca ātmanaḥ pradhāna paramāṇu ādi yāvat kiñcid acetanam tad kartṛkam svayam dṛṣṭam buddhimat kāraṇam vinā jagat ca kartṛ sāpekṣam kāryam sa avayavam yatas an ādi nidhanaḥ ca ayam mahat aiśvarya saṃyutaḥ saḥ eva jagataḥ kartā mahādevaḥ maheśvarāḥ pātā hartā ca sarvasya tatas pṛthak ananvayaḥ pariṇāmaḥ pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ puruṣasya ca iti iyam śāśvatī niṣṭhā satām manasi vartate yāvat ādi samāraṃbhaḥ yāvat yaḥ pralayaḥ mahān tāvat apyeti sakalam brahmaṇaḥ śāradām śatam avyaktam ātmanaḥ kāryam ādāya ātmani tiṣṭhati sādharmyeṇa adhitiṣṭhete pradhāna puruṣau ubhau śānta vāta eka nīre ca na prājñāyata kiṃcana upāsya rajanīm kṛtsnām parām māheśvarīm tatas prabhātāyām tu śarvaryām pradhāna puruṣau ubhau praviśya kṣobhayāmāsa māyā yogāt maheśvaraḥ tatas punar aśeṣāṇām bhūtānām prabhava apyayāt avyaktāt abhavat sṛṣṭiḥ ājñayā parameṣṭhinaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva bhāge sṛṣṭipālanapralayakartṛtvavarṇanam nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca puruṣa dhiṣṭhitāt pūrvam avyaktāt īśvara ājñayā buddhi ādayaḥ viśeṣa antāḥ vikārāḥ ca abhavan kramāt kāraṇa tvena sarveṣām trayaḥ devāḥ prajajñire jñānam apratimam śaśvat aiśvaryam ca aṇima ādikam sṛṣṭi sthiti laya ākhyeṣu karmasu triṣu hetutām prabhu tvena saha eteṣām prasīdati maheśvaraḥ sarga rakṣā laya ācāram pratyekam pradadau ca saḥ na anena teṣām ādhikyam aiśvaryam ca atiricyate mūrkhāḥ nindanti tān vāgbhiḥ saṃraṃbha abhiniveśinaḥ yātudhānāḥ bhavanti eva piśācāḥ ca na saṃśayaḥ devaḥ guṇatraya atītaḥ catur vyūhaḥ maheśvaraḥ saḥ ayam ātmā trayasya asya prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca līlā kṛta jagat sṛṣṭiḥ īśvara tve vyavasthitaḥ saḥ eva ca tad ādhāraḥ tad ātmā tad adhiṣṭhitaḥ tasmāt maheśvaraḥ ca eva prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ tathā sadāśiva bhavaḥ viṣṇuḥ brahmā sarva śiva ātmakam pradhānāt prathamam jajñe vṛddhiḥ khyātiḥ matiḥ mahān ahaṃkāraḥ ca bhūtāni tanmātrāni indriyāṇi ca vaikārikāt ahaṃkārāt sattva udriktāt tu sāttvikaḥ buddhīndriyāṇi paṃca eva paṃca karmendriyāṇi ca tamaḥ yuktāt ahaṃkārāt bhūta tanmātra saṃbhavaḥ bhūtānām ādi bhūta tvāt bhūtādiḥ kathyate tu saḥ bhūtādeḥ śabda mātram syāt tatra ca ākāśa saṃbhavaḥ ākāśāt sparśaḥ utpannaḥ sparśāt vāyu samudbhavaḥ gandhāt ca pṛthivī jātā bhūtebhyaḥ nyat carācaram puruṣa dhiṣṭhita tvāt ca avyakta anugraheṇa ca mahat ādi viśeṣa antāḥ hi aṇḍam utpādayanti te tatra kāryam ca karaṇam saṃsiddham brahmaṇaḥ yadā tad aṃḍe su pravṛddhaḥ abhūt kṣetrajñaḥ brahma saṃjñitaḥ ādikartā sa bhūtānām brahma agre samavartata tasya īśvarasya pratimā jñāna vairāgya lakṣaṇā dharma aiśvarya karī buddhiḥ brāhmī yajñe vaśī vikṛtvāt traiguṇyāt sāpekṣa tvāt svabhāvataḥ viṣṇu tve kevalam sattvam guṇa vṛddhiḥ tridhā vibhau caturddhā pravibhakta tvāt cāturvyūhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ādi tvāt ādidevaḥ asau ajāta tvāt ajaḥ smṛtaḥ pāti yasmāt prajāḥ sarvāḥ prajāpatiḥ iti smṛtaḥ garbha udakam samudrāḥ ca jarāyuḥ ca api parvatāḥ adbhiḥ daśaguṇābhiḥ tu bāhya toṇḍam samāvṛtam āpaḥ daśaguṇena eva tejasā bahis āvṛtāḥ tejaḥ daśaguṇena eva vāyunā bahis āvṛtam ākāśena āvṛtaḥ vāyuḥ kham ca bhūtādinā āvṛtam bhūtādiḥ mahatā tadvat avyaktena āvṛtaḥ mahān etaiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ aṇḍam saptabhiḥ bahis āvṛtam etat āvṛttya ca anyonyam aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ sthitāḥ sṛṣṭi pālana vidhvaṃsa karma kartryaḥ dvijottamāḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāvena vikārāḥ tu vikāriṣu kūrma ūṃgāni yathā pūrvam prasāryya viniyacchati vikārān ca tathā avyaktam sṛṣṭvā bhūyas niyacchati guṇāḥ kāla vaśāt eva bhavanti viṣamāḥ samāḥ guṇa sāmye layaḥ jñeyaḥ vaiṣamye sṛṣṭiḥ ucyate tat idam brahmaṇaḥ yoniḥ etat aṃḍam ghanam mahat brahmaṇaḥ kṣetram uddiṣṭam brahmā kṣetrajñaḥ ucyate iti īdṛśānām aṇḍānām koṭyaḥ jñeyāḥ sahasraśas sṛṣṭā pradhānena tathā labdhvā śaṃbhoḥ tu sannidhim aṇḍāt jajñe vibhuḥ brahmā lokāḥ tena kṛtāḥ tu ime ātyantikaḥ ca pralaya unta kāle līlā kṛtaḥ kevalam īśvarasya yat tat smṛtam kāraṇam aprameyam brahmā pradhānam prakṛteḥ prasūtiḥ anādi madhya antam ananta vīryam śuklam su raktam puruṣeṇa yuktam aṣṭau vikārān api ca ādi kāle sṛṣṭvā samaśnāti tathā antakāle prakṛti avasthāpita kāraṇānām yā ca sthitiḥ yā ca punar pravṛttiḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām brahmāṃḍasthitivarṇanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ munayaḥ ūcuḥ manvantarāṇi sarvāṇi kalpa bhedān ca sarvaśas vāyuḥ uvāca kāla saṃkhyā vivṛttasya parārddhaḥ brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ tāvān ca eva asya kālaḥ nyaḥ tasya ante pratisṛjyate caturdaśa mahābhāgāḥ manūnām parivṛttayaḥ anādi tvāt ananta tvāt ajñeya tvāt ca kṛtsnaśas manvantarāṇi kalpāḥ ca na śakyāḥ vacanāt pṛthak ukteṣu api ca sarveṣu śṛṇvatām vaḥ vacaḥ mama tatra saṃkṣipya vartante sṛṣṭayaḥ pratisṛṣṭayaḥ yaḥ tu ayam vartate kalpaḥ vārāhaḥ nāma nāmataḥ svāyaṃbhuva ādayaḥ sapta sapta sāvarṇika ādayaḥ manvantareṣu sarveṣu sarga saṃhāra vṛttayaḥ prāyas samābhavanti iti tarkaḥ kāryaḥ vijānatā pūrva kalpe parāvṛtte pravṛtte kālamārute samunmūlita mūleṣu vṛkṣeṣu ca vaneṣu ca vṛṣṭyā bhuvi niṣiktāyām viveleṣu arṇaveṣu ca dikṣu sarvāsu magnāsu vāripūre mahīyasi tad adbhiḥ caṭula ākṣepaiḥ taraṃga bhuja maṇḍalaiḥ prārabdha caṇḍa nṛtyeṣu tatas pralaya vāriṣu brahmā nārāyaṇaḥ bhūtvā suṣvāpa salile sukham imam ca udāharan mantram ślokam nārāyaṇam prati tam śṛṇudhvam muni śreṣṭhāḥ tad artham ca akṣara āśrayam āpaḥ nārāḥ iti proktāḥ āpaḥ vai nara sūnavaḥ ayanam tasya tāḥ yasmāt tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ śiva yoga mayīm nidrām kurvantam tridaśeśvaram baddhāṃjali puṭāḥ siddhāḥ jana loka nivāsinaḥ stotraiḥ prabodhayāmāsuḥ prabhāta samaye surāḥ yathā sṛṣṭi ādi samaye īśvaram śrutayaḥ purā udaikṣata diśaḥ sarvāḥ yoga nidrā alasa īkṣaṇaḥ sa vismayaḥ iva āsīnaḥ parām cintām upāgamat kva sā bhagavatī yā tu manojñā mahatī mahī nānāvidha mahā śaila nadī nagara kānanā jñātavān salile magnām dharaṇīm dharaṇīpatiḥ tatas bhūmeḥ samuddhāram kartu kāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ jala krīḍā ucitam divyam vārāham rūpam asmarat mahā parvata varṣmāṇam mahā jalada niḥsvanam nīla megha pratīkāśam dīpta śabdam bhayānakam pīna vṛtta ghana skandha pīna unnata kaṭī taṭam hrasva vṛtta ūru jaṃghā agram su tīkṣṇa pura maṇḍalam padmarāga maṇi prakhyam vṛtta bhīṣaṇa locanam udīrṇa ucchvāsa niśvāsa ghūrṇita pralaya arṇavam maṇibhiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ citraiḥ mahā ratnaiḥ pariṣkṛtam āsthāya vipulam rūpam vārāham amitam vidhiḥ pṛthivī uddharaṇa arthāya praviveśa rasātalam sa tadā śuśubhe atīva sūkaraḥ giri saṃnibhaḥ liṃga ākṛteḥ maheśasya pāda mūlam gataḥ yathā tatas sa salile magnām pṛthivīm pṛthivīṃdharaḥ uddhṛtya āliṃgya daṃṣṭrābhyām unmamajja rasātalāt tam dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ siddhāḥ jana loka nivāsinaḥ vapuḥ mahāvarāhasya śuśubhe puṣpa saṃvṛtam tatas saṃsthānam ānīya varāhaḥ mahatīm mahīm svam eva rūpam āsthāya sthāpayāmāsa vai vibhuḥ pṛthivīm ca samīkṛtya pṛthivyām sthāpayan girīn bhūḥ ādyān caturaḥ lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām sṛṣṭyādivarṇanam nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca tamaḥ mohaḥ mahā mohaḥ tāmisraḥ ca andha saṃjñitaḥ avidyā pañcamī ca eṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ sarvvatas tamasā atīva bīja kumbha vat āvṛtaḥ bahis antar ca aprakāśaḥ stabdhaḥ niḥsaṃjñaḥ eva ca tasmāt teṣām vṛtā buddhiḥ mukhāni karaṇāni ca tasmāt te saṃvṛta ātmānaḥ nagāḥ mukhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ tam dṛṣṭvā asādhakam brahmā prathamam sargam īdṛśam antar prakāśāḥ tiryyaṃcaḥ āvṛtāḥ ca bahis punar paśu ātmānaḥ tatas jātāḥ utpatha grāhiṇaḥ ca te te sukha prīti bahulāḥ bahis antar ca na āvṛtāḥ prakāśāḥ bahis antar ca svabhāvāt eva saṃjñitāḥ manuṣya nāmā sañjātaḥ sargaḥ duḥkha samutkaṭaḥ prakāśāḥ abahir antar te tama udriktāḥ rajaḥ adhikāḥ viparyyayeṇa śaktyā ca tuṣṭyā asiddhyā tathā eva ca te a parigrāhiṇaḥ sarvve saṃvibhāga ratāḥ punar khādanāḥ ca api aśīlāḥ ca bhūta ādyāḥ parikīrttitāḥ tanmātrāṇām dvitīyaḥ tu bhūta sargaḥ saḥ ucyate iti eṣa prakṛteḥ sargaḥ sambhṛtaḥ a buddhi pūrvakaḥ mukhya sargaḥ caturthaḥ tu mukhyāḥ vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ tat ūrddhvasrotasaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ deva sargaḥ tu sa smṛtaḥ tatas srotasām sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ aṣṭamaḥ anugrahaḥ sargaḥ kaumāraḥ navamaḥ smṛtaḥ prākṛtāḥ ca trayaḥ pūrve sargāḥ te abuddhi pūrvakāḥ buddhi pūrvvam pravarttante mukhya ādyāḥ pañca vaikṛtāḥ agre sasarjja vai brahmā mānasān ātmanaḥ samān sanandam sanakam ca eva vidvāṃsam ca sanātanam ṛbhum sanatkumārañca pūrvvam eva prajāpatiḥ sarvve te yoginaḥ jñeyāḥ vīta rāgāḥ vimatsarāḥ iśvara āsakta manasaḥ na cakruḥ sṛṣṭaye matim teṣu sṛṣṭi anapekṣeṣu gateṣu sanaka ādiṣu sraṣṭu kāmaḥ punar brahmā tatāpa paramam tapaḥ tatas dīrgheṇa kālena duḥkhāt krodhaḥ vyajāyata krodha āviṣṭasya netrābhyām prāpatan aśru bindavaḥ sarvān tān aśru jān dṛṣṭvā brahmā ātmānam anindata tasya tīvrā abhavat mūrcchā krodha amarṣa samudbhavā mūrcchitaḥ tu jahau prāṇān krodha āviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ tatas prāṇeśvaraḥ rudraḥ bhagavān nīlalohitaḥ prasādam atulam karttum prādurāsīt prabhoḥ mukhāt daśadhā ca ekadhā cakre sva ātmānam prabhuḥ īśvaraḥ te tena uktāḥ mahātmānaḥ daśadhā ca ekadhā kṛtāḥ yūyam sṛṣṭāḥ mayā vatsāḥ loka anugraha kāraṇāt rodanāt drāvaṇāt ca eva te rudrāḥ nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ ye rudrāḥ te khalu prāṇāḥ ye prāṇāḥ te mahātmakāḥ tatas mṛtasya devasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ghṛṇī dadau punar prāṇān brahma putraḥ maheśvaraḥ prahṛṣṭa vadanaḥ rudraḥ prāṇa pratyāgamāt vibhoḥ abhyabhāṣata viśveśaḥ brahmāṇam paramam vacaḥ mā ābhaiḥ mā ābhaiḥ mahābhāga viriṃca jagatām guro mayā te prāṇitāḥ prāṇāḥ sukham uttiṣṭha suvrata tathā pratyāgata prāṇaḥ snigdha gambhīrayā girā uvāca vacanam brahmā tam uddiśya kṛtāñjaliḥ tvam hi darśana mātreṇa ca ānandayasi me manaḥ kaḥ bhavān viśvamūrtyāḥ vā sthitaḥ ekādaśa ātmakaḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā vyājahāra maheśvaraḥ spṛśan kārābhyām brahmāṇam su sukhābhyām sureśvaraḥ mām viddhi paramātmānam tava putra tvam āgatam ete ca ekādaśa rudrāḥ tvām su rakṣitum āgatāḥ tasmāt tīvrām imām mūrcchām vidhūya mad anugrahāt nānā aṣṭakena viśvātmā tuṣṭāva parameśvaram śarvāya kṣiti rūpāya nandī surabhaye namaḥ īśāya vasave tubhyam namaḥ sparśa maya ātmane paśūnām pataye ca eva pāvakāya ati tejase bhīmāya vyoma rūpāya śabda mātrāya te namaḥ ugrāya ugra svarūpāya yajamāna ātmane namaḥ evam stutvā mahādevam brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ prārthayāmāsa viśveśam girā praṇati pūrvayā sṛṣṭi hetoḥ tvam utpannaḥ mama aṃge anaṃga nāśanaḥ sahāyam kuru sarvatra sraṣṭum arhasi sa prajāḥ bāḍham iti eva tām vāṇīm pratijagrāha śaṃkaraḥ sraṣṭum tena abhyanujñātaḥ tathā anyāḥ ca asṛjat prajāḥ iti ete brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ dvādaśa ādau prakīrtitāḥ saha rudreṇa saṃbhūtāḥ purāṇāḥ gṛhamedhinaḥ teṣām dvādaśa vaṃśāḥ syuḥ divyāḥ deva gaṇa anvitāḥ prajāvantaḥ kriyāvantaḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ atha deva asura pitR̥n manuṣyān ca catuṣṭayam saha rudreṇa sisṛkṣuḥ aṃbhasi etāni vai vidhiḥ sa sṛṣṭi artham samādhāya brahmā ātmānam ayūyujat mukhāt ajanayat devān pitR̥n ca eva upapakṣataḥ jaghanāt asurān sarvān prajanāt api mānuṣān avaskare kṣudhā āviṣṭāḥ rākṣasāḥ tasya jajñire putrāḥ tamaḥ rajaḥ prāyāḥ balinaḥ te niśācarāḥ sarpāḥ yakṣāḥ tathā bhūtāḥ gandharvāḥ saṃprajajñire vayāṃsi pakṣataḥ sṛṣṭāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ vakṣasaḥ asṛjat mukha tojān tathā pārśvāt uragān ca vinirmame padbhyām ca aśvān sa mātaṃgān śarabhān gavayān mṛgān uṣṭrān aśvatarān ca eva nyaṃkūn anyāḥ ca jātayaḥ gāyatrīm ca ṛcam ca eva trivṛt sāma rathantaram agniṣṭomam ca yajñānām nirmame prathamān mukhāt yajūṃṣi traiṣṭubham chandaḥstomam paṃcadaśam tathā bṛhatsāma tathā uktham ca dakṣiṇāt asṛjat mukhāt sāmāni jagatī chandaḥ stomam saptadaśam tathā vairūpyam atirātram ca paścimāt asṛjat mukhāt ekaviṃśam atharvāṇam āptoryāmāṇam eva ca anuṣṭubham sa vairājam uttarāt asṛjat mukhāt uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyaḥ tasya jajñire yakṣāḥ piśācāḥ gandharvāḥ tathā eva apsarasām gaṇāḥ nara kinnara rakṣāṃsi vayaḥ paśu mṛga uragāḥ teṣām vai yāni karmāṇi prāc sṛṣṭāni prapedire tāni eva te prapadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punar punar hiṃsra ahiṃsre mṛdu krūre dharma adharma āvṛta anṛte mahābhūteṣu nānātvam indriya artheṣu muktiṣu nāma rūpam ca bhūtānām prākṛtānām prapaṃcanam ārṣāṇi ca eva nāmāni yāḥ ca vedeṣu vṛttayaḥ śarvarī ante prasūtānām tāni eva ebhyaḥ dadau ajaḥ yathā ṛtau ṛtu liṃgāni nānā rūpāṇi paryyaye dṛśyante tāni tāni eva tathā bhāvāḥ yuga ādiṣu mahat ādyaḥ viśeṣa antaḥ vikāraḥ prakṛteḥ svayam candra sūrya prabhā juṣṭaḥ graha nakṣatra maṃḍitaḥ nadībhiḥ ca samudraiḥ ca parvataiḥ ca sa maṃḍitaḥ mahābhūta pramāṇaḥ ca viśeṣa amala pallavaḥ dharma adharma su puṣpa āḍhyaḥ sukha duḥkha phala udayaḥ ājīvyaḥ sarva bhūtānām brahmavṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ dyām mūrddhānam tasya viprāḥ vadanti kham vai nābhim candra sūryau ca netre diśaḥ śrotre caraṇau ca kṣitim ca saḥ acintya ātmā sarva bhūta praṇetā vaktrāt tasya brahmaṇāḥ saṃprasūtāḥ tad vakṣasaḥ kṣatriyāḥ pūrvabhāgāt vaiśyāḥ urubhyām tasya padbhyām ca śūdrāḥ sarve varṇāḥ gātrataḥ saṃprasūtāḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe sṛṣṭivarṇanam nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ bhavatā kathitā sṛṣṭiḥ bhavasya paramātmanaḥ deva śreṣṭhaḥ virūpākṣaḥ dīptaḥ śūla dharaḥ haraḥ kāla ātmā bhagavān rudraḥ kapardī nīlalohitaḥ yasya brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca praṇāmam kurutaḥ bhayāt devaḥ svakāt aṃgāt brahma viṣṇū purā sṛjat sa katham bhagavān rudraḥ ādidevaḥ purātanaḥ sṛṣṭau parasparasya aṃgāt iti prāk api śuśruma katham punar aśeṣāṇām bhūtānām hetu bhūtayoḥ guṇa pradhāna bhāvena prādurbhāvaḥ parasparāt na a pṛṣṭam bhavatā kiṃcid na a śrutam ca kathaṃcana vayam śraddhālavaḥ tāta śrotum īśvara sat yaśaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca sthāne pṛṣṭam idam viprāḥ bhavadbhiḥ praśna kovidaiḥ idam eva purā pṛṣṭaḥ mama prāha pitāmahaḥ trayaḥ te kāraṇa ātmānaḥ jatāḥ sākṣāt maheśvarāt parama aiśvarya saṃyuktāḥ parameśvara bhāvitāḥ tad śaktyā adhiṣṭhitāḥ nityam tad kārya karaṇa kṣamāḥ pitrā niyamitāḥ pūrvam trayaḥ api triṣu karmasu brahmā sarge hariḥ trāṇe rudraḥ saṃharaṇe tathā tathā api anyonya mātsaryāt anyonya atiśaya āśinaḥ tapasā toṣayitvā svam pitaram parameśvaram labdhvā sarva ātmanā tasya prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ brahma nārāyaṇau pūrvam rudraḥ kalpa antare asṛjat viṣṇuḥ ca bhagavān rudram brahmāṇam asṛjat punar nārāyaṇam punar brahmā brahmāṇam asṛjat punar evam kalpeṣu kalpeṣu brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ śṛṇu teṣām kathām citrām puṇyām pāpa pramocinīm kalpe tatpuruṣe vṛttām brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ purā nārāyaṇaḥ nāma kalpe vai meghavāhane tasya bhāvam samālakṣya viṣṇoḥ viśva jagat guruḥ śaktim labdhvā tu sarvātmā śivāt sarva īśvarāt tadā sasarja bhagāvan viṣṇuḥ viśvam viśvasṛjā saha viṣṇoḥ tat vaibhavam dṛṣṭvā sṛṣṭaḥ tena pitāmahaḥ īrṣyayā parayā grastaḥ prahasan idam abravīt gaccha viṣṇo mayā jñātam tava sargasya kāraṇam āvayoḥ adhikaḥ ca asti sa rudraḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ tasya deva adhidevasya prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ sraṣṭā tvam bhagavān ādyaḥ pālakaḥ paramārthataḥ aham ca tapasā ārādhya rudram tridaśa nāyakam tvayā saha jagat sarvam srakṣyāmi atra na saṃśayaḥ evam viṣṇum upālabhya bhagavān abja sambhavaḥ evam vijñāpayāmāsa tapasā prāpya śaṃkaram tava vāma aṃga jaḥ viṣṇuḥ dakṣiṇa aṃga bhavaḥ hi aham sa matsarāt upālabdhaḥ tvad āśraya balāt mayā tasya bhaktyā yathāpūrvam prasādam kṛtavān asi tathā mama api tat sarvam dātum arhasi śaṃkara nyāyena vai dadau sarvam tasya api sa ghṛṇā nidhiḥ labdhvā evam īśvarāt eva brahmā sarva ātma tām kṣaṇāt kṣīrārṇava ālaye śubhre vimāne sūrya saṃnibhe ananta bhoga śayyāyām śayānam paṃkaja īkṣaṇam catur bhujam udāra aṃgam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam dharā mṛdu kara aṃbhoja sparśa rakta pada aṃbujam kṣīrārṇava amṛtam iva śayānam yoganidrayā tamasā kālarudra ākhyam rajasā kanaka aṃḍa jam tam dṛṣṭvā puruṣam brahmā pragalbham idam abravīt grasāmi tvām aham viṣṇo tvam ātmānam yathā purā udaikṣata mahā bāhuḥ smitam īṣat cakāra ca sṛṣṭaḥ ca brahmaṇā sadyas bhruvoḥ madhyāt ayatnataḥ tasmin avasare sākṣāt bhagavān indu bhūṣaṇaḥ śaktim tayoḥ api draṣṭum arūpaḥ rūpam āsthitaḥ praṇematuḥ ca bahuśas bahu mānena dūratas iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe brahmaviṣṇusṛṣṭikathanam nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca prati kalpam pravakṣyāmi rudra āvirbhāva kāraṇam yatas vicchinna saṃtānā brahma sṛṣṭiḥ pravartate kalpe kalpe prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā brahmā brahmāṃḍa saṃbhavaḥ a vṛddhi hetoḥ bhūtānām mumoha bhṛśa duḥkhitaḥ tasya duḥkha praśānti artham prajānām ca vivṛddhaye tad tad kalpeṣu kāla ātmā rudraḥ rudra gaṇa adhipaḥ nirdiṣṭaḥ pamameśena maheśaḥ nīlalohitaḥ putraḥ bhūtvā anugṛhṇāti brahmāṇam brahmaṇaḥ anujaḥ saḥ eva bhagavān īśaḥ tejorāśiḥ anāmayaḥ an ādi nidhanaḥ dhātā bhūta saṃkocakaḥ vibhuḥ tad nāma nāmā tad rūpaḥ tad kārya karaṇa kṣamaḥ tad tulya vyavahāraḥ ca tad ājñā paripālakaḥ sahasra āditya saṃkāśaḥ candra avayava bhūṣaṇaḥ bhagna daṃṣṭra aṃkura ākrānta prānta kānta dharādharaḥ savya śravaṇa pārśva anta maṃḍalīkṛta kuṇḍalaḥ evam ghora mahā rūpaḥ brahmaputrīm maheśvaraḥ pravāha rūpataḥ nityā prajā sṛṣṭiḥ pravartate kadācid prārthitaḥ sraṣṭum brahmaṇā nīlalohitaḥ sva ātmanā sadṛśān sarvān sasarja manasā vibhuḥ kaparddinaḥ nirātaṃkān nīlagrīvān tri locanān jarā maraṇa nirmuktān dīpta śūla vara āyudhān tān dṛṣṭā vividhān rudrān rudram āha pitāmahaḥ namaḥ te devadeveśa mā asrākṣīḥ īdṛśīḥ prajāḥ anyāḥ sṛja tvam bhadram te prajāḥ mṛtyu samanvitāḥ iti uktaḥ prahasan prāha brahmāṇam parameśvaraḥ na asti me tādṛśaḥ sargaḥ sṛja tvam aśubhāḥ prajāḥ ye tu ime manasā sṛṣṭāḥ mahātmānaḥ mahā balāḥ cariṣyanti mayā sārddham sarve eva hi yājñikāḥ iti uktvā viśvakarmāṇam viśva bhūta īśvaraḥ haraḥ saha rudraiḥ prajā sargāt nivṛtta ātmā vyatiṣṭhata tatas prabhṛti devaḥ asau na prasūte prajāḥ śubhāḥ ūrddhvaretāḥ sthitaḥ sthāṇuḥ yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe rudrāvirbhāvavarṇanam nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca yadā punar prajāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ na vyavarddhanta vedhasaḥ tadā maithuna jām sṛṣṭim brahmā kartum amanyata na nirgatam purā yasmāt nārīṇām kulam īśvarāt tena maithuna jām sṛṣṭim na śaśāka pitāmahaḥ prajānam eva vṛddhi artham praṣṭavyaḥ parameśvara evam saṃcintya viśvātmā tapaḥ kartum pracakrame tad ādyā paramā śaktiḥ anantā loka bhāvinī ādyā sūkṣmatarā śuddhā bhāva gamyā manoharā nirguṇā niṣprapaṃcā ca niṣkalā nirupaplavā nirantaratarā nityā nityam īśvara pārśva gā saṃcintya hṛdaye brahmā tatāpa paramam tapaḥ tīvreṇa tapasā tasya yuktasya parameṣṭhinaḥ tatas kenacid aṃśena mūrtim āviśya kām api arddhanārīśvaraḥ bhūtvā yayau devaḥ svayam haraḥ tam dṛṣṭvā paramam devam tamasaḥ param avyayam advitīyam anirdeśyam adṛśyam akṛtātmabhiḥ acalam nirguṇam śāntam ananta mahima āspadam sarva upamāna nirmuktam śaraṇyam śāśvatam śivam praṇamya daṃḍa vat brahmā samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ śraddhā vinaya saṃpannaiḥ śrāvyaiḥ saṃskara saṃyutaiḥ tuṣṭāva devam devīm ca sūktaiḥ sūkṣma artha gocaraiḥ jaya śāśvatika aiśvarye jaya śāśvatika ālaya jaya śāśvatika ākāra jaya śāśvatika anuga jaya avalokana āyatta jagat kāraṇa bṛṃhaṇa jaya deva adya vijñeye sva ātma sūkṣma dṛśā ujjvale jaya vyāpta carācare jaya asura śiraḥ niṣṭha śreṣṭha anuga kadaṃbaka jaya upāśrita saṃrakṣā saṃvidhāna paṭīyasi jaya unmūlita saṃsāra viṣa vṛkṣa aṃkura udgame jaya prādeśika aiśvarya vīrya śaurya vijṛṃbhaṇa jaya praṇīta paṃcārtha prayoga parama amṛta jaya paṃcārtha vijñāna sudhā stotra svarūpiṇi jaya anādi mala ajñāna tamaḥ paṭala candrike vijñāpya evaṃvidhaiḥ sūktaiḥ viśvakarmā caturmukhaḥ namaścakāra rudrāya radrāṇyai ca muhur muhur idam stotra varam puṇyam brahmaṇā samudīritam arddhanārīśvaram nāma śivayoḥ harṣa varddhanam yaḥ idam kīrttayet bhaktyā yasya kasya api śikṣayā sa tat phalam avāpnoti śivayoḥ prīti kāraṇāt sakala bhuvana bhūta bhāvanābhyām janana vināśa vihīna vigrahābhyām nara vara yuvatī vapurddharābhyām satatam aham praṇataḥ asmi śaṃkarābhyām iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām śivaśivāstutivarṇanam nāma paṃcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca vācā madhura gaṃbhīra śiva da ślakṣṇa varṇayā artha saṃpanna padayā rāja lakṣaṇa yuktayā aśeṣa viṣaya āraṃbha rakṣā vimala dakṣayā saṃbabhāṣe su saṃpītaḥ viśvakarmāṇam īśvaraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca prajānām eva bṛddhi artham tapaḥ taptam tvayā adhunā iti uktvā parama udāram svabhāva madhuram vacaḥ sasarja vapuṣaḥ bhāgāt devīm deva varaḥ haraḥ yām āhuḥ brahma vidvāṃsaḥ devīm divya guṇa anvitām parasya paramām śaktim bhavasya paramātmanaḥ yā bhavānī bhavasya aṃgāt samāvirabhavat kila sā bhartuḥ vapuṣaḥ bhāgāt jātā iva samadṛśyata yā sā jagat idam kṛtsnam mahimnā vyāpya tiṣṭhati śarīriṇī iva sa devī vicitram samalakṣyata sarvam jagat idam ca eṣā saṃmohayati māyayā īśvarāt sā eva jātā abhūt ajātā paramārthataḥ na yasyāḥ paramaḥ bhāvaḥ surāṇām api gocaraḥ viśva amara īśvarī ca eva vibhaktā bhartuḥ aṃgataḥ tām dṛṣṭvā parameśānīm sarva loka mahā īśvarīm sarvajñām sarva gām sūkṣmām sat asat vyakti varjitām paramām nikhilam bhāsā bhāsayantīm idam jagat praṇipatya mahādevīm prārthayāmāsa vai virāj na vṛddhim upagacchanti sṛjyamānāḥ punar punar mithuna prabhavām eva kṛtvā sṛṣṭim atas param na nirgatam purā tvattaḥ nārīṇām kulam avyayam tena nārī kulam sraṣṭum śaktiḥ mama na vidyate sarvāsām eva śaktīnām tvattaḥ khalu samudbhavaḥ tasmāt sarvatra sarveṣām sarva śakti pradāyinīm tvām eva vara dām māyām prārthayāmi sureśvarīm evam sā yācitā devī brahmaṇā brahma yoninā tām ājñām parameśasya śirasā pratigṛhya sā dattvā evam atulām śaktim brahmaṇe brahma rūpiṇīm tadā prabhṛti loke asmin striyām bhogaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ brahmā api prāpa sa ānandam santoṣam muni puṃgavāḥ puṇya vṛddhi karam śrāvyam puṇyam sarvam avāpnoti putrān ca labhate śubhān iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe devīśaktyudbhavaḥ nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca evam labdhvā parām śaktim īśvarāt eva śāśvatīm maithuna prabhavām sṛṣṭim kartṛ kāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ yā arddhena nārī sā tasmāt śatarūpā vyajāyata sa vai svāyaṃbhuvaḥ pūrvam puruṣaḥ manuḥ ucyate sā devī śatarūpā tu tapaḥ kṛtvā su duścaram bharttāram dīpta yaśasam manum eva anvapadyata tasmāt tu śatarūpā sā putra dvayam asūyata kanye dve ca mahābhāge yābhyām jātāḥ tu imāḥ prajāḥ ākūtiḥ ekā vijñeyā prasūtiḥ aparā smṛtā svāyaṃbhuvaḥ prasūtim ca dadau dakṣāya tām prabhuḥ ruceḥ prajāpatiḥ ca eva cākūtim samapādayat ākūtyām mithunam jajñe mānasasya ruceḥ śubham yajñaḥ ca dakṣiṇā ca eva yābhyām saṃvartitam jagat svāyaṃbhuva sutāyām tu prasūtyām loka mātaraḥ śraddhā lakṣmīḥ dhṛtiḥ puṣṭiḥ tuṣṭiḥ medhā kriyā tathā buddhiḥ lajjā vapuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrtiḥ trayodaśī patnī artham pratijagrāha dharmaḥ dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ tābhyaḥ śiṣṭāḥ yavīyasyaḥ ekādaśa su locanāḥ khyātiḥ satī artha saṃbhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ prītiḥ kṣamā tathā sannatiḥ ca anasūyā ca ūrjjā svāhā svadhā tathā bhṛguḥ śarvaḥ marīciḥ ca aṃgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ pulastyaḥ atriḥ viśiṣṭhaḥ ca pāvakaḥ pitaraḥ tathā khyāti ādyāḥ jagṛhuḥ kanyā munayaḥ muni sattamāḥ kāma ādyāḥ tu yaśaḥ antāḥ ye te trayodaśa sūnavaḥ dharmasya jajñire tāḥ tu śraddhā ādyāḥ su sukha uttarāḥ duḥkha uttarāḥ ca hiṃsāyām adharmasya ca saṃtatau nikṛti ādayaḥ utpannāḥ putrāḥ ca dharma lakṣaṇāḥ na eṣām bhāryāḥ ca putrāḥ vā sarve tu aniyamāḥ smṛtāḥ yā sā dakṣasya duhitā rudrasya dayitā satī bhartṛ nindā prasaṃgena tyaktvā dākṣāyiṇīm tanum dakṣam ca dakṣa bhāryyām ca vinindya saha bandhubhiḥ sā menāyām āvirabhūt putrī himavataḥ gireḥ rudraḥ tu tām satīm dṛṣṭvā rudrān tu ātma sama prabhān yathā asṛjat asaṃkhyātān tathā kathitam eva ca bhṛgoḥ khyātyām samutpannā lakṣmīḥ nārāyaṇa priyā devau dhātṛ vidhātārau manvantara vidhāriṇau tayoḥ vai putra pautra ādyāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas svāyaṃbhuve antare nītāḥ sarve te bhārgavāḥ matāḥ marīceḥ api saṃbhūtiḥ paurṇamāsam asūyata kanyā catuṣṭayam ca eva mahīyāṃsaḥ tad anvayāḥ yeṣām vaṃśe samutpannaḥ bahuputrasya kaśyapaḥ smṛtiḥ ca aṃgirasaḥ patnī janayāmāsa vai sutau āgnīdhram śarabham ca eva tathā kanyā catuṣṭayam tadīyāḥ putra pautrāḥ ca yā iti itāḥ te sahasraśas prītyām pulastya bhāryāyām dantogniḥ abhavat sutaḥ tad saṃtatīyāḥ bahavaḥ paulastyāḥ iti viśrutāḥ kṣamā tu suṣuve putrān pulahasya prajāpateḥ kardamaḥ ca suriḥ ca eva sahiṣṇuḥ ca iti te trayaḥ tretāgni varcasaḥ sarve yeṣām vaṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ na eṣām bhāryāḥ ca putrāḥ ca sarve te hi ūrdhvaretasaḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ tāni sahasrāṇi vālakhilyāḥ iti smṛtāḥ atreḥ bhāryā anusūyā ca pañca ātreyān asūyata kanyakām ca śrutim nāma mātā śaṃkhapadasya ca satyanetraḥ ca havyaḥ ca āpomūrtiḥ śanaiścaraḥ somaḥ ca paṃcamaḥ tu ete paṃca ātreyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ teṣām putrāḥ ca pautrāḥ ca hi ātreyāṇām mahātmanām svāyaṃbhuve antare atītāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas ūrjāyām tu vasiṣṭhasya putrāḥ vai sapta jajñire jyāyasī ca svasā teṣām puṃḍarīkā sumadhyamā rajaḥ ca savanaḥ ca anayaḥ ca yaḥ sutapāḥ śukraḥ iti ete sapta saptarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ gotrāṇi nāmabhiḥ teṣām vāsiṣṭhānām mahātmanām svāyaṃbhuve antare atītāni arbudāni śatāni ca iti eṣaḥ ṛṣi sargaḥ tu sa anubandhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ samāsāt vistarāt vaktum aśakyaḥ ayam iti dvijāḥ svāhā tasya priyā lebhe putrān trīn amita ojasaḥ pāvakaḥ pavamānaḥ ca śuciḥ iti eṣa te trayaḥ nirmanthyaḥ pavamānaḥ syāt vaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ sūrye tapati yaḥ ca asau śuciḥ sauraḥ udāhṛtaḥ havyavāhaḥ kavyavāhaḥ saharakṣāḥ iti trayaḥ trayāṇām kramaśas putrāḥ deva pitṛ surāḥ ca te eteṣām putra pautrāḥ ca catvāriṃśat nava eva te sarve rudra ātmakaḥ ca eva sarve rudra parāyaṇāḥ tat sarvam rudram uddiśya dattam syāt na atra saṃśayaḥ iti evam niścayaḥ agnīnām anukrāntaḥ yathātatham yasmāt ṣaṭ ṛtavaḥ teṣām sthānam sthāna abhimāninām ṛtavaḥ pitaraḥ tasmāt iti eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ yuṣmāt ṛtuṣu sarve hi jāyante sthāsnu jaṃgamā evam pitR̥ṇām eteṣām ṛtu kāla abhimāninām ātma aiśvaryāḥ mahātmānaḥ tiṣṭhanti iha abbhra saṃgamāt āgniṣvāttāḥ barhiṣadaḥ pitaraḥ dvividhāḥ smṛtāḥ ayajvānaḥ ca yajvānaḥ kramāt te mṛhamedhinaḥ menām ca dharaṇīm ca eva yābhyām viśvam idam dhṛtam agniṣvātta sutā menā dharaṇī barhiṣad sutā menā himavataḥ patnī mainākam krauṃcam eva ca gaurīm gaṃgām ca suṣuve bhava aṃga āśleṣa pāvanīm sākṣāt śrīkaṃṭha nāthasya śivasya āvasatham gataḥ sā asūtā dharaṇī bhūyas triṃśat kanyāḥ ca viśrutāḥ velām ca niyatim ca eva tṛtīyām api ca āyatim suṣuve sāgarāt velā kanyām ekām aninditām savarṇām nāma sāmudrīm patnīm prācīnabarhiṣaḥ sāmudrī suṣuve putrān daśa prācīnabarhiṣaḥ sarve prācetasāḥ nāma dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ yeṣām svāyaṃbhuve dakṣaḥ putra tvam agamat purā triyambakasya śāpena cākṣuṣasya antare manoḥ iti ete brahma putrāṇām dharma ādīnām mahātmanām na ati saṃkṣepataḥ viprāḥ na ati vistarataḥ kramāt varṇitāḥ vai mayā vaṃśāḥ divyāḥ deva gaṇa anvitāḥ kriyāvantaḥ prajāvantaḥ mahā ṛddhibhiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ prajānām saṃniveśaḥ ayam prajāpati samudbhavaḥ na hi śakyaḥ prasaṃkhyātum varṣa koṭi śataiḥ api rājñām api ca yaḥ vaṃśaḥ dvidhā saḥ api pravartate sūryavaṃśaḥ somavaṃśaḥ iti puṇyatamaḥ kṣitau ikṣvākuḥ ambarīṣaḥ ca yayātiḥ nāhuṣa ādayaḥ puṇya ślokāḥ śrutāḥ ye tad tad vaṃśa saṃbhavāḥ anye ca rāja ṛṣayaḥ nānā vīrya samanvitā kim taiḥ phalam anutkrāntaiḥ ukta pūrvaiḥ purātanaiḥ kim ca īśvara kathā vṛttā yatra tatra anya kīrtanam prasaṃgāt īśvarasya eva prabhāva dyotanāt api iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe sṛṣṭikathanam nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ devī dakṣasya tanayā tyaktvā dākṣāyaṇī tanum katham himavataḥ putrī menāyām abhavat purā utpannaḥ ca katham dakṣaḥ abhiśāpāt bhavasya tu cākṣuṣasya antare pūrvam manoḥ prabrūhi māruta vāyuḥ uvāva śṛṇvantu kathayiṣyāmi dakṣasya laghu cetasaḥ vṛttam pāpāt pramādāt ca viśva amara vidūṣaṇam purā sura asurāḥ sarve siddhāḥ ca parama ṛṣayaḥ kadācid draṣṭum īśānam himavat śikharam yayuḥ darśanam dadatuḥ teṣām deva ādīnām dvijottamāḥ jāmātaram haram draṣṭum draṣṭum ca ātma sutām satīm deva ādibhyaḥ viśeṣeṇa na kadācid abhūt smṛtiḥ tasya tasyāḥ param bhāvam ajñātuḥ ca api kevalam putrī iti evam vimūḍhasya tasyām vairam ajāyata na ajuvāha bhavam dakṣaḥ dīkṣitaḥ tām api dviṣan anyān jāmātaraḥ sarvān āhūya sa yathākramam śataśas puṣkalām arcān cakāra ca pṛthak pṛthak tathā tān saṃgatān śrutvā nāradasya mukhāt tadā yayau rudrāya rudrāṇī vijñāpya bhavanam pituḥ atha saṃnihitam divyam vimānam viśvatomukham lakṣaṇa āḍhyam sukha āroham atimātra manoharam muktā āmaya vitāna agnyam sraj dāma samalaṃkṛtam tapta kaṃcana nirvyūham ratna staṃbha śata āvṛtam puṣpa paṭṭa paristīrṇam citra ratna mahā āsanam maṇi daṃḍa manojñena mahā vṛṣabha lakṣmaṇā alaṃkṛta purobhāgam abbhra śubbhreṇa ketunā ratna kaṃcuka gupta aṃgaiḥ citra vetraka pāṇibhiḥ adhiṣṭhita mahā dvāram apradhṛṣyaiḥ guṇa īśvaraiḥ mṛdaṃga tāla gīta ādi veṇu vīṇā viśāradaiḥ vidagdha veṣa bhāṣaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ strī janaiḥ vṛtam cāmāra vyañjanam tasyāḥ vajra daṃḍa manohare chatram śaśi nibham tasyāḥ cūḍā upari su mālinī upari amṛta bhāṃḍasya maṃḍalam śaśinaḥ yathā atha ca agre samāsīnā su smita āsyā śubhāvatī suyaśāḥ pāduke devyāḥ śubhe ratna pariṣkṛte anyā kāṃcana cāru aṃgī dīptam jagrāha darpaṇam aparā tālavṛntam ca parā tāṃbūla peṭikām kācid krīḍā śukam cāru kare akuruta bhāminī kācid tu su manojñāni puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi ca kācid ābharaṇa ādhāram babhāra kamala īkṣaṇā kācid ca punar ālepam su prasūtam śubha aṃjanam anyāḥ ca sadṛśāḥ tāḥ tāḥ yathāsvam ucita kriyāḥ āvṛttyā tām mahādevīm asevanta samantataḥ atīva śuśubhe tāsām antare parameśvarī tārā pariṣadaḥ madhye candra lekhā iva śāradī prāsthānikaḥ mahā nādaḥ paṭahaḥ samatāḍyata anāhatāni sanneduḥ kāhalānām śatāni ca sa āyudhānām gaṇeśānām maheśa sama tejasām sahasrāṇi śatāni aṣṭau tadānīm puratas yayuḥ teṣām madhye vṛṣa ārūḍhaḥ gaja ārūḍhaḥ yathā guruḥ jagāma gaṇapaḥ śrīmān somanandīśvara arcitaḥ sasṛjuḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭim ca vitāna upari vāridāḥ tadā deva gaṇaiḥ ca anyaiḥ pathi sarvatra saṃgatā kṣaṇāt iva pituḥ geham praviveśa maheśvarī tām dṛṣṭvā kupitaḥ dakṣaḥ ca ātmanaḥ kṣaya kāraṇāt tasyāḥ yavīyasībhyaḥ api cakre pūjām satkṛtām tadā śaśimukhī devī pitaram sadasi sthitam aṃbikā yuktam avyagram uvāca akṛpaṇam vacaḥ brahma ādayaḥ piśāca antāḥ yasya ājñā vaśa vartinaḥ sa devaḥ sāṃpratam tāta vidhinā na arcitaḥ kila tadā āstām mama jyāyasyāḥ putryāḥ pūjām kim īdṛśīm asatkṛtām avajñāya kṛtavān asi garhitam evam uktaḥ abravīt enām dakṣaḥ krodhāt amarṣitaḥ tvattaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ viśiṣṭāḥ ca pūjyāḥ bālāḥ sutāḥ mama tāsām tu ye ca bharttāraḥ te me bahu matāḥ mudā stabdha ātmā tāmasaḥ śarvaḥ tvam imam samupāśritā tathā uktā pitaram dakṣam kruddhā devī tam abravīt śṛṇvatām eva sarveṣām ye yajña sadasi sthitāḥ akasmāt mama bhartāram ajāta aśeṣa dūṣaṇam vācā dūṣayase dakṣa sākṣāt loka mahā īśvaram te ete bahu pāpmānaḥ sarve daṃḍyāḥ iti śrutiḥ tasmāt ati utkaṭasya asya pāpasya sadṛśaḥ bhṛśam sahasā dāruṇaḥ daṃḍaḥ tava daivāt bhaviṣyati tasmāt tava kulam duṣṭam naṣṭam iti avadhāraya iti uktvā pitaram ruṣṭā satī saṃtyakta sādhvasā tad artham eva kṛtavān suciram duścaram tapaḥ tasmāt tam anugṛhṇāti bhūdhara īśvaram īśvarī yadā gatā satī dakṣam vinindya bhaya vihvalā dakṣāya ca ṛṣibhyaḥ ca cukopa ca śaśāpa tān yasmāt avamatā dakṣa matkṛte anāgasā satī pūjitāḥ ca itarāḥ sarvāḥ sva sutāḥ bhartṛbhiḥ saha bhavitā mānuṣaḥ rājā cākṣuṣasya tvam anvaye prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraḥ ca api pracetasaḥ tena evam vyāhṛtaḥ dakṣaḥ rudreṇa amita tejasā svāyaṃbhuvīm tanum tyaktvā papāta bhuvi duḥkhitaḥ tatas prācetasaḥ dakṣaḥ jajñe vai cākṣuṣe antare prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraḥ ca eva pracetasām antare brahmaṇaḥ yajñe vāruṇīm bibhrataḥ tanum tadā dakṣasya dharma artham yajñe tasya durātmanaḥ maheśaḥ kṛtavān vighnam manāḥ sati iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe satīdehatyāgaḥ nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ katham dakṣasya dharma artham pravṛttasya durātmanaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca saṃkīḍati tayā sārddham kāle bahutare gate tatas himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe dakṣaḥ vai yajñam āharat gaṃgādvāre śubhe deśe ṛṣi siddha niṣevite ādityāḥ vasavaḥ rudrāḥ sādhyāḥ saha marut gaṇaiḥ ūṣmapāḥ somapāḥ ca eva ājyapāḥ dhūmapāḥ tathā aśvinau pitaraḥ ca eva tathā ca anye mahā ṛṣayaḥ viṣṇunā sahitāḥ sarve svāgatāḥ yajña bhāginaḥ dṛṣṭvā devakulam sarvam īśvareṇa vinā āgatam dadhīcaḥ manyunā āviṣṭaḥ dakṣam evam abhāṣata dadhīcaḥ uvāca a prapūjye ca eva pūjā pūjyānām ca api a pūjane naraḥ pāpam avāpnoti mahat vai na atra saṃśayaḥ daṃḍaḥ deva kṛtaḥ tatra sadyas patati dāruṇaḥ evam uktvā tu viprarṣiḥ punar dakṣam abhāṣata pūjyam tu paśubhartāram kasmāt nā arcayase prabhum dakṣaḥ uvāca santi me bahavaḥ rudrāḥ śūla hastāḥ kapardinaḥ ekādaśā avasthitāḥ ye na anyam vedmi maheśvaram dadhīcaḥ uvāca rājā ced adhvarasya asya na rudraḥ pūjyate tvayā brahma viṣṇu maheśānām sraṣṭā yaḥ prabhuḥ avyayaḥ brahma ādayaḥ piśāca antāḥ yasya kaiṃkarya vādinaḥ prakṛtīnām paraḥ ca eva puruṣasya ca yaḥ paraḥ yaḥ sraṣṭā ca eva saṃhartā bhartā ca eva maheśvaraḥ tasmāt anyam na paśyāmi śaṃkara ātmānam adhvare dakṣaḥ uvāca dadhīcaḥ uvāca tasmāt dakṣa tava aśeṣaḥ yajñaḥ ayam na bhaviṣyati etasmin eva kāle tu jñātvā etat sarvam īśvarāt devyā saṃcoditaḥ devaḥ dakṣa adhvara jighāṃsayā sasarja sahasā vīram vīrabhadram gaṇeśvaram śūla ṭaṃka gadā hastam dīpta kārmuka dhāriṇam daṃṣṭrā karālam bibhrāṇam mahā vaktram mahā udaram vidyut jihvam pralaṃba uṣṭham megha sāgara niḥsvanam gaṇḍa dvitaya saṃsṛṣṭa maṇḍalīkṛta kuṇḍalam vara amara śiraḥ mālā āvalī kalita śekharam raṇat nūpura keyūra mahā kanaka bhūṣitam ratna saṃcaya saṃdīptam tāra hāra āvṛta urasam mahā śarabha śārdūla siṃhaiḥ sadṛśa vikramam śaṃkha cāmara kunda indu mṛṇāla sadṛśa prabham sa tuṣāram iva adri indram sākṣāt jaṃgama tām gatam jvālā mālā parikṣiptam dīpta mauktika bhūṣaṇam sa jānubhyām mahīm gatvā praṇataḥ prāṃjaliḥ tatas pārśvatas devadevasya paryatiṣṭhat gaṇeśvaraḥ manyunā ca asṛjat bhadrām bhadrakālīm maheśvarīm tam dṛṣṭvā avasthitam vīrabhadram kālāgni sannibham sa ca vijñāpayāmāsa saha devyā maheśvaram ājñāpaya mahādeva kim kāryam karavāṇi aham vīrabhadram mahā bāhum vācā vipula nādayā prācetasasya dakṣasya yajñam sadyas vināśaya bhadrakālyā saha asi tvam etat kṛtyam gaṇeśvara aham api anayā sārddham raibhya āśrama sapīpataḥ sthitvā vīkṣe gaṇeśāna vikramam tava duḥsaham kana khale ye tu gaṃgādvāra samīpa gāḥ suvarṇa śṛṃgasya gireḥ meru mandara saṃnibhāḥ āliṃgya ca samāghrāya mūrdhni ṣaḍvadanam yathā dakṣam vaireṇa tam tasmāt bhindhi yajñam gaṇeśvara yajña lakṣmīm alakṣmīm tvam bhadra kṛtvā mama ājñayā yajamānam ca tam hatvā vatsa hiṃsaya bhadrayā aśeṣām iva tām ājñām śivayoḥ citra kṛtyayoḥ atha eṣa bhagavān kruddhaḥ preta āvāsa kṛta ālayaḥ sasarja romakūpebhyaḥ romaja ākhyān gaṇa īśvarān dakṣiṇāt bhuja deśāt tu śata koṭi ga viśvarān pādāt tathā ūru deśāt ca pṛṣṭhāt pārśvāt mukhāt galāt guhyāt gulphāt śiraḥ madhyāt kaṃṭhāt āsyāt tathā udarāt saṃchāditam abhūt sarvam sa ākāśa vivaram jagat śūla śakti gadā hastāḥ ṭaṃka upala śilā dharāḥ kālāgni rudra sadṛśāḥ tri netrāḥ ca jaṭā dharāḥ nipetuḥ bhṛśam ākāśe śataśas siṃhavāhanāḥ vineduḥ ca mahā nādān jaladāḥ iva bhadrajāḥ kāla anala śataiḥ yuktaḥ yathā ante kālabhairavaḥ teṣām madhye samāruhya vṛṣa indram vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ jagāma bhagavān bhadraḥ śubham abhram yathā bhavaḥ babhāra mauktikam chatram gṛhīta sita cāmaraḥ bhagavān iva śaila indraḥ pārśve viśva jagat guroḥ saḥ api tena babhau bhadraḥ śveta cāmara pāṇinā bāla somena saumyena yathā śūla vara āyudhaḥ bhānu kaṃpaḥ mahā tejāḥ hema ratnaiḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ vavṛṣuḥ śataśas mūrdhni puṣpa varṣam balāhakāḥ phullānām madhu garbhāṇām puṣpāṇām gandha bandhavaḥ mārga anukūla saṃvāhāḥ vabuḥ ca pathi mārutāḥ tatas gaṇeśvarāḥ sarve mattāḥ yuddha bala uddhatāḥ tad kṣaṇāt eva dakṣasya yajña vāṭam raṇmayam praviveśa mahā bāhuḥ vīrabhadraḥ mahā anugaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe vīrabhadrotpattivarṇanam nāma ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca tatas viṣṇu pradhānānām surāṇām amita ojasām sudarbha ṛtu saṃstīrṇam su samiddha hutāśanam kāṃcanaiḥ yajña bhāṃḍaiḥ ca bhrājiṣṇubhiḥ alaṃkṛtam ṛṣibhiḥ yajña paṭubhiḥ yathāvat karma kartṛbhiḥ vidhinā veda dṛṣṭena su anuṣṭhita bahu kramam deva aṃganā sahasra āḍhyam apsaraḥ gaṇa sevitam veṇu vīṇā ravaiḥ juṣṭam veda ghoṣaiḥ ca bṛṃhitam dṛṣṭvā dakṣa adhvare vīraḥ vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān siṃha nādam tadā cakre gaṃbhīraḥ jaladaḥ yathā tatas kilakilā śabdaḥ ākāśam pūrayan iva gaṇeśvaraiḥ kṛtaḥ jajñe mahān nyakkṛta sāgaraḥ dudruvuḥ paritas bhītāḥ srasta vastra vibhūṣaṇāḥ kim svid bhagnaḥ mahā meruḥ kim svid saṃdīryate mahī kim idam kim idam vā iti jajalpuḥ tridaśāḥ bhṛśam mṛga indrāṇām yathā nādam gaja indrāḥ gahane vane śrutvā tathāvidham kecid tatyajuḥ jīvitam bhayāt marutaḥ ca vyaghūrṇanta cukṣubhe makara ālayaḥ grahāḥ ca na prakāśante nakṣatrāṇi ca tārakāḥ tam dṛṣṭvā bhīta bhītaḥ api dakṣaḥ dṛḍhaḥ iva sthitaḥ vīrabhadraḥ mahā tejāḥ megha saṃbhīra nissvanaḥ smayan iva tam ālokya dakṣam devāḥ ca ṛtvijaḥ vayam hi anucarāḥ sarve śarvasya amita tejasaḥ bhāga abhilipsayā prāptāḥ bhāgaḥ naḥ saṃpradīyatām kathyatām kāraṇam tatra yudhyatām vā mayā amaraiḥ iti uktāḥ te gaṇa indreṇa devāḥ dakṣa purogamāḥ ūcuḥ mantrāḥ pramāṇam naḥ na vayam prabhavaḥ tu iti mantrāḥ ūcuḥ surāḥ yūyam moha upahata cetasaḥ mantra uktāḥ api te devāḥ sarve saṃmūḍha cetasaḥ bhadrāya na daduḥ bhāgam tad prahāṇam abhīpsavaḥ yadā tathyam ca pathyam ca sva vākyam tat vṛthā abhavat athā uvāca gaṇādhyakṣaḥ devān viṣṇu purogamān mantrāḥ pramāṇam na kṛtāḥ yuṣmābhiḥ bala garvitaiḥ yakṣa vāṭam mahā kūṭam yathā atisraḥ puras haraḥ yūpān utpāṭya hotR̥ṇām kaṃṭheṣu ābadhya rajjubhiḥ yajña pātrāṇi citrāṇi bhittvā saṃcūrṇya vāriṇi gṛhītvā ca eva yajña aṃgam gaṃgā srotasi cikṣipuḥ tatra divya anna pānānām rāśayaḥ parvata upamāḥ kṣīra nadyaḥ amṛta srāvāḥ su snigdha dadhi kardamāḥ uccāvacāni māṃsāni bhakṣyāṇi surabhīṇi ca rasavanti ca pānāni lehya coṣyāṇi tāni vai vajraiḥ cakraiḥ mahā śūlaiḥ śaktibhiḥ pāśa paṭṭiśaiḥ musalaiḥ asibhiḥ ṭaṃkaiḥ bhidhi pālaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ uddhatān tridaśān sarvān lokapāla purassarān bibhiduḥ balinaḥ vīrāḥ vīrabhadra aṃga saṃbhavāḥ chindhi bhindhi kṣipa kṣipram māryatām dāryatām iti saṃraṃbha prabhavāḥ krūrāḥ śabdāḥ śravaṇa śaṃkavaḥ yatra tatra gaṇeśānām jajñire samara ucitāḥ vivṛtta nayanāḥ kecid daṣṭa daṃṣṭra uṣṭha tālavaḥ āśrama sthān samākṛṣya mārayanti tapodhanāt kalaśān api bhindantaḥ chindantaḥ maṇi vedikāḥ rakta āsavam pibantaḥ ca nanṛtuḥ gaṇa puṃgavāḥ nirmathya sa indrān amarān gaṇa indrān vṛṣa indra nāga indra mṛgendra sārāḥ cakruḥ bahūni apratima bhāvāḥ sa harṣa romāṇi viceṣṭitāni ākṣipya kecid ca vara āyudhāni mahā bhujaṃgān iva vainateyāḥ utpāṭya ca utpāṭya gṛhāṇi kecid sa jālavātāyana vedikāni vikṣipya vikṣipya jalasya madhye kāla aṃbuda ābhāḥ pramathāḥ nineduḥ udvartita dvāra kapāṭa kuḍyam vidhvasta śālā valabhī gavākṣam aho bata abhajyata yajña vāṭam anātha vat vākyam iva ayathārtham utpāṭyamāneṣu gṛheṣu nāryaḥ hi ānātha śabdān bahuśas pracakruḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe yajñavidhvaṃsanaḥ nāma viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca tatas tridaśa mukhyāḥ te viṣṇu śakra purogamāḥ nijaiḥ a dūṣitaiḥ aṃgaiḥ dṛṣṭvā devān upadrutān daṃḍyān a daṃḍitān matvā cukopa gaṇa puṃgavaḥ tatas triśūlam ādāya śarva śakti nibarhaṇam ūrdhva dṛṣṭiḥ mahā bāhuḥ mukhāt jvālāḥ samutsṛjan vārāṇasyā iva mattasya jagāma prekṣaṇīya tām mahā sarovaram yadvat mattaḥ vāraṇa yūthapaḥ vikurvan bahudhā varṇān nīla pāṃḍura lohitān tatra tatra mahā vegāt carantam śūla dhāriṇam prabhayā iva yuga anta agniḥ calayā dhūma dhūmrayā kalpe śeṣa anala jvālā dagdha a viśva jagat yathā tadā sa vājinam sūryam rudrān rudra gaṇa agraṇīḥ bhadraḥ mūrdhni jaghāna āśu vāma pādena līlayā asibhiḥ pāvakam bhadraḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ tu yamam yamī rudrān dṛḍhena śūlena mudgaraiḥ varuṇam dṛḍhaiḥ parighaiḥ nirṛtim vāyum ṭaṃkaiḥ ṭaṃka dharaḥ svayam nirbibheda raṇe vīraḥ līlayā eva gaṇeśvaraḥ sarvān deva gaṇān sadyas munīn śaṃbhoḥ virodhinaḥ tatas devaḥ sarasvatyāḥ nāsikā agram su śobhanam ciccheda ca kuṭhāreṇa bāhu daṃḍam vibhāvasoḥ agratas dvi aṃgulām jihvām mātuḥ devyāḥ lulāva ca svāhādevyāḥ tathā devaḥ dakṣiṇam nāsikā puṭam prasahya utpāṭayāmāsa bhadraḥ parama vegavān pūṣṇaḥ daśana rekhām ca dīptām muktā āvalīm iva jaghāna dhanuṣaḥ koṭyā sa tena aspaṣṭa vāc abhūt tatas candramasam devaḥ pādāṃguṣṭhena līlayā kṣaṇam kṛmi vat ākramya gharṣayāmāsa bhū tale tat prahṛṣṭā samādāya śiraḥ tāla phala upamam sā devī kaṃḍuka krīḍām cakāra samara aṃgaṇe tatas dakṣasya yajña strī kuśīlā bhartṛbhiḥ yathā pādābhyām ca eva hastābhyām hanyate sma gaṇeśvaraiḥ bahuputram ca aṃgirasam kṛśāśvam kaśyapam tathā gale pragṛhya balinaḥ gaṇapāḥ siṃha vikramāḥ bhartsayantaḥ bhṛśam vāgbhiḥ nirjaghnuḥ mūrdhni muṣṭibhiḥ dharṣitāḥ bhūta vetālaiḥ dārāḥ suta parigrahāḥ pradīpita mahā śālam prabhinna dvāra toraṇam utpāṭita sura anīkam hanyamānam tapodhanam praśānta brahma nirghoṣam prakṣīṇa jana saṃcayam krandamāna ātura strīkam hata aśeṣa paricchadam śūnya araṇya nibham jajñe yajña vāṭam tadā arditam śūla vega prarugṇāḥ ca bhinna bāhu ūru vakṣasaḥ vinikṛtta uttamāṃgāḥ ca petuḥ urvyām sura uttamāḥ hateṣu teṣu deveṣu patita iṣuḥ sahasraśas praviveśa gaṇa īśānaḥ kṣaṇāt āhavanīyakam praviṣṭam atha tam dṛṣṭvā bhadram kālāgni saṃnibham dudrāva maraṇāt bhītaḥ yajñaḥ mṛga vapuḥ dharaḥ sa visphāryya mahat cāpam dṛḍha jyā ghoṣaṇa bhīṣaṇam ākarṇapūrṇam ākṛṣṭam dhanuḥ ambuda saṃnibham nādayāmāsa ca jyām dyām kham ca bhūmim ca sarvaśas śaraṇa ardhena vakreṇa sa vīraḥ adhvara pūruṣam mṛga rūpeṇa dhāvantam viśiraskam tadā akarot tam īdṛśam avajñātam dṛṣṭvā vai sūrya saṃbhavam viṣṇuḥ parama saṃkruddhaḥ yuddhāya abhavat udyataḥ sarveṣām vayasām rājā garuḍaḥ pannagāśanaḥ devāḥ ca hata śiṣṭāḥ ye devarāja purogamāḥ pracakruḥ tasya sāhāyyam prāṇān tyaktum iva udyatāḥ viṣṇunā sahitān devān mṛgendraḥ kroṣṭukān iva dṛṣṭvā jahāsa bhūta indraḥ mṛgendraḥ iva vivyathaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe devadaṃḍavarṇanam nāma ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sahasra sūrya saṃkāśaḥ cāru cīra vṛṣa dhvajaḥ sañcita aneka divya astra śastra ratna pariṣkṛtaḥ sa tam ratha varam brahmā śāsanāt eva śūlinaḥ hareḥ samīpam ānīya kṛtāñjaliḥ abhāṣata bhagavan bhadra bhadrāṃga bhagavān indu bhūṣaṇaḥ ājñāpayati vīraḥ tvām ratham āroḍhum avyayaḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā sa vīraḥ gaṇa kuñjaraḥ tatas śaṃkha varam dīptam pūrṇa candra sama prabham pradadhmau vadane kṛtvā bhānu kaṃpaḥ mahā balaḥ śrutvā bhayena devānām jajvāla jaṭhara analaḥ yakṣa vidyādhara ahi indraiḥ siddhaiḥ yuddha didṛkṣubhiḥ kṣaṇena nibaḍībhūtāḥ sa ākāśa vivarāḥ diśāḥ tatas śārGgeṇa ca apāGkāt sa nārāyaṇa nīradaḥ mahatā bāṇa dīptam āśīviṣa upamam jagrāha gaṇapaḥ śrīmān svayam ugra parākramaḥ bāṇa uddhāre bhujaḥ hi asya tūṇī vadana saṃgataḥ pratyadṛśyata valmīkam vivekṣuḥ iva pannagaḥ samuddhṛtaḥ kare tasya tad kṣaṇam vṛṣaḥ tatas tu aśani kalpena krūra āsyena mahā iṣuṇā visasarja śaram vegāt vīrabhadraḥ mahā balaḥ sa ca viṣṇuḥ punar bhadram bhadraḥ viṣṇum tathā punar sa ca tam sa ca tam viprāḥ śaraiḥ tau anujaghnatuḥ tayoḥ parasparam vegāt śarān āśu vimuṃcatoḥ hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt ākāśe khecara īritaḥ tatas tu anala tuṃḍena śareṇa āditya varcasā vivyādha su dṛḍham bhadraḥ viṣṇoḥ mahati vakṣasi sa tu tīvra prapātena śareṇa dṛḍham āhataḥ mahatīm rujam āsādya nipapāta vimohitaḥ punar kṣaṇāt iva utthāya labdha saṃjñaḥ tadā hariḥ sarvāṇi api ca divya astrāṇi atha enam pratyavāsṛjat sa ca viṣṇuḥ dhanuḥ muktān sarvān śarva camūpatiḥ sahasā vārayāmāsa ghoraiḥ pratiśaraiḥ śarān tatas viṣṇuḥ sva nāma aṃkam bāṇam avyāhatam kvacid tam bāṇam bāṇa varyeṇa bhadraḥ bhadra āhvayeṇa tu atha ekena iṣuṇā śārGgam dvābhyām pakṣau garutmataḥ tatas yoga balāt viṣṇuḥ dehāt devān su dāruṇān śaṃkha cakra gadā hastān visasarja sahasraśas sarvān tān kṣaṇa mātreṇa traipurān iva śaṃkaraḥ nirdadāha mahā bāhuḥ netra sṛṣṭena vahninā smayan iva gaṇeśānaḥ vyaṣṭaṃbhayat ayatnataḥ icchan api samutsraṣṭum na viṣṇuḥ abhavat kṣamaḥ atiṣṭhat alasaḥ bhūtvā pāṣāṇaḥ iva niścalaḥ viśarīraḥ yathā ājīvaḥ viśṛGgaḥ vā yathā vṛṣaḥ vidaṃṣṭraḥ ca yathā siṃhaḥ tathā viṣṇuḥ avasthitaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā durdaśā āpannam viṣṇum indra ādayaḥ surāḥ samunnaddhāḥ gaṇa indreṇa mṛga indreṇa iva go vṛṣāḥ pragṛhīta āyudhāḥ yauddhuṃkruddhāḥ sisṛkṣoḥ eva udvajraḥ citrīkṛtaḥ iva abhavat anyeṣām api sarveṣām sa raktāḥ api bāhavaḥ alasānām iva āraṃbhāḥ tādṛśāḥ pratiyānti uta evam bhagavatā tena vyāhata aśeṣa vaibhavāt amarāḥ samare tasya vīraḥ visṛjan babhau visṛjan sarva bhūtāni yathā ādau viśva saṃbhavaḥ tathā vīraḥ kṣaṇāt eva śaraiḥ prācchādayat diśaḥ kha maṃḍale gaṇa indrasya śarāḥ kanaka bhūṣitāḥ mahāntaḥ te sura gaṇān maṃḍūkān iva ḍuṃḍubhāḥ prāṇaiḥ viyojayāmāsuḥ papuḥ ca rudhira āsavam nikṛtta bāhavaḥ kecid kecid lūna vara ānanāḥ pārśve vidāritāḥ kecid nipetuḥ amarāḥ bhuvi vivṛtta nayanāḥ kecid nipetuḥ bhū tale mṛtāḥ gām praveṣṭum iva icchantaḥ kham gantum iva lipsavaḥ bhūmau kecid praviviśuḥ parvatānām guhāḥ pare evam deva balam sarvam dīnam bībhatsa darśanam gaṇeśvara samutpannam kṛpaṇam vapuḥ ādade tadā tridaśa vīrāṇām asṛj salila vāhinī prāvartata nadī ghorā prāṇinām bhaya śaṃsinī rakta ārdra vasanā śyāmā hata śuṃbhā iva kaiśikī tasmin mahati saṃvṛtte samare bhṛśa dāruṇe petuḥ ca ulkāḥ mahā utpātāḥ śākhāḥ ca mumucuḥ drumāḥ aprasannāḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ pavanaḥ ca aśivaḥ vavau dharma ādayaḥ sadasyāḥ ca rakṣitā garuḍadhvajaḥ bhāgān ca pratigṛhṇanti sākṣāt indra ādayaḥ surāḥ tasmāt na a veda nirdiṣṭam na ca īśvara bahiṣkṛtam na asat parigṛhītam ca karma kuryāt kadācana kṛtvā api su mahat puṇyam iṣṭvā yajña śataiḥ api kṛtvā api su mahat pāpam bhaktyā yajati yaḥ śivam mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvaiḥ na atra kāryā pradudruvuḥ gāḍha rujā abhibhūtāḥ celuḥ kvacid kecana śīrṇa keśāḥ seduḥ kvacid kecana dīrgha gātrāḥ kecid ca tatra tridaśāḥ vipannāḥ visrasta vastra ābharaṇa astra śastrāḥ babhau gaṇeśaḥ sa mantriṇaḥ dhārayantaḥ añjalīn mūrdhni tuṣṭuvuḥ vividhaiḥ stavaiḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ namaḥ śivāya śāntāya yajña hantre triśūline rudra bhadrāya rudrāṇām pataye rudra bhūtaye kālāgni rudra rūpāya kāla kāma aṃga hāriṇe devatānām śiraḥ hantre dakṣasya ca durātmanaḥ saṃsargāt asya pāpasya dakṣasya akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ śāsitāḥ samare vīra tvayā vayam aninditā dagdhāḥ ca amī vayam sarve tvattaḥ bhītāḥ ca bho prabho tvam eva gatiḥ asmākam trāhi naḥ śaraṇa āgatān vāyuḥ uvāca tuṣṭaḥ tu evam stutaḥ devān visṛjya nigaḍāt prabhuḥ sa gaṇaḥ sarvagaḥ śarvaḥ sarva loka mahā īśvaraḥ tam dṛṣṭvā parameśānam devāḥ viṣṇu purogamāḥ prītāḥ api ca bhītāḥ ca namaḥ cakruḥ maheśvaram dṛṣṭvā tān amarān bhītān praṇata ārti haraḥ haraḥ idam āha mahādevaḥ prahasan prekṣya pārvatīm mahādevaḥ uvāca mā abhaiṣṭa tridaśāḥ sarve yūyam vai māmikāḥ prajāḥ anugraha artham eva iha dhṛtaḥ daṃḍaḥ kṛpālunā bhavatām nirjjarāṇām hi kṣāntaḥ asmābhiḥ vyatikramaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca iti uktāḥ tridaśāḥ sarve śarveṇa amita tejasā devāḥ ūcuḥ nimajjanāt mṛtaḥ prāpa sukham mihira jājaliḥ saubhāgyam atulam prāpa somavāravratāt sutān śrīkarāya dadau devaḥ svīyam padam anuttamam sudarśanam arakṣaḥ tvam nṛpa maṃḍala bhītitaḥ meduram tārayāmāsa sa dāram ca ghṛṇā nidhiḥ śāradām vidhavām cakre sa dhavām kriyayā bhavān viṣṇuḥ uvāca tvam śaṃbho kahari īśāḥ ca rajaḥ sattva tamaḥ guṇaiḥ kartā pātā tathā hartā jana anugraha kāṃkṣayā sarva vidyā ādi gūḍhaḥ ca sarva anugraha kārakaḥ tvattaḥ sarvam ca tvam sarvam tvayi sarvam giri īśvara trāhi trāhi punar trāhi kṛpām kuru mama upari atha asmin antare brahmā praṇipatya kṛtāṃjaliḥ evam tu avasaram prāpya vyajñāpayata śūline īdṛśeṣu aparādheṣu kaḥ anyaḥ tvattaḥ prasīdati yat idam devadevānām kṛta mantuṣu dūṣaṇam tat idam bhūṣaṇam manyeta aṃgīkāra gauravāt iti vijñāpyamānaḥ tu brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā deva ādīnām yathāpūrvam aṃgāni pradadau prabhuḥ prathama ādyaiḥ ca yāḥ devyaḥ daṃḍitāḥ devamātaraḥ tāsām api yathāpūrvāṇi aṃgāni giriśaḥ dadau dakṣasya bhagavān eva svayam brahmā pitāmahaḥ saḥ api saṃjñām tatas labdhvā sa dṛṣṭvā jīvitaḥ sudhī bhītaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ śaṃbhum tuṣṭāva pralapan bahu dakṣaḥ uvāca kṛpām kuru maheśāna aparādham me kṣamasva ha mayā jñātam viśeṣeṇa viṣṇu ādi sakala īśvaraḥ tvayā eva vitatam sarvam vyāptam sṛṣṭam na nāśitam na hi tvad adhikāḥ kecid īśāḥ te acyutaka ādayaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca tam tathā vyākulam bhītam pralapantam kṛta āgasam smayan iva avadat prekṣya mā bhaiḥ iti ghṛṇā nidhiḥ gāṇapatyam dadau tasmai dakṣāya akṣayam īśvaraḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ praśrayā vācā śaṃkaram girijādhipam brahma ādayaḥ ūcuḥ jaya śaṃkara deveśa dīnānātha mahā prabho kṛpām kuru maheśāna aparādham no kṣamasva vai kṛpām kuru maśāna aparādham naḥ kṣamasva vai duṣṭa daṇḍa prada svāmin kṛpām kuru namaḥ astu te tvam prabho garva hartā vai duṣṭānām tvām a jānatām rakṣakaḥ hi viśeṣeṇa satām tvad sakta cetasām adbhutam caritam te hi niścitam kṛpayā tava sarva aparādhaḥ kṣantavyaḥ vibhavaḥ dīna vatsalāḥ vāyuḥ uvāca cakāra anugraham teṣām brahma ādīnām divaukasām dadau narān ca su prītyā śaṃkaraḥ dīna vatsalaḥ sa ca tatas tridaśān śaraṇa āgatān parama kāruṇikaḥ parameśvaraḥ anugata smita lakṣaṇayā girā śamita sarva bhayaḥ samabhāṣata śivaḥ uvāca iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe giriśānunayaḥ nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kva yātaḥ kutra vāsaḥ kim kṛtvā virarāma ha vāyuḥ uvāca mahīdhara varaḥ śrīmān mandaraḥ citra kandaraḥ tapaḥ mahat kṛtam tena voḍhum sva śirasā śivau na śakyam vistarāt vaktum varṣa koṭi śataiḥ api parvata antara saundaryyam sādhāraṇa vidhāraṇāt ṛddhyā kayā api saundaryam īśvara āvāsa yogya tā atīva ramaṇīyaḥ yam giriḥ antaḥpurīkṛtaḥ pitṛbhyām jagataḥ nityam snāna pāna upayogataḥ adhirājyena ca adrīṇām adrīreṣaḥ abhiṣicyate niśāsu śikhara prāntar vartinā sa śiloccayaḥ candreṇa acala sāmrājya chatreṇa iva virājate sa śailaḥ caṃcalībhūtaiḥ bālaiḥ ca amara yoṣitām darpaṇe deha saubhāgyam draṣṭu kāmaḥ iva sthitaḥ kūjat vihaṃga vācālaiḥ vāta uddhṛta latā bhujaiḥ jaya āśiṣā saha abhyarcya niṣevyate iva adrirāj prapatan iva pātāle bhū pṛṣṭhāt utpatan iva ajīrṇa lāvaṇya tayā jṛṃbhamāṇaḥ iva acalaḥ nivāsa bhūmayaḥ tāḥ tāḥ darpaṇa pratimā udarāḥ tiraskṛta ātapāḥ snigdha āśrama chāyā mahīruhāḥ sarit saraḥ taḍāga ādi saṃparka śiśira anilāḥ tatra tatra niṣaṇṇābhyām śivābhyām saphalīkṛtāḥ tam imam sarvatas śreṣṭham smṛtvā sāmbaḥ triyambakaḥ raibhya āśrama samīpa sthaḥ ca antardhānam gataḥ yayau rarāma ramaṇīyāsu devyā antaḥpura bhūmiṣu tathā gateṣu kāleṣu pravṛddhāsu prajāsu ca daityau śuṃbha niśuṃbha ākhyau bhrātarau saṃbabhūvatuḥ tābhyām tapaḥ balāt dattam brahmaṇā parameṣṭinā ayoni jā tu yā kanyā hi aṃbikā aṃśa samudbhavā a jāta puṃsparśa ratiḥ a vilaṃghya parākramā tayā tu nau vadhaḥ saṃkhye tasyām kāma abhibhūtayoḥ tatas prabhṛti śakra ādīn vijitya samare surān niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāram jagat cakratuḥ akramāt vinindya api rahasyam vām krodhayitvā yathā tathā tad varṇa kośa jām śaktim akāmām kanyakā ātmikām kāli iti āha rahasyam vām nindayan iva sa smitaḥ tatas kruddhā tadā devī suvarṇā varṇa kāraṇāt smayantī ca āha bhartāram asamādheyayā girā evāvantam ciram kālam katham eṣā niyamyate yā ca nā abhimatā bhartuḥ api sarva aṃga sundarī sā vṛthā eva hi jāyeta sarvaiḥ api guṇa antaraiḥ tathā asatī anyathābhūtā nārī kutra upayujyate varṇa antaram bhajiṣye vā na bhajiṣyāmi vā svayam iti uktvā utthāya śayanāt devī sā ācaṣṭa gadgadam pādayoḥ praṇaman eva bhavānīm pratyabhāṣata īśvaraḥ uvāca a jānatī ca krīḍā uktim priye kim kupitā asi me pṛthagjanānām rataye kāma ātmā kalpitaḥ mayā tatas katham upālabdhaḥ kāma dāhāt aham tvayā mām vai tridaśa sāmānyam manyamānaḥ manobhavaḥ vihāraḥ upya āvayoḥ asya jagataḥ trāṇa kāraṇāt śruta pūrvam hi bhagavan tava cāṭu vacaḥ mayā prāṇān api apriyā bhartuḥ nārī yā na parityajet kula aṃganā śubhā sadbhiḥ kutsitā eva hi gamyate krīḍā uktiḥ api kāli iti ghaṭate katham anyathā śivaḥ uvāca mama icchayā sva icchayā vā varṇa antaravatī bhava brahmāṇam tapasā ārādhya kṣipram gaurī bhavāmi aham īśvaraḥ uvāca mad prasādāt purā brahmā brahma tvam prāptavān purā tam āhūya mahādevi tapasā kim kariṣyasi tathā api ārādhya tapasā brahmāṇam tvad niyogataḥ purā kila satī nāmnā dakṣasya duhitā abhavam jagatām patim evam tvām patim prāptavatī tathā na tām nirbandhayāmāsa deva kārya cikīrṣayā iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe śivamandaragirinivāsakrīḍoktavarṇanam nāma caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca tatas pradakṣiṇīkṛtya patim ambā pativratā tapaḥ kṛtavatī pūrvam deśe yasmin sakhī janaiḥ tatas sva pitaram dṛṣṭvā mātaram ca tayoḥ gṛhe praṇamya vṛttam vijñāpya tābhyām ca anumatā satī punar tapaḥ vanam gatvā bhūṣaṇāni visṛjya ca snātvā tapasvinaḥ veṣam kṛtvā parama pāvanam saṃkalpya ca mahā tīvram tapaḥ parama duścaram tam eva kṣaṇike liṃge dhyātvā bāhya vidhānataḥ tathā tapaḥ carantīm tām kāle bahutithe gate dṛṣṭaḥ kaścid mahā vyāghraḥ duṣṭa bhāvāt upāgamat gātram citra arpitam iva stabdham tasyāḥ sakāśatas tam dṛṣṭvā api tathā vyāghram duṣṭa bhāvāt upāgatam sa tu viṣṭabdha sarva aṃgaḥ bubhukṣā paripīḍitaḥ nirīkṣyamāṇaḥ satatam devīm eva tadā aniśam devyāḥ ca hṛdaye nityam mama eva ayam upāsakaḥ trātā ca duṣṭa sattvebhyaḥ iti pravavṛte kṛpā tasyāḥ eva kṛpā yogāt sadyas naṣṭa mala trayaḥ babhūva sahasā vyāghraḥ devīm ca bubudhe tadā tadā parama bhāvena jñātvā kārtārthyam ātmanaḥ duṣṭānām api sattvānām tathā anyeṣān durātmanām tapaḥ ca vavṛdhe devyāḥ tīvram tīvratara ātmakam devāḥ ca daitya nirbandhāt brahmāṇam śaraṇam gatāḥ cakruḥ nivedanam devāḥ sva duḥkhasya ari pīḍanāt saḥ api śrutvā vidhiḥ duḥkham surāṇām kṛpayā anvitaḥ āsīt daitya vadhāya eva smṛtvā hetu āśrayām kathām dadarśa ca suraśreṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhe tapasi niṣṭhitām pratiṣṭhām iva viśvasya bhavānīm parameśvarīm rudrasya ca pituḥ bhāryām āryām adrīśvara ātmajām brahmāṇam āgatam dṛṣṭvā devī deva gaṇaiḥ saha tapaḥ phalānām sarveṣām tvad adhīnāḥ hi siddhayaḥ bhartāram ātmanā prāpya prāptam ca tapasaḥ phalam sarga ādau bhavataḥ devāt utpattiḥ śrūyate yadā tadā prajānām prathamaḥ tvam me prathama jaḥ sutaḥ yadā punar prajā vṛddhyai lalāṭāt bhavataḥ bhavaḥ utpannaḥ abhūt tadā tvam me guruḥ śvaśura bhāvataḥ tat īdṛśasya bhavataḥ lokayātrā vidhāyinaḥ kim atra bahunā dehe yaḥ ca ayam mama kālimā etāvatā kimarthena tīvram devi tapaḥ kṛtam svecchā eva kim aparyāptā krīḍā iyam hi tava īdṛśī atas mama iṣṭam anayā phalam kim api sādhyatām niśuṃbha śuṃbha nāmānau daityau datta varau mayā alam vilaṃbanena atra tvam kṣaṇena sthirā bhava brāhmaṇa abhyarthitā ca eva devī giri vara ātmajā tvac kośam sahasā utsṛjya gaurī sā samajāyata sā tvak kośa ātmanā utsṛṣṭā kauśikī nāma nāmataḥ kālī kāla ambuda prakhyā kanyakā samapadyata sā tu māyā ātmikā śaktiḥ yoganidrā ca vaiṣṇavī śaṃkha cakra triśūla ādi sa āyudha aṣṭa mahā bhujā saumyā ghorā ca miśrā ca trinetrā candraśekharā ajāta
