puṃsparśa ratiḥ adhṛṣyā ca ati sundarī dattā ca brahmaṇe devyā śaktiḥ eṣā sanātanī niśuṃbhasya ca śuṃbhasya nihantrī daitya siṃhayoḥ brahmaṇā api prahṛṣṭena tasyai parama śaktaye vindhye ca vasatim tasyāḥ pūjām āsava pūrvakaiḥ māṃsaiḥ matsyaiḥ apūpaiḥ ca nirvartya asau samādiśat sā ca eva saṃmatā śaktiḥ brahmaṇaḥ viśvakarmaṇaḥ praṇamya mātaram gaurīm brahmāṇam ca anupūrvaśas śaktibhiḥ ca api tulyābhiḥ sva ātmajābhiḥ anekaśas tad bāṇaiḥ kāma bāṇaiḥ ca chinna bhinna aṃga mānasau ūhanīyam parasmāt ca prastutam varṇayāmi vaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe devīgauratvabhavanam nāma paṃcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca utpādya kauśikīm gaurī brahmaṇe pratipādya tām dṛṣṭaḥ kim eṣa bhavatā śārdūlaḥ mad upāśrayaḥ bhavitavyam anena atas mama antaḥpura cāriṇā gaṇeśvara padam ca asmai prītyā dāsyati śaṃkaraḥ pradīyatām anujñā me prajānām patinā tvayā tasya tīvraiḥ purāvṛttaiḥ daurātmyam samavarṇayat paśau devi mṛgāḥ krūrāḥ kva ca te anugrahaḥ śubhaḥ āśīviṣa mukhe sākṣāt amṛtam kim niṣicyate vyāghra mātreṇa san eṣa duṣṭaḥ kaḥ api niśācaraḥ anena bhakṣitāḥ gāvaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca tapodhanāḥ tarpayan tān yathākāmam kāmarūpī carati asau avaśyam khalu bhoktavyam phalam pāpasya karmaṇaḥ atas kim kṛpayā kṛtyam īdṛśeṣu durātmasu anena devyāḥ kim kṛtyam prakṛtyā kaluṣa ātmanā yat uktam bhavatā sarvam tathyam astu ayam īdṛśaḥ tathā api mām prapannaḥ abhūt na tyājyaḥ mām upāśritaḥ puṇya karmā api kim kuryyāt tvadīya ajñāna apekṣayā ajā prajñā purāṇī ca tvam eva parameśvarī tvad adhīnā hi sarveṣām bandha mokṣa vyavasthitiḥ tvat ṛte paramā śaktiḥ saṃsiddhiḥ kasya karmaṇā tvam eva vividhā śaktiḥ bhavānām atha vā svayam aśaktaḥ karma karaṇe kartā vā kim kariṣyati viṣṇoḥ ca mama ca anyeṣām deva dānava rakṣasām tad tad aiśvarya samprāptyai tava eva ājñā hi kāraṇam atītāḥ khalu asaṃkhyātāḥ brahmāṇaḥ harayaḥ bhavāḥ anāgatāḥ tu asaṃkhyātāḥ tvad ājñā anuvidhāyinaḥ tvām an ārādhya deveśi puruṣa artha catuṣṭayam sukṛtam duṣkṛtam ca api tvayā iva sthāpitam yatas an ādi madhya nidhanā śaktiḥ ādyā sanātanī samasta lokayātrā artham mūrtim āviśya kām api krīḍase vividhaiḥ bhāvaiḥ kaḥ tvām jānāti tattvataḥ iti ātmanaḥ param bhāvam smārayitvā anurūpataḥ devīm ca mātaram dṛṣṭvā menām himavatā saha praṇamya āśvāsya bahudhā pitarau viraha asahau viprayoga śucā iva agre puṣpa bāṣpam vimuṃcataḥ tad tuccha ākhā samārūḍha vihagaḥ dīritaiḥ rutaiḥ vyākulam bahudhā dīnam vilāpam iva kurvataḥ sarveṣām jagatām dhātā kartā pātā vināśa kṛt iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe vyāghragativarṇanam nāma ṣaḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kṛtvā gauram vapuḥ divyam devī giri vara ātmajā katham dadarśa bhartāram praviṣṭā manditam satī gaṇeśaiḥ kim kṛtam devaḥ tān dṛṣṭvā kim tadā akarot vāyuḥ uvāca pravaktum aṃjasā yena praṇaya garbheṇa bhāvaḥ bhāvavatām hṛtaḥ śaṃkamānā praviṣṭā antar tat ca sā samapaśyata praṇamya nā utthitā yāvat tāvat tām parameśvaraḥ pragṛhya dorbhyām āśliṣya paritas parayā mudā sva aṃke dhartum pravṛttā api sā paryyaṃke nyaṣīdata tayā saṃbhāṣaṇāya īśaḥ pūrva bhāṣitam abravīt sā daśā ca vyatītā kim tava sarva aṃga sundari sva icchayā api na kālī iti na anya varṇavatī iti ca tvad svabhāva āhṛtam cittam subhru ciṃtā āvaham mama vismṛtaḥ paramaḥ bhāvaḥ katham sva icchā aṃga yogataḥ aham agni śiraḥ niṣṭhaḥ tvam soma śirasi sthitā agnīṣoma ātmakam viśvam āvābhyām samadhiṣṭhitam jagat hitāya caratoḥ sva icchā dhṛta śarīrayoḥ tvam hi vāc amṛtam sākṣāt aham artha amṛtam param vidyā vedya ātmanoḥ eva viśleṣaḥ katham āvayoḥ na karmaṇā sṛjāmi idam jagat pratisṛjāmi ca sarvasya ājñā eka labhya tvāt ājñā tvam hi garīyasī ājñā eka sāram aiśvaryyam yasmāt svātantrya lakṣaṇam ājñayā viprayuktasya ca aiśvaryyam mama kīdṛśam devānām kāryyam uddiśya līlā uktim kṛtavān aham iti priyaṃvade sākṣāt īśvare parameśvare śṛṃgāra bhāva sārāṇām janma bhūmiḥ akṛtrimā lajjayā na kim api ūce kauśikī varṇanāt param tat eva varṇayāmi adya śṛṇu devyāḥ ca varṇanam kim devena na sā dṛṣṭā yā sṛṣṭā kauśikī mayā tādṛśī kanyakā loke na bhūtā na bhaviṣyati tasyāḥ vīryyam balam vindhya nilayam vijayam tathā śuṃbhasya ca niśuṃbhasya māraṇe ca raṇe tayoḥ lokānām rakṣaṇam śaśvat brahmā vijñāpayiṣyati iti saṃbhāṣamāṇāyāḥ devyāḥ eva ājñayā tadā vyāghraḥ sakhyā samānīya puras avasthāpitaḥ tadā tam prekṣya āha punar devī deva ānītam upāyatam vyāghram paśya na ca anena sadṛśaḥ mad upāsakaḥ atīva mama bhaktaḥ ca viśrabdhaḥ ca sva rakṣaṇāt sva deśam ca parityajya prasāda artham samāgataḥ yadi prītiḥ abhūt mattaḥ parām prītim karoṣi me vāyuḥ uvāca madhuram praṇaya udarkam śrutvā devyāḥ śubham vacaḥ prītaḥ asmi iti āha tam devaḥ sa ca adṛśyata tad kṣaṇāt churikām uraga prakhyām gaṇeśaḥ rakṣa veṣa dhṛk somanandī iti vikhyātaḥ tasmāt eṣa samākhyayā ittham devyāḥ priyam kṛtvā devaḥ ca ṛddha indu bhūṣaṇaḥ bhūṣayāmāsa tat divyaiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ ratna bhūṣitaiḥ tatas sa gaurīm giriśaḥ girīndrajām sa gauravām sarva manoharām haraḥ paryyaṃkam āropya varāṃga bhūṣaṇaiḥ vibhūṣayāmāsa śaśāṃka bhūṣaṇaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ devīm samādadhānena devena idam kim īritam agniṣoma ātmakam viśvam vāc artha ātmakam iti api ājñā eka sāram aiśvaryyam ājñā tvam iti ca uditam tat idam śrotum icchāmaḥ yathāvat anupūrvaśas vāyuḥ uvāca somaḥ śāktaḥ amṛta mayaḥ śakteḥ śānti karī tanuḥ amṛtam yat pratiṣṭhā sā tejaḥ vidyā kalā svayam bhūta sūkṣmeṣu sarveṣu te eva rasa tejasī dvividhā tejasaḥ vṛtti sūryya ātmā ca anala ātmikā tathā eva rasa vṛttiḥ ca soma ātmā ca jala ātmikā haviṣe sasya sampattiḥ vṛṣṭiḥ sasya abhivṛddhaye vṛṣṭeḥ eva haviḥ tasmāt agnīṣoma dhṛtam jagat agniḥ ūrddhvam jvalati eṣa yāvat saumyam para amṛtam yāvat ādahanam ca ūrddhvam adhas ca āplāvanam bhavet ādhāra śaktyā eva dhṛtaḥ kālāgniḥ ayam ūrddhva gaḥ tathā eva nimna gaḥ somaḥ śiva śakti pada āspadaḥ śivaḥ ca ūrddhvam adhas śaktiḥ ūrddhvam śaktiḥ adhas śivaḥ tat ittham śiva śaktibhyāt na avyāptam iha kiñcana yaḥ ca ittham bhasma sadbhāvam jñātvā snāti ca bhasmanā śāktena amṛtavarṣeṇa ca adhikārāt nivartayet atas mṛtyuṃjayāya ittham amṛta plāvanam sadā śiva śakti amṛta sparśe labdham yena kutas mṛtiḥ agnīṣoma padam hitvā na sa bhūyas abhijāyate śiva agninā tanum dagdhvā śakti saumyā mṛtena yaḥ agnīṣoma ātmakam viśvam jagat iti anurūpatas iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe bhasmatattvavarṇanam nāma aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca nivedayāmi jagataḥ vāc arthātmyam kṛtam yathā ṣaḍadhva vedanam samyak samāsāt na tu vistarāt nā asti kaścid aśabda arthaḥ nā api śabdaḥ nirarthakaḥ prakṛteḥ pariṇāmaḥ dvidhā śabda artha bhāvanā tām āhuḥ prākṛtīm mūrtim śivayoḥ parama ātmanoḥ śabda ātmikā vibhūtiḥ yā sā tridhā kathyate budhaiḥ sthūlā sūkṣmā parā ca iti sthūlā yā śruti gocarā sūkṣmā cintā mayī proktā ciṃtayā rahitā parā yā śaktiḥ sā parā śaktiḥ śiva tattva samāśrayā jñānaśakti samāyogāt icchā upodbalikā tathā sarva śakti samaṣṭi ātmā śakti tattva samākhyayā samasta kārya jātasya mūlaprakṛti tām gatā sā eva kuṇḍalinī māyā śuddha adhva paramā satī sā vibhāga svarūpā eva ṣaḍadhva ātmā vijṛṃbhate tatra śabdāḥ trayaḥ adhvānaḥ trayaḥ ca arthāḥ samīritāḥ sarveṣām api vai puṃsām naija śuddhi anurūpataḥ parasyāḥ prakṛteḥ ādau paṃcadhā pariṇāmataḥ kalāḥ ca tāḥ nivṛttya ādyāḥ paryyāptāḥ iti niścayaḥ mantrādhvā ca padādhvā ca varṇādhvā ca iti śabdataḥ bhuvana adhvā ca tattva adhvā kalā adhvā ca arthataḥ kramāt atra anyonyam ca sarveṣām vyāpya vyāpaka tā ucyate mantrāḥ sarvaiḥ padaiḥ vyāptāḥ vākya bhāvāt padāni ca varṇaiḥ varṇa samūham hi padam āhuḥ vipaścitaḥ varṇāḥ tu bhuvanaiḥ vyāptāḥ teṣām teṣu upalaṃbhanāt vyāptāni kāraṇaiḥ tattvaiḥ ārabdha tvāt anekaśas paurāṇikāni ca anyāni vijñeyāni śiva āgame śiva śāstra prasiddhāni tatonyāni api kṛtsnaśas parasyāḥ prakṛteḥ ādau paṃcadhā pariṇāmataḥ kalāḥ ca tāḥ nivṛttya ādyāḥ vyāptāḥ paṃca yathottaram vyāpikā atas parā śaktiḥ avibhaktā ṣaḍadhvanām vyāptam ekena tena eva mṛdā kuṃbha ādikam yathā śaivam tat paramam dhāma yat prāpyam ṣaḍbhiḥ adhvabhiḥ tat ūrdhvam vidyayā madhye yāvat viśveśvara avadhi śāntyā tad ūrdhvam madhu ante viśuddhiḥ śānti atītayā yām āhuḥ paramam vyoma para prakṛti yogataḥ śaktipāta samāyogāt ṛte tattvāni tattvataḥ tad vyāptiḥ tad vivṛddhiḥ ca jñātum evam na śakyate śaktiḥ ājñā parā śaivī cit rūpā marameśvarī śivaḥ adhitiṣṭhati akhilam yayā kāraṇa bhūtayā na ātmanaḥ nā eva māyā eṣā na vikāraḥ vicārataḥ sarva aiśvarya parākāṣṭā śivasya vyabhicāriṇī samāna dharmiṇī tasya taiḥ taiḥ bhāvaiḥ viśeṣataḥ sa tayā eva gṛhī sā api tena eva gṛhiṇī sadā ekaḥ eva śivaḥ sākṣāt dvidhā asau samavasthitaḥ apare tu parā śaktiḥ śivasya samavāyinī tasmāt śivaḥ paraḥ hetuḥ tasya ājñā parameśvarī tayā eva preritā śaivī mūlaprakṛtiḥ avyayā mahāmāyā ca māyā ca prakṛtiḥ triguṇā iti ca trividhā kārya vedhena sā prasūte ṣaḍadhvanaḥ sa vāc artha mayaḥ ca adhvā ṣaḍvidhaḥ nikhilam jagat asya eva vistaram prāhuḥ śāstra jātam aśeṣatas iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe vāgarthakatattvavarṇanam nāma ekonatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ caritāni vicitrāṇi gṛhyāṇi gahanāni ca durvijñeyāni devaiḥ ca mohayanti manāṃsi naḥ brahma ādayaḥ lokānām sṛṣṭi sthiti anta hetavaḥ yadi evam īdṛśa aiśvaryyam tat tu svātantrya lakṣaṇam mūrta ātmā sakalaḥ kaścid sa ca anyaḥ niṣphalaḥ śivaḥ mūrti ātmā eva tadā mūrtiḥ śivasya asya bhavet iti anyathā nirapekṣeṇa mūrtiḥ svīkriyate katham mūrti svīkaraṇam tasmāt mūrtau sādhya phala īpsayā sva icchā eva tādṛśī puṃsām yasmāt karma anusāriṇī brahma ādayaḥ piśāca antāḥ kim te karma ativartinaḥ icchayā deha nirmāṇam indrajāla upamam viduḥ aṇima ādi guṇa aiśvaryya vaśīkāra anatikramāt viśva rūpam dadhat viṣṇuḥ dadhīcena mahā ṛṣiṇā śarīravat tayā anya ātma sādharmyam pratibhāti naḥ sarva anugrāhakam prāhuḥ śivam parama kāraṇam sa nirgṛhṇāti devānām sarva anugrāhakaḥ katham ciccheda bahuśas devaḥ brahmaṇaḥ pañcamam śiraḥ viṣṇoḥ api nṛsiṃhasya rabhasā śarabha ākṛtiḥ deva strīṣu ca deveṣu dakṣasya adhvara kāraṇāt vīreṇa vīrabhadreṇa na hi kaścid a daṇḍitaḥ krośatām eva devānām hutaḥ netra hutāśane sa ruṣā prekṣya devena tad kṣaṇe bhasmasātkṛtaḥ jalaṃdhara asuraḥ dīrṇaḥ cakrīkṛtya jalam padā baddhvā anantena yaḥ viṣṇum cikṣepa śata yojanam tam eva jala saṃdhāyī śūlena eva jaghāna saḥ jighāṃsatām surārīṇām kulam nirghṛṇa cetasām triśūlena andhakasya uraḥ śikhinā eva upatāpitam kaṇṭhāt kāla aṃganām sṛṣṭvā dārakaḥ api nipātitaḥ kauśikīm janayitvā tu gauryāḥ tvac kośa gocarām śuṃbhaḥ saha niśuṃbhena prāpitaḥ maraṇam raṇe śrutam ca mahat ākhyānam skānde skanda samāśrayam vihṛtya su ciram devyāḥ rasām rasātalam nītām iva kṛtvā abhidhām tatas devīm ca vaṃcayan tasyām sva vīrya mati durvaham a visṛjya visṛjya agnau haviḥ pūtam iva amṛtam gaṃgā ādiṣu api nikṣipya vahni dvārā tad aṃśataḥ svāhayā kṛttikā rūpāt sva bhartrā ramamāṇayā suvarṇībhūtayā nyastam merau śaravaṇe kvacid saṃdīpayitvā kālena tasya bhāsā diśaḥ daśa rañjayitvā girīn sarvān kāṃcanīkṛtya meruṇā kumāre sukumāra aṅge kumārāṇām nidarśane tat śaiśavam sva rūpam ca tasya dṛṣṭvā manoharam devaḥ svayam āyātaḥ putra darśana lālasaḥ pīta amṛtam iva sneha vivaśena antarātmanā anubhūya ca tad krīḍām saṃbhāvya ca parasparam stanyam ājñāpayan devyāḥ pāyayitvā amṛta upamam tava avatāraḥ jagatām hitāya iti anuśāsya ca tatas śakreṇa saṃdhāya bibhyatā tāraka asurāt kārayitvā abhiṣekam ca senāpatye divaukasām cheditam tārakasya api śiraḥ śakra bhiyā saha stutim cakruḥ viśeṣeṇa hari dhātṛ mukhāḥ surāḥ tathā rakṣodhipaḥ sākṣāt rāvaṇaḥ bala garvitaḥ pada aṃguṣṭha parispandāt mamajja mṛditaḥ bhuvi baṭoḥ kenacid arthena sva āśritasya gata āyuṣaḥ sva vāhanam a vijñāya vṛṣa indram vaḍavānalaḥ śāntaḥ eva sadā sarvam anugṛhṇāti ced śivaḥ kāraṇam khalu karma api bhavet īśvara kāritam iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe śivatattvapraśnaḥ nāma triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca jijñāsā hi na nāstikyam sādhayet sādhu buddhiṣu asatām tu anyathābhāvaḥ prasādena vinā prabhoḥ param sarvam anugrāhyam paśu pāśa ātmakam jagat parasya anugraha artham tu patyuḥ ājñā samanvayaḥ patiḥ ājñāpakaḥ sarvam anugṛhṇāti sarvvadā atas svātantrya śabdārthān anapekṣa tva lakṣaṇaḥ mūrta ātmanaḥ śiva ajñāna nivartanāt ajñāna dhiṣṭhitam śambhoḥ na kiṃcid iha vidyate sa mūrti ātmā śivaḥ śaiva mūrtiḥ iti upacaryate na hi asau niṣkalaḥ sākṣāt śivaḥ parama kāraṇam sa ākāreṇa anubhāvena kena api anupalakṣitaḥ pramāṇa gamya tā mātram tad svabhāva upapādakam na tāvatā atra upekṣā dhīḥ upalakṣaṇam antarā ātma upama ulvaṇam sākṣāt mūrtiḥ eva hi kācana śivasya mūrtiḥ mūrti ātmā paraḥ tasya upalakṣaṇam yathā kāṣṭheṣu an ārūḍhaḥ na vahniḥ upalabhyate evam śivaḥ api mūrti ātmani anārūḍhaḥ iti sthitiḥ yathā agnim ānaya iti ukte jvalat kāṣṭhāt ṛte svayam na agniḥ ānīyate tadvat pūjyaḥ mūrti ātmanā śivaḥ mūrti ātmani kṛtam sākṣāt śive eva kṛtam yatas liṃga ādau api tat kṛtyam arcāyām ca viśeṣataḥ yathā anugṛhyate saḥ api mūrti ātmā pārameṣṭhinā tathā mūrti ātma niṣṭhena śivena paśavaḥ vayam loka anugrahaṇāya eva śivena parameṣṭhinā sadāśiva ādayaḥ sarve mūrti ātmanaḥ adhiṣṭhitāḥ ātmanām eva bhogāya mokṣāya ca viśeṣataḥ tattva atattva svarūpeṣu mūrti ātmasu śiva anvayaḥ bhogaḥ karma vipāka ātmā sukha duḥkha ātmakaḥ mataḥ sarvam śivaḥ anugṛhṇāti na nigṛhṇāti kiṃcana nigṛhṇatām tu ye doṣāḥ śive teṣām asaṃbhavāt ye punar nigrahāḥ kecid brahma ādiṣu nidarśitāḥ te api loka hitāya eva kṛtāḥ śrīkaṇṭha mūrtinā brahmāṇḍasya ādhipatyam hi śrīkaṇṭhasya na saṃśayaḥ śrīkaṇṭha ākhyām śivaḥ mūrtim krīḍatīm adhitiṣṭhati sa doṣāḥ eva deva ādyāḥ nigṛhītāḥ yathā uditam tatas te pi vipāpmānaḥ prajāḥ ca api gata jvarāḥ nigrahaḥ sva rūpeṇa viduṣām na jugupsitaḥ atas eva hi daṇḍyeṣu daṇḍaḥ rājñām praśasyate na sa ced īśatām kuryāt jagataḥ katham īśvaraḥ īśa icchā ca vidhātṛ tvam vidheḥ ājñāpanam param ājñā vaśyam idam kuryāt na kuryāt iti śāsanam tad śāsana anuvarti tvam sādhu bhāvasya lakṣaṇam viparīta samādhoḥ syāt na sarvam tat tu dṛśyate sādhu saṃrakṣaṇīyam ced vinivartyam asādhu yat hita artha lakṣaṇam ca idam daṇḍa antam anuśāsanam hite sadā niṣaṇṇānām īśvarasya nidarśanam ayukta kāriṇaḥ loke garhaṇīyā aviveki tā na hi dveṣṭi pitā putram yaḥ nigṛhya ati śikṣayet mādhyasthena api nigrāhya anyaḥ nigṛhṇāti mārgataḥ tasmāt duḥkha ātmikām hiṃsām kurvāṇaḥ yaḥ sa nirghṛṇaḥ nidāna jñasya bhiṣajaḥ rugṇaḥ hiṃsām prayuṃjataḥ na kiṃcid api nairghṛṇyam ghṛṇā eva atra prayojikā ghṛṇā api na guṇāya eva hiṃsreṣu pratiyogiṣu tādṛśeṣu ghṛṇī bhrāntyā ghṛṇā antarita nirghṛṇaḥ upekṣā api iha doṣā āha rakṣyeṣu pratiyogiṣu doṣa ābhāsān samutprekṣya phalataḥ saḥ api nirghṛṇaḥ tasmāt ghṛṇā guṇāya eva sarvathā iti na saṃmatam mūrti ātmasu api rāga ādyāḥ doṣāḥ santi eva vastutas agnau api samāviṣṭam tāmram khalu sa kālikam iti na agniḥ asau duṣyet tāmra saṃsarga kāraṇāt na agneḥ aśuci saṃsargāt aśuci tvam apekṣate evam śodhya ātma saṃsargāt na hi aśuddhaḥ śivaḥ bhavet ayasi agnau samāviṣṭe dāhaḥ agneḥ eva na ayasaḥ mūrtta ātmani evam aiśvaryyam īśvarasya eva na ātmanām kāṣṭhasya aṃgāra tā nā agneḥ evam atra api yojyatām atas eva jagati asmin kāṣṭha pāṣāṇa mṛtsu api śiva āveśa vaśāt eva śiva tvam upacaryate maitrī ādayaḥ guṇāḥ gauṇāḥ tasmāt te bhinna vṛttayaḥ taiḥ guṇaiḥ uparaktānām doṣāya ca guṇāya ca yat tu gauṇam agauṇam ca tat sarvam anugṛhṇataḥ na guṇāya na doṣāya śivasya guṇa vṛttayaḥ na ca anugraha śabda artham gauṇam āhuḥ vipaścitaḥ saṃsāra mocanam kim tu śaivam ājñā mayam hitam hitam tat ājñā karaṇam yat hitam tat anugrahaḥ sarvam hite niyuñjāvaḥ sarva anugraha kārakaḥ tasya api hita rūpa tvāt śivaḥ sarva upakārakaḥ yathā vikāsayati eva raviḥ padmāni bhānubhiḥ svabhāvaḥ api hi bhāvānām bhāvinaḥ arthasya kāraṇam suvarṇam eva nā aṃgāram drāvayati agni saṃgamaḥ svabhāva vimalaḥ yadvat sarva anugrāhakaḥ śivaḥ svabhāva malināḥ tadvat ātmanaḥ jīva saṃjñitāḥ āgantuka tve kasya api bhāvyam kena api hetunā ātmatāyāḥ samatve api baddhāḥ muktāḥ pare yatas jñāna aiśvarya ādi vaiṣamyam bhajante sa uttara adharāḥ kecid mūrti ātma tām yānti kecid āsanna gocarāḥ mūrti ātmasu śivāḥ kecid adhvanām mūrddhasu sthitāḥ madhye maheśvarāḥ rudrāḥ tu arvācīna pade sthitāḥ āsanne ca māyāyāḥ parasmāt kāraṇāt trayam tatra api ātmā sthitaḥ adhastāt antarātmā ca madhyatas parastāt paramātmā iti brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ vartante vasavaḥ kecid parama ātma pada āśrayāḥ śānti atīta pade śaivāḥ śānte māheśvare tatas vidyāyāntu yathā raudrāḥ pratiṣṭhāyām tu vaiṣṇavāḥ nivṛttau ca tathā ātmānaḥ brahmā brahma aṃga yonayaḥ pakṣi ādayaḥ paṃcayonayaḥ tāḥ caturdaśa uttara adhara bhāvaḥ jñeyaḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ malaḥ yathā āma bhāvaḥ muktasya pūrvam paścāt tu pakva tā malaḥ api āmaḥ ca pakvaḥ ca bhavet saṃsāra kāraṇam āme tu adhara tā puṃsām pakve tu uttara tā kramāt paśu ātmānaḥ tridhā bhinnāḥ eka dvi tri malāḥ kramāt atra uttarāḥ eka malāḥ dvi malāḥ madhyamāḥ matāḥ tri malāḥ tu adhamāḥ jñeyāḥ yathottaram adhiṣṭhitāḥ aśiva ātmakam api etat śivena adhiṣṭhitam yathā aṇḍa antā hi mahā bhūmiḥ śata rudra ādi adhiṣṭhitā māyā antam antarikṣam tu hi amara īśa ādibhiḥ kramāt mahāmāyā avasānā dyauḥ vāyu ādyaiḥ bhuvana adhipaiḥ anāśrita antaiḥ adhva antarvarttibhiḥ samadhiṣṭhitāḥ te hi sākṣāt diviṣadaḥ tu antarikṣa sadaḥ tathā pṛthivī padaḥ iti evam devā deva vrataiḥ stutā nidāna bhūtaiḥ saṃsāra rogaḥ puṃsām pravartate bhiṣaj ājñāpakaḥ śambhuḥ śivaḥ parama kāraṇam aduḥkhena a api śaktaḥ asau paśūn mocayitum śivaḥ katham duḥkham karoti iti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā katham duḥkham aduḥkham syāt svabhāvaḥ hi aviparyayaḥ na hi rogī hi arogī syāt bhiṣaj bhaiṣajya kāraṇāt evam svabhāva malinān svabhāvāt duḥkhinaḥ paśūn sva ajña auṣadha vidhānena duḥkhāt mocayate śivaḥ na bhiṣaj kāraṇam roge śivaḥ saṃsāra kāraṇam duḥkhe svabhāva saṃsiddhe katham tad kāraṇam śivaḥ svābhāvikaḥ malaḥ puṃsām sa hi saṃsārayati amūn saṃsāra kāraṇam yat tu malam māyā ādi acetanam yathā maṇiḥ ayaskāntaḥ sānnidhyāt upakārakaḥ na nivartayitum śakyam sānnidhyam sat akāraṇam adhiṣṭhātā tatas nityam ajñātaḥ jagataḥ śivaḥ śaktiḥ rājñā ātmikā tasya niyantrī viśvatomukhī tayā tatam idam śaśvat tathā api sa na duṣyati an idam prathamam sarvam īśitavyam saḥ īśvaraḥ īśanāt ca tadīya ājñā tathā api sa na duṣyati etasmin antare vyomnaḥ śrutāḥ vāgarīriṇī tatas hṛṣṭatarāḥ sarvve vinaṣṭa aśeṣa saṃśayāḥ munayaḥ vismaya āviṣṭāḥ preṇemuḥ pavanam prabhum na ete pratiṣṭhita jñānāḥ iti matvā evam abravīt vāyuḥ uvācva parokṣam aparokṣam ca dvividham jñānam iṣyate hetu upadeśa gamyam yat tat parokṣam pracakṣate aparokṣam punar śreṣṭhāt anuṣṭhānāt bhaviṣyati na aparokṣāt ṛte mokṣaḥ iti kṛtvā viniścayam śreṣṭha anuṣṭhāna siddhi artham prayatadhvam atandritāḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe jñānopadeśaḥ nāma ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kim tat śreṣṭam anuṣṭhānam mokṣaḥ yena parokṣitaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca śaivaḥ hi paramaḥ dharmaḥ śreṣṭha anuṣṭhāna śabditaḥ yatra aparokṣaḥ lakṣyeta sākṣāt mokṣa pradaḥ śivaḥ sa tu paṃcavidhaḥ jñeyaḥ paṃcabhiḥ parvabhiḥ kramāt parokṣam aparokṣam ca jñānam yatra ca mokṣa dam dharma śabda abhidheya ṛthe pramāṇam śrutiḥ eva naḥ a paśu ātma adhikāra tvāt yaḥ dharamaḥ paramaḥ mataḥ sādhāraṇaḥ tatas anyaḥ tu sarveṣām adhikārataḥ dharma śāstra ādibhiḥ samyak sa aṃgaḥ eva upabṛṃhitaḥ śaivaḥ yaḥ paramaḥ dharmaḥ śreṣṭha anuṣṭhāna śabditaḥ itihāsa purāṇābhyām kathaṃcid upabṛṃhitaḥ śaiva āgamaiḥ tu saṃpannaḥ saha aṃgopām vistaraḥ tad saṃskāra adhikāraiḥ ca samyak eva upabṛṃhitaḥ śaiva āgamaḥ hi dvividhaḥ śrautaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ svatantraḥ daśadhā pūrvam tathā aṣṭādaśadhā punar kāmikā ādi samākhyābhiḥ siddhaḥ siddhānta saṃjñitaḥ param pāśupatam yatra vratam jñānam ca kathyate yuga āvarteṣu śiṣyeta yoga ācāryya svarūpiṇā saṃkṣipya asya pravaktāraḥ catvāraḥ parama ṛṣaya ruruḥ dadhīcaḥ agastyaḥ ca upamanyuḥ mahā yaśāḥ te ca pāśupatāḥ jñeyāḥ saṃhitānām pravartakāḥ tad santatīyāḥ guravaḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas teṣu pāśupataḥ yogaḥ śivam pratyakṣayet dṛḍham tasmāt śreṣṭham anuṣṭhānam yogaḥ pāśupataḥ mataḥ nāma aṣṭaka mayaḥ yogaḥ śivena parikalpitaḥ tena yogena sahasā śaivī prajñā prajāyate prasīdati śivaḥ tasya yasya jñānam pratiṣṭhitam prasādāt paramaḥ yogaḥ yaḥ śivam ca aparokṣayet śiva aparokṣāt saṃsāra kāraṇena viyujyate śivaḥ maheśvaraḥ ca eva rudraḥ viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ saṃsāra vaidyaḥ sarvajñaḥ paramātmā iti mukhyatas nāma aṣṭakam idam mukhyam śivasya pratipādakam ādi antu pañcakam jñeyam śānti atīta ādi anukramāt saṃjñā sadāśiva ādīnām paṃca upādhi parigrahāt padam eva hi tat nityam anityāḥ padinaḥ smṛtāḥ ātma antara abhidhānam syāt yat ādyam nāma pañcakam anyat tu tritayam nāmnām upādāna ādi yogataḥ anādi mala saṃśleṣaḥ prāgabhāvāt svabhāvataḥ athavā aśeṣa kalyāṇa guṇa eka dhanaḥ īśvaraḥ prakṛteḥ tu param prāhuḥ puruṣam pañcaviṃśakam yam veda ādau svaram prāhuḥ vācya vācaka bhāvataḥ veda eka vedya yāthātmyāt vedānte ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ tad adhīna pravṛtti tvāt prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca māyām tu prakṛtim vidyāt māyinam tu maheśvaram rud duḥkham duḥkha hetuḥ vā tat rāvayati naḥ prabhuḥ tattva ādi bhūta paryantam śarīra ādiṣu atandritaḥ vyāpya adhitiṣṭhati śivaḥ tatas rudraḥ itas tatas jagataḥ pitṛ bhūtānām śivaḥ mūrti ātmanām api pitṛ bhāvena sarveṣām pitāmahaḥ udīritaḥ saṃsārasya īśvaraḥ nityam sa mūlasya nivartakaḥ tri kāla bhāvinaḥ bhāvān sthūlān sūkṣmān aśeṣatas aṇavaḥ nā eva jānanti māyayā eva mala āvṛtāḥ svasmāt parātma virahāt paramātmā śivaḥ svayam nāma aṣṭakam idam ca eva labdhvā ācārya prasādataḥ nivṛttya ādi kalā granthim śiva ādyaiḥ paṃca nāmabhiḥ yathāsvam kramaśas chitvā śodhayitvā yathāguṇam chittvā paryaṣṭaka ākāram sva ātmānam ca suṣumṇayā saṃhṛtyam vadanam paścāt yathā saṃskaraṇam layāt śāktena amṛta varṣeṇa saṃsiktāyām tanau punar avatārya svam ātmānam amṛta ātma ākṛtim hṛdi dvādaśāntar sthitasya indoḥ parastāt śveta paṃkaje samāsīnam mahādevam śaṃkaram bhakta vatsalam arddhanārīśvaram devam nirmalam madhura ākṛtim śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśam prasannam śītala dyutim śiva nāma aṣṭakena eva bhāva puṣpaiḥ samarcayet abhyarccana ante tu punar prāṇān āyamya mānavaḥ samyak cittam samādhāya śārvam nāma aṣṭakam japet nābhau ca aṣṭa āhutīḥ hutvā pūrṇāhutyā namaḥ tatas evam kṛtvā cirāt eva jñānam pāśupatam śubham labhate tad pratiṣṭhām ca vṛttam ca anuttamam tathā yogam ca paramam labdhvā mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe śreṣṭhānuṣṭhānavarṇanam nāma dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ brahma ādayaḥ api yat kṛtvā sarve pāśupatāḥ smṛtāḥ vāyuḥ uvāca vratam pāśupatam śrautam atharvaśirasi śrutam kālaḥ caitrī paurṇamāsī deśaḥ śiva parigrahaḥ kṣetra ārāma ādi araṇyam vā praśastaḥ śubha lakṣaṇaḥ tatra pūrvam trayodaśyām su snātaḥ su kṛta āhnikaḥ anujñāpya svam ācāryam saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca pūjām vaiśeṣikīm kṛtvā śukla aṃbara dharaḥ svayam śukla yajña upavītī ca śukla mālya anulepanaḥ darbha āsane samāsīnaḥ darbha muṣṭim pragṛhya ca prāṇāyāma trayam kṛtvā prāc mukhaḥ vā api uda mukhaḥ dhyātvā devam ca devīm ca tad vijñāpana vartmanā yāvat śarīrapātam vā dvādaśa abdam atha api vā tad ardham vā tad ardham vā māsa dvādaśakam tu vā tad ardham vā tad ardham vā māsam ekam atha api vā dina dvādaśakam vā atha dina ṣaṭkam atha api vā agnim ādhāya vidhivat virajā homa kāraṇāt pūrṇām āpūrya tām bhūyas tattvānām śuddhim uddiśan pañcabhūtāni tanmātrāḥ pañca karma indriyāṇi ca jñāna karma vibhedena pañcakarma vibhāgaśaḥ tvak ādi dhātavaḥ sapta pañca prāṇa ādi vāyavaḥ manaḥ buddhiḥ aham khyātiḥ guṇāḥ prakṛti pūruṣau māyā ca śuddhi vidyā ca maheśvara sadāśivau śaktiḥ ca śivatattvam ca tattvāni kramaśas viduḥ śiva anugraham āsādya jñānavān sa hi jāyate atha gomayam ādāya piṇḍīkṛtya abhimantrya ca prabhāte tu caturdaśyām kṛtvā sarvam purā uditam dine tasmin nirāhāraḥ kālam śeṣam samāpayet prātar parvaṇi ca api evam kṛtvā homāḥ vasānataḥ upasaṃhṛtya rudra agnim gṛhṇīyāt bhasma yatnatas tatas ca jaṭilaḥ muṇḍī śikhā eka jaṭaḥ eva vā bhūtvā snātvā tatas vīta lajjaḥ ced syāt digambaraḥ api kāṣāya vasanaḥ carma cīra ambaraḥ atha vā eka ambaraḥ valkalī vā bhavet daṇḍī ca mekhalī prakṣālya caraṇau paścāt dvis ācamya ātmanaḥ tanum agniḥ ityādibhiḥ mantraiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ātharvaṇaiḥ kramāt vibhṛjya aṃgāni mūrddha ādi caraṇa antāni taiḥ spṛśet sarva aṃga uddhūlanam kuryāt praṇavena śivena vā śiva bhāvam samāgamya śiva yogam atha ācaret tad paśu tvam parityajya kṛtvā pāśupatam vratam pūjanīyaḥ mahādevaḥ liṃga mūrtiḥ sanātanaḥ padmam tasya api abhāve tu kevalam bhāvanā mayam tad padma karṇikā madhye kṛtvā liṃgam kanīyasam sphīṭikam pīṭhikā upetam pūjayet vidhivat kramāt pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānena tad liṃgam kṛta śodhanam parikalpya āsanam mūrtim paṃcavaktra prakārataḥ paṃcagavya ādibhiḥ pūrṇaiḥ yathā vibhava saṃbhṛtaiḥ snāpayet kalaśaiḥ pūrṇaiḥ aṣṭāpada samudbhavaiḥ sa vedikam samālipya liṃgam bhūṣaṇa bhūṣitam puṇyaiḥ praśastaiḥ patraiḥ ca citraiḥ dūrvā akṣata ādibhiḥ samabhyarcya yathālābham mahā pūjā vidhānataḥ dhūpam dīpam tathā ca api naivedyam ca samādiśet iṣṭāni ca viśiṣṭāni nyāyena upārjitāni ca sarva dravyāṇi deyāni vrate tasmin viśeṣataḥ śrīpatra utpala padmānām saṃkhyā sāhasrikī matā pratyekam aparā saṃkhyā śatam aṣṭa uttaram dvijāḥ aṣṭāGgam arghyam utkṛṣṭam dhūpa ālepau viśeṣataḥ candanam vāmadeva ākhye haritālam ca pauruṣe īśāne bhasitam kecid ālepanam iti īdṛśām sita agurum aghora ākhye mukhe kṛṣṇa agurum punar īśāne api hi uśīra ādi deyāt dhūpam viśeṣataḥ śarkarā madhu karpūra kapilā ghṛta saṃyutam candana aguru kāṣṭha ādyam sāmānyam saṃpracakṣate karpūra varti rājya āḍhyā deyā dīpa āvaliḥ tatas brahmāṃgāni tatas ca eva prathama āvaraṇa īrcite dvitīya āvaraṇe pūjyāḥ vighna īśāḥ cakravartinaḥ tṛtīya āvaraṇe pūjyāḥ bhava ādyāḥ aṣṭa mūrtayaḥ mahādeva ādayaḥ tatra tathā ekādaśa mūrtayaḥ caturtha āvaraṇe pūjyāḥ sarve eva gaṇeśvarāḥ daśa dikpatayaḥ pūjyāḥ sa astrāḥ sa anucarāḥ tathā brahmaṇaḥ mānasāḥ putrāḥ sarve api jyotiṣām gaṇāḥ sarvāḥ devyaḥ ca devāḥ ca sarve sarve ca khecarāḥ pātāla vāsinaḥ ca anye sarve muni gaṇāḥ api kṣetrapālāḥ ca sa gaṇāḥ sarvam ca etat carācaram pūjanīyam śiva prītyā mat tvā śaṃbhu vibhūtimat atha āvaraṇa pūjā ante saṃpūjya parameśvaram sa ājyam savyam janam hṛdyam haviḥ bhaktyā nivedayet mukha vāsa ādikam dattvā tāmbūlam sa upadaṃśakam alaṃkṛtya ca bhūyas api nānā puṣpa vibhūṣaṇaiḥ nīrājana ante vistīrya pūjā śeṣam samāpayet caṣakam sa upakāram ca śayanam ca samarpayet candra saṃkāśa hāram ca śayanīyam samarpayet ādyam nṛpa ucitam hṛdyam tat sarvam anurūpataḥ kṛtvā ca kārayitvā ca hitvā ca pratipūjanam stotram vyapohanam japtvā vidyām paṃcākṣarīm japet pradakṣiṇām praṇāmam ca kṛtvā ātmānam samarpayet dattvā arghyam aṣṭau puṣpāṇi devam udvāsya liṃgataḥ saṃpūjya ca gurūn viprān vratinaḥ ca viśeṣataḥ bhaktān dvijān ca śaktaḥ ced dīna anāthān ca toṣayet svayam ca anaśane śaktaḥ phala mūla aśane atha vā payaḥ vrataḥ vā bhikṣā āśī bhavet eka aśanaḥ tathā naktam yukta aśanaḥ nityam bhū śayyā nirataḥ śuciḥ bhasma śāyī tṛṇeśāyī cīra ajina dhṛtaḥ athavā arkavāre tathā ārdrāyām paṃcadaśyām ca pakṣayoḥ aṣṭamyām ca caturdaśyām śaktaḥ tu upavaset api pākhaṇḍi patita udakyāḥ sūtakāntya ja pūrvakān kṣama dāna dayā satya ahiṃsā śīlaḥ sadā bhavet santuṣṭaḥ ca praśāntaḥ ca japa dhyāna rataḥ tathā kuryāt triṣavaṇa snānam bhasma snānam atha api vā pūjām vaiśeṣikīm ca eva manasā vacasā girā pramādāt tu tathā ācāre nirūpya gurulāghave ucitām niṣkṛtim kuryāt pūjā homa japa ādibhiḥ godānam ca vṛṣotsargam kuryāt pūjām ca saṃpadā sāmānyam etat kathitam vratasya asya samāsatas pratimāsam viśeṣam ca pravadāmi yathāśrutam vaiśākhe vajraliṃgam tu jyeṣṭhe mārakatam śubham āṣāḍhe mauktikam vidyāt śrāvaṇe nīla nirmitam āśvine māsi vidyāt vai liṃgam gomedakam varam kārtikyām vaidrumam liṃgam vaidūryam mārgaśīrṣake puṣparāga mayam pauṣe māghe dyumaṇi jan tathā sarva māseṣu ratnānām alābhe haimam eva vā haima abhāve rājatam vā tāmra jam śailajam tathā mṛd mayam vā yathālābham jātuṣam ca anyat eva vā kṛtvā vaiśeṣikīm pūjām hutvā ca eva yathā purā saṃpūjya ca tathā ācāryam vratinaḥ ca viśeṣataḥ deśikena api anujñātaḥ prāc mukhaḥ vā api uda mukhaḥ darbha āsanaḥ darbha pāṇiḥ prāṇa apānau niyamya ca japitvā śaktitaḥ mūlam dhyātvā sa ambam triyambakam anujñāpya yathāpūrvam namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ tatas daṇḍa jaṭā cīra mekhalāḥ api ca utsṛjet yaḥ kṛtvā ātyantikīm dīkṣām ā dehāntam an ākulaḥ saḥ atyāśramī ca vijñeyaḥ mahāpāśupataḥ tathā saḥ eva tapatām śreṣṭha saḥ eva ca mahāvratī na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścid kṛtakṛtyaḥ mumukṣuṣu yaḥ anvaham dvādaśa aham vā vratam etat samācaret ghṛta aktaḥ yaḥ caret etat vratam vrata parāyaṇaḥ śiva arpita ātmā satatam na tena sadṛśaḥ kvacid pāpaiḥ su dāruṇaiḥ sadyas mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu vīryavān bhasma saṃyutaḥ bhasma niṣṭhasya naśyanti bhasma agni saṃgamāt bhasma snāna viśuddha ātmā bhasma niṣṭhaḥ iti smṛtaḥ bhasmanā digdha sarva aṃgaḥ bhasma dīpta tripuṃḍrakaḥ bhasma snāyī ca puruṣaḥ bhasma niṣṭhaḥ iti smṛtaḥ bhūta preta piśāsāḥ ca rogāḥ ca atīva dussahāḥ bhasma niṣṭhasya sānnidhyāt vidravanti na saṃśayaḥ bhāsanāt bhāsitam proktam bhasma kalmaṣa bhakṣaṇāt bhūti bhūti karī ca eva rakṣā rakṣā karī param parama astram ca śaivānām bhasma etat pārameśvaram iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe paśupativratavidhānavarṇanam nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ dhaumya agrajena śuśunā kṣīra artham hi tapaḥ kṛtam tasmāt kṣīrārṇavaḥ dattaḥ tasmai devena śūlinā sa katham śiśukaḥ lebhe śiva śāstra pravaktṛ tām katham vā śiva sadbhāvam jñātvā tapasi niṣṭhitaḥ katham ca labdha vijñānaḥ tapaḥ caraṇa parvaṇi vāyuḥ uvāca na hi eṣa śiśukaḥ kaścid prākṛtaḥ kṛtavān tapaḥ janma antareṇa saṃsiddhaḥ kena api khalu hetunā sva pada pracyutaḥ diṣṭyā prāptaḥ muni kumāra tām mahādeva prasādasya bhāgya āpannasya bhāvinaḥ dugdha abhilāṣa prabhava dvāra tām agamat tapaḥ atas sarva gaṇa īśa tvam kumāra tvam ca śāśvatam tasya jñāna āgama upyasya prasādāt eva śāṃkarāt kaumāram hi param sākṣāt jñānam śakti mayam viduḥ dṛṣṭam tu kāraṇam tasya śiva jñāna samanvaye sva mātṛ vacanam sākṣāt śoka jam kṣīra kāraṇāt kadācid kṣīram ati alpam pītavān mātula āśrame īrṣayaya mātula sutam santṛpta kṣīram uttamam pītvā sthitam yathākāmam dṛṣṭvā vai mātula ātmajam upamanyuḥ vyāghrapādiḥ prītyā provāca mātaram gavyam kṣīram ati svādu na alpam uṣṇam pibāmi aham vāyuḥ uvāca vyāghrapādasya mahiṣī duḥkham āpat tadā ca sā upalālya atha su prītyā putram āliṃgya sa ādaram duḥkhitā vilalāpa atha smṛtvā nairdhanyam ātmanaḥ smṛtvā a smṛtvā punar kṣīram upamanyuḥ sa bālakaḥ dehi dehi iti tām āha rudran bhūyas mahā dyutiḥ tat haṭham sā parijñāya dvija patnī tapasvinī śāntaye tad haṭhasya atha śubha upāyam arīracat uñcha vṛttyā arjitān bījān svayam dṛṣṭvā ca sā tadā bīja piṣṭam atha āloḍya toyena kala bhāṣiṇī āliṃgya ādāya duḥkha ārtā pradadau kṛtrimam payaḥ pītvā ca kṛtrimam kṣīram mātrām dattam sa bālakaḥ na etat kṣīram iti prāha mātaram ca ati vihvalaḥ duḥkhitā sā tadā prāha saṃprekṣya āghrāya mūrddhani taṭinīḥ ratna pūrṇāḥ tāḥ svarga pātāla gocarāḥ bhāgya hīnāḥ na paśyanti bhakti hīnāḥ ca ye śive rājyam svargam ca mokṣam ca bhojanam kṣīra saṃbhavam na labhante priyāṇi eṣām na tuṣyati yadā śivaḥ kṣīram tatra kutas asmākam vane nivasatām sadā kṛtsna abhāvena dāridryāt mayā te bhāgya hīnayā mithyādugdham idam dattam piṣṭam āloḍya vāriṇā tvam mātula gṛhe su alpam pītvā svādu payaḥ śṛtam jñātvā svādu tvayā pītam tad jātīyam anusmaran dattam na payaḥ iti uktvā rudan duḥkhīkaroṣi mām sa kāmānām yathā kāmam yathā ukta phala dāyakaḥ dhanāni uddiśya na asmābhiḥ itas prāk arcitaḥ śivaḥ atas daridrāḥ saṃjātāḥ vayam tasmāt na te payaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca iti mātṛ vacaḥ śrutvā tathyam śoka ādi sūcakam śokena alam itaḥ mataḥ sa aṃbaḥ yadi asti śaṃkaraḥ tyaja śokam mahābhāge sarvam bhadram bhaviṣyati cirāt vā hi acirāt vā api kṣīrodam sādhayāmi aham vāyuḥ uvāca praytuvāca tadā mātā su prasannā manasvinī mātā uvāca śubham vicāritam tāta tvayā mad prīti varddhanam vilaṃbam mā kathāḥ tvam hi bhaja sa aṃbam sadāśivam tat kṛtam hi jagat sarvam brahma ādyāḥ tasya kiṃkarāḥ tad prasāda kṛta aiśvaryāḥ dāsāḥ tasya vayam prabhoḥ tam vinā anyam na jānīmaḥ śaṃkaram loka śaṃkaram anyān devān parityajya karmaṇā manasā girā tam eva sa aṃbam sa gaṇam bhaja bhāva purassaram sākṣāt namaḥ śivāya iti mantraḥ ayam vācakaḥ smṛtaḥ sapta koṭi mahā mantrāḥ sarve sa praṇavāḥ pare sa prasādāḥ ca te mantrāḥ sva adhikāra ādi apekṣayā sarva adhikāraḥ tu ekaḥ ayam mantraḥ eva īśvara ājñayā yathā nikṛṣṭān utkṛṣṭān sarvān api ātmanaḥ śivaḥ sarva rakṣā kṣamaḥ api eṣa na aparaḥ kaścid iṣyate tasmāt mantra antarān tyaktvā paṃcākṣara paraḥ bhava adhorāstram ca śaivānām rakṣā hetuḥ anuttamam mantram ca te mayā dattam gṛhāṇa mad anujñayā vāyuḥ uvāca evam mātrā samādiśya śivam astu iti udīrya ca tam āha ca tadā mātā śubham kurvantu te surāḥ himavat parvatam prāpya vāyubhakṣaḥ samāhitaḥ aṣṭa iṣṭakābhiḥ prasādam kṛtvā liṃgam ca mṛd mayam tatra āvāhya mahādevam sa aṃbam sa gaṇam avyayam bhaktyā pañcākṣareṇa eva putraiḥ puṣpaiḥ vana udbhavaiḥ samabhyarcya ciram kālam cacāra paramam tapaḥ tatas tapaḥ carat tam tam bālam ekākinam kṛśam purā marīcinā śaptāḥ kecid muni piśācakāḥ saṃpīḍya rākṣasaiḥ bhāvaiḥ tapasaḥ vighnam ācaran sadā namaḥ śivāya iti krośati smārta nāda vat tad nāda śravaṇāt eva tapasaḥ vighna kāriṇaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe upamanyutapovarṇanam nāma catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vāyuḥ uvāca atha sarve pradīpta aṃgāḥ vaikuṇṭham prayayuḥ drutam praṇamya āhuḥ ca tat sarvam haraye deva sattamāḥ śrutvā teṣām tadā vākyam bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ kim idantu iti saṃcintya jñātvā tad kāraṇam ca saḥ jagāma mandaram tūrṇam maheśvara didṛkṣayā dṛṣṭvā devam praṇamya evam provāca su kṛta aṃjaliḥ viṣṇuḥ uvāca kṣīra artham adahat sarvam tapasā tat nivāraya vāyuḥ uvāca iti śrutvā vacaḥ viṣṇoḥ prāha devaḥ maheśvaraḥ śiśum nivārayiṣyāmi tat tvam gaccha svam āśramam tat śrutvā śaṃbhu vacanam sa viṣṇuḥ deva vallabhaḥ jagāma āśvāsya tān sarvān sva lokam amara ādikān śakrasya rūpam āsthāya gantum cakre matim tatas sa vāraṇaḥ cāru tadā vibhum tam nivījya vāla vyajanena divyam dadhāra śacyā sahitam sura indram kareṇa vāmena śita ātapatram rarāja bhagavān somaḥ śakra rūpī sadāśivaḥ āsthāya evam hi śakrasya sva rūpam parameśvaraḥ tam dṛṣṭvā parameśānam śakra rūpa dharam śivam praṇamya śirasā prāha mahā muni varaḥ svayam pāvitaḥ ca āśramaḥ saḥ ayam mama deveśvara svayam vāyuḥ uvāca evam uktvā sthitam prekṣya kṛta aṃjali puṭam dvijam prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā śakra rūpa dharaḥ haraḥ śakraḥ uvāca vāyuḥ uvāca vārayāmi śive bhaktim iti uvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ tat niśamya hariḥ prāha mām na jānāsi lekhapam rudreṇa nirguṇena api kim te kāryam bhaviṣyati deva paGkti bahis bhūtaḥ yaḥ piśāca tvam āgataḥ vāyuḥ uvāca prasaṃgāt eva devasya nirguṇa tvam mahātmanaḥ brahma viṣṇu maheśānām janaka prakṛteḥ param upāsate yam tattva jñāḥ varam tasmāt vṛṇomi aham na asti śaṃbhoḥ param tattvam sarva kāraṇa kāraṇāt brahma viṣṇu ādi devānām sraṣṭuḥ guṇa parāt vibhoḥ bhava antare kṛtam pāpam śrutā nindā bhavasya ced śrutvā nindām bhavasya atha tad kṣaṇāt eva santyajet āstām tāvat mama iccheyam kṣīram prati sura adhama nihatya tvām śiva astreṇa tyajāmi etam kalevaram vāyuḥ uvāca kṣīre vāñchām api tyaktvā nihantum śakram udyataḥ smṛtvā śaṃbhu pada dvandvam sva deham dugdhum udyataḥ āgneyīm dhāraṇām bibhrat upamanyuḥ avasthitaḥ vārayāmāsa saumyena dhāraṇām tasya yoginaḥ tat visṛṣṭam aghora astram nandīśvara niyogataḥ jagṛhe madhyatas kṣiptam nandī śaṃkara vallabhaḥ svam rūpam eva bhagavān āsthāya parameśvaraḥ darśayāmāsa śiprāya bāla indu kṛta śekharam kṣīrārṇava sahasram ca pīyūṣa arṇavam eva vā dadhi ādeḥ arṇavān ca eva ghṛta uda arṇavam eva ca phala arṇavam ca bālasya bhakṣya bhojya arṇavam tathā apūpānām girim ca eva darśayāmāsa sa prabhuḥ evam sa dadṛśe devaḥ devyā sārddham vṛṣā upari gaṇeśvaraiḥ triśūla ādyaiḥ divya astraiḥ api saṃvṛtaḥ divi dundubhayaḥ neduḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca papāta daṇḍa vat bhūmau bhakti namreṇa cetasā ehi ehi iti tam āhūya mūrdhni āghrāya dadau varān śivaḥ uvāca bhakṣya bhojyāni athākāmam bāndhavaiḥ bhukṣva sarvadā upamanyo mahābhāga tava ambā eṣā hi pārvatī mayā putrīkṛtaḥ hi adya dattaḥ kṣīra udaka arṇavaḥ madhunaḥ ca arṇavaḥ ca eva dadhi anna arṇavaḥ eva ca ājya odana arṇavaḥ ca eva phala ādi arṇavaḥ eva ca ete dattāḥ mayā te hi tvam gṛhṇīṣva mahā mune amara tvam mayā dattam gāṇapatyam ca śāśvatam varān varaya su prītyā mano abhilaṣitān parān prasannaḥ aham pradāsyāmi na atra kāryā vicāraṇā vāyuḥ uvāca evam uktvā mahādevaḥ karābhyām upagṛhyatam kṣīrābdhiḥ api sa ākāraḥ kṣīram svādu kare dadhat upasthāya dadau piṇḍībhūtam kṣīram anaśvaram yoga aiśvaryam sadā tuṣṭim brahma vidyām anaśvarām samṛddhim paramān tasmai dadau santuṣṭa mānasaḥ atha śaṃbhuḥ prasanna ātmā dṛṣṭvā tasya tapaḥ mahaḥ vratam pāśupatam jñānam vrata yogam ca tattvataḥ tasmāt śivāt ca tasyāḥ ca śivāyāḥ muditaḥ tatas prasanna cetaskaḥ su praṇamya kṛtāṃjaliḥ sva dāsyam paramam sneham sānnidhyam ca eva sarvadā evam uktvā prasanna ātma aharṣa gadgadayā girā prasīda karuṇā sindho sa amba śaṃkara sarvadā vāyuḥ uvāca evam uktaḥ mahādevaḥ sarveṣām ca vara pradaḥ śivaḥ uvāca dṛḍha bhaktaḥ asi viprarṣe mayā vijñāsitaḥ hi asi yaśasvī tejasā yuktaḥ divya jñāna samanvitaḥ akṣayāḥ bāndhavāḥ ca eva kulam gotram ca te sadā bhaviṣyati dvijaśreṣṭha mayi bhaktiḥ ca śāśvatī sānnidhyam ca āśrame nityam kariṣyāmi dvijottama upa kaṃṭham mama tvam vai sa ānandam vihariṣyasi īśānaḥ sa varān dattvā tatra eva antardadhe haraḥ upamanyuḥ prasanna ātmā prāpya tasmāt varāt varān jagāma jananī sthānam sukham prāpa adhikam ca saḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe vaiyāsikyām caturviṃśati sāhasryām saṃhitāyām tad antargatāyām saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe upamanyucaritavarṇanam nāma pañcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ u ayam saptamyāḥ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāḥ pūrva khaṇḍaḥ śrīḥ śrī gaṇeśāya namaḥ śrī gaurī śaṃkarābhyām namaḥ atha saptamyām vāyavīya saṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍaḥ prārabhyate gaurī kuca taṭa dvandva kuṃkuma aṃkita vakṣase sūtaḥ uvāca ṛṣayaḥ ca api te sarve naimiṣa araṇya vāsinaḥ atha ayam arthaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ iti kṛtvā viniścayam kṛtvā yathā svakam kṛtyam pratyaham te yathā purā bhagavantam upāyāntam samīkṣya samupāviśan sukha āsana upaviṣṭaḥ ca vāyuḥ loka namaskṛtaḥ śrīmat vibhūtim īśasya hṛdi kṛtvā idam abravīt iti ākarṇya śubhām vāṇīm ṛṣayaḥ kṣīṇa kalmaṣāḥ vibhūti vistaram śrotum ūcuḥ te paramam vacaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kṣīra arthena api tapasā yat prāptam parameśvarāt dṛṣṭaḥ asau vāsudevena kṛṣṇena akliṣṭa karmaṇā prāptam ca paramam jñānam iti prāk eva śuśruma katham sa labdhavān kṛṣṇaḥ jñānam pāśupatam param vāyuḥ uvāca sva icchayā hi avatīrṇaḥ upi vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ nindayan iva mānuṣyam deha śuddhim cakāra saḥ āśramam munibhiḥ dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭavān tatra vai munim bhasma avadāta sarva aṃgam tripuṃḍra aṃkita mastakam rudra akṣa mālā ābharaṇam jaṭā maṃḍala maṃḍitam tad śiṣya bhūtaiḥ munibhiḥ śāstraiḥ vedam iva āvṛtam śiva dhyāna ratam śāntam upamanyum mahā dyutim namaścakāra tam dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭa sarva tanūruhaḥ bahu mānena kṛṣṇaḥ asau tris kṛtvā tu pradakṣiṇām stutim cakāra su prītyā nata skandhaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ tasya avalokanāt eva muneḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ naṣṭam āsīt malam sarvam māyā jam kārmam eva ca tapaḥ kṣīṇam alam kṛṣṇam upamanyuḥ yathā vidhiḥ atha pāśupatam sākṣāt vratam dvādaśa māsikam tadā prabhṛti tam kṛṣṇam munayaḥ śaṃsita vratāḥ divyāḥ pāśupatāḥ sarve parivṛtya upatasthire tatas guru niyogāt vai kṛṣṇaḥ parama śaktimān tapaḥ cakāra putra artham sa aṃbam uddiśya śaṃkaram tena varṣa ante dṛṣṭaḥ asau parameśvaraḥ śriyā paramayā yuktaḥ sa aṃbaḥ ca sa gaṇaḥ śivaḥ vara artham āvirbhūtasya harasya subhaga ākṛteḥ stutim cakāra natvā asau kṛṣṇaḥ samyak kṛtāṃjaliḥ sa aṃbam sama gaṇa vyagraḥ labdhavān putram ātmanaḥ tapasā tuṣṭa cittena dattam viṣṇoḥ śivena vai yasmāt sa aṃbaḥ mahādevaḥ pradadau putram ātmanaḥ tasmāt jāṃbavatī sūnum sāṃbam cakre sa nāmataḥ tat etat kathitam sarvam kṛṣṇasya amita karmaṇaḥ mahā ṛṣeḥ jñāna lābhaḥ ca putra lābhaḥ ca śaṃkarāt yaḥ idam kīrtayet nityam śṛṇuyāt śrāvayet tathā sa viṣṇoḥ jñānam āsādya tena eva saha modate iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe kṛṣṇaputraprāptivarṇanam prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kim tat pāśupatam jñānam katham paśupatiḥ śivaḥ katham dhaumya agrajaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇena akliṣṭa karmaṇā etat sarvam samācakṣva vāyo śaṃkara vigraha sūtaḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ teṣām mahā ṛṣīṇām prabhaṃjanaḥ saṃsmṛtya śivam īśānam pravaktum upacakrame vāyuḥ uvāca purā sākṣāt maheśena śrīkaṃṭha ākhyena mandare devyai devena kathitam jñānam pāśupatam param tat eva pṛṣṭam kṛṣṇena viṣṇunā viśvayoninā paśu tvam ca sura ādīnām pati tvam ca śivasya ca yathā upadiṣṭam kṛṣṇāya muninā hi upamanyunā tathā samāsatas vakṣye tat śṛṇudhvam atandritāḥ purā upamanyum āsīnam viṣṇuḥ kṛṣṇa vapuḥ dharaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca divyam pāśupatam jñānam vibhūtim vā asya kṛtsnaśas katham paśupatiḥ devaḥ paśavaḥ ke prakīrtitāḥ iti saṃcoditaḥ śrīmān upamanyuḥ mahātmanā praṇamya devam devīm ca prāha puṣṭaḥ yathā tathā brahma ādyāḥ sthāvara antāḥ ca devadevasya śūlinaḥ paśavaḥ parikīrtyante saṃsāra vaśa vartinaḥ teṣām pati tvāt deveśaḥ śivaḥ paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ mala māyā ādibhiḥ pāśaiḥ sa badhnāti paśūn patiḥ saḥ eva mocakaḥ teṣām bhaktyā samyak upāsitaḥ caturviṃśati tattvāni māyā karma guṇāḥ amī viṣayāḥ iti kathyante pāśāḥ jīva nibandhanāḥ brahma ādi stamba paryantān paśūn baddhvā maheśvaraḥ pāśaiḥ etaiḥ patiḥ devaḥ kāryam kārayati svakam tasya ājñayā maheśasya prakṛtiḥ puruṣa ucitām buddhim prasūte sā buddhiḥ ahaṃkāram ahaṃkṛtiḥ indriyāṇi daśa ekam ca tanmātra pañcakam tathā śāsanāt devadevasya śivasya śiva dāyinaḥ tanmātrāṇi api tasya eva śāsanena mahīyasā mahābhūtāni aśeṣāṇi bhāvayanti anupūrvaśas brahma ādīnām tṛṇa antānām dehinām deha saṃgatim mahābhūtāni aśeṣāṇi janayanti śiva ājñayā śrotra ādīni ca gṛhṇanti śabda ādīn viṣayān pṛthak svān eva na anyān devasya divyena ājñā balena vai vāc ādīni api yāni āsan tāni karmendriyāṇi ca yathā svam karma kurvanti na anyat kiṃcid śiva ājñayā avilaṃghyā hi sarveṣām ājñā śaṃbhoḥ garīyasī avakāśam aśeṣāṇām bhūtānām saṃprayacchati ākāśaḥ parameśasya śāsanāt eva sarva gaḥ havyam vahati devānām kavyam kavya āśinām api pāka ādyam ca karoti agniḥ parameśvara śāsanāt saṃjīvana ādyam sarvasya kurvati āpaḥ tad ājñayā viśvambharāḥ jagat nityam dhatte viśveśvara ājñayā ādhipatyam apām nityam kurute varuṇaḥ sadā pāśaiḥ badhnāti ca yathā daṃḍyān tasya eva śāsanāt dadāti nityam yakṣa indraḥ draviṇam draviṇa īśvaraḥ puṇya anurūpam bhūtebhyaḥ puruṣasya anuśāsanāt karoti saṃpadaḥ śaśvat jñānam ca api sumedhasām nigraham ca api asādhūnām īśānaḥ śiva śāsanāt dhatte tu dharaṇīm mūrdhnā śeṣaḥ śiva niyogataḥ yām āhuḥ tāmasīm raudrīm hareḥ sṛjati aśeṣam īśasya śāsanāt caturānanaḥ anyābhiḥ mūrtibhiḥ svābhiḥ pāti ca ante nihanti ca viṣṇuḥ pālayate viśvam kāla kālasya śāsanāt kālaḥ karoti sakalam kālaḥ saṃharati prajāḥ kālaḥ pālayate viśvam kāla kālasya śāsanāt tribhiḥ aṃśaiḥ jagat bibhrat tejobhiḥ vṛṣṭim ādiśan puṣṇāti oṣadhi jātāni bhūtāni āhlādayati api devaiḥ ca pīyate candraḥ candrabhūṣaṇa śāsanāt khecarāḥ ṛṣayaḥ siddhāḥ bhoginaḥ manujāḥ mṛgāḥ paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ ca eva kīṭa ādyāḥ sthāvarāṇi ca nadyaḥ samudrāḥ girayaḥ kānanāni sarāṃsi ca vedāḥ sa aṃgāḥ ca śāstrāṇi mantra stoma makha ādayaḥ kālāgni ādi śiva antāni bhuvanāni saha adhipaiḥ brahmāṃḍāni api asaṃkhyāni teṣām āvaraṇāni ca vartamānāni atītāni bhaviṣyanti api kṛtsnaśas diśaḥ ca vidiśaḥ ca eva kāla bhedāḥ kalā ādayaḥ tat sarvam śaṃkarasya ājñā balena samadhiṣṭhitam ājñā balāt tasya dharā sthitā iha dharādharāḥ vāridharāḥ samudrāḥ jyotiḥ gaṇāḥ śakra mukhāḥ ca devāḥ sthiram ciram vā cit acit yat asti ati āścaryam idam kṛṣṇa śaṃbhoḥ amita karmaṇaḥ ājñā kṛtam śṛṇuṣva etat śrutam śruti mukhe mayā tadā maheśvaraḥ teṣām madhyatas vara veṣa dhṛk sva lakṣaṇaiḥ vihīna aṃgaḥ svayam yakṣaḥ iva abhavat sa tān āha surān ekam tṛṇam ādāya bhū tale yakṣasya vacanam śrutvā vajrapāṇiḥ śacīpatiḥ kiṃcid kruddhaḥ vihasya enam tṛṇam ādātum udyataḥ na tat tṛṇam upadātum manasā api ca śakyate tat vajram nija vajreṇa saṃsṛṣṭam iva sarvatas tṛṇena abhihatam tena tiryak agram papāta ha tatas ca anye su saṃrabdhāḥ lokapālāḥ mahā balāḥ sasṛjuḥ tṛṇam uddiśya sva āyudhāni sahasraśas evam devaiḥ samārabdham tṛṇam uddiśya yatnataḥ vyartham āsīt aho kṛṣṇa yakṣasya ātma balena vai tat āha yakṣam deva indraḥ kaḥ bhavān iti amarṣitaḥ tad antare haimavatī devī divya vibhūṣaṇā āvirāsīt nabhoḥ aṃge śobhamānā śuci smitā tām dṛṣṭvā vismaya āviṣṭāḥ devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ praṇamya yakṣam papracchuḥ kaḥ asau yakṣaḥ vilakṣaṇaḥ sā abravīt sa smitam devī sa yuṣmākam agocaraḥ tena idam bhramyate cakram saṃsāra ākhyam carācaram devāḥ ca vismitāḥ sarve tām praṇamya divam yayuḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṃḍe dvitīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu kṛṣṇa maheśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ sa śivaḥ sarvam eva idam svakīyābhiḥ ca mūrtibhiḥ brahmā viṣṇuḥ tathā rudraḥ maheśānaḥ sadāśivaḥ atha anyāḥ ca api tanavaḥ paṃca brahma samāhvayāḥ īśānaḥ puruṣaḥ aghoraḥ vāmaḥ sadyaḥ tathā eva ca brahmāṇi etāni devasya mūrttayaḥ paṃca viśrutāḥ īśāna ākhyā tu yā tasya mūrttiḥ ādyā garīyasī bhoktāram prakṛteḥ sākṣāt kṣetrajñam adhitiṣṭhati sthāṇoḥ tatpuruṣa ākhyā yā mūrttiḥ mūrttimataḥ prabhoḥ guṇa āśraya ātmakam bhogyam avyaktam adhitiṣṭhati dharma ādi aṣṭa aṅga saṃyuktam buddhi tattvam pinākinaḥ adhitiṣṭhati aghora ākhyā mūrttiḥ atyanta pūjitā vāmadeva āhvayām mūrttim mahādevasya vedhasaḥ ahaṃkṛteḥ adhiṣṭhātrīm āhuḥ āgama vedinaḥ sadyas jāta āhvayām mūrttim śambhoḥ amita varcasaḥ mānasaḥ samadhiṣṭhātrīm matimantaḥ pracakṣate īśvarīm īśvarasya imām īśa ākhyām hi viduḥ budhāḥ tvak pāṇi sparśa vāyūnām īśvarīm mūrtim aiśvarīm puruṣa ākhyam viduḥ sarve purāṇa artha viśāradāḥ cakṣuṣaḥ caraṇasya api rūpasya agneḥ tathā eva ca aghora ākhyām adhiṣṭhātrīm mūrtim āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ ramanāyāḥ ca pāyoḥ ca rasasya apām tathā eva ca īśvarīm vāmadeva ākhyām mūrttim tad niratām viduḥ sadyas jāta āhvayām mūrtim īśvarīm saṃpracakṣate mūrtayaḥ paṃca devasya vandanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ tasmin vyāpya sthitam viśvam sūtre maṇi gaṇāḥ iva śarvaḥ bhavaḥ tathā rudraḥ ugraḥ bhīmaḥ paśoḥ patiḥ īśānaḥ ca mahādevaḥ mūrttayaḥ ca aṣṭa viśrutāḥ bhūmi aṃbhaḥ agni marut vyoma kṣetrajña arka niśākarāḥ adhiṣṭhitāḥ maheśasya śarva ādyaiḥ aṣṭa mūrttibhiḥ carācara ātmakam viśvam dhatte viśvaṃbharā ātmikā śārvīḥ śiva āhvayā mūrtiḥ iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ bhāvi iti gīyate mūrtti bhavasya paramātmanaḥ bahis antargatā viśvam vyāpya tejaḥ mayī śubhā raudrī rudra avyayā mūrtiḥ āsthitā ghora rūpiṇī mūrtiḥ bhīmasya bhīma ākhyā bhūta vṛndasya bhedikā sarva ātmanām adhiṣṭhātrī sarva kṣetra nivāsinī mūrtiḥ paśupateḥ jñeyā paśu pāśa nikṛṃtanī dīpayantī jagat sarvam divākara samāhvayā īśāna ākhya maheśasya mūrtiḥ divi visarpati āpyāyayati yaḥ viśvam amṛtāṃśuḥ niśākaraḥ mahādevasya sā mūrtiḥ mahādeva samāhvayā ātmā tasya aṣṭamī mūrtiḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ vyāpikā itara mūrtīnām viśvam tasmāt śiva ātmakam vṛkṣasya mūla sekena śākhāḥ puṣyanti vai yathā sarva abhaya pradānam ca sarva anugrahaṇam tathā sarva upakāra karaṇam śivasya ārādhanam viduḥ tathā sarvasya saṃprītyā prītaḥ bhavati śaṃkaraḥ aniṣṭam aṣṭamūrteḥ tat kṛtam eva na saṃśayaḥ aṣṭamūrti ātmanā viśvam adhiṣṭhāya sthitam śivam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca mūrtibhiḥ viśvam eva idam yathā vyāptam tathā śrutam athā etat jñātum icchāmi yāthātmyam pamā īśayoḥ strī puṃs bhāva ātmakam ca idam tābhyām katham adhiṣṭhitam śrīmat vibhūtim śivayoḥ yāthātmyam ca samāsatas śaktiḥ sākṣāt mahādevī mahādevaḥ ca śaktimān dvayam śuddham aśuddham ca param ca aparam eva ca śivasya ca śivāyāḥ ca svāmyam ca etad svabhāvataḥ śivayoḥ vai vaśe viśvam na viśvasya vaśe śivau īśitavyam idam yasmāt tasmāt viśveśvarau śivau yathā śivaḥ tathā devī yathā devī tathā śivaḥ na bhāti vidyamānaḥ api tathā śaktyā vinā śivaḥ prabhā ca bhānunā tena sutarām tad upāśrayā evam paraspara apekṣā śakti śaktimatoḥ sthitā na śivena vinā śaktiḥ na śaktyā ca vinā śivaḥ ādyā sā ekā parā śaktiḥ cit mayī śiva saṃśrayā samāna dharmiṇīm eva śivasya paramātmanaḥ sā ekā parā ca cit rūpā śaktiḥ prasava dharmiṇī vibhajya bahudhā viśvam vidadhāti śiva icchayā sā mūlaprakṛtiḥ māyā triguṇā ca tridhā smṛtā śiva icchayā parāśaktiḥ śivatattva eka tām gatā tatas kriyā ākhyayā śaktyā śaktau śaktimat utthayā tasyām vikṣobhyamāṇāyām ādau nādaḥ samudbabhau nādāt viniḥsṛtaḥ binduḥ bindodevaḥ sadāśivaḥ tasmāt maheśvaraḥ jātaḥ śuddhavidyā maheśvarāt sā vācām īśvarī śaktiḥ vāgīśa ākhyāḥ hi śūlinaḥ yā sā varṇa svarūpeṇa mātṛkā ipi vijṛmbhate atha ananta samāveśāt māyā kālam avāsṛjat niyatim ca kalām vidyām kalātas rāga pūruṣau māyātaḥ punar eva abhūt avyaktam triguṇa ātmakam triguṇāt ca tatas vyaktāt vibhaktāḥ syuḥ trayaḥ guṇāḥ guṇebhyaḥ kṣobhyamāṇebhyaḥ guṇeśa ākhyāḥ trimūrttayaḥ tebhyaḥ syuḥ aṇḍa piṇḍāni tu asaṃkhyāni śiva ājñayā adhiṣṭhitāni ananta ādyaiḥ vidyeśaiḥ cakravartibhiḥ śarīra antara bhedena śakteḥ bhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ nānā rūpāḥ tu vijñeyāḥ sthūla sūkṣma vibhedataḥ rudrasya raudrī sā śaktiḥ viṣṇauḥ vai vaiṣṇavī matā śakya ātmanā eva tat vyāptam yathā dehe antarātmanā kalā yā paramā śaktiḥ kathitā paramātmanaḥ evam eṣā parā śaktiḥ īśvara icchā anuyāyinī sthiram caram ca yat viśvam sṛjati iti viniścayaḥ jñāna kriyā cikīrṣābhiḥ tisṛbhiḥ sva ātma śaktibhiḥ śaktimān īśvaraḥ śaśvat viśvam vyāpya adhitiṣṭhati icchā śaktiḥ maheśasya nityā kāryya niyāmikā jñānaśaktiḥ tu tat kāryam karaṇam kāraṇam tathā kalpayati akhilam kāryam kṣaṇāt saṃkalpa rūpiṇī yathā śakti traya utthānam śakti prasava dharmiṇī śaktyā paramayā nunnā prasūte sakalam jagat evam śakti samāyogāt śaktimān ucyate śivaḥ śakti śaktimat uttham tu śāktam śaivam idam jagat yathā na jāyate putraḥ pitaram mātaram vinā tathā bhavam bhavānīm ca vinā nā etat carācaram strīpuṃsa prabhavam viśvam strīpuṃsa ātmakam eva ca strīpuṃsayoḥ vibhūtiḥ ca strīpuṃsābhyām adhiṣṭhitam paramātmā śivaḥ proktaḥ śivā sā ca prakīrtitā śivaḥ sadāśivaḥ proktaḥ śivā sā ca manonmanī śivaḥ maheśvaraḥ jñeyaḥ śivā māyā iti kathyate puruṣaḥ parameśānaḥ prakṛtiḥ parameśvarī rudraḥ maheśvaraḥ sākṣāt rudrāṇī rudra vallabhā viṣṇuḥ viśveśvaraḥ devaḥ lakṣmīḥ viśveśvara priyā brahmā śivaḥ yadā sraṣṭā brahmāṇī brahmaṇaḥ priyā bhāskaraḥ bhagavān śaṃbhuḥ prabhā bhagavatī śivā jātavedāḥ mahādevaḥ svāhā śarva arddha dehinī nirṛtiḥ bhagavān īśaḥ nairṛtī naganandanī varuṇaḥ bhagavān rudraḥ vāruṇī bhūdhara ātmajā bāla indu śekharaḥ vāyuḥ śivā śiva manoharā yakṣaḥ yajñaśiraḥ hartā ṛddhiḥ himagiri indrajā īśānaḥ parameśānaḥ tad āryā parameśvarī puruṣa ākhyaḥ manuḥ śaṃbhuḥ śatarūpā śivapriyā dakṣaḥ sākṣāt mahādevaḥ prasūtiḥ parameśvarī bhṛguḥ bhaga akṣi hā devaḥ khyātiḥ trinayana priyā marīci bhagavān rudraḥ saṃbhūtiḥ śarva vallabhā gaṃgādharaḥ aṃgirāḥ jñeyaḥ smṛtiḥ sākṣāt umā smṛtā pulastyaḥ śaśabhṛt mauliḥ prītiḥ kāntā pinākinaḥ kratu dhvaṃsī kratuḥ proktaḥ saṃnatiḥ dayitā vibhoḥ trinetraḥ atriḥ umā sākṣāt anasūyā smṛtā budhaiḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ manmatha arātiḥ devī sākṣāt arundhatī śaṃkaraḥ puruṣāḥ sarve striyaḥ sarvā maheśvarī sarve strī puruṣāḥ tasmāt tayoḥ eva vibhūtayaḥ viṣayī bhagavān īśaḥ viṣayaḥ parameśvarī śrāvyam sarvam umā rūpam śrotā śūla vara āyudhaḥ praṣṭavyam vastu jātam tu dhatte śaṃkara vallabhā praṣṭā saḥ eva viśvātmā bāla candra avataṃsakaḥ draṣṭā viśveśvaraḥ devaḥ śaśi khaṃḍa śikhāmaṇiḥ rasa jātam mahādevī devaḥ rasayitā śivaḥ preya jātam ca girijā preyān ca eva gara aśanaḥ mantavya vastu tām dhatte sadā devī maheśvarī mantā saḥ eva viśvātmā mahādevaḥ maheśvaraḥ prāṇaḥ pinākī sarveṣām prāṇinām bhagavān prabhuḥ prāṇa sthitiḥ tu sarveṣām aṃbikā ca ambu rūpiṇī kṣetrajña tvam tadā dhatte bhagavān antaka antakaḥ ahar śūla āyudhaḥ devaḥ śūlapāṇi priyā niśā ākāśaḥ śaṃkaraḥ devaḥ pṛthivī śaṃkara priyā samudraḥ bhagavān īśaḥ velā śailendra kanyakā puṃlliṃgam akhilam dhatte bhagavān puraśāsanaḥ strī liṃgam ca akhilam dhatte devī deva manoramā śabda jālam aśeṣam tu dhatte sarvasya vallabhā yasya yasya padārthasya yā yā śaktiḥ udāhṛtā sā sā viśveśvarī devī sa sa sarvaḥ maheśvaraḥ tat tat āha mahābhāgāḥ tayoḥ tejaḥ vijṛṃbhitam yathā dīpasya dīptasya śikhā dīpayate gṛham tṛṇa ādi śiva mūrti antam viśva khyā atiśaya kramaḥ sannikarṣa krama vaśāt tayoḥ iti parā śrutiḥ sarva ākāra ātmakau etau sarva śreyaḥ vidhāyinau pūjanīyau namaskāryau ciṃtanīyau ca sarvadā yathāprajñam idam kṛṣṇa yāthātmyam parameśayoḥ tat katham śakyate vaktum yāthātmyam parameśayoḥ antargatam ananyānām īśvara arpita cetasām anyeṣām buddhi anārūḍham ārūḍham ca yathā eva tat yā iyam uktā vibhūtiḥ vai prākṛtī sā parā matā aprākṛtām parām anyām guhyām guhya vidaḥ viduḥ aprākṛtī parā ca eṣā vibhūtiḥ pārameśvarī sā eva iha paramā kāṣṭhā vibhūtiḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ tām prāptum prayatante atra jita śvāsāḥ jita indriyāḥ garbhakārāḥ gṛha dvāram niśchidram ghaṭitum yathā saṃsāra āśīviṣa ālīḍha mṛta saṃjīvana auṣadham yaḥ parām aparām ca eva vibhūtim vetti tattvataḥ saḥ aparaḥ bhūtim ullaṃghya parām bhūtim samaśnute etat te kathitam kṛṣṇa yāthātmyam parama ātmanoḥ na a śiṣyebhyaḥ api a śaivebhyaḥ na abhaktebhyaḥ kadācana vyāharet īśayoḥ bhūtim iti veda anuśāsanam tvādṛśebhyaḥ anurūpebhyaḥ kathaya etat na ca anyathā saṃsāra sāgarāt muktaḥ śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt kīrtanāt asya naśyanti mahāntyaḥ pāpa koṭayaḥ bhaktiḥ parāḥ śive sa ambe sa anuge sa paricchide yat yat iṣṭatamam ca anyat tat tat āpnoti asaṃśayam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe gaurīśaṃkaravibhūtiyogaḥ nāma caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ tat evam na vijānanti paśavaḥ pāśa gauravāt a jānantaḥ param bhāvam avikalpam mahā ṛṣayaḥ aparam brahma rūpam ca param brahma ātmakam tathā bhūta indriya antaḥkaraṇa pradhāna viṣaya ātmakam bṛhat tvāt bṛhaṇa tvāt vā brahma ca iti abhidhīyate vidyā avidyā svarūpī iti kaiścid īśaḥ nigadyate vidyām tu cetanām prāhuḥ tathā avidyām acetanām vidyā ca eva viśvam viśva guroḥ vibhoḥ rūpam eva na saṃdehaḥ viśvam tasya vaśe yatas bhrāntiḥ vidyā parā ca iti śārvam rūpam param viduḥ kṣara akṣara ātmakam prāhuḥ kṣara akṣara param pare kṣaraḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni kūṭasthaḥ akṣaraḥ ucyate tayoḥ paraḥ śivaḥ śāntaḥ kṣara akṣara aparaḥ smṛtaḥ samaṣṭi vyaṣṭhi rūpam ca samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi kāraṇam samaṣṭim āhuḥ avyaktam vyaṣṭim vyaktam tathā eva ca te rūpe parameśasya tad icchāyāḥ pravartanāt tayoḥ kāraṇa bhāvena śivam parama kāraṇam kāraṇa artha vidaḥ prāhuḥ samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi kāraṇam jāti vyakti svarūpī iti kathyate kaiścid īśvaraḥ vyaktiḥ vyāvṛtti rūpam tam piṇḍa jāteḥ samāśrayam jātayaḥ vyaktayaḥ ca eva tad ājñā paripālitāḥ pradhānapuruṣa vyakta kāla ātmā kathyate śivaḥ pradhānam prakṛtim prāhuḥ kṣetrajñam puruṣam tathā trayoviṃśati tattvāni vyaktam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ kālaḥ kāryya prapaṃcasya pariṇāma eka kāraṇam eṣām īśaḥ āvirbhāva tirobhāva hetuḥ ekaḥ svarāj ajaḥ tasmāt pradhānapuruṣa vyakta kāla svarūpavān hetuḥ netā adhipaḥ teṣām dhātā ca uktā maheśvaraḥ virāj hiraṇyagarbha ātmā kaiścid īśaḥ nigadyate hiraṇyagarbhaḥ lokānām hetuḥ viśva ātmakaḥ virāj antaryāmī paraḥ ca iti kathyate kavibhiḥ śivaḥ mātā mānam ca meyam ca matim ca āhuḥ atha apare kartā kriyā ca kāryyam ca karaṇam kāraṇam pare tam āhuḥ viguṇam kecid guṇavantam pare viduḥ kecid saṃsāriṇam prāhuḥ tam asaṃsāriṇam pare rāgavantam pare prāhuḥ vīta rāgam tathā pare niṣkriyam ca pare prāhuḥ sa kriyam ca itare janāḥ arūpam kecid āhuḥ vai rūpavantam pare viduḥ adṛśyam apare prāhuḥ dṛśyam iti apare viduḥ śabda ātmakam pare prāhuḥ śabdātītam atha apare kecid cintā mayam prāhuḥ cintayā rahitam pare jñāna ātmakam pare prāhuḥ vijñānam iti ca apare evam vikalpyamānam tu yāthātmyam parameṣṭhinaḥ na adhyavasyanti munayaḥ nānā pratyaya kāraṇāt yāvat paśuḥ na eva paśyati anīśam purāṇam bhuvanasya īśitāram tāvat duḥkhe vartate baddha pāśaḥ saṃsāre asmin cakra nemi krameṇa yadā paśyaḥ paśyate rukma varṇam kartāram īśam puruṣam brahma yonim iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe paśupatitvajñānayogaḥ nāma paṃcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ na śivasya āṇavaḥ bandhaḥ kāryaḥ māyā iyaḥ eva vā prākṛtaḥ vā atha boddhā vā hi ahaṃkāra ātmakaḥ tathā na rāgaḥ na ca vidveṣaḥ śaṃbhoḥ amita tejasaḥ na ca asti abhiniveśaḥ asya kuśalā akuśalāni api āśayaiḥ nā api saṃbandhaḥ saṃskāraiḥ karmaṇām api na tasya kāraṇam kartā na ādiḥ antaḥ tathā antaram na karma karaṇam vā api na akāryam kāryam eva ca na janma maraṇe tasya na kāṃkṣitam a kāṃkṣitam kalyāṇam sakalam ca asti paramātmā śivaḥ yatas apracyutaḥ svatas bhāvaḥ sthitaḥ sthāṇuḥ atas smṛtaḥ śivena adhiṣṭhitam yasmāt jagat sthāvara jaṃgamam sarva rūpaḥ smṛtaḥ śarvaḥ tathā jñātvā na muhyati hiraṇyabāhuḥ bhagavān hiraṇyapatiḥ īśvaraḥ aṃbikā patiḥ īśānaḥ pinākī vṛṣavāhanaḥ ekaḥ rudraḥ param brahma puruṣaḥ kṛṣṇa piṃgalaḥ bālāgra mātraḥ hṛd madhye viciṃtyaḥ dahara antare hiraṇyakeśaḥ padmākṣaḥ hi aruṇaḥ tāmraḥ eva ca saumyaḥ ghoraḥ tathā miśraḥ ca akṣāraḥ ca amṛtaḥ sa puṃviśeṣaḥ paramaḥ bhagavān antaka antakaḥ śivena atiśaya tvena jñāna aiśvarye vilokite lokeśa atiśaya tvena sthitam prāhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ pratisarga prasūtānām brahmaṇām śāstra vistaram upadeṣṭā saḥ eva ādau kāla avaccheda vartinām kāla avaccheda yuktānām gurūṇām api asau guruḥ sarveṣām eva sarva īśaḥ kāla avaccheda varjitaḥ śuddhā svābhāvikī tasya śaktiḥ sarva atiśāyinī tejaḥ prabhāvaḥ vīryam ca kṣamā kāruṇyam eva ca śiva rudra ādi śabdānām praṇavaḥ hi paraḥ smṛtaḥ śaṃbho praṇava vācyasya bhavanāt tad japāt api yā siddhiḥ sā parā prāpyā bhavati eva na saṃśayaḥ tasmāt ekākṣaram devam āhuḥ āgama pāragāḥ vācya vācakayoḥ aikyam manyamānāḥ manasvinaḥ asya mātrāḥ samākhyātāḥ catasraḥ veda mūrddhani akāraḥ ca api ukāraḥ ca makāraḥ nādaḥ iti api akāram bahvṛcam prāhuḥ ukāraḥ yajuḥ ucyate makāraḥ sāma nādaḥ asya śrutiḥ ātharvaṇī smṛtāḥ akāraḥ ca mahābījam rajaḥ sraṣṭā caturmukhaḥ ukāraḥ prakṛtiḥ yoniḥ sattvam pālayitā hariḥ makāraḥ puruṣaḥ bījam tamaḥ saṃhārakaḥ haraḥ nādaḥ paraḥ pumān īśaḥ nirguṇaḥ niṣkriyaḥ śivaḥ sarvam tisṛbhiḥ evā idam mātrābhiḥ nikhilam tridhā abhidhāya śiva ātmānam bodhayati ardha mātrayā yasmāt param na aparam asti kiṃcid yasmāt na aṇīyaḥ na jyāyaḥ asti kiṃcid vṛkṣaḥ iva stabdhaḥ divi tiṣṭhati ekaḥ tena idam pūrṇam puruṣeṇa sarvam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivatattvavarṇanam nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ śaktiḥ svābhavikī tasya vidyā viśva vilakṣaṇā eka anekasya rūpeṇa bhāti bhānoḥ iva prabhā anantāḥ śaktayaḥ yasyāḥ icchā jñāna kriyā ādayaḥ māyā ādyāḥ ca abhavan vahnoḥ visphuliṃgāḥ yathā tathā sadāśiva īśvara ādyāḥ hi vidyā avidyā īśvara ādayaḥ abhavan puruṣāḥ ca asyāḥ prakṛtiḥ ca parātparā mahat ādi viśeṣa antāḥ tu aja ādyāḥ ca api mūrttayaḥ yat ca anyat asti tat sarvam tasyāḥ kāryyam na saṃśayaḥ sā śaktiḥ sarva gā sūkṣmā prabodha ānanda rūpiṇī śaktimān ucyate devaḥ śivaḥ śītāṃśu bhūṣaṇaḥ vedyaḥ śivaḥ śivā vidyā prajñā ca eva śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ dhṛtiḥ eṣā sthitiḥ niṣṭhā jñāna icchā karma śaktayaḥ śuddhavidyā śuddha kalā sarvam śakti kṛtam yatas māyā ca prakṛtiḥ jīvaḥ vikāraḥ vikṛtiḥ tathā sā devī māyayā sarvam brahmāṃḍam sacarācaram anayā saha sarva īśaḥ saptaviṃśa prakārayā saṃśaya āviṣṭa manasaḥ vismṛśanti yathātatham kim kāraṇam kutas jātāḥ jīvāmaḥ kena vā vayam kutra asmākam saṃpratiṣṭhā kena vā adhiṣṭhitāḥ vayam kena vartāmahe śaśvat sukheṣu anyeṣu ca aniśam avilaṃghyā ca viśvasya vyavasthā kena vā kṛtā bhūtāni yoniḥ puruṣaḥ yogī ca eṣām paraḥ atha vā acetana tvāt kāla ādeḥ cetana tve pi ca ātmanaḥ sukha duḥkhāni bhūta tvāt anīśa tvāt vicāryate tad dhyāna yoga anugatām prapaśyan śaktim aiśvarīm pāśa vicchedikām sākṣāt nigūḍhām sva guṇaiḥ bhṛśam tayā vicchinna pāśāḥ te sarva kāraṇa kāraṇam śaktimantam mahādevam apaśyan divya cakṣuṣā yaḥ kāraṇāni aśeṣāṇi kāla ātma sahitāni ca aprameyaḥ anayā śaktyā sakalam yaḥ adhitiṣṭhati dṛṣṭena bhakti yogena divyaḥ gatim avāpnuyuḥ tasmāt saha tathā śaktyā hṛdi paśyanti ye śivam teṣām śāśvatikī śāntiḥ na etareṣām iti śrutiḥ tasmāt śakteḥ śaktimataḥ tādātmyāt nirvṛtiḥ dvayoḥ kramaḥ vivakṣitaḥ nūnam vimuktau jñāna karmaṇoḥ devaḥ vā dānavaḥ vā api paśuḥ vā vihagaḥ api vā kīraḥ vā atha kṛmiḥ vā api mucyate tad prasādataḥ garbha sthaḥ jāyamānaḥ vā bālaḥ vā taruṇaḥ api vā vṛddhaḥ vā mriyamāṇaḥ vā svarga sthaḥ vā atha nārakī patitaḥ vā api dharma ātmā paṃḍitaḥ mūḍhaḥ eva vā prasāde tad kṣaṇāt eva mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ ayogyānām ca kāruṇyāt bhaktānām parameśvaraḥ prasāda pūrvikā yā iyam bhukti mukti vidhāyinī aneka janma siddhānām śrauta smārta anuvartinām viraktānām prabuddhānām prasīdati maheśvaraḥ na yoni yantra pīḍāyai bhavet na eva atra saṃśayaḥ sāṃgā ca yā sevā sā bhaktiḥ iti kathyate śiva rūpa ādi ciṃtā yā sā sevā mānasī smṛtā japa ādiḥ vācikī sevā karma pūjā ādi kāyikī sā iyam tri sādhanā sevā śiva dharmaḥ ca kathyate sa tu paṃcavidhaḥ proktaḥ śivena paramātmanā tapaḥ karma japaḥ dhyānam jñānam ca iti samāsatas ca tapaḥ cāndrāyaṇa ādikam japaḥ tridhā śiva abhyāsaḥ cintā dhyānam śivasya tu śiva āgama uktam yat jñānam tat atra jñānam ucyate śrīkaṃṭhena śivena uktam śivāyai ca śiva āgamaḥ śiva āśritānām kāruṇyāt śreyasām eka sādhanam tyajet ca viṣaya āsaṃgam śreyaḥ arthī matimān naraḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivatattvakathanam nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca vedasāre śiva jñānam sva āśritānām vimuktaye abhaktānām abuddhīnām ayuktānām agocaram arthaiḥ daśa ṛddhaiḥ saṃyuktam gūḍham aprājña ninditam vedāt ṣaṣ aṃgāt uddhṛtya sāṃkhyāt yogāt ca kṛtsnaśas śata koṭi pramāṇena vistīrṇam grantha saṃkhyayā kathitam parameśena tatra pūjā katham prabhoḥ kasya adhikāraḥ pūjā ādau jñāna yoga ādayaḥ katham śaivam saṃkṣipya veda uktam śivena paribhāṣitam sisṛkṣayā purā avyaktāt śivaḥ sthāṇuḥ maheśvaraḥ janayāmāsa ca tadā ṛṣiḥ viśva adhikaḥ prabhuḥ devānām prathamam devam brahmāṇam brahmaṇaspatim brahmā api pitaram devam jāyamānam nyavaikṣata tam jāyamānam janakaḥ devaḥ prāpaśyat ājñayā dṛṣṭaḥ rudreṇa devaḥ asau asṛjat viśvam īśvaraḥ varṇa āśrama vyavasthām ca cakāra sa pṛthak pṛthak dharā ca vahniḥ sūryaḥ ca yajñaḥ viṣṇuḥ śacīpatiḥ te ca anye ca surāḥ rudram rudrādhyāyena tuṣṭuvuḥ apahṛtya sva līlā artham teṣām jñānam maheśvaraḥ tam apṛcchan tatas devāḥ kaḥ bhavān iti mohitāḥ āsam prathamam eva aham vartāmi ca sura uttamāḥ a paśyantaḥ tam īśānam stuvantaḥ ca eva sāmabhiḥ vratam pāśupatam kṛtvā tu atharvaśirasi sthitam bhasma saṃchanna sarva aṃgāḥ babhūvuḥ amarāḥ tadā atha teṣām prasāda artham paśūnām patiḥ īśvaraḥ sa gaṇaḥ ca umayā sārddham sānnidhyam akarot prabhuḥ yam vinidrāḥ jita śvāsāḥ yoginaḥ dagdha kilbiṣāḥ hṛdi paśyanti tam devam dadṛśuḥ deva puṃgavāḥ yām āhuḥ paramām śaktim īśvara icchā anuvartinīm tām apaśyat maheśasya vāmatas vāma locanām ye vinirdhūta saṃsārāḥ prāptāḥ śaivam param padam nitya siddhāḥ ca ye vā anyam te ca dṛṣṭāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ atha tam tuṣṭuvuḥ devāḥ devyā saha maheśvaram devaḥ api devān ālokya ghṛṇayā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ tuṣṭaḥ asmi iti āha su prītaḥ svabhāva madhurām giram devāḥ ūcuḥ kasya adhikāraḥ pūjāyām vaktum arhasi tattvataḥ sva rūpam darśayāmāsa ghoram sūrya ātmakam param śaktibhiḥ mūrtibhiḥ ca aṃgaiḥ grahaiḥ devaiḥ ca saṃvṛtam dṛṣṭvā evam adbhuta ākāram devāḥ viṣṇu purogamāḥ buddhvā divākaram devam devīm ca eva niśākaram pañcabhūtāni śeṣāṇi tad mayam ca carācaram sindūra varṇāya su maṇḍalāya suvarṇa varṇa ābharaṇāya tubhyam padma ābha netrāya sa paṃkajāya brahma indra nārāyaṇa kāraṇāya su ratna pūrṇam sa suvarṇa toyam su kuṃkuma ādyam sa kuśam sa puṣpam namaḥ śivāya śāntāya sa gaṇāya ādi hetave rudrāya viṣṇave tubhyam brahmaṇe sūrya mūrtaye yaḥ śivam maṇḍale saure saṃpūjya eva samāhitaḥ praṇamet vā paṭhet etān ślokān śruti mukhān imān tasmāt abhyarcayet nityam śivam āditya rūpiṇam dharma kāma artha mukti artham manasā karmaṇā girā atha devān samālokya maṇḍala sthaḥ maheśvaraḥ sarva āgama uttaram dattvā śāstram antaradhāt haraḥ tatra pūjā adhikāraḥ jñātvā praṇamya deveśam devāḥ jagmuḥ yathāgatam tayā sa coditaḥ devaḥ devyā candra vibhūṣaṇaḥ mayā agastyena guruṇā dadhīcena mahā ṛṣiṇā svayam api avatīrya urvyām yuga āvarteṣu śūladhṛk sva āśritānām vimukti artham kurute jñāna santatim ṛbhuḥ satyaḥ bhārgavaḥ ca hi aṃgirāḥ savitā dvijāḥ mṛtyuḥ śatakratuḥ dhīmān vasiṣṭhaḥ muni puṃgavaḥ sārasvataḥ tridhāmā ca trivṛtaḥ muni puṃgavaḥ śata tejāḥ svayam dharmaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ iti śrutaḥ svarakṣaḥ ca aruṇiḥ dhīmān tathā ca eva kṛtaṃjayaḥ vācaḥsravāḥ muniḥ sākṣāt tathā sūkṣmāyaṇiḥ śuciḥ tṛṇabinduḥ muniḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śaktiḥ śākteyaḥ uttaraḥ jātūkarṇyaḥ hariḥ sākṣāt kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ vyāsa avatārān śṛṇvantu kalpa yoga īśvarān kramāt laiṃge vyāsa avatārāḥ hi teṣu suvratāḥ yoga ācārya avatārāḥ ca tathā śiṣyeṣu śūlinaḥ tatra tatra vibhoḥ śiṣyāḥ catvāraḥ syuḥ mahā ojasaḥ śiṣyāḥ teṣām praśiṣyāḥ ca śataśas atha sahasraśas teṣām saṃbhāvanāt loke śaiva ājñā karaṇa ādibhiḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivatattvajñāne vyāsāvatāravarṇanam nāma aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca avatārān hi śarvasya śiṣyān ca bhagavan vada laugākṣiḥ ca mahā māyaḥ jaigīṣavyaḥ tathā eva ca supālakaḥ gautamaḥ ca tathā vedaśirāḥ muniḥ gokarṇaḥ ca guhāvāsī śikhaṇḍī ca aparaḥ smṛtaḥ jaṭāmālī ca aṭṭahāsaḥ dārukaḥ lāṃgulī tathā mahākālaḥ ca śūlī ca ḍaṃḍī muṇḍīśaḥ eva ca sa viṣṇuḥ somaśarmā ca lakuli īśvaraḥ eva ca aṣṭāviṃśati saṃkhyātāḥ yoga ācāryāḥ yuga kramāt śiṣyāḥ pratyekam eteṣām catvāraḥ śānta cetasaḥ śveta ādayaḥ ca ruṣya antān tān bravīmi yathākramam śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaḥ ca eva śvetāśvaḥ śvetalohitaḥ dundubhiḥ śatarūpaḥ ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumant tathā vikośaḥ ca vikeśaḥ ca vipāśaḥ pāśanāśanaḥ sudhāmā virajāḥ ca eva śaṃkhaḥ ca aṃḍajaḥ eva ca sārasvataḥ ca meghaḥ ca meghavāhaḥ suvāhakaḥ kapilaḥ ca āsuriḥ paṃcaśikhaḥ bāṣkalaḥ eva ca parāśarāḥ ca gargaḥ ca bhārgavaḥ ca aṃgirāḥ tathā balabandhuḥ nirāmitrāḥ ketuśṛṃgaḥ tapodhanaḥ ca sudhāmā kaśyapaḥ ca eva vasiṣṭhaḥ virajāḥ tathā atriḥ ugraḥ guru śreṣṭhaḥ śravanāḥ utha śraviṣṭakaḥ kuṇiḥ ca kuṇibāhuḥ ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ kāśyapaḥ hi uśanāḥ ca eva cyavanaḥ ca bṛhaspatiḥ utathyaḥ vāmadevaḥ ca mahākālaḥ mahā anilaḥ vācaḥśravāḥ suvīraḥ ca śyāvakaḥ ca yatīśvaraḥ hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyaḥ lokākṣiḥ kuthumiḥ tathā plakṣaḥ dārbhāyaṇiḥ ca eva ketumān gautamaḥ tathā śālihotraḥ suveṣaḥ ca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ akṣapādaḥ kaṇādaḥ ca ulūkaḥ vatsaḥ eva ca ete śiṣyāḥ maheśasya yoga ācārya svarūpiṇaḥ saṃkhyā ca śatam eteṣām saha dvādaśa saṃkhyayā sarve pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasma uddhūlita vigrahāḥ sarva śāstra artha tattva jñāḥ veda vedāṃga pāragāḥ śiva āśrama ratāḥ sarve śiva jñāna parāyaṇāḥ sarve saṃga vinirmuktāḥ śiva eka āsakta cetasaḥ sarva dvandva sahāḥ dhīrāḥ sarva bhūta hite ratāḥ ṛjavaḥ mṛdavaḥ svasthāḥ jita krodhāḥ jita indriyāḥ rudra akṣa mālā ābharaṇāḥ tripuṃḍra aṃkita mastakāḥ śikhā jaṭāḥ sarva jaṭāḥ ajaṭāḥ muṃḍa śīrṣakāḥ phala mūla aśana prāyāḥ prāṇāyāma parāyaṇāḥ śiva abhimāna saṃpannāḥ śiva dhyāna eka tatparāḥ samunmathita saṃsāra viṣa vṛkṣa aṃkura udgamāḥ prayātum eva sannaddhāḥ param śiva puram prati sa deśikān imān matvā nityam yaḥ śivam arcayet sa yāti śiva sāyujyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā iti śrī śivamahāpur saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivasya yogāvatāravarṇanam nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca prāyas tvam avatīrya urvyām pāśa vicchittaye nṛṇām tvattaḥ nyaḥ paramam bhāvam kaḥ jānīyāt śiva ātmakam tasmāt tava mukha udgīrṇam sākṣāt iva pinākinaḥ śiva jñāna amṛtam pītvā na me tṛptam abhūt manaḥ sākṣāt sarva jagat kartuḥ bhartuḥ aṃkam samāśritā sthāne pṛṣṭam tvayā kṛṣṇa tat vakṣyāmi yathātatham tadā devyāḥ priya sakhī su smita āsyā śubhāvatī phullāni ati manojñāni puṣpāṇi samudāharat tatas svam aṃkam āropya devīm alaṃkṛtya ca taiḥ puṣpaiḥ āste hṛṣṭataraḥ svayam atha antaḥpura cāriṇyaḥ devyaḥ divya vibhūṣaṇāḥ antaraṃgāḥ gaṇa indrāḥ ca sarva loka maheśvarīm bhartāram paripūrṇam ca sarva loka mahā īśvaram cāmara āsakta hastāḥ ca devīm devam siṣevire tatas priyāḥ kathāḥ vṛttāḥ vinodāya maheśayoḥ trāṇāya ca nṛṇām loke ye śivam śaraṇam gatāḥ kena vaśyaḥ mahādevaḥ martyānām manda cetasām ātma tattva ādi aśaktānām ātmanām akṛtātmanām īśvaraḥ uvāca na karmaṇā na tapasā na japaiḥ na āsana ādibhiḥ na jñānena na ca anyena vaśyaḥ aham śraddhayā vinā śraddhā mayi asti ced puṃsām yena kena api hetunā vaśyaḥ spṛśyaḥ ca dṛśyaḥ ca pūjyaḥ saṃbhāṣyaḥ eva ca sādhyā tasmāt mayi śaddhā mām vaśīkartum icchatā śraddhā hetuḥ svadharmasya rakṣaṇam varṇinām iha sva varṇa āśrama dharmeṇa vartate yaḥ tu mānavaḥ āmnāya siddham akhilam dharmam āśramiṇām iha brahmaṇā kathitam pūrvam mama eva ājñā purassaram na atyanta phala bhūyiṣṭhaḥ sa samanvitaḥ tena dharmeṇa mahatām śraddhām prāpya su durllabhām varṇinaḥ ye prapadyante mām an anya samāśrayāḥ teṣām sukhena mārgeṇa dharma kāma artha muktayaḥ varṇa āśrama samācāraḥ mayā bhūyas prakalpitaḥ tasmin bhaktimatām eva madīyānām tu varṇinām adhikāraḥ na ca anyeṣām iti ājñā naiṣṭhikī mama tad ājñaptena mārgeṇa varṇinaḥ mad upāśrayāḥ mala māyā ādi pāśebhyaḥ vimuktāḥ mad prasādataḥ param madīyam āsādya punarāvṛtti durlabham paramam mama sādharmyam prāpya nirvṛtim āyayuḥ alabdha lābhaḥ eva eṣa koṭi koṭi guṇa adhikaḥ mama avatārāḥ hi śubhe yoga ācārya chalena tu ayuktānām abuddhīnām abhaktānām sureśvari durlabham santati jñānam tatas yatnāt samāśrayet yat anyatra śramam kuryyāt mokṣa mārga bahiṣkṛtaḥ jñānam kriyā ca caryā ca yogaḥ ca iti sureśvari catuṣpādaḥ samākhyātaḥ mama dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ paśu pāśa pati jñānam jñānam iti abhidhīyate aśvamedha gaṇāt śreṣṭham devi citta prasādhanam mukti dam ca tathā hi etat duṣprāpyam viṣaya eṣiṇām vairāgyāt jāyate jñānam jñānāt yogaḥ pravartate yoga jñaḥ patitaḥ vā api mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ dayā kāryā atha satatam ahiṃsā jñāna saṃgrahaḥ adhyāpanam ca adhyayanam yajanam yājanam tathā dhyānam īśvara bhāvaḥ ca satatam jñāna śīla tā acirāt eva vijñānam labdhvā yogam ca vindati dagdhvā deham imam jñānī kṣaṇāt jñāna agninā priye tasmāt niyogataḥ yogī puṇya apuṇyam vivarjayet jñāna yoga rataḥ bhūtvā paścāt yogam samabhyaset na yajanti hi mām yuktāḥ sama loṣṭa aśma kāṃcanāḥ nitya yuktaḥ muniḥ śreṣṭhaḥ mad bhaktaḥ ca samāhitaḥ jñāna yoga rataḥ yogī mama sāyujyam āpnuyāt atha a virakta cittāḥ ye varṇinaḥ mad upāśritāḥ dvidhā mad pūjanam jñeyam bāhyam ābhyantaram tathā vāc manaḥ kāya bhedāt ca tridhā mad bhajanam viduḥ tapaḥ karma japaḥ dhyānam jñānam vā iti anupūrvaśas mad nāma niratā vāṇī vā a matā khalu na itarā liṃgaiḥ mad śāsana ādiṣṭaiḥ tripuṃḍra ādibhiḥ aṃkitaḥ mama upacāra nirataḥ kāyaḥ kāyaḥ na ca itaraḥ mad arcā karma vijñeyam bāhye yāga ādinā ucyate japaḥ paṃcākṣara abhyāsaḥ praṇava abhyāsaḥ eva ca rudra adhyāya ādika abhyāsaḥ na veda adhyayana ādikam na ātma ādi artha samādhayaḥ mama āgama artha vijñānam jñānam na anya artha vedanam prāk vāsanā vaśāt devi tattva niṣṭhām samācaret bāhyāt ābhyantaram śreṣṭham bhavet śataguṇa adhikam asaṃkara tvāt doṣāṇām dṛṣṭānām api asambhavāt śaucam ābhyantaram vidyāt na bāhyam śaucam ucyate antar śauca vimukta ātmā śuciḥ api aśuciḥ yatas bahis vā abhyantaram vā atha mayā bhāvaḥ hi gṛhyate bhāva eka ātmā kriyā devi mama dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ manasā karmaṇā vācā hi an apekṣya phalam kvacid phala arthī tad abhāve mām parityaktum kṣamaḥ yatas phala anapekṣayā yeṣām manaḥ mad pravaṇam bhavet prārthayeyuḥ phalam paścāt bhaktāḥ te api mama priyāḥ prāk saṃskāra vaśāt eva ye viciṃtya phala aphale vivaśāḥ mām prapadyante mama priyatamāḥ matāḥ mama api lābhaḥ tad lābhāt na aparaḥ parameśvari mahātmanām ananyānām mayi saṃnyasta cetasām aṣṭadhā lakṣaṇam prāhuḥ mama dharma adhikāriṇām mad bhakta jana vātsalyam pūjāyām ca anumodanam mad kathā śravaṇe bhaktiḥ svara netra aṃga vikriyāḥ mama anusmaraṇam nityam yaḥ ca mām upajīvati sa vipra indraḥ muniḥ śrīmān sa yatiḥ sa ca paṃḍitaḥ tasya aham na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivabhaktivarṇanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca atha vakṣyāmi deveśi bhaktānām adhikāriṇām viduṣām dvijamukhyānām varṇa dharma samāsatas tris snānam ca agni kāryam ca liṃga arcanam anukramam dānam īśrara bhāvaḥ ca dayā sarvatra sarvadā satyam santoṣam āstikyam ahiṃsā sarva jantuṣu vyākhyānam brahmacaryam ca śravaṇam ca tapaḥ kṣamā śaucam śikhā upavītam ca uṣṇīṣam ca uttarīyakam niṣiddha asevanam ca eva bhasma rudrākṣa dhāraṇam parvaṇi abhyarcanam devi caturdaśyām viśeṣataḥ pānam ca brahmakūrcasya māsi māsi yathāvidhi abhyarcanam viśeṣeṇa tena eva snāpya mām priye tathā paryuṣita annasya yāvakasya viśeṣataḥ sāmānyam sarva varṇānām brāhmaṇānām viśeṣataḥ kṣamā śāntiḥ ca santoṣaḥ satyam asteyam eva ca sarva saṃga nivṛttiḥ ca daśa etāni viśeṣataḥ liṃgāni yoginām bhūyas divā bhikṣā aśanam tathā vānaprastha āśrama sthānām samānam idam iṣyate rātrau na bhojanam kāryam sarveṣām brahmacāriṇām adhyāpanam yājanam ca kṣatriyasya a pratigrahaḥ vaiśyasya ca viśeṣeṇa mayā na atra vidhīyate rakṣaṇam sarva varṇānām yuddhe śatru vadhaḥ tathā duṣṭa pakṣi mṛgāṇām ca duṣṭānām śātanam nṛṇām aviśvāsaḥ ca sarvatra viśvāsaḥ mama yogiṣu strī saṃsargaḥ ca kāleṣu camū rakṣaṇam eva ca sadā saṃcāritaiḥ cāraiḥ loka vṛttānta vedanam sadā astra dhāraṇam ca eva bhasma kaṃcuka dhāraṇam rājñām mama āśrama sthānām eṣa dharmasya saṃgrahaḥ gorakṣaṇam ca vāṇijyam kṛṣiḥ vaiśyasya kathyate śuśrūṣā itara varṇānām dharmaḥ śūdrasya kathyate udyāna karaṇam ca eva mama kṣetra samāśrayaḥ brahmacaryam vanasthānām yatīnām brahmacāriṇām strīṇām tu bhartṛ śuśrūṣā dharmaḥ na anyaḥ sanātanaḥ yā nārī bhartṛ śuśrūṣām vihāya vrata tatparā sā nārī narakam yāti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā atha bhartṛ vihīnāyāḥ vakṣye dharmam sanātanam vratam dānam tapaḥ śaucam bhū śayyā naktabhojanam brahmacaryam sadā snānam bhasmanā salilena vā śāntiḥ maunam kṣamā nityam saṃvibhāgaḥ yathāvidhi aṣṭābhyām ca caturdaśyām paurṇamāsyām viśeṣataḥ ekādaśyām ca vidhivat upavāsa umama arcanam iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ mayā āśrama niṣeviṇām brahma kṣatra viśām devi yatīnām brahmacāriṇām tathā eva vānaprasthānām gṛhasthānām ca sundari śūdrāṇām atha nārīṇām dharmaḥ eṣa sanātanaḥ dhyeyaḥ tvayā aham deveśi sadā jāpyaḥ ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ atha ye mānavāḥ loke sva icchayā dhṛta vigrahāḥ bhāva atiśaya saṃpannāḥ pūrva saṃskāra saṃyutāḥ viraktā vā anuraktā vā strī ādīnām viṣayeṣu api teṣām mama ātma vijñānam viśuddhānām vivekinām mad prasādāt viśuddhānām duḥkham āśrama rakṣaṇāt na asti kṛtyam akṛtyam ca samādhiḥ vā parāyaṇam na vidhiḥ na niṣedhaḥ ca teṣām mama yathā tathā tathā eva kṛtakṛtyānām teṣām api na saṃśayaḥ mad bhaktānām hita arthāya mānuṣam bhāvam āśritāḥ rudra lokāt paribhraṣṭāḥ te rudrāḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ mama anuśāsanam yadvat brahma ādīnām pravartakam tathā narāṇām anyeṣām tad niyogaḥ pravartakaḥ mama ājñā dhāra bhāvena sadbhāva atiśayena ca mayi bhāvavatām puṃsām prāk adṛṣṭa artha gocarāḥ kaṃpa svedaḥ kaṇṭhe ca svara vikriyā ānanda ādi upalabdhiḥ ca bhavet ākasmikī muhur prākṛtān iva manvānaḥ na avajānīta paṃḍitaḥ avajñānam kṛtam teṣu naraiḥ vyāmūḍha cetanaiḥ āyuḥ śriyam kulam śīlam hitvā nirayam āvahet brahma viṣṇu sureśānām api tūlāyate padam mattaḥ nyat anapekṣāṇām uddhṛtānām mahātmanām aśuddham bauddham aiśvaryam prākṛtam pauruṣam tathā guṇa īśānām atas tyājyam guṇa atīta pada eṣiṇām ittham śrīkaṇṭha nāthena śivena paramātmanā hitāya jagatām uktaḥ jñāna sāra artha saṃgrahaḥ vijñāna saṃgrahasya asya veda śāstrāṇi kṛtsnaśas sa itihāsa purāṇāni vidyā vyākhyāna vistaraḥ jñānam jñeyam anuṣṭheyam adhikāraḥ atha sādhanam sādhyam ca iti ṣaṣ arthānām saṃgraha tva eṣa saṃgrahaḥ guroḥ adhikṛtam jñānam jñeyam pāśaḥ paśuḥ patiḥ liṃga arcana ādi anuṣṭheyam bhaktaḥ tu adhikṛtaḥ api yaḥ sādhanam śiva mantra ādyam sādhyam śiva samāna tā ṣaṣ artha saṃgrahasya asya jñānāt sarvajña tā ucyate prathamam karma yajña ādeḥ bhaktyā vitta anusārataḥ na karma karaṇīyam hi bahis tasya mahātmanāḥ jñāna amṛtena tṛptasya bhaktyā śaiva śiva ātmanaḥ na antar na ca bahis kṛṣṇa kṛtyam asti kadācana jñānena jñeyam ālokya ajñānam ca api parityajet na ekāgram ced śive cittam kim kṛtena api karmaṇā ekāgram eva ced cittam kim kṛtena api karmaṇā tasmāt karmāṇi a kṛtvā vā kṛtvā vā antar bahis kramāt śive niviṣṭa cittānām pratiṣṭhita dhiyām satām iha unnamaḥ śivāya iti mantreṇa anena siddhayaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṃḍe śivajñānavarṇanam nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca paṃcākṣarasya māhātmyam śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ paṃcākṣarasya māhātmyam varṣa koṭi śataiḥ api aśakyam vistarāt vaktum tasmāt saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu vede śiva āgame ca ayam ubhayatra ṣaṣ akṣareḥ sarveṣām śiva bhaktānām aśeṣa artha sādhakaḥ tat alpa akṣaram artha āḍhyam veda sāram vimukti dam ājñā siddham asaṃdigdham vākyam etat śiva ātmakam nānā siddhi yutam divyam loka citta anuraṃjakam su niścita artham gaṃbhīram vākyam tat pārameśvaram prāha unnamaḥ śivāya iti sarvajñaḥ sarva dehinām tat bījam sarva vidyānām mantram ādyam ṣaṣ akṣaram ati sūkṣmam mahā artham ca jñeyam tat vaṭa bīja vat devaḥ guṇa traya atītaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva kṛt prabhuḥ iśāna ādyāni sūkṣmāṇi brahmāṇi eka akṣarāṇi tu mantre ṣaṣ akṣare sūkṣme paṃca brahma tanuḥ śivaḥ vācya vācaka bhāvena sthitaḥ sākṣāt svabhāvataḥ vācyaḥ śiva uprameya tvāt mantraḥ tad vācakaḥ smṛtaḥ vācya vācaka bhāvaḥ ayam anādi saṃsthitaḥ tayoḥ yathā ghora saṃsāra sāgaraḥ śivaḥ api hi tathā anādi saṃsārāt mocakaḥ sthitaḥ vyādhīnām bheṣajam yadvat pratipakṣaḥ svabhāvataḥ tadvat saṃsāra doṣāṇām pratipakṣaḥ śivaḥ smṛtaḥ pradhāna paramāṇu ādi yāvat kiṃcid acetanam na tat kartṛ svayam dṛṣṭam buddhimat kāraṇam vinā dharma adharma upadeśaḥ ca bandha mokṣau vicāraṇāt na sarvajñam vinā puṃsām ādisargaḥ prasiddhi ati vaidyam vinā nirānandāḥ kliśyante rogiṇaḥ yathā tasmāt anādiḥ sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaḥ sadāśivaḥ asti nāthaḥ paritrātā puṃsām saṃsāra sāgarāt sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaḥ ca śivaḥ jñeyaḥ śiva āgame abhidhāna abhidheya tvāt mantraḥ siddhaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ etāvat tu śiva jñānam etāvat paramam padam yat om namaḥ śivāya iti śiva vākyam ṣaṣ akṣaram vidhi vākyam idam śaivam na artha vādam śiva ātmakam yaḥ sarvajñaḥ su saṃpūrṇaḥ svabhāva vimalaḥ śivaḥ loka anugraha karttā ca sa mṛṣārtham katham vadet yat yathā avasthitam vastu guṇa doṣaiḥ svabhāvataḥ yāvat phalam ca tat pūrṇam sarvajñaḥ tu yathā vadet rāga ajñāna ādibhiḥ doṣaiḥ grasta tvāt anṛtam vadet ajñāta aśeṣa doṣeṇa sarva jñeya śivena yat praṇītam amalam vākyam tat pramāṇam na saṃśayaḥ tasmāt īśvara vākyāni śraddheyāni vipaścitā vākyam muni varaiḥ śāntaiḥ tat vijñeyam subhāṣitam rāga dveṣa anṛta krodha kāma tṛṣṇā anusāri yat saṃskṛtena api kim tena mṛdunā lalitena vā avidyā rāga vākyena saṃsāra kleśa hetunā yat śrutvā jāyate śreyaḥ rāga ādīnām ca saṃśayaḥ bahu tve api hi mantrāṇām sarvajñena śivena yaḥ sa aṃgāni veda śāstrāṇi saṃsthitāni ṣaṣ akṣare mantraḥ ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ bhinnaḥ sūtram vṛtyā ātmanā yathā śiva jñānāni yāvanti yāni ca ṣaṣ akṣarasya sūtrasya tāni bhāṣyam samāsatas yasya unnamaḥ śivāya iti mantraḥ ayam hṛdi saṃsthitaḥ tena adhītam śrutam tena kṛtam sarvam anuṣṭhitam yena unnamaḥ śivāya iti mantra abhyāsaḥ sthirīkṛtaḥ namaskāra ādi saṃyuktam śivāya iti akṣara trayam antyajaḥ vā adhamaḥ vā api mūrkhaḥ vā paṃḍitaḥ api vā paṃcākṣara jape niṣṭhaḥ mucyate pāpa paṃjarāt iti uktam parameśena devyā pṛṣṭena śūlinā hitāya sarva martyānām dvijānām tu viśeṣataḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe paṃcākṣaramāhātmyavarṇanam nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ kṣīṇe varṇa āśrama ācāre saṃkaṭe samupasthite īśvaraḥ uvāca āśritya paramām vidyām hṛdyām paṃcākṣarīm mama bhaktyā ca bhāvitātmānaḥ mucyante kali jāḥ narāḥ dūṣitānām kṛtaghnānām nindakānām chala ātmanām lubdhānām vakra manasām api mad pravaṇa ātmanām mama paṃcākṣarī vidyā saṃsāra bhaya tāriṇī īśvaraḥ uvāca sa mantrakam mām patitaḥ pūjayet yadi mohitaḥ nārakī syāt na sandehaḥ mama paṃcākṣaram vinā abbhakṣāḥ vāyubhakṣāḥ ca ye ca anye vrata karśitāḥ bhaktyā paṃcākṣareṇa eva yaḥ hi mām sakṛt arcayet tasmāt tapāṃsi yajñāḥ ca vratāni niyamāḥ tathā paṃcākṣara arcanasya ete koṭi aṃśena api no samaḥ baddhaḥ vā api atha muktaḥ vā pāśāt paṃcākṣareṇa yaḥ pūjayet mām sa mucyeta na atra kāryā vicāraṇā arudraḥ vā sa rudraḥ vā sakṛt paṃca akṣareṇa yaḥ pūjayet patitaḥ vā api mūḍhaḥ vā mucyate naraḥ ṣaṣ akṣareṇa vā devi tathā paṃca akṣareṇa vā alabdha alabdhaḥ evā iha koṭi koṭi guṇa adhikaḥ labdhvā saṃpūjayet yaḥ tu maitrī ādi guṇa saṃyutaḥ mama paṃca akṣare mantre tasmāt śreṣṭhataraḥ hi saḥ paṃcākṣara prabhāveṇa loka veda mahā ṛṣayaḥ tiṣṭhanti śāśvatāḥ dharmāḥ devāḥ sarvam idam jagat sarvam prakṛtim āpannam tatra saṃlayam eṣyati tadā vedāḥ ca śāstrāṇi sarve paṃcākṣare sthitāḥ te nāśam nā eva saṃprāptāḥ mad śaktyā hi anupālitāḥ tatas sṛṣṭiḥ abhūt mattaḥ prakṛti ātma prabhedataḥ guṇa mūrti ātmanām ca eva tatas vā antara saṃhṛtiḥ tadā nārāyaṇaḥ śete devaḥ māyā mayīm tanum tad nābhi paṃkajāt jātaḥ paṃcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ sisṛkṣamāṇaḥ lokān trīn na saktaḥ hi asahāyavān munīn daśa sasarja ādau mānasān amita ojasaḥ teṣām siddhi vivṛddhi artham mām provāca pitāmahaḥ mad putrāṇām mahādeva śaktim dehi maheśvara pañca akṣarāṇi kramaśas proktavān padmayonaye sa pañca vadanaiḥ tāni gṛhṇan lokapitāmahaḥ vācya vācaka bhāvena jñātavān mām maheśvaram jñātvā prayogam vividham siddha mantraḥ prajāpatiḥ te ca labdhvā mantra ratnam sākṣāt lokapitāmahāt tad ājñaptena mārgeṇa mad ārādhana kāṃkṣiṇaḥ mad priyaḥ satatam śrīmān mad bhaktaiḥ rakṣitaḥ sadā tasya abhyāśe tapaḥ tīvram lokam sraṣṭum samutsukāḥ divyam varṣa sahasram tu vāyubhakṣāḥ samācaran teṣām
