bhaktim aham dṛṣṭvā sadyas pratyakṣatām iyām ṛṣim chandaḥ ca kīlam ca bīja śaktim ca daivatam nyāsam ṣaḍaṃgam digbandham viniyogam aśeṣatas proktavān aham āryāṇām jagat sṛṣṭi vivṛddhaye tatas te mantra māhātmyāt ṛṣayaḥ tapasā idhitāḥ sṛṣṭim vitanvate samyak sa deva asura mānuṣīm ādau namaḥ prayoktavyam śivāya tu tatas param sā eṣā pañcākṣarī vidyā sarva śrutiśiraḥ gatā sarva jātasya sarvasya bīja bhūtā sanātanī prathamam mad mukha udgīrṇā sā mama eva asti vācikā catur bhujā tri nayanā bāla indu kṛta śekharā padma utpala karā saumyā vara da abhaya pāṇikā sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannā sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitā sita padmāsana āsīnā nīla kuṃcita mūrddhajā asyāḥ pañcavidhāḥ varṇāḥ prasphurat raśmi maṃḍalāḥ pītaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tathā dhūmraḥ svarṇa ābhaḥ raktaḥ eva ca pṛthak prayojyāḥ yadi ete bindu nāda vibhūṣitāḥ bījam dvitīyam bījeṣu mantrasya asya varānane dīrgha pūrvam turīyasya pañcamam śaktim ādiśet vāmadevaḥ nāma ṛṣiḥ paṅktiḥ chandaḥ udāhṛtam devatā śivaḥ eva aham mantrasya asya varānane gautamaḥ atriḥ varārohe viśvāmitraḥ tathā aṃgirāḥ bharadvājaḥ ca varṇānām kramaśas ca ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ gāyatrī anuṣṭubh triṣṭubh ca chandāṃsi bṛhatī virāj mama paṃca mukhāni āhuḥ sthāne teṣām varānane pūrva ādeḥ ca ūrddhva paryantam nakāra ādi yathākramam adāttaḥ prathamaḥ varṇaḥ caturthaḥ ca dvitīyakaḥ paṃcamaḥ svaritaḥ ca eva tṛtīyaḥ nihataḥ smṛtaḥ mūlavidyā śivam śaivam sūtram paṃcākṣaram tathā nāmāni asya vijānīyāt śaivam me hṛdayam mahat yakāraḥ phaṭ iti api ca varṇānām ante yadā tadā tatra api paṃcamaḥ varṇaḥ dvādaśa svara bhūṣitaḥ tāḥ asmāt anena mantreṇa manaḥ vāc kāya bhedataḥ āvayoḥ arcanam kuryyāt japa homa ādikam tathā yathāprajñam yathākālam yathāśāstram yathāmati yathāśakti yathāsaṃpad yathāyogam yathārati yadā kadāpi vā bhaktyā yatra kutra api vā kṛtā yena kena api vā devi pūjā muktim nayiṣyate mad priyam ca śivam ca eva krameṇa api akrameṇa vā tathā api mama bhaktāḥ ye na atyanta vivaśāḥ punar teṣām sarveṣu śāstreṣu mayā iva niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ tatra ādau saṃpravakṣyāmi mantra saṃgrahaṇam śubham yam vinā niṣphalam jāpyam yena vā saphalam bhavet iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe paṃcākṣaramāhātmyavarṇanam nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca ājñā hīnam kriyā hīnam śraddhā hīnam varānane ājñā artham dakṣiṇā hīnam sadā japtam ca niṣphalam ājñā siddham kriyā siddham śraddhā siddham mama ātmakam jāpitam sat guṇa upetam dhyāna yoga parāyaṇam ācāryam pūjayet vipraḥ sarvadā ati prayatnataḥ hasti aśva ratha ratnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca bhūṣaṇāni ca vāsāṃsi dhānyāni ca dhanāni ca vitta śāṭhyam na kurvīta yadi icchet siddhim ātmanaḥ ādadīta guroḥ mantram jñānam ca eva krameṇa tu evam tuṣṭaḥ guruḥ śiṣyam pūjakam vatsara uṣitam śuśrūṣum anahaṃkāram snātam śucim upoṣitam snāpayitvā viśuddhi artham pūrṇa kuṃbha ghṛtena vai alaṃkṛtya su veṣam ca gandha sraj vastra bhūṣaṇaiḥ puṇyāham vācayitvā ca brāhmaṇān abhipūjya ca samudra tīre nadyām ca goṣṭhe devālaye api vā anugṛhya tatas dadyāt jñānam mama yathāvidhi śivam ca astu śubham ca astu śobhanaḥ astu priyaḥ astu iti evam dadyāt guruḥ mantram ājñām ca eva tatas param evam labdhvā guroḥ mantram ājñām ca eva samāhitaḥ japet akṣara lakṣam vai catur guṇitam ādarāt nakta āśī saṃyamī yaḥ sa pauraścaraṇikaḥ smṛtaḥ yaḥ puraścaraṇam kṛtvā nitya jāpī bhavet punar snānam kṛtvā śucau deśe baddhvā rucira mānasam tvayā mām hṛdi saṃciṃtya saṃciṃtya sva gurum tatas udak mukhaḥ prāc mukhaḥ vā maunī ca ekāgra mānasaḥ viśodhya paṃcatattvāni dahana plāvana ādibhiḥ mantra nyāsa ādikam kṛtvā saphalīkṛta vigrahaḥ āvayoḥ vigrahau dhyāyan prāṇa apānau niyamya ca vidyā sthānam svakam rūpam ṛṣin chandaḥ adhidaivatam bījam śaktim tathā vākyam smṛtvā paṃcākṣarīm japet uttamam mānasam jāpyam upāṃśum ca eva madhyamam adhamam vācikam prāhuḥ āgama artha viśāradāḥ yat ucca nīca svaritaiḥ spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa pada akṣaraiḥ mantram uccārayet vācā vācikaḥ ayam japaḥ smṛtaḥ jihvā mātra parispandāt īṣat uccāritaḥ api vā aparaiḥ aśrutaḥ kiṃcid śrutaḥ vā upāṃśuḥ ucyate dhiyā yat akṣara śreṇyā varṇāt varṇam padāt padam śabda artha ciṃtanam bhūyas kathyate mānasaḥ japaḥ vācikaḥ tu ekaḥ eva syāt upāṃśuḥ śatam ucyate sāhasram mānasaḥ proktaḥ sagarbhaḥ tu śata adhikaḥ ādi antayoḥ agarbhaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ praśasyate catvāriṃśat samāvṛttīḥ prāṇān āyamya saṃsmaret mantram mantra artha vid dhīmān aśaktaḥ śaktitaḥ japet paṃcakam trikam ekam vā prāṇāyāmam samācaret eṣu paṃcavidheṣu ekaḥ karttavyaḥ śaktitaḥ japaḥ rekhayā aṣṭaguṇam vidyāt putrajīvaiḥ daśa adhikam śatam syāt śaṃkha maṇibhiḥ pravālaiḥ tu sahasrakam padmākṣaiḥ daśa lakṣam tu sauvarṇaiḥ koṭiḥ ucyate triṃśat akṣaiḥ kṛtā mālā dhana dā japa karmaṇi saptaviṃśati saṃkhyātaiḥ akṣaiḥ puṣṭi pradā bhavet paṃcaviṃśati saṃkhyātaiḥ kṛtā muktim prayacchati aṃguṣṭham mokṣa dam vidyāt tarjjanīm śatru nāśinīm madhyamām dhana dām śāntim karoti eṣā hi anāmikā aṣṭottaraśatam mālā tatra syāt uttamottamā śata saṃkhyā uttamā mālā paṃcāśadbhiḥ tu madhyamā catuḥ paṃcāśat akṣaiḥ tu hṛd śreṣṭhā hi prakīrtitā iti evam mālayā kuryāt japam kasmai na darśayet kaniṣṭhā kṣariṇī proktā japa karmaṇi śobhanā aṃguṣṭhena vinā japyam kṛtam tat aphalam yatas gṛhe japam samam vidyāt goṣṭhe śataguṇam viduḥ puṇya araṇye tathā ārāme sahasraguṇam ucyate ayutam parvate puṇye nadyām lakṣam udāhṛtam viprāṇām ca gavām ca eva sannidhau śasyate japaḥ tad pūrva abhimukham vaśyam dakṣiṇam ca ābhicārikam paścimam dhanadam vidyāt auttaram śātidam bhavet sūryya agni vipra devānām gurūṇām api sannidhau anyeṣām ca prasaktānām mantram na vimukhaḥ japet uṣṇīṣī kuṃcukī namraḥ mukta keśaḥ gala āvṛtaḥ krodham madam kṣutam trīṇi niṣṭhīvana vijṛṃbhaṇe darśanam ca śva nīcānām varjayet japa karmaṇi ācamet saṃbhave teṣām smaret vā mām tvayā saha jyotīṃṣi ca prapaśyet vā kuryāt vā prāṇasaṃyamam anāsanaḥ śayāne vā gacchan utthitaḥ eva vā yāna śayyā adhirūḍhaḥ vā ciṃtā vyākulitaḥ atha vā sat ācāraḥ japan śuddham dhyāyan bhadram samaśnute ācāraḥ paramaḥ dharmaḥ ācāraḥ paramam dhanam ācāraḥ paramā vidyā ācāraḥ paramā gatiḥ ācāra hīnaḥ puruṣaḥ loke bhavati ninditaḥ paratra ca sukhī na syāt tasmāt ācāravān bhavet tasya tena samācāraḥ sat ācāraḥ na ca itaraḥ sat ācārasya tasya āhuḥ āstikyam mūla kāraṇam āstikaḥ ced pramāda ādyaiḥ sat ācārāt avicyutaḥ na duṣyati naraḥ nityam tasmāt āstika tām vrajet yathā iha asti sukham duḥkham sukṛtaiḥ duṣkṛtaiḥ api na vācyam yasya kasya api nāstikasya atha vā paśoḥ paṃcākṣarāt param na asti paritrāṇam kalau yuge aśuceḥ vā śuceḥ vā api mantraḥ ayan na ca niṣphalaḥ anācāravatām puṃsām aviśuddha ṣaḍadhvanām an ādiṣṭaḥ api guruṇā mantraḥ ayam na ca niṣphalaḥ asādhitaḥ sādhitaḥ vā sidhya tvena na saṃśayaḥ tasmāt mantra antarān tyaktvā sa apāyā anadhikārataḥ āśramet paramām vidyām sākṣāt paṃcākṣarīm budhaḥ ye doṣāḥ sarva mantrāṇām na te asmin saṃbhavanti api sahasā viniyuṃjīta tasmāt eṣa mahā balaḥ evam sākṣāt mahādevyai mahādevena śūlinā jagatām uktaḥ pañcākṣara vidhiḥ yathā yaḥ idam kīrttayet bhaktyā śṛṇuyāt vā samāhitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṃḍe paṃcākṣaramahimavarṇanam nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca tad prayoga vidhānam ca sākṣāt śruti samam yathā idānīm śrotum icchāmi śiva saṃskāram uttamam saṃskāram paramam puṇyam śivena pati bhāṣitam samyak kṛta adhikāraḥ syāt pūjā ādiṣu naraḥ yatas dīyate yena vijñānam kṣīyate pāśa bandhanam tasmāt saṃskāraḥ eva ayam dīkṣā iti api ca kathyate śāṃbhavī ca eva śāktī ca māntrī ca eva śiva āgame dīkṣā upadiśyate tredhā śivena paramātmanā guroḥ āloka mātreṇa sparśāt saṃbhāṣaṇāt api sadyas saṃjñā bhavet jantoḥ pāśa upakṣaya kāriṇī sā dīkṣā śāṃbhavī proktā sā punar bhidyate dvidhā tīvrā tīvratarā ca iti pakṣaya bhedataḥ yayā syāt nirvṛtiḥ sadyas sā eva tīvratarā matā tīvrā tu jīvatā atyantam puṃsaḥ pāpa viśodhikā śaktī jñānavatī dīkṣā śiṣya deham praviśya tu guruṇā yoga mārgeṇa kriyate jñānacakṣuṣā māntrī kriyāvatī dīkṣā kuṃḍa maṃḍala pūrvikā manda mandatara uddeśāt kartavyā guruṇā bahis śaktipāta anusāreṇa śiṣyaḥ anugraham arhati śaiva dharma anusārasya tad mūla tvāt samāsatas tasmāt liṃgāni saṃvīkṣya śaktipātasya bhūyasaḥ jñānena kriyayā vā atha guruḥ śiṣyam viśodhayet tasmāt sarva prakāreṇa guruḥ śiṣyam parīkṣayet lakṣaṇam śaktipātasya prabodha ānanda saṃbhavaḥ sā yasmāt paramā śaktiḥ prabodha ānanda rūpiṇī ānanda bodhayoḥ liṃgam antaḥkaraṇa vikriyāḥ yathā syāt kaṃpa romāñca svara netra aṃga vikriyāḥ śiṣyaḥ api lakṣaṇaiḥ ebhiḥ kuryyāt guru parīkṣaṇam tad saṃparkaiḥ śiva arcā ādau saṃgataiḥ vā atha tad gataiḥ śiṣyaḥ tu śikṣaṇīya tvāt guroḥ gaurava kāraṇāt yaḥ guruḥ sa śivaḥ proktaḥ yaḥ śivaḥ sa guruḥ smṛtaḥ guruḥ vā śivaḥ eva atha vidyākāreṇa saṃsthitaḥ yathā śivaḥ tathā vidyā yathā vidyā tathā guruḥ śiva vidyā gurūṇām ca pūjayā sadṛśam phalam tasmāt sarva prayatnena yasya ājñām śirasā vahet śreyaḥ arthī yadi guru ājñām manasā api na laṃghayet guru ājñā pālakaḥ yasmāt jñāna saṃpattim aśnute samakṣam yadi kurvīta sarvam ca anujñayā guroḥ guroḥ gṛhe samakṣam vā na yathā iṣṭa āsanaḥ bhavet guruḥ devaḥ yatas sākṣāt tat gṛham deva mandiram pāpinām ca yathā saṃgāt tad pāpāt patitaḥ bhavet tathā pāpam vilīyeta hi ācāryasya samīpatas tathā ayam api santuṣṭaḥ guruḥ pāpam kṣaṇāt dahet manasā karmaṇā vācā guroḥ krodham na kārayet tasya krodhena dahyante hi āyuḥ śrī jñāna satkriyāḥ tad krodha kāriṇaḥ ye syuḥ teṣām yajñāḥ ca niṣphalāḥ yamaḥ ca niyamāḥ ca eva na atra kāryyā vicāraṇā manasā karmaṇā vācā gurum uddiśya yatnataḥ śreyaḥ arthī ced naraḥ dhīmān na mithyā ācāram ācaret guroḥ hitam priyam kuryāt ādiṣṭaḥ vā na vā sadā asamakṣam samakṣam vā tasya kāryam samācaret guru priya karaḥ śiṣyaḥ śaiva dharmān tatas arhati guruḥ ced guṇavān prājñaḥ parama ānanda bhāsakaḥ na punar nāma mātreṇa saṃvid ārahitaḥ tu yaḥ anyonyam tārayet naukā kim śilā tārayet śilām etasyāḥ nāma mātreṇa muktiḥ vai nāmamātrikā paśubhiḥ preritaḥ ca api paśu tvam na ativartate gurum tam eva vṛṇuyāt na aparam matimān naraḥ yāvat vijñāyate tāvat sevanīyaḥ mumukṣubhiḥ jñāte tasmin sthirā bhaktiḥ yāvat tattvam samāśrayet vatsarāt api śiṣyeṇa saḥ anyam gurum upāśrayet tatra ādau upasaṃgamya brāhmaṇam vedapāragam gurum ārādhayet prājñam śubhagam priya darśanam sarva abhaya pradātāram karuṇā ākrānta mānasam toṣayet tam prayatnena manasā karmaṇā girā tasmāt dhanāni ratnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca bhūṣaṇāni ca vāsāṃsi yāna śayyā āsanāni ca etāni gurave dadyāt bhaktyā vitta anusārataḥ vitta śāṭhyam na kurvīta yadi icchet paramām gatim nivedya paścāt sva ātmānam sa anvayam sa parigraham yadā śivāya sva ātmānam dattavān deśika ātmane guruḥ ca sva āśritam śiṣyam varṣam ekam parīkṣayet brāhmaṇam kṣatriyam vaiśyam dvi varṣam ca tri varṣakam prāṇa dravya pradāna ādyaiḥ ādeśaiḥ ca sama asamaiḥ uttamān ca adhame kṛtvā nīcān uttama karmaṇi ākruṣṭāḥ tāḍitāḥ vā api ye viṣādam na yānti api te yogyāḥ saṃyatāḥ śuddhāḥ śiva saṃskāra karmaṇi ṛjavaḥ mṛdavaḥ su acchāḥ vinītāḥ sthira cetasaḥ śauca ācāra samāyuktāḥ śiva bhaktāḥ dvijātayaḥ evam vṛtta samopetāḥ vā manaḥ kāya karmabhiḥ śodhyāḥ bodhyāḥ yathānyāyam iti śāstreṣu niścayaḥ na adhikāraḥ svatas nāryāḥ śiva saṃskāra karmaṇi tathā eva bhartṛ hīnāyāḥ putra ādeḥ abhyanujñayā adhikāraḥ bhavati eva kanyāyāḥ pituḥ ājñayā śūdrāṇām martya jātīnām patitānām viśeṣataḥ tathā saṃkara jātīnām na adhva śuddhiḥ vidhīyate pāda udaka pradāna ādyaiḥ kuryuḥ pāpa viśodhanam atra anuloma jātāḥ ye yuktāḥ eva dvijātiṣu teṣām adhva viśuddhi ādi kuryāt mātṛ kula ucitam yā tu kanyā sva pitṛ ādyaiḥ śiva dharme niyojitā sā bhaktāya pradātavyā na aparāya virodhine kṛtakṛtyā abhavat pūrvam tapasā ārādhya śaGkaram yathā nārāyaṇam devam tapasā ārādhya pāṃḍavān asvātantrya kṛtaḥ doṣaḥ na iha asti paramārthataḥ śiva dharme niyuktāyāḥ śiva śāsana gauravāt guroḥ ālokanāt eva sparśāt saṃbhāṣaṇāt api yasya saṃjāyate prajñā tasya na asti parājayaḥ kriyāvān yaḥ tu saṃskāraḥ kuṃḍa maṃḍapa pūrvakaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe dīkṣāvidhāne gurumāhātmyam nāma pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ deśikaḥ prathamam kuryāt saṃskāram samaya āhvayam parīkṣya bhūmim vidhivat gandha varṇa rasa ādibhiḥ śilpi śāstra ukta mārgeṇa maṇḍapam tatra kalpayet kṛtvā vedim ca tad madhye kuṇḍāni parikalpayet aṣṭa dikṣu tathā dikṣu tatra aiśānyām punar kramāt pradhāna kuṃḍam kurvīta yat vā paścima bhāgataḥ pradhānam ekam eva atha kṛtvā śobhām prakalpayet vitāna dhvaja mālābhiḥ vividhābhiḥ anekaśas vedi madhye tatas kuryāt maṃḍalam śubha lakṣaṇam rakta hema ādibhiḥ cūrṇaiḥ īśvara āvāhana ucitam sindūra śālinī vāra cūrṇaiḥ eva atha nirddhanaḥ eka hastam dvi hastam vā sitam vā raktam eva vā eka hastasya padmasya karṇikā aṣṭa aṃgulā matā kesarāṇi tad arddhāni śeṣam ca aṣṭadala ādikam kṛtvā śobhā upaśobhā āḍhyam aiśānyām tasya kalpayet vrīhi tandula siddhārtha tila puṣpa kuśa āstṛte tatra lakṣaṇa saṃyuktam śiva kuṃbham prasādhayet sauvarṇam rājatam vā api tāmra jam mṛd mayam tu vā gandha puṣpa akṣata ākīrṇam kuśa dūrvā aṃkura ācitam sita sūtra āvṛtam kaṃṭhe nava vastra yuga āvṛtam śuddha ambu pūrṇam utkūrcam sa dravyam sa pidhānakam bhṛGgāram vardhanīm ca api śaṃkham ca cakram eva vā vinā sūtra ādikam sarvam padma patram atha api vā maṇḍalasya tatas prācyām mantra kuṃbhe ca pūrvavat kṛtvā vidhivat īśasya mahā pūjām samācaret atha arṇavasya tīre vā nadyām goṣṭhe api vā girau kṛtvā pūrva uditam sarvam vinā vā maṃḍapa ādikam maṃḍalam pūrvavat kṛtvā sthaṃḍilam ca vibhāvasoḥ praviśya pūjā bhavanam prahṛṣṭa vadanaḥ guruḥ mahā pūjām maheśasya kṛtvā maṇḍala madhyatas śiva kuṃbhe tathā bhūyas śivam āvāhya pūjayet paścima abhimukham dhyātvā yajñarakṣakam īśvaram kṛtvā mudrā ādikam sarvam mantra yāgam samācaret tatas śiva anale homam kuryāt deśika sattamaḥ pradhānakuṇḍe paritas juhuyuḥ ca apare dvijāḥ ācāryāt pādam arddham vā homaḥ teṣām vidhīyate pradhānakuṇḍe eva atha juhuyāt deśika uttamaḥ japam ca vidhivat ca anye śiva bhakti parāyaṇāḥ nṛtyam gītam ca vādyam ca maṃgalāni aparāṇi ca pūjanam ca sadasyānām kṛtvā samyak vidhānataḥ puṇyāham kārayitvā atha punar saṃpūjya śaṃkaram prārthayet deśikaḥ devam śiṣya anugraha kāmyayā vimocaya enam viśveśa ghṛṇayā ca ghṛṇā nidhe atha ca evam karomi iti labdha anujñaḥ tu deśikaḥ ānīya upoṣitam śiṣyam haviṣya āśinam eva vā eka aśanam vā viratam snātam prātar kṛta kriyam japantam praṇavam devam dhyāyantam kṛta maṃgalam dvārasya paścimasya agra maṇḍale dakṣiṇasya vā darbha āsane samāsīnam vidhāya uda mukham śiśum svayam prāc vadanaḥ tiṣṭhan ūrdhva kāyam kṛta aṃjalim puṣpa kṣepeṇa santāḍya badhnīyāt locanam guruḥ tatas praveśayet śiṣyam guruḥ dvāreṇa maṃḍalam saḥ api tena īritaḥ śaṃbhoḥ ācaret tris pradakṣiṇam tatas suvarṇa saṃmiśram dattvā puṣpa aṃjalim prabhoḥ prāñc mukhaḥ ca udañc mukhaḥ vā praṇamet daṇḍa vat kṣitaḥ sa dṛṣṭvā maṃḍalam bhūyas praṇamet sa añjaliḥ prabhum atha āsīnam śiva ācāryaḥ maṃḍalasya tu dakṣiṇe upaveśya ātmanaḥ savye śiṣyam darbha āsane guruḥ ārādhya ca mahādevam śiva hastam pravinyaset śiva tejaḥ mayam pāṇim śiva mantram udīrayet sarva aṃga ālaṃbanam ca eva kuryāt tena eva deśikaḥ śiṣyaḥ praṇamet bhūmau deśikā kṛtam īśvaram huta āhuti trayam śiṣyam upaveśya yathā purā darbha agraiḥ saṃspṛśan tam ca vidyayā ātmānam āviśet namaskṛtya mahādevam nāḍīsaṃdhānam ācaret śiva śāstra ukta mārgeṇa kṛtvā prāṇasya nirgamam śiṣya deha praveśam ca smṛtvā mantrān tu tarpayet deyāḥ tisraḥ tathā aṃgānām aṃgaiḥ eva yathākramam tatas pūrṇāhutim dattvā prāyaścittāya deśikaḥ punar saṃpūjya deveśam samyak ācamya deśikaḥ hutvā ca eva yathānyāyam sva jātyā vaiśyam uddharet tasya evam janayet kṣātram uddhāram ca tatas punar rājanyam ca evam uddhṛtya kṛtvā vipram punar tayoḥ prokṣaṇam tāḍanam kṛtvā śiśoḥ sva ātmānam ātmani nāḍyā yathā uktayā vāyum recayet mantratas guruḥ nirgamya praviśet nāḍyā śiṣyasya hṛdayam tathā tam ādāya tayā nāḍyā mantrī saṃhāra mudrayā na pūrakeṇa niveśya enam ekībhāva artham ātmanaḥ kuṃbhakena tathā nāḍyā recakena yathā purā tasmāt ādāya śiṣyasya hṛdaye tat niveśayet hutvā paścāt dadyāt pūrṇāhutim tatas devasya dakṣiṇe śiṣyam upaveśya varāsane svastika āsanam ārūḍham vidhāya svayam samādāya ghaṭam pūrṇam pūrṇam eva prasāditam dhyāyamānaḥ śivam śiṣyam ābhiṣiṃceta deśikaḥ athā apanudya snāna aṃbu paridhāya sita aṃbaram ācānta ulaṃkṛtaḥ śiṣyaḥ prāṃjaliḥ maṃḍapam vrajet upaveśya yathāpūrvam tam guruḥ darbha viṣṭare saṃpūjya maṃḍalam devam kara nyāsam samācaret samālabheta pāṇibhyām śiśum śivam udīrayet sakalīkaraṇam kṛtvā mātṛkā nyāsa vartmanā tatas śiva āsanam dhyātvā śiṣya mūrddhni deśikaḥ tatra āvāhya yathānyāyam arcayet manasā śivam iti vijñāpya tam śaṃbhoḥ tejasā bhāsuram smaret saṃpūjya atha śivam śaivīm ājñām prāpya śiva ātmikām karṇe śiṣyasya śanakais śiva mantram udīrayet sa tu baddhāṃjaliḥ śrutvā mantram tad gata mānasaḥ śanais tam vyāharet śiṣya śiva ācāryasya śāsanāt tatas śāktam ca saṃdiśya mantram mantra vicakṣaṇaḥ uccārayitvā ca sukham tasmai maṃgalam ādiśet tatas samāsāt mantra artham vācya vācaka yogataḥ samadiśya īśvaram rūpam yogam āsanam ādiśet atha guru ājñayā śiṣyaḥ śiva agni guru sannidhau bhaktyā evam abhisaṃdhāya dīkṣā vākyam udīrayet varam prāṇa parityāgaḥ chedanam śirasaḥ api vā tāvat ārādhayet devam tad niṣṭhaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ tatas sa samayaḥ nāma bhaviṣyati śiva āśrame labdha adhikāraḥ guru ājñā pālakaḥ tad vaśaḥ bhavet dadyāt śiṣyāya mūlena rudrākṣam ca abhimantritam pratimā vā api devasya gūḍha deham atha api vā pūjā homa japa dhyāna sādhanāni ca saṃbhave saḥ api śiṣyaḥ śiva ācāryāt labdhāni bahu mānataḥ ādadīta ājñayā tasya deśikasya na ca anyathā ācāryāt āptam akhilam śirasi ādhāya bhaktitaḥ rakṣayet pūjayet śaṃbhum maṭhe vā gṛhe eva vā atas param śiva ācāram ādiśet asya deśikaḥ bhakti śraddhā anusāreṇa prajñāyāḥ ca anusārataḥ yat uktam yat samājñātam yat ca eva anyat prakīrtitam śiva ācāryeṇa samaye tat sarvam śirasā vahet śiva āgamasya grahaṇam vācanam śravaṇam tathā deśika deśataḥ kuryāt na sva icchātaḥ na ca anyatas iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ saṃskāraḥ samaya āhvayaḥ sākṣāt śiva pura prāptau nṛṇām parama sādhanam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṃḍe śiṣyasaṃskāravarṇanam nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atas param samāvekṣya guruḥ śiṣyasya yogyatām kalām tattvam ca bhuvanam varṇam padam atas param mantraḥ ca iti samāsena ṣaḍadhvā paripaṭhyate nivṛttya ādyāḥ kalāḥ paṃca kalādhvā kathyate budhaiḥ vyāptāḥ kalābhiḥ itare tu adhvānaḥ paṃca paṃcabhiḥ śivatattva ādi bhūmi antam tattvādhvā samudāhṛtaḥ ṣaḍviṃśat saṃkhyayā upetaḥ śuddha aśuddha ubhaya ātmakaḥ ādhāra ādi unmanā antaḥ ca bhuvanādhvā prakīrtitaḥ vinā bheda upabhedābhyām ṣaṣṭi saṃkhyā samanvitaḥ paṃcāśat rudra rūpāḥ tu varṇāḥ varṇa adhva saṃjñitāḥ aneka bheda saṃpannaḥ padādhvā samudāhṛtaḥ yathā śivaḥ na tattveṣu gaṇyate tattva nāyakaḥ kalā adhvanaḥ vyāpaka tvam vyāpya tvam ca itara adhvanām vyāpya vyāpaka tā tena jñātum eva na śakyate tasmāt adhva svarūpam ca vyāpya vyāpaka tām tathā kuṃḍa maṃḍala paryantam tatra kṛtvā yathā purā dvi hasta mānam kurvīta prācyām kalaśa maṃḍalam tatas snātaḥ śiva ācāryaḥ sa śiṣyaḥ kṛta naityakaḥ praviśya maṃḍalam śaṃbhoḥ pūjām pūrvavat ācaret tatra āḍhaka avaraiḥ siddham tandulaiḥ pāyasam prabhoḥ puratas kalpite vā atha maṃḍale varṇi maṃḍite sthāpayet paṃca kalaśān dikṣu madhye ca deśikaḥ teṣu brahmāṇi mūla arṇaiḥ bindu nāda samanvitaiḥ īśānam madhyame kuṃbhe puruṣam puratas sthite aghoram dakṣiṇe vāme vāmam sadyam ca paścime rakṣām vidhāya mudrā ca baddhvā kuṃbha abhimantraṇam kṛtvā śiva analaiḥ homam prārabhet yathā purā yad arddham pāyasam pūrvam homa artham parikalpitam tarpaṇa antam ca mantrāṇām kṛtvā karma yathā purā hutvā pūrṇāhutim teṣām tatas kuryyāt pradīpanam okārāt anu huṃkāram tatas mūlam phaṭ antakam svāhā antam dīpane prāhuḥ aṃgāni ca yathākramam teṣām āhutayaḥ tisraḥ deyāḥ dīpana karmaṇi triguṇam triguṇī kṛtya dvija kanyā kṛtam sitam sūtram sūtreṇa saṃmantrya śikhā agre bandhayet śiśoḥ caraṇa aṃguṣṭha paryyantam ūrddhvakāyasya tiṣṭhataḥ laṃbayitvā tu tat sūtram suṣumṇām tatra yojayet śāntayā mudrayā ādāya mūlamantreṇa mantra vid hṛdi santāḍya śiṣyasya puṣpa kṣepeṇa pūrvavat caitanyam samupādāya dvādaśānte nivedya ca sūtram sūtreṇa saṃyojya saṃrakṣya astreṇa varmaṇā avaguṃṭhya atha tat sūtram śiṣya deham viciṃtayet mūla traya mayam pāśam bhoga bhogya tva lakṣaṇam vyoma ādi bhūta rūpiṇyaḥ śānti atīta ādayaḥ kalāḥ athavā bīja bhūtaiḥ tat kṛtvā pūrva uditam kramāt kalā vyāptim mala ādau ca hutvā saṃdīpayet kalāḥ śiṣyam śirasi santāḍya sūtram dehe yathākramam śānti atīta pade sūtram lāñchayet mantram uccaran evam kṛtvā nivṛtti antam śānti atītam anukramāt hutvā āhuti trayam paścāt maṇḍale ca śivam yajet devasya dakṣiṇe śiṣyam upaveśya uttarā mukham sa darbhe maṇḍale dadyāt homa śiṣṭam carum guruḥ śiṣyaḥ tad guruṇā dattam satkṛtya śiva pūrvakam apare maṇḍale dadyāt paṃcagavyam tathā guruḥ tṛtīye maṇḍale śiṣyam upaveśya yathā purā pradadyāt dantapavanam yathā śāstra ukta lakṣaṇam agreṇa tasya mṛdunā prāc mukhaḥ vā api uda mukhaḥ vācam niyamya ca āsīnaḥ śiṣyaḥ dantān viśodhayet praviśet deśika ādiṣṭaḥ prāṃjaliḥ śiva maṇḍalam tyaktam tat dantapavanam dṛśyate guruṇā yadi aśasta āśā mukhe tasmin guruḥ tad doṣa śāntaye śatam arddham tad arddham vā ājuhuyāt mūlamantrataḥ tatas śiṣyam samālabhya japitvā karṇayoḥ śivam devasya dakṣiṇe bhāge tam śiṣyam adhivāsayet ahata āstaraṇa āstīrṇe sa darbha śayane śuciḥ mantrite antar śivam dhyāyan śayīta prāc śirāḥ niśi śikhāyām baddha sūtrasya śikhayā tad śikhām guruḥ ābadhya ahata vastreṇa tam ācchādya ca varmaṇā kṛtvā astra japtaiḥ tad vāhye digīśānām balim haret iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivadīkṣāvidhānavarṇanam nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatas snāna ādikam sarvam samāpya ācārya coditaḥ gacchet baddhāṃjaliḥ dhyāyan śiva maṇḍala pārśvatas atha pūjām vinā sarvam kṛtvā pūrva dine yathā baddha netreṇa śiṣyeṇa puṣpa avakiraṇe kṛte yatra āpatanti puṣṇāṇi tasya nāmā saṃdiśet tam ca upanīya nirmālya maṇḍale asmin yathā purā pūjayet devam īśānam juhuyāt ca śiva anale śiṣyeṇa yadi duḥsvapnaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tad doṣa śāntaye śatam arddham tad arddham vā juhuyāt mūlavidyayā tatas sūtram śikhā baddham laṃbayitvā yathā purā ādhāra pūjā prabhṛti yat nivṛtti kalā āśrayam vāgīśvarī pūjana antam kuryāt homa purassaram atha praṇamya vāgīśam nivṛtteḥ vyāpikām satīm prāpayet ca śiśoḥ prāptim yugapad sarva yoniṣu sūtra dehe atha śiṣyasya tāḍana prokṣaṇa ādikam kṛtvā ātmānam samādāya dvādaśānte nivedya ca tatas api ādāya mūlena mudrayā śāstra dṛṣṭayā devānām jātayaḥ ca aṣṭau tiraścām paṃca jātayaḥ jātyā ekayā ca mānuṣyāḥ yonayaḥ ca caturdaśa tāsu sarvāsu yugapad praveśāya śiśoḥ ddhiyā vāgīśānyām yathānyāyam śiṣya ātmānam niveśayet ārjavam bhoga niṣpattiḥ kuryāt prītim parām tathā niṣkṛti artham ca jāti āyuḥ bhoga saṃskāra siddhaye bhoktṛ tva viṣaya asaṃga malam tat kāya śodhanam kṛtvā evam eva śiṣyasya chindyāt pāśa trayam tatas hutvā pūrṇāhutim vahnau brahmāṇam pūjayet tatas hutvā āhuti trayam tasmai śiva ājñām bāla arka sadṛśa ākārām bhāsayantīm diśaḥ daśa tatas śeṣam yathāpūrvam kṛtvā devam maheśvaram āvāhya ārādhya hutvā asmai śiva ājñām manasā diśet maheśvaram tathā utsṛjya kṛtvā anyām ca kalām imām meḍhra ūru jānuṣu jaṃghā sphic kaṭi pārśveṣu vāmadevasya bhāvayet aṣṭatriṃśat kalā nyāsam evam kṛtvā anupūrvaśas paścāt praṇava vid dhīmān praṇava nyāsam ācaret pārśva udara ūru jaṃgheṣu pādayoḥ pṛṣṭhatas tathā ittham praṇava vinyāsam kṛtvā nyāsa vicakṣaṇaḥ haṃsa nyāsam prakurvīta śivaśāstre yathā uditam vibhajya bāhu netra āsya lalāṭe ghrāṇayoḥ api kaṭhyoḥ pāṇyoḥ gulphayoḥ ca yat vā paṃcāṃga vartmanā haṃsa nyāsam imam kṛtvā nyaset pañcākṣarīm tatas yathā pūrva ukta mārgeṇa śiva tvam yena jāyate na aśivaḥ śivam abhyasyet na aśivaḥ śivam arcayet na aśivaḥ tu śivam dhyāyet na aśivam prāpnuyāt śivam tasmāt śaivīm tanum kṛtvā tyaktvā ca paśu bhāvanām dhyāna yajñaḥ jñāna yajñaḥ pañca yajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥ karma yajña ratāḥ kecid tapaḥ yajña ratāḥ pare japa yajña ratāḥ ca anye dhyāna yajña ratāḥ tathā jñāna yajña ratāḥ ca anye viśiṣṭāḥ ca uttarottaram krama yajñaḥ dvidhā proktaḥ kāma a kāma vibhedataḥ kāmān kāmī tatas bhuktvā kāma āsaktaḥ punar bhavet tapaḥ yajña rataḥ bhūtvā jāyate na atra saṃśayaḥ japa dhyāna rataḥ bhūtvā jāyate bhuvi mānavaḥ jñānam labdhvā acirāt eva śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt tasmāt muktaḥ śiva ājñaptaḥ karma yajñaḥ api dehinām akāmaḥ kāma saṃyuktaḥ bandhāya eva bhaviṣyati tasmāt pañcasu yajñeṣu dhyāna jñāna paraḥ bhavet dhyānam jñānam ca yasya asti tīrṇaḥ tena bhava arṇavaḥ hiṃsā ādi doṣa nirmuktaḥ viśuddhaḥ citta sādhanaḥ bahis karmakarāḥ yadvat na atīva phala bhāginaḥ dṛṣṭvā narendra bhavane tadvat atrā api karmiṇaḥ dhyāninām hi vapuḥ sūkṣmam bhavet pratyakṣam aiśvaram yathā iha karmaṇām sthūlam mṛd kāṣṭha ādyaiḥ prakalpitam dhyāna yajña ratāḥ tasmāt devān pāṣāṇa mṛṇmayān ātma stham yaḥ śivam tyaktvā bahis abhyarcayet naraḥ jñānāt dhyānam bhavet dhyānāt jñānam bhūyas pravartate dvādaśānte tathā mūrdhni lalāṭe bhrū yuga antare nāsā agre vā tathā āsye vā kandhare hṛdaye tathā nābhau vā śāśvata sthāne śraddhā viddhena cetasā bahis yāga upacāreṇa devam devīm ca pūjayet athavā pūjayet nityam liṃge vā kṛtake api vā vahnau vā sthaṇḍile vā atha bhaktyā vitta anusārataḥ antaryāga rataḥ pūjām bahis kurvīta vā na vā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivaśāstroktanityanaimittikakarmavarṇanam nāma dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyākhyām pūjā vidhānasya pravadāmi samāsatas śivaśāstre śivena eva śivāyai kathitasya tu aṃgam abhyantaram yāgam agni kārya avasānakam vidhāya vā na vā paścāt bahis yāgam samācaret dhyātvā vināyakam devam pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ dakṣiṇe ca uttare ca eva nandīśam suyaśam tathā ārādhya manasā samyak āsanam kalpayet budhaḥ ārādhana ādikaiḥ yuktaḥ siṃha yoga āsana ādikam sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannam sarva avayava śobhanam sarva atiśaya saṃyuktam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam rakta āsya pāṇi caraṇam kunda candra smita ānanam vara da abhaya hastam ca mṛga ṭaṃka dharam haram bhujaṃga hāra valayam cāru nīla gala antaram tatas saṃcintayet tasya vāma bhāge maheśvarīm praphulla utpala patra ābhām vistīrṇa āyata locanām pūrṇa candra ābha vadanām nīla kuṃcita mūrdhajām nīlotpala dala prakhyām candra arddha kṛta śekharām tanu madhyām pṛthu śroṇīm pīta sūkṣma vara ambarām sarva ābharaṇa saṃpannām lalāṭa tilaka ujjvalām vicitra puṣpa saṃkīrṇa keśapāśa upaśobhitām sarvatas anuguṇa ākārām kiṃcid lajjā nata ānanām hema aravindam vilasat dadhānām dakṣiṇe kare daṃḍa vat ca aparam haste nyasya āsīnām mahā āsane pāśa vicchedikām sākṣāt saccidānanda rūpiṇīm evam devam ca devīm ca dhyātvā āsana vare śubhe śaivīm sadāśiva ākhyām vā tathā māheśvarīm parām ṣaḍviṃśaka abhidhānām vā śrīkaṃṭha ākhyām atha api vā mantra nyāsa ādikām ca api kṛtvā svasyām tanau yathā asyām mūrtau mūrtimantam śivam sat asataḥ param dhyātvā bāhya krameṇa eva pūjām nirvarttayet dhiyā samidh ājya ādibhiḥ paścāt nābhau homam ca bhāvayet bhrū madhye ca śivam dhyāyet śuddha dīpa śikhā ākṛtim atha ciṃtā mayam sarvam samāpya ārādhana kramam liṃge ca pūjayet devam sthaṃḍile vā anale api vā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe pūjāvidhānavyākhyānavarṇanam nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ prokṣayet mūlamantreṇa pūjā sthānam viśuddhaye astreṇa utsārya vai vighnān avaguṇṭhya ca varmaṇā tatra darbhān paristīrya kṣālayet prokṣaṇa ādibhiḥ saṃśodhya sarva pātrāṇi dravya śuddhim samācaret prokṣaṇīm ardhya pātram ca pādya pātram atas param tathā eva ācamanīyasya pātram ca iti catuṣṭayam prakṣālya prokṣya vīkṣya atha kṣipet teṣu jalam śivam puṇya dravyāṇi sarvāṇi yathālābham vinikṣipet ratnāni rajatam hema gandha puṣpa akṣata ādayaḥ phala pallava darbhān ca puṇya dravyāṇi anekadhā snāna udake sugandha ādi pānīye ca viśeṣataḥ śītalāni kusuma ādīni nikṣipet jāti kaṃkola karpūra bahumūla tamālakān kṣipet ācamanīye ca cūrṇayitvā viśeṣataḥ elām pātreṣu sarveṣu karpūram candanam tathā kuśa agrāṇi akṣatān ca eva yava vrīhi tilān api ājya siddhārtha puṣpāṇi bhasitam ca arghya pātrake kuśa puṣpa yava vrīhi bahu mūla tamālakān prakṣipet prokṣaṇī pātre bhasitam ca yathākramam sarvatra mantram vinyasya varmaṇā āveṣṭya bāhyatas paścāt astreṇa saṃrakṣya dhenumudrām pradarśayet pūjā dravyāṇi sarvāṇi prokṣaṇī pātra vāriṇā pātrāṇām prokṣaṇīm ekām alābhe sarva karmasu tatas vināyakam devam bhakṣya bhojya ādibhiḥ kramāt pūjayitvā vidhānena dvāra pārśve atha dakṣiṇe antaḥpura adhipam sākṣāt nandinam samyak arcayet cāmīkara acala prakhyam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam dīpta śūla mṛgī ṭaṃka tigma vetra dharam prabhum uttare dvāra pārśvasya bhāryyām ca marutām sutām suyaśām suvratām ambām pāda maṇḍana tatparām pūjayitvā praviśya antar bhavanam parameṣṭhinaḥ aiśānyām caṇḍam ārādhya nirmālyam tasya dāpayet kalpayet āsanam paścāt ādhāra ādi yathākramam ādhāra śaktim kalyāṇīm śyāmām dhyāyet adhas bhuvi tasyāḥ purastāt utkaṃṭham anantam kuṇḍala ākṛtim dhavalam paṃca phaṇinam lelihānam iva ambaram tasya upari āsanam bhadram kaṇṭhī rava catuṣpadam dharmaḥ jñānam ca vairāgyam aiśvaryam ca padāni vai āgneya ādi śveta rakta pīta śyāmāni varṇataḥ adharma ādīni pūrva ādīni uttara antāni anukramāt rājāvarta maṇi prakhyān nyasya gātrāṇi bhāvayet aṣṭa patrāṇi tasya āhuḥ aṇima ādi guṇa aṣṭakam kesarāṇi ca vāma ādyāḥ rudra vāma ādi śaktibhiḥ bījāni api ca tāḥ eva kandaḥ ca śiva dharma ātmā karṇikā ante tri maṇḍale sarva āsana upari sukham vicitra āstaraṇa āstṛtam āvāhanam sthāpanam ca sannirodham nirīkṣaṇam namaskāram ca kurvīta badhvāḥ mudrāḥ pṛthak pṛthak pādyam ācamanam ca arghyam gandham puṣpam tatas param dhūpam dīpam ca tāṃbūlam dattvā atha svāpayet śivau sakalīkṛtya mūlena brahma ābhiḥ ca aparaiḥ tathā āvāhayet tatas devyā śivam parama kāraṇam śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśam devam niścalam akṣaram kāraṇam sarva lokānām sarva loka mayam param bhaktānām aprayatnena dṛśyam īśvaram avyayam ādi madhya anta rahitam bheṣajam bhava rogiṇām liṃga mūrttiḥ maheśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ snāna kāle prakurvīta jaya śabda ādi maṃgalam pañcagavya ghṛta kṣīra dadhi madhu ādi pūrvakaiḥ mūlaiḥ phalānām sāraiḥ ca tila sarṣapa saktubhiḥ bījaiḥ yava ādibhiḥ śastaiḥ cūrṇaiḥ māṣa ādi saṃbhavaiḥ saṃsnāpya ālipya piṣṭa ādyaiḥ snāpayet uṣṇa vāribhiḥ tatas saṃśodhya salilaiḥ liṃgam beram atha api vā asaṃbhave tu dravyāṇām yathā saṃbhava saṃbhṛtaiḥ kalaśena atha śaṃkhena varddhanyā pāṇinā tathā liṃga sūkta ādi sūktaiḥ ca śirasā ātharvaṇena ca ṛgbhiḥ ca sāmabhiḥ śaivaiḥ brahmabhiḥ ca api paṃcabhiḥ yathā devasya devyāḥ ca kuryāt snāna ādikam tathā na tu kaścid viśeṣaḥ asti tatra tau sadṛśau yatas prathamam devam uddiśya kṛtvā snāna ādikāḥ kriyāḥ devyaiḥ praścāt prakurvīta devadevasya śāsanāt tatra tatra upacārāṇām liṃge vā anyatra vā kvacid kṛtvā abhiṣekam liṃgasya śucinā ca sugandhinā saṃmṛjya vāsasā dadyāt aṃbaram ca upavītakam pādyam ācamanam ca arghyam gandham puṣpam ca bhūṣaṇam dhūpam dīpam ca naivedyam pānīyam mukha śodhanam punar ca ācamanīyam ca mukha vāsam tatas param mukuṭam ca śubham bhadram sarva ratnaiḥ alaṃkṛtam bhūṣaṇāni pavitrāṇi mālyāni vividhāni ca vyajane cāmare chatram tālavṛṃtam ca darpaṇam dattvā nīrājanam kuryāt sarva maṃgala nisvanaiḥ gīta nṛtya ādibhiḥ ca eva jaya śabda samanvitaḥ haime ca rājate tāmre pātre vā mṛd maye śubhe padmakaiḥ śobhitaiḥ puṣpaiḥ bījaiḥ dadhi akṣata ādibhiḥ triśūla śaṃkha yugma abja nandyāvartaiḥ karīṣa jaiḥ aṣṭau pradīpān paritas vidhāya ekam tu madhyame teṣu vāmā ādikāḥ cintyāḥ pūjyāḥ ca nava śaktayaḥ kavacena samācchādya saṃrakṣya astreṇa sarvatas dhenumudrām ca saṃdarśya pāṇibhyām pātram uddharet athavā āropayet pātre paṃca dīpān yathākramam tris pradakṣiṇa yogena bhrāmayet mūlavidyayā kṛtvā puṣpa aṃjalim paścāt upahārān nivedayet pānīyam ca tatas dadyāt dattvā vā ācamanam punar prokṣayet prokṣaṇīyāni gāna nāṭyāni kārayet liṃga ādau śivayoḥ cintām kṛtvā śakti ajapet śivam pradakṣiṇam praṇāmam ca stavam ca ātma samarpaṇam vijñāpanam ca kāryāṇām kuryāt vinaya pūrvakam arghyam puṣpa aṃjalim dattvā baddhvā mudrām yathāvidhi paścāt kṣamāpayet devam udvāsya ātmani ciṃtayet pādya ādi mukha vāsa antam arghya ādyam ca ati saṃkaṭe puṣpa vikṣepa mātram vā kuryāt bhāva purassaram a saṃpūjya na bhuñjīta śivam ā prāṇasaṃcarāt yadi pāpaḥ tu bhuṃjīta svairam na niṣkṛtiḥ paredyus śaktitas dattvā suvarṇa ādyam śivāya ca śiva bhaktāya vā kṛtvā mahā pūjām śuciḥ bhavet iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śāstroktaśivapūjanavarṇanam nāma caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ an uktam ca atra pūjāyāḥ kamala upabhayāt iva haviḥ nivedanāt pūrvam dīpa dānāt anantaram kuryāt āvaraṇa abhyarcām prāpte nīrājane atha vā tatra īśāna ādi sadya antam rudra ādi astra antam eva ca śivasya vā śivāyāḥ ca prathama āvaraṇe japet aiśānyām pūrva bhāge ca dakṣiṇe ca uttare tathā paścime ca tathā āgneyyām aiśānyām nairṛte tathā vāyavyām punar aiśānyām catur dikṣu tatas param garbhāvaraṇam ākhyātam mantra saṃghātam eva vā tad bahis pūrvatas śakram yamam dakṣiṇatas yajet varuṇam vāruṇe bhāge dhanadam ca uttare budhaḥ īśa maiśe analam svīye nairṛte nirṛtim yajet mārute mārutam viṣṇum nairṛte vidhim aiśvare bahis padmasya vajra ādyāni abja antāni āyudhāni api prasiddha rūpāṇi āśāsu lokeśānām kramāt yajet devam devīm ca saṃprekṣya sarva āvaraṇa devatāḥ baddha aṃjali puṭāḥ dhyeyāḥ samāsīnāḥ yathāsukham sarva āvaraṇa devānām sva abhidhānaiḥ namaḥ yutaiḥ puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjanam kuryāt natvā sarvān yathākramam garbha āvaraṇam eva api yajet sva āvaraṇena vā haviḥ ca ṣaḍvidham deyam śuddham mudga annam eva ca pāyasam dadhi saṃmiśram gauḍam ca madhunā āplutam eteṣu ekam anekam vā nānā vyaṃjana saṃyutam bhakṣyāṇi apūpa mukhyāni svādumanti phalāni ca raktacandana puṣpa āḍhyam pānīyam ca ati śītalam mṛdu elā rasa aktam ca khaṇḍam pūga phalasya ca dalāni nāgavallyāḥ ca yuktāni khadira ādibhiḥ gaurāṇi svarṇa varṇāni vihitāni śivāni ca śailam eva sitam cūrṇam na ati rūkṣam na dūṣitam karpūram ca atha kaṃkolam jāti ādi ca navam śubham ālepanam candanam syāt mūlakāṣṭham rajomayam kastūrikā kuṃkumam ca rasaḥ mṛgamada ātmakaḥ puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi eva pavitrāṇi śubhāni ca nirgandhāni ugra gandhāni dūṣitāni uṣitāni ca svayam eva viśīrṇāni na deyāni śiva arcane vāsāṃsi ca mṛdūni eva tapanīya mayāni ca vidyut valaya kalpāni bhūṣaṇāni viśeṣataḥ sarvāṇi etāni karpūra niryāsa aguru candanaiḥ ādhūpitāni puṣpa oghaiḥ vāsitāni samantataḥ candana aguru karpūra kāṣṭha guggulu cūrṇikaiḥ nityam pradīpitāḥ dīpāḥ śastāḥ karpūra saṃyutāḥ kapilā sambhavam śambhoḥ iṣṭam snāne ca pānake suvarṇa ratna yuktāni citrāṇi āstaraṇāni ca mṛdu upadhāna yuktāni sūkṣma tūla mayāni ca uccāvacāni ramyāṇi śayanāni sukhāni ca nadyaḥ samudra gāminyāḥ naṭāt vā ambhaḥ samāhṛtam śītam ca vastra pūtam tat viśiṣṭam snāna pānayoḥ chatram śaśi nibham cāru muktā dāma virājitam cāmare ca site sūkṣme cāmīkara pariṣkṛte rājahaṃsa dvaya ākāre ratna daṃḍa upaśobhite samantāt ratna sañchannam sraj vairaiḥ ca api bhūṣitam āsva pṛṣṭha ādi deśeṣu ratna cāmīkara ācitaḥ kāhalāni ca ramyāṇi nānā nāda karāṇi ca suvarṇa nirmitāni eva mauktika alaṃkṛtāni ca bherī mṛdaṃga muraja timiccha paṭaha ādayaḥ samudra kalpa san nādāḥ kalpanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ bhāṃḍāni api ca ramyāṇi patrāṇi api ca kṛtsnaśas tad ādhārāṇi sarvāṇi sauvarṇāni eva sādhayet ālayam ca maheśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ rāja āvasatha vat kalpyam śilpa śāstra ukta lakṣaṇam ucca prākāra saṃbhinnam bhūdhara ākāra gopuram tapta jāṃbūnada mayam ratna stambha śata āvṛtam muktā dāma vitāna āḍhyam vidruma dvāra toraṇam cāmīkara mayaiḥ divyaiḥ mukuṭaiḥ kumbha lakṣaṇaiḥ rājanya arha nivāsaiḥ ca rāja vīthi ādi śobhitaiḥ procchrita prāṃśu śikharaiḥ prāsādaiḥ ca samantataḥ atyanta alaṃkṛta prāntam antar āvaraṇaiḥ iva uttama strī sahasraiḥ ca nṛtya geya viśāradaiḥ rakṣitam rakṣibhiḥ vīraiḥ gaja vāji ratha anvitaiḥ aneka puṣpa vāṭībhiḥ anekaiḥ ca sarovaraiḥ veda vedānta tattva jñaiḥ śiva śāstra parāyaṇaiḥ śiva āśrama rataiḥ bhaktaiḥ śiva śāstra ukta lakṣaṇaiḥ śāntaiḥ smita mukhaiḥ sphītaiḥ sat ācāra parāyaṇaiḥ śaivaiḥ māheśvaraiḥ ca eva śrīmadbhiḥ sevita dvijaiḥ sthāne śilā maye dānte dārave ca iṣṭakā maye kevalam mṛd maye vā api puṇya araṇye atha vā girau nadyām devālaye anyatra deśe vā atha gṛhe śubhe āḍhyaḥ vā atha daridraḥ vā svakām śaktim avaṃcayan bhaktyā vitta anusāreṇa śivam uddiśya yat kṛtam guhyāt guhyataram kṛṣṇa sarvatra parameśvare dānam adhyayanam sarve bhāva artham na atra saṃśayaḥ cāndrāyaṇa sahasraiḥ ca prājāpatya śataiḥ tathā māsa upavāsaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca śiva bhaktasya kim punar abhaktāḥ mānavāḥ ca asmin loke giri guhāsu ca rājasam siddhi dam kuryuḥ karmiṇaḥ rajasā āvṛtāḥ asurāḥ rākṣasāḥ ca eva tamaḥ guṇa samanvitāḥ aihika artham yajanti īśam narāḥ ca anye tādṛśāḥ tāmasam rājasam vā api sāttvikam bhāvam eva ca āśritya bhaktyā pūjā ādyam kurvan bhadram samaśnute yatas pāpa arṇavāt trātum bhaktiḥ nauḥ iva nirmitā śivam prapannaḥ ced kṛṣṇa pūjyaḥ sarva sura asuraiḥ abhuktānām kvacid api phalam na asti yatas tatas vakṣyāmi ati rahasyam te śṛṇu kṛṣṇa vacaḥ mama iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivaśāstroktapūjanavarṇanam nāma paṃcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ brahma ghnaḥ vā surāpaḥ vā steyī vā gurutalpa gaḥ mātṛ hā pitṛ hā vā api vīra hā bhrūṇa hā api vā saṃpūjya amantrakam bhaktyā śivam parama kāraṇam taiḥ taiḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyeta varṣaiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ kramāt bhaktaḥ ced na aparaḥ kaścid bhikṣā āhāraḥ jita indriyaḥ kṛtvā api su mahat pāpam bhaktyā paṃcākṣareṇa tu pūjayet yadi deveśam tasmāt pāpāt pramucyate abbhakṣāḥ vāyubhakṣāḥ ca ye ca anye vrata karśitāḥ teṣām etaiḥ vrataiḥ na asti śiva loka samāgamaḥ bhaktyā paṃcākṣareṇa eva yaḥ śivam sakṛt arcayet tasmāt tapāṃsi yajñān ca sarve sarva sva dakṣiṇāḥ śiva mūrti arcanasya ete koṭi aṃśena api no samāḥ baddhaḥ vā api atha muktaḥ vā paścāt pañca akṣareṇa ced pūjayan mucyate bhaktaḥ na atra kāryā vicāraṇā yaḥ sakṛt patitaḥ vā api mūḍhaḥ vā mucyate naraḥ ṣaḍakṣareṇa vā devam sūkta mantreṇa pūjayet alabdhāt labdhaḥ eva atra viśiṣṭaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ tasmāt nityam śivam bhaktyā sūkta mantreṇa pūjayet eka kālam dvi kālam vā tri kālam nityam eva vā ye arcayanti mahādevam vijñeyāḥ te maheśvarāḥ jñānena ātma sahāyena na arcitaḥ bhagavān śivaḥ sa ciram saṃsarati asmin saṃsāre duḥkha sāgare durllabham prāpya mānuṣyam mūḍhaḥ nā arcayate śivam teṣām hi saphalam janma kṛtārthāḥ te nara uttamāḥ bhavanāni manojñāni vibhrama ābharaṇāḥ striyaḥ dhanam ca atṛpti paryyantam śiva pūjā vidheḥ phalam ye vāñchanti mahā bhogān rājyam ca tridaśālaye te vāñchanti sadā kālam harasya caraṇa ambujam saubhāgyam kāntimat rūpam sattvam tyāga ārdra bhāva tā tasmāt sarvam parityajya śiva eka āhita mānasaḥ śiva pūjā vidhim kuryāt yadi icchet śivam ātmanaḥ tvaritam jīvitam yāti tvaritam yāti yauvanam tvaritam vyādhiḥ abhyeti tasmāt pūjyaḥ pinākadhṛk yāvat na āyāti maraṇam yāvat na ākramate jarā iti vijñāya yatnena pūjanīyaḥ sadāśivaḥ dvāra yāgam javanikām parivāra bali kriyām puṣpam dhūpam ca dīpam ca dadyāt annam jalaiḥ saha tatas dadyāt mahā pīṭhe tiṣṭhan balim udañc mukhaḥ tat sarvam sa avaśeṣam vā caṇḍāya vinivedayet hutvā ca vidhivat paścāt pūjā śeṣam samāpayet kṛtvā prayogam vidhivat yāvat mantram japam tatas nitya utsavam prakurvīta yathā uktam śiva śāsane astram pāśupatam divyam tatra āvāhya samarcayet śivasya āropyaḥ tat pātram dvijasya alaṃkṛtasya ca nyasta astra vapuṣā tena dīpta yaṣṭi dharasya ca nṛtya geya ādibhiḥ ca eva saha dīpa dhvaja ādibhiḥ pradakṣiṇa trayam kṛtvā na drutam ca avilambitam mahāpīṭham samāvṛtya tris pradakṣiṇa yogataḥ punar praviṣṭaḥ dvāra sthaḥ yajamānaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ ādāya abhyantaram nītvā hi astram udvāsayet tatas pradakṣiṇa ādikam kṛtvā yathāpūrva uditam kramāt ādāya ca aṣṭa puṣpāṇi pūjām atha samāpayet iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe sāṃgopāṃgapūjāvidhānavarṇanam nāma ṣaḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha agni kāryam vakṣyāmi kuṇḍe vā sthaṃḍile api vā vedyām vā hi āyase pātre mṛd maye vā nave śubhe ādhāya agnim vidhānena saṃskṛtya ca tatas param kuṇḍam dvi hasta mānam vā hasta mātram atha api vā vṛttam vā catur asram vā kuryāt vedim ca maṇḍalam kuṇḍam vistāravat nimnam tad madhye aṣṭa dala ambujam aṃgulaiḥ kathyate sadbhiḥ caturviṃśatibhiḥ karaḥ mekhalānām trayam vā api dvayam ekam atha api vā yathāśobham prakurvīta ślakṣṇam iṣṭam mṛdā sthiram mekhalā madhyatas kuryāt paścime dakṣiṇe api vā śobhanām agnitaḥ kiṃcid nimnām unmīlikām śanais agreṇa kuṇḍa abhimukhīm kiṃcid utsṛjya mekhalām na utsedha niyamaḥ vedyāḥ sā mārdī vā atha saikatī maṃḍalam go śakṛt toyaiḥ mānam pātrasya na uditam kuṇḍam ca mṛd mayam vedim ālipet gomaya aṃbunā prakṣālya tāpayet pātram prokṣayet anyat aṃbhasā sva sūtra ukta prakāreṇa kuṇḍa ādau villikhet tatas arcana artham ca homa artham sarva dravyāṇi sādhayet prakṣālya kṣālanīyāni prokṣaṇyā prokṣya śodhayet maṇi jam kāṣṭha jam vā atha śrotriya āgāra sambhavam anyam vā abhyarhitam vahnim tatas sa ādhāram ānayet tris pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya kuṇḍa ādeḥ upari kramāt vahnibījam samuccārya tu ādadhīta agnim āsane yoni mārgeṇa vā tadvat ātmanaḥ saṃmukhena vā niyogaḥ pradeśa sarvam kuṃḍam kuryāt vicakṣaṇaḥ nirgamya pāvake bahye līnam biṃba ākṛti smaret śiva mūrtim samabhyarcya tatas dakṣiṇa pārśvataḥ nyasya mantram ghṛte mudrām darśayet dhenu saṃjñitām yajña dāru mayau vā api smārtau vā śilpa sammatau pāra ārṣa ṛcya sva sūtra ukta krameṇa śiva pūrvakaiḥ bhruṃ stum bruśrum krameṇa eva puṃḍrandram iti atas param bījāni sapta saptānām jihvānām anupūrvaśas tri śikhā madhyamā jihvā bahu rūpa samāhvayā raktā āgneyī nairṛtī ca kṛṣṇā anyā suprabhā matā atiriktā marujjihvā sva nāma anuguṇa prabhā sva bija anantaram vācyā svāhā antaḥ ca yathākramam sarpiṣā vā samidbhiḥ vā pariṣecanam ācaret evam kṛte śiva agniḥ syāt smaret tatra śiva āsanam tatra āvāhya yajet devam ardhanārīśvaram śivam dīpa antam pariṣicya atha samidh homam samācaret tāḥ pālāśyaḥ parāḥ vā api yājñiyāḥ dvādaśa aṃgulāḥ avakrāḥ na svayam śuṣkāḥ sa tvacaḥ nirvraṇāḥ samāḥ daśa aṃgulāḥ vā vihitāḥ kaniṣṭhā aṃguli saṃmitāḥ prādeśa mātrāḥ vā alābhe hotavyāḥ sakalāḥ api dūrvā patra sama ākārām catur aṃgulam āyatām dadyāt ājya āhutim paścāt annam akṣa pramāṇataḥ lājān tathā sarṣapān ca yavān ca eva tilān tathā sarpiṣā aktāni bhakṣyāṇi lehya coṣyāṇi sambhave daśa eva āhutayaḥ tatra pañca vā tritayam ca vā hotavyāḥ śaktitas dadyāt ekam eva atha vā āhutim śruveṇa ājyam samitya ādyā srucā aśeṣāt kareṇa vā tatra divyena hotavyam tīrthena ārṣeṇa vā tathā tatas homa viśiṣṭena ghṛtena āpūryya vai srucam nidhāya puṣpam tasya agre śruveṇa adhomukhena tām vauṣaṭ antena juhuyāt dhārām tu yava saṃmitām ittham pūrṇāhutim kṛtvā pariṣiṃcet ca pūrvavat tam api udvāsya vā nābhau yajet saṃdhāya nityaśas athavā vahnim ānīya śiva śāstra ukta vartmanā vāgīśī garbha saṃbhūtam saṃskṛtya vidhivat yajet anvādhānam punar kṛtvā paridhīn paridhāya ca pātrāṇi dvandva rūpeṇa nikṣipya iṣṭvā śivam tatas saṃśodhya prokṣaṇī pātram prokṣyatāni tat aṃbhasā praṇītā pātram aiśānyām vinyasya ā pūritam jalaiḥ ājya saṃskāra paryantam kṛtvā saṃśodhya sraj sruvau garbhādhānam puṃsavanam sīmantonnayanam tatas kṛtvā pṛthak pṛthak hutvā jātam agnim vicintayet tri pādam sapta hastam ca catur śṛṃgam dvi śīrṣakam raktam rakta ambara ālepam mālya bhūṣaṇa bhūṣitam tomaram tālavṛṃtam ca ghṛta pātram tathā itaraiḥ jātam dhyātvā evam ākāram jātakarma samācaret nāla apanayanam kṛtvā tatas saṃśodhya sūtakam śiva agni ruci nāmā asya kṛtvā āhuti purassaram aptoryāma avasāna antam kṛtvā saṃskāram asya tu ājya dhārā ādi homam ca kṛtvā sviṣṭakṛtam tatas brahma viṣṇu śiva īśānām lokeśānām tathā eva ca tad astrāṇām ca paritas kṛtvā pūjām yathākramam sādhayitvā ājya pūrvāṇi dravyāṇi punar eva ca kalpayitvā āsanam vahnau tatra āvāhya yathā purā saṃpūjya devam devīm ca tatas pūrṇa antam ācaret atha vā sva āśrama uktam tu vahni karma śiva arpaṇam buddhvā śiva āśramī kuryāt na ca tatra aparaḥ vidhiḥ kapilāyāḥ śakṛt śastam gṛhītam gagane patat na klinnam na ati kaṭhinam na durgandham na śoṣitam upari adhas parityajya gṛhṇīyāt patitam yadi piṃḍīkṛtya śiva agni ādau tat kṣipet mūlamantrataḥ ādāya vā samāloḍya bhasma ādhāre vinikṣipet taijasam dāravam vā api mṛd mayam śailam eva ca anyat vā śobhanam śuddham bhasma ādhāram prakalpayet na saṃspṛśet ca nīca aṃgaiḥ na upekṣeta na laṃghayet tasmāt bhasitam ādāya viniyuṃjīta mantrataḥ kāleṣu ukteṣu na anyatra na ayogyebhyaḥ pradāpayet udvāsane kṛte yasmāt caṇḍa bhasma prajāpate agni kārye kṛte paścāt śiva śāstra ukta mārgataḥ vidyā kośam pratiṣṭhāpya yajet puṣpa ādibhiḥ kramāt vidyāyāḥ puratas kṛtvā guroḥ api ca maṇḍalam tatra āsana varam kṛtvā puṣpa ādyaiḥ gurum arcayet niveditam ca vā deve tat śeṣam ca ātma śuddhaye na tu tatra śivaḥ asmi iti buddhim kuryāt vicakṣaṇaḥ bhuktvā ācamya śivam dhyātvā hṛdaye mūlam uccaret kāla śeṣam nayet yogyaiḥ śiva śāstra kathā ādibhiḥ rātrau vyatīte pūrva aṃśe kṛtvā pūjām manoharām śivayoḥ śayanam tu ekam kalpayet ati śobhanam bhakṣya bhojya aṃbara ālepa puṣpa mālā ādikam tathā manasā karmaṇā vā api kṛtvā sarvam manoharam gṛhasthaḥ bhāryayā sārddham tad anye api tu kevalāḥ pratyūṣa samayam buddhvā mātrām ādyām udīrayet praṇamya manasām devam sa aṃbam sa gaṇam avyayam deśa kāla ucitam kṛtvā śauca ādyam api śaktitaḥ nirvartya śivayoḥ pūjām prārabheta purā uditam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe agnikāryavarṇanam nāma saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atas param pravakṣyāmi śiva āśrama niṣeviṇām aṣṭābhyām ca caturdaśyām tathā parvāṇi ca kramāt ayane viṣuve ca eva grahaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ kartavyā mahatī pūjā hi adhikā vā api śaktitaḥ māsi māsi yathānyāyam brahmakūrcam prasādhya tu snāpayitvā śivam tena pibet śeṣam upoṣitaḥ brahmahatyā ādi doṣāṇām atīva mahatām api niṣkṛtiḥ brahmakūrcasya pānāt na anyā viśiṣyate pauṣe puṣya nakṣatre kuryāt nīrājanam vibhoḥ caitre citrā paurṇamāsyām dolām kuryāt yathāvidhi vaiśākhyām tu viśākhāyām kuryāt puṣpa mahālayam jyeṣṭhe mūla ākhya nakṣatre śītakumbham pradāpayet āṣāḍhe ca uttarāṣāḍhe pavitra āropaṇam tathā śrāvaṇe prākṛtāni āpi maṇḍalāni prakalpayet śraviṣṭhā ākhye tu nakṣatre prauṣṭhapadyām tatas param prokṣayet ca jala krīḍām pūrvāṣāḍhā āśraye dine āśvayujyām tatas dadyāt pāyasam ca navodanam kārtikyām kṛtikā yoge dadyāt dīpa sahasrakam mārgaśīrṣe tathā ārdrāyām ghṛtena snāpayet śivam aśaktaḥ teṣu kāleṣu kuryāt utsavam eva vā āsthānam vā mahā pūjām adhikam vā samarcanam āvṛtte api ca kalyāṇe praśasteṣu api karmasu daurmanasye durācāre duḥsvapne duṣṭa darśane snāna pūjā japa dhyāna homa dāna ādikāḥ kriyaḥ nirmita anuguṇāḥ kāryyāḥ puraścaraṇa pūrvikāḥ divyam śrīkaṃṭha nāthasya sthānam ādyam sa gacchati saṃprāpya vaiṣṇavam brāhmam rudra lokam viśeṣataḥ tatra uṣitvā ciram kālam bhuktvā bhogān yathā uditān śrīkaṇṭhāt jñānam āsādya tasmāt śaiva puram vrajet paścāt jñānam samāsādya śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt saṃprāpya pauruṣam raudra sthānam adri indrajāpateḥ puṇya kṣaye kṣitim prāpya kule mahati jāyate tatra api pūrva saṃskāra vaśena sa mahā dyutiḥ bhogān ca vividhān bhuktvā vidyeśvara padam vrajet aṇḍasya antar bahis vā atha sakṛt āvartate punar tatas labdhvā śiva jñānam parām bhaktim avāpya ca yaḥ ca atīva śive bhaktaḥ viṣaya āsakta citta vat eka āvṛttaḥ dvis āvṛttaḥ tris āvṛttaḥ nivartakaḥ tasmāt śiva āśritaḥ bhūtvā yena kena api hetunā saṃsāra kāraṇam yeṣām na praroḍhum alam bhavet prakṛti anuguṇam tasmāt vimṛśya etat aśeṣatas iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe nityanaimittikavidhivarṇanam nāma aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca bhagavan tvad mukhāt eva śrutam śruti samam mayā sva āśritānām śiva proktam nityanaimittikam tathā idānīm śrotum icchāmi śiva dharma adhikāriṇām aihika āmuṣmikam ca api tat ca pañcavidham punar kriyā mayam tathā bhinnam homa dāna arcana kramāt sarva śaktimatām eva na anyeṣām saphalam bhavet śaktiḥ ca ājñā mad īśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ tasmāt kāmyāni karmāṇi kuryāt ājñā dharaḥ udvijaḥ śaivaiḥ māheśvaraiḥ ca eva kāryam antar bahis kramāt yathā tathā na bhidyante śaivāḥ māheśvarāḥ api śiva āśritāḥ hi te śaivāḥ jñāna yajña ratāḥ narāḥ māheśvarāḥ samākhyātā karma yajña ratāḥ bhuvi tasmāt ābhyantare kuryuḥ śaivāḥ māheśvarāḥ vahis parīkṣya bhūmim vidhivat gandha varṇa rasa ādibhiḥ supralipte mahī pṛṣṭhe darpaṇa udara saṃnibhe prācīm utpādayet pūrvam śāstra dṛṣṭena vartmanā eka hastam dvi hastam vā maṇḍalam parikalpayet ālikhet vimalam padmam aṣṭa patram sa karṇikam ratna hema ādibhiḥ cūrṇaiḥ yathā saṃbhava saṃbhṛtaiḥ pañca āvaraṇa saṃyuktam bahu śobhā samanvitam daleṣu siddhayaḥ kalpyāḥ kesareṣu sa śaktikāḥ rudrāḥ vāma ādayaḥ tu aṣṭau pūrva ādi dalataḥ kramāt karṇikāyām ca vairāgyam bījeṣu nava śaktayaḥ skande śiva ātmakaḥ dharmaḥ nāle jñānam śiva āśrayam paṃca āvaraṇa saṃyuktam pūjayet aṃbayā saha śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśam prasannam śītala dyutim vidyut valaya saṃkāśa jaṭā mukuṭa bhūṣitam śārdūla carma vasanam kiñcid smita mukha aṃbujam sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam paṃcavaktram daśa bhujam candra khaṇḍa śikhāmaṇim asya pūrva mukham saumyam bāla arka sadṛśa prabham tri locana aravinda āḍhyam kṛta bāla indu śekharam dakṣiṇam nīla jīmūta samāna rucira prabham bhrukuṭī kuṭilam ghoram rakta vṛtta īkṣaṇa trayam daṃṣṭrā karālam durddharṣam sphurita adhara pallavam uttaram vidruma prakhyam nīla alaka vibhūṣitam savilāsam trinayanam candra ābharaṇa śekharam dakṣiṇe śūla paraśu vajra khaḍga anala ujjvalam savye ca nāga nārāca ghaṇṭā pāśa aṃkuśa ujjvalam nivṛttyā a jānu saṃbaddha māna ābheḥ ca pratiṣṭhayā ākaṃṭham vidyayā tadvat ālalāṭam tu śāntayā tad ūrddhvam śānti atīta ākhya kalayā parayā tathā paṃca adhva vyāpinam sākṣāt kalā paṃcaka vigraham īśāna mukuṭam devam puruṣa ākhyam purātanam sadya pādam ca tad mūrtim aṣṭatriṃśat kalā mayam mātṛkā mayam īśānam paṃca brahma mayam tathā okāra ākhya mayam ca eva haṃsa śaktyā samanvitam tathā icchā ātmikayā śaktyā samārūḍha aṃka maṃḍalam jñāna ākhyayā dakṣiṇatas vāmatas ca kriyā ākhyayā tattva traya mayam sākṣāt vidyā mūrtim sadāśivam mūrti mūlena saṃkalpya sakalīkṛtya ca kramāt saṃpūjya ca yathānyāyam argha antam mūlavidyayā mūrtimantam śivam sākṣāt śaktyā paramayā saha paṃca upakaraṇam kṛtvā pūjayet parameśvaram brahmabhiḥ ca ṣaḍaGgaiḥ ca tatas mātṛkayā saha śāntena vā tathā anyaiḥ ca veda mantraiḥ ca kṛtsnaśas pādya ādi mukha vāsa antam kṛtvā prasthāpanam vinā paṃca āvaraṇa pūjām tu hi ārabheta yathākramam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe kāmyakarmavarṇanam nāma ekonatriṃśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatra ādau śivayoḥ pārśve dakṣiṇe vāmatas kramāt tatas brahmāṇi paritas īśāna ādi yathākramam sa śaktikāni sadya antam prathama āvaraṇe yajet ṣaṣ aṃgāni api tatra eva hṛdaya ādīni anukramāt śivasya ca śivāyāḥ ca vāhneya ādi samarcayet tatra vāmā ādikān rudrān aṣṭau vāma ādi śaktibhiḥ arcayet vā na vā paścāt pūrva ādi paritas kramāt dvitīya āvaraṇam prītyā procyate śraddhayā śṛṇu sūkṣmam dakṣiṇa diś patre saha śaktyā samarcayet śrīkaṇṭham nairṛte patre tad śaktim tasya vāmatas tathā eva mārute patre śikhaṃḍīśam samarcayet tṛtīya āvaraṇe pūjyāḥ śaktibhiḥ ca aṣṭamūrtayaḥ aṣṭasu kramaśas dikṣu pūrva ādi paritas kramāt bhavaḥ śarvaḥ tathā īśānaḥ rudraḥ paśupatiḥ tatas ugraḥ bhīmaḥ mahādevaḥ iti aṣṭau mūrtayaḥ kramāt anantaram tatas ca eva mahādeva ādayaḥ kramāt śaktibhiḥ saha saṃpūjyāḥ tatra ekādaśa mūrttayaḥ mahādevaḥ śivaḥ rudraḥ śaṃkaraḥ nīlalohitaḥ kapardī īśaḥ ca kathyante tathā ekādaśa śaktayaḥ tatra aṣṭau prathamam pūjyāḥ vāhneya ādi yathākramam devadevaḥ pūrva patre īśānam ca agni gocare tasmin āvaraṇe bhūyas vṛṣa indram puratas yajet nandinam dakṣiṇe tasya mahākālam tathā uttare śāstāram vahni diś patre mātR̥ dakṣiṇa diś dale gajāsyam nairṛte patre ṣaṇmukham vāruṇe punar jyeṣṭhām vāyudale gaurīm uttare caṃḍam aiśvare śāstṛ nandīśayoḥ madhye muni indram vṛṣabham yajet śāstṛ mātṛ samūhasya madhye bhṛṃgīśvaram tatas jyeṣṭhā kumārayoḥ madhye śriyam śiva pada arccitām jyeṣṭhā gaṇāmbayoḥ madhye mahāmoṭīm samarcayet gaṇa ambā caṇḍayoḥ madhye devīm durgām prapūjayet atra eva āvaraṇe bhūyas śiva anucara saṃhatim rudra prathama bhūta ākhyām vividhām ca sa śaktikām śivāyāḥ ca sakhī varggam japet dhyātvā samāhitaḥ evam tṛtīya āvaraṇe vitate pūjite sati bhānuḥ pūrva dale pūjyaḥ dakṣiṇe caturānanaḥ caturṇām api devānām pṛthak āvaraṇāni atha tasya aṃgāni ṣaḍ eva ādau dīptā ādyābhiḥ ca śaktibhiḥ dīptā sūkṣmā jayā bhadrā vibhūtiḥ vimalā kramāt amoghā vidyutā ca eva pūrva ādi paritas sthitāḥ dvitīya āvaraṇe pūjyāḥ catasraḥ mūrtayaḥ kramāt pūrva ādi uttara paryantāḥ śaktayaḥ ca tatas param ādityaḥ bhāskaraḥ bhānuḥ raviḥ ca iti anupūrvaśas pūrva digbhāge sutarām dakṣiṇe sthitāḥ bodhanī paścime bhāge āpyāyinī uttare punar uṣām prabhām tathā prājñām sandhyām api tatas param aiśāna ādiṣu vinyasya dvitīya āvaraṇe yajet bṛhaspatim bṛhat buddhim bhārgavam tejasām nidhim śanaiścaram tathā rāhum ketum dhūmram bhayaṃkaram samantataḥ yajet etān tṛtīya āvaraṇe kramāt athavā dvādaśa ādityāḥ dvitīya āvaraṇe yajet tṛtīya āvaraṇe ca eva rāśīn dvādaśa pūjayet ṛṣīn devān ca gandharvān pannagān apsaraḥ gaṇān grāmaṇyaḥ ca tathā yakṣān yātudhānān tathā hayān sapta chandaḥ mayān ca eva vālakhilyān ca pūjayet evam tṛtīya āvaraṇe samabhyarcya divākaram brahmāṇam arcayet paścāt tribhiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ sahaḥ hiraṇyagarbham pūrvasyām virājam dakṣiṇe tatas kālam paścima digbhāge puruṣam ca uttare yajet kālaḥ jāti aṃjana prakhyaḥ puruṣaḥ sphaṭika upamaḥ triguṇaḥ rājasaḥ ca eva tāmasaḥ sāttvikaḥ tathā catvāraḥ ete kramaśas prathama āvaraṇe sthitāḥ dvitīya āvaraṇe pūjyāḥ pūrva ādi paritas kramāt sanatkumāraḥ sanakaḥ sanandaḥ ca sanātanaḥ tṛtīya āvaraṇe paścāt arcayet ca prajāpatīn aṣṭau pūrvān ca pūrva ādau trīn prāk paścāt anukramāt dakṣaḥ ruciḥ bhṛguḥ ca eva marīciḥ ca tathā aṃgirāḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca iti vikhyātāḥ prajānām patayaḥ tu ime teṣām bhāryyāḥ ca taiḥ sārddham pūjanīyāḥ yathākramam prasūtiḥ ca tathā khyātiḥ sambhūtiḥ eva ca dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ kṣamā ca eva sannatiḥ ca anasūyakā devamātā arundhatī ca sarvāḥ khalu pativratāḥ śiva arcana rataḥ nityam śrīmatyaḥ priya darśanāḥ prathama āvaraṇe vedān caturaḥ vā prapūjayet itihāsa purāṇāni dvitīya āvaraṇe punar tṛtīya āvaraṇe paścāt dharmaśāstra purassarāḥ vaidikyaḥ nikhilāḥ vidyāḥ pūjyāḥ eva samantataḥ aṣṭadhā vā caturdhā vā kṛtvā pūjām samantataḥ dakṣiṇe paścime paścāt rudram sa āvaraṇam yajet tasya brahma ṣaṣ aṃgāni prathama āvaraṇam smṛtam dvitīya āvaraṇe ca eva vidyeśvara mayam tathā catasraḥ mūrtayaḥ tasya pūjyāḥ pūrva ādeḥ kramāt triguṇāḥ sakalaḥ devaḥ purastāt śiva saṃjñakaḥ rājasaḥ dakṣiṇe brahmā sṛṣṭi kṛt pūjyate bhavaḥ tāmasaḥ paścime ca agniḥ pūjyaḥ saṃhārakaḥ haraḥ sāttvikaḥ sukha kṛt saumye viṣṇuḥ viśvapatiḥ mṛḍaḥ evam paścima digbhāge śambhoḥ ṣaḍviṃśakam śivam vāsudevam puraskṛtvā prathama āvaraṇe yajet aniruddham dakṣiṇatas pradyumnam paścime tatas saumye saṃkarṣaṇam paścāt vyatyastau vā yajet imau prathama āvaraṇam proktam dvitīya āvaraṇam śubham matsyaḥ kūrmaḥ varāhaḥ ca narasiṃhaḥ utha vāmanaḥ rāmaḥ ca anyatamaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ bhavān aśvamukhaḥ api ca tṛtīya āvaraṇe cakruḥ pūrva bhāge samarcayet nārāyaṇa ākhyām yāmya istram kvacid avyāhatam yajet evam tri āvaraṇaiḥ sākṣāt viśva ākhyām paramam harim mahāviṣṇum sadā viṣṇum mūrtīkṛtya samarcayet ittham viṣṇoḥ catur vyūha kramāt mūrti catuṣṭayam gaṇāṃbikā ca vāyavye lakṣmīm raudre samarcayet evam bhānu ādi mūrttīnām tad śaktīnām anantaram pūjām vidhāya lokeśān tatra eva āvaraṇe yajet indram agnim yamam ca eva nirṛtim varuṇam tathā vāyum somam kuberam ca paścāt īśānam arcayet evam caturtha āvaraṇam pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ āyudhāni maheśasya paścāt bāṃhyam samarcayet śrīmat triśūlam aiśāne vajram māhendra diś mukhe nairṛte tu yajet khaḍgam pāśam vāruṇa gocare aṃkuśam mārute bhāge pinākam ca uttare yajet paścima abhimukham raudram kṣetrapālam samarcayet pañcama āvaraṇam ca eva sampūjya anantaram bahis sarva āvaraṇa devānām bahis vā pañcame athavā tatas samantataḥ pūjyāḥ sarvāḥ vai devayonayaḥ khecarāḥ ṛṣayaḥ siddhāḥ daityāḥ yakṣāḥ ca rākṣasāḥ ananta ādyāḥ ca nāga indrāḥ nāgaiḥ tad tad kula udbhavaiḥ ḍākinī bhūta vetāla preta bhairava nāyakāḥ pātāla vāsinaḥ ca anye nānā yoni samudbhavāḥ nadyaḥ samudrāḥ girayaḥ kānanāni sarāṃsi ca paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ vṛkṣāḥ kīṭa ādyāḥ kṣudra yonayaḥ narāḥ ca vividha ākārāḥ mṛgāḥ ca kṣudra yonayaḥ bhuvanāni antar aṇḍasya tatas brahmāṇḍa koṭayaḥ bahiraṃḍāni asaṃkhyāni bhuvanāni saha adhipaiḥ brahmāṃḍa dhārakāḥ rudrāḥ daśa dikṣu vyavasthitāḥ yat gauḍa yat ca māmeyam yat vā śāktam tatas param tat sarvam śivayoḥ pārśve buddhvā sāmānyatas yajet kṛta aṃjali puṭāḥ sarve aciṃtyāḥ smita mukhāḥ tathā prītyā saṃprekṣamāṇāḥ ca devam devīm ca sarvadā ittham āvaraṇa abhyarcām kṛtvā a vikṣepa śāntaye su vyañjana samāyuktam śuddham cāru mahā carum dvātriṃśat āḍhakaiḥ mukhyam adhamam tu āḍhaka avaram tatas nivedya pānīyam tāṃbūlam ca upadaṃśakaiḥ nīrājana ādikam kṛtvā pūjā śeṣam samāpayet bhoga upayogya dravyāṇi viśiṣṭāni eva sādhayet śaṭhasya upekṣakasya api vyaṃgyam ca eva anutiṣṭhataḥ na phalanti eva karmāṇi kāmyāni iti satām kathā tasmāt samyak upekṣām ca tyaktvā sarva aṃga yogataḥ kuryāt kāmyāni karmāṇi phala siddhim yadi icchati ittham pūjām samāpya atha devam devīm praṇamya ca tatas stotram upāsya ante tu aṣṭottaraśata avarām japet pañcākṣarīm vidyām sahasra uttaram utsukaḥ vidyā pūjām guroḥ pūjām kṛtvā paścāt yathākramam yathodayam yathāśrāddham sadasyān api pūjayet tatas udvāsya deveśam sarvaiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ saha maṇḍalam gurave dadyāt yāga upakaraṇaiḥ saha śiva āśritebhyaḥ vā dadyāt sarvam eva anupūrvaśas samabhyarcya yathānyāyam sarva āvaraṇa devatāḥ eṣa yogeśvaraḥ nāma triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ aihikam vā phalam kiṃcid āmuṣmika phalam tu vā śreyaḥ rūpasya kṛtsnasya tat idam śreṣṭa sādhanam mahādevam samuddiśya kṛtam karma prayujyatām tasmāt an anya labhyeṣu śatru mṛtyuṃjaya ādiṣu phaleṣu dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭeṣu kuryāt etat vicakṣaṇaḥ mahatsu api ca pāteṣu mahā rāga bhaya ādiṣu durbhikṣa ādiṣu śānti artham śāntim kuryyāt anena tu bahunā kim pralāpena mahā vyāpad nivārakam ātmīyam astram śaivānām idam āha maheśvaraḥ tasmāt itas param nā asti paritrāṇam iha ātmanaḥ iti matvā prayuṃjānaḥ karma idam śubham aśnute stotra mātram śuciḥ bhūtvā yaḥ paṭhet su samāhitaḥ saḥ upi abhīṣṭatamāt arthāt aṣṭa aṃśa phalam āpnuyāt artham tasya anusandhāya parvaṇi anaśanaḥ paṭhet aṣṭābhyām vā caturdaśyām phalam arddham samāpnuyāt māsam ekam japet stotram sa kṛtsnam phalam āpnuyāt iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śaivānām kāmyakavarṇanam īśvaraḥ api na śaknuyāt janma prabhṛti deveśi janaḥ yam tvat upāśritaḥ śiva bhakti samārūḍhaḥ śānti atītaḥ sadāśivaḥ bhaktyā mayā arcitaḥ mahyam prārthitam śam prayacchatu sadāśiva aṃkam ārūḍhā śaktiḥ icchā śiva āhvayā śiva anubhāvau sarva jñau śiva jñāna amṛta āśinau tṛptau parasparam snigdhau śivābhyām nitya satkṛtau sva icchā avatāram kurvantau sva aṃśa bhedaiḥ anekaśas tau imau śivayoḥ pārśve nityam ittham mayā arcitau tayoḥ ājñām puraskṛtya prārthitam me prayacchatām śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśam īśāna ākhyam sadāśivam mūrddha abhimāninī mūrtiḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ śiva arcana ratam śāntam śānti atītam makha āsthitam paṃcākṣara antimam bījam kalābhiḥ paṃcabhiḥ yutam prathama āvaraṇe pūrvam śaktyā saha samarcitam bāla sūrya pratīkāśam puruṣa ākhyam purātanam pūrva vaktra abhimānam ca śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ śānti ātmakam marut saṃstham śambhoḥ pāda arcane ratam prathamam śiva bījeṣu kalāsu ca catuṣkalam añjana ādi pratīkāśam aghoram ghora vigraham vidyā pādam samārūḍham vahni tṛtīyam śivabījeṣu kalābhiḥ ca aṣṭabhiḥ yutam śivasya tu śivāyāḥ ca hṛd mūrti śiva bhāvite tayoḥ ājñām puraskṛtya te me kāmam prayacchatām śivasya ca śivāyāḥ ca śikhā mūrti śiva āśrite satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām te me kāmam prayacchatām śivasya ca śivāyāḥ ca varmaṇā śiva bhāvite satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām te me kāmam prayacchatām śivasya ca śivāyāḥ ca netra mūrti śiva āśrite satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām te me kāmam prayacchatām satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām te me kāmam prayacchatām vāmau jyeṣṭhaḥ tathā rudraḥ kālaḥ vikaraṇaḥ tathā sarva bhūtasya damanaḥ tādṛśāḥ ca aṣṭa śaktayaḥ atha anantaḥ ca sūkṣmaḥ ca
