aṣṭau tāsām api ca śaktayaḥ mahādeva ādayaḥ ca anye tathā ekādaśa mūrtayaḥ śaktibhiḥ sahitāḥ sarve tṛtīya āvaraṇe sthitāḥ satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām diśantu phalam īpsitam sita abhra śikhara ākāraḥ kakudā pariśobhitaḥ rakta āsya śṛṃga caraṇau rakta prāya vilocanaḥ praśasta lakṣaṇaḥ śrīmān prajvalat maṇi bhūṣaṇaḥ śiva priyaḥ śiva āsaktaḥ śivayoḥ dhvaja vāhanaḥ tathā tad caraṇa nyāsa pāvita apara vigrahaḥ tayoḥ ājñām puraskṛtya sa me kāmam prayacchatu śarvasya antaḥpura dvāri sārddham parijanaiḥ sthitaḥ sarveṣām śiva dharmāṇām adhyakṣa tve abhiṣecitaḥ śiva priyaḥ śiva āsaktaḥ śrīmat śūla vara āyudhaḥ śiva āśriteṣu saṃsaktaḥ tu anuraktaḥ ca taiḥ api satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām sa me kāmam prayacchatu mahākālaḥ mahā bāhuḥ mahādevaḥ iva aparaḥ mahādeva āśritānām tu nityam eva abhirakṣatu śiva priyaḥ śiva āsaktaḥ śivayoḥ arcakaḥ sadā satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam sarva śāstra artha tattva jñaḥ śāstā viṣṇoḥ parā tanuḥ tayoḥ ājñām puraskṛtya sa me kāmam prayacchatu brahmāṇī ca eva māheśī kaumārī vaiṣṇavī tathā vārāhī ca eva māhendrī cāmuṃḍā caṃḍavikramā matta mātaṃga vadanaḥ gaṃgā umā śaṃkara ātmajaḥ ākāśa dehaḥ diś bāhuḥ soma sūrya agni locanaḥ śiva jñāna mada udbhinnaḥ tridaśānām avighna kṛt vighna kṛt ca asura ādīnām vighneśaḥ śiva bhāvitaḥ satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam ṣaṇmukhaḥ śiva sambhūtaḥ śakti vajra dharaḥ prabhuḥ gaṃgāyāḥ ca gaṇāṃbāyāḥ kṛttikānām tathā eva ca viśākhena ca śākhena naigameyena ca āvṛtaḥ śailānām meru mukhyānām vedhakaḥ ca sva tejasā tapta cāmīkara prakhyaḥ śatapatra dala īkṣaṇaḥ kumāraḥ sukumārāṇām rūpa udāharaṇam mahat satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā vara dā śivayoḥ yajane ratā tayoḥ ājñām puraskṛtya sā me diśatu kāṃkṣitam trailokya vanditā sākṣāt ulkā ākārā gaṇa aṃbikā jagat sṛṣṭi vivṛddhi artham brahmaṇā abhyarthitā śivāt śivāyāḥ pravibhaktāyāḥ bhruvoḥ antara nissṛtāḥ dakṣāyaṇī satī menā tathā haimavatī hi umā aparṇāyāḥ ca jananī pāṭalāyāḥ tathā eva ca śiva arcana ratā nityam rudrāṇī rudra vallabhā satkṛṭya śivayoḥ ājñām sā me diśatu kāṃkṣitam caṃḍaḥ sarva gaṇa īśānaḥ śaṃbhoḥ vadana saṃbhavaḥ satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam piṃgalaḥ gaṇapaḥ śrīmān śiva āsaktaḥ śiva priyaḥ ājñayā śivayoḥ eva sa me kāmam prayacchatu bhṛṃgīśaḥ nāma gaṇapaḥ śiva rādhana tatparaḥ prayacchatu sa me kāmam patyuḥ ājñā puraḥsaram bhadrakālī priyaḥ nityam mātR̥ṇām ca abhirakṣitā yajñasya ca śiraḥ hartā dakṣasya ca durātmanaḥ upendra indra yama ādīnām devānām aṃga takṣakaḥ śivasya anucaraḥ śrīmān śiva śāsana pālakaḥ śivayoḥ śāsanāt eva sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam śivayoḥ pūjane saktā sa me diśatu kāṃkṣitam viṣṇoḥ vakṣaḥ sthitā lakṣmīḥ śivayoḥ pūjane ratā śivayoḥ śāsanāt eva sā me diśatu kāṃkṣitam mahāmoṭī mahādevyāḥ pāda pūjā parāyaṇā tasyāḥ eva niyogena sā me diśatu kāṃkṣitam kauśikī siṃham ārūḍhā pārvatyāḥ paramā sutā viṣṇoḥ nidrā mahāmāyā mahā mahiṣa mardinī satkṛtya śāsanam mātuḥ sā me diśatu kāṃkṣitam bhūta ākhyāḥ ca mahā vīryyāḥ mahādeva sama prabhāḥ sa śaktayaḥ sa anucarāḥ sarva loka namaskṛtāḥ sarveṣām eva lokānām sṛṣṭi saṃharaṇa kṣamāḥ śiva priyatamāḥ nityam śiva lakṣaṇa lakṣitāḥ saumya ādhārāḥ tathā miśrāḥ ca antarāla dvaya ātmikāḥ virūpāḥ ca surūpāḥ ca nānā rūpa dharāḥ tathā satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām te me kāmam diśantu vai devyā priya sakhī vargaḥ devī lakṣaṇa lakṣitaḥ sahitaḥ rudra kanyābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ ca api anekaśas tṛtīya āvaraṇe śaṃbhoḥ bhaktyā nityam samarcitaḥ satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām sa me diśatu maṃgalam divākaraḥ maheśasya mūrtiḥ dīpti su maṃḍalaḥ nirguṇaḥ guṇa saṃkīrṇaḥ tathā eva guṇa kevalaḥ avikāra ātmakaḥ ca ādyaḥ ekaḥ sāmānya vikriyaḥ asādhāraṇa karmā ca sṛṣṭi sthiti laya kramāt evam tridhā caturddhā ca vibhaktāḥ paṃcadhā punar caturtha āvaraṇe śaṃbhoḥ pūjitaḥ ca anugaiḥ saha śiva priyaḥ śiva āsaktaḥ śiva pāda arcane rataḥ satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām sa me diśatu maṃgalam divākara ṣaṣ aṃgāni dīptā ādyāḥ ca aṣṭa śaktayaḥ ādityaḥ bhāskaraḥ bhānuḥ raviḥ ca iti anupūrvaśas arkaḥ brahmā tathā rudraḥ viṣṇuḥ ca āditya mūrtayaḥ vistara asutara abodhinī āpyāyinī aparāḥ punar uṣā prabhā tathā prājñā sandhyā ca iti api śaktayaḥ soma ādi ketu paryantāḥ grahāḥ ca śiva bhāvitāḥ śivayoḥ ājñayā anunnāḥ maṃgalam pradiśantu me athavā dvādaśa ādityāḥ tathā dvādaśa śaktayaḥ ṛṣayaḥ deva gandharvāḥ pannaga apsarasām gaṇāḥ grāmaṇyaḥ ca tathā yakṣāḥ rākṣasāḥ ca asurāḥ tathā vālakhilyāḥ sarve śiva pada arcakāḥ satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām maṃgalam pradiśantu me brahmā atha devadevasya mūrtiḥ bhū maṇḍala adhipaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭi guṇa aiśvaryaḥ buddhi tattve pratiṣṭhitaḥ nirguṇaḥ guṇa saṃkīrṇaḥ tathā eva guṇa kevalaḥ avikāra ātmakaḥ devaḥ tatas sādhāraṇaḥ puras asādhāraṇa karmā ca sṛṣṭi sthiti laya kramāt bhuvam tridhā caturddhā ca vibhaktaḥ paṃcadhā punar caturtha āvaraṇe śaṃbho pūjitaḥ ca saha anugaiḥ śiva priyaḥ śiva āsaktaḥ śiva pāda arcane rataḥ satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām sa me diśatu maṃgalam hiraṇyagarbhaḥ loka īśaḥ virāj kālaḥ ca pūruṣaḥ sanatkumāraḥ sanakaḥ sanandaḥ ca sanātanaḥ prajānām patayaḥ ca eva dakṣa ādyāḥ brahma sūnavaḥ śiva arcana ratāḥ ca ete śiva bhakti parāyaṇāḥ śiva ājñā vaśa gāḥ sarve diśantu mama maṃgalam catvāraḥ ca tathā vedāḥ sa itihāsa purāṇakāḥ dharma śāstrāṇi vidyābhiḥ vaidikībhiḥ samanvitāḥ paraspara viruddha arthāḥ śiva prakṛti pādakāḥ satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām maṃgalam pradiśantu me atha rudraḥ mahādevaḥ śaṃbhoḥ mūrtiḥ garīyasī vāhneya maṇḍala adhīśaḥ pauruṣa aiśvaryavān prabhuḥ śiva abhimāna saṃpannaḥ nirguṇaḥ triguṇa ātmakaḥ kevalam sāttvikaḥ ca api rājasaḥ ca eva tāmasaḥ asādhāraṇa karmā ca sṛṣṭi ādi karaṇāt pṛthak janakaḥ tanayaḥ ca api viṣṇoḥ api niyāmakaḥ śiva priyaḥ śiva āsaktaḥ śiva pāda arcane rataḥ śivasya ājñām puraskṛtya sa me diśatu maṃgalam tasya brahma ṣaṣ aṃgāni vidyeśa antam tathā aṣṭakam catvāraḥ mūrti bhedāḥ ca śiva pūrvāḥ śiva arcakāḥ śivaḥ bhavaḥ haraḥ ca eva mṛḍaḥ ca eva tathā aparaḥ śivasya ājñām puraskṛtya maṃgalam pradiśantu me atha viṣṇuḥ maheśasya śivasya eva parā tanuḥ vāri tattva adhipaḥ sākṣāt avyakta pada saṃsthitaḥ asādhāraṇa karmā ca sṛṣṭi ādi karaṇāt pṛthak dakṣiṇa aṃga bhavena api sparddhamānaḥ svayaṃbhuvā ādyena brahmaṇā sākṣāt sṛṣṭaḥ sraṣṭā ca tasya tu aṃḍasya antar bahis vartī viṣṇuḥ loka dvaya adhipaḥ asura anta karaḥ cakrī śakrasya api tathā anujaḥ prādurbhūtaḥ ca daśadhā bhṛgu śāpa chalāt iha bhū bhāra nigraha arthāya sva icchayā āvāta rakṣitau mūrtim kṛtvā mahā viṣṇum sadāśiṣṇum atha api vā vaiṣṇavaiḥ pūjitaḥ nityam mūrti traya maya āsane śivasya ājñām puraskṛtya sa me diśatu maṃgalam saṃkarṣaṇaḥ samākhyātāḥ catasraḥ mūrtayaḥ hareḥ matsyaḥ kūrmaḥ varāhaḥ ca nārasiṃhaḥ atha vāmanaḥ rāma trayam tathā kṛṣṇaḥ viṣṇuḥ turaga vaktrakaḥ cakram nārāyaṇasya astram pāṃcajanyam ca śārGgakam satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām maṃgalam pradiśantu me prabhā sarasvatī gaurī lakṣmīḥ ca śiva bhāvitā śivayoḥ śāsanāt etāḥ maṃgalam pradiśantu me vāyuḥ somaḥ kuberaḥ ca tathā īśānaḥ triśūladhṛk sarve śiva arcana ratāḥ śiva sadbhāva bhāvitāḥ satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām maṃgalam pradiśantu me triśūlam atha vajram ca tathā paraśu sāyakau khaḍga pāśa aṃkuśāḥ ca eva pinākaḥ ca āyudha uttamaḥ divya āyudhāni devasya devyāḥ ca etāni nityaśas satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām rakṣām kurvantu me sadā vṛṣa rūpa dharaḥ devaḥ saurabheyaḥ mahā balaḥ vaḍavā ākhya anala sparddhām pañca gomātṛbhiḥ vṛtaḥ tayoḥ ājñām puraskṛtya sa me kāmam prayacchatu nandā sunandā surabhiḥ suśīlā sumanāḥ tathā paṃca go mātaraḥ tu etāḥ śiva loke vyavasthitāḥ śiva bhakti parāḥ nityam śiva arcana parāyaṇāḥ śivayoḥ śāsanāt eva diśantu mama vāṃchitam kṣetrapālaḥ mahā tejāḥ nīla jīmūta sannibhaḥ daṃṣṭrā karāla vadanaḥ sphurat rakta adhara ujjvalaḥ rakta ūrddhva mūrddhajaḥ śrīmān bhrukuṭī kuṭila īkṣaṇaḥ nagnaḥ triśūla pāśa asi kapāla udyata pāṇikaḥ kṣetre kṣetre samāsīnaḥ sthitaḥ yaḥ rakṣakaḥ satām śiva praṇāma paramaḥ śiva sadbhāva bhāvitaḥ śiva śritān viśeṣeṇa rakṣan putrān iva aurasān satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām sa me diśatu maGgalam tāla jaGgha ādayaḥ tasya prathama āvaraṇa īrcitāḥ satkṛtya śivayoḥ ājñām catvāraḥ samavantu mām bhairava ādyāḥ ca ye ca anye samantāt tasya veṣṭitāḥ te api mām anugṛhṇantu śiva śāsana gauravāt nārada ādyāḥ ca munayaḥ divyāḥ devaiḥ ca pūjitāḥ sādhyāḥ māgāḥ ca ye devāḥ janaloka nivāsinaḥ vinivṛtta adhikārāḥ ca mahar loka nivāsinaḥ sarve śiva arcana ratāḥ śiva ājñā vaśa vartinaḥ śivayoḥ ājñayā mahyam diśantu mama kāṃkṣitam gandharva ādyāḥ piśāca antāḥ catasraḥ devayonayaḥ siddhāḥ vidyādhara ādyāḥ ca ye api ca anye nabhaścarāḥ asurāḥ rākṣasāḥ ca eva pātāla tala vāsinaḥ ananta ādyāḥ ca nāga indrāḥ vainateya ādayaḥ dvijāḥ kūṣmāṃḍāḥ preta vetālāḥ grahāḥ bhūta gaṇāḥ pare ḍākinyaḥ ca api yoginyaḥ śākinyaḥ ca api tādṛśāḥ kṣetra ārāma gṛha ādīni tīrthāni āyatanāni ca dvīpāḥ samudrāḥ nadyaḥ ca nadāḥ ca anye sarāṃsi ca girayaḥ ca sumeru ādyāḥ kananāni samantataḥ paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ vṛkṣāḥ kṛmi kīṭa ādayaḥ mṛgāḥ bhuvanāni api sarvāṇi bhuvanānām adhīśvaraḥ aṇḍāni āvaraṇaiḥ sārddham māsāḥ ca daśa diggajāḥ varṇāḥ padāni mantrāḥ ca tattvāni api saha adhipaiḥ brahmāṃḍa dhārakāḥ rudrāḥ rudrāḥ ca anye sa śaktikāḥ yat ca kiṃcid jagati asmin dṛṣṭam ca anumitam śrutam sarve kāmam prayacchantu śivayoḥ eva śāsanāt atha vidyā parā śaivī paśu pāśa vimocinī paṃcārtha saṃjñitā divyā paśu vidyā bahiṣkṛtā śāstram ca śiva dharma ākhyam dharma ākhyam ca tat uttaram śaiva ākhyam śiva dharma ākhyam purāṇam śruti saṃmitam śaiva āgamāḥ ca ye ca anye kāmika ādyāḥ caturvidhāḥ śivābhyām aviśeṣeṇa satkṛtya iha samarcitāḥ tābhyām eva samājñātā mama abhipreta siddhaye śveta ādyāḥ nakulīśa antāḥ sa śiṣyāḥ ca api deśikāḥ śaivāḥ māheśvarāḥ ca eva jñāna karma parāyaṇāḥ laukikāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ sarve kṣatriyāḥ ca viśaḥ kramāt veda vedāṃga tattva jñāḥ sarva śāstra viśāradāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ vaiśeṣikāḥ ca eva yaugāḥ naiyāyikāḥ narāḥ saurāḥ brahmāḥ tathā raudrāḥ vaiṣṇavāḥ ca apare narāḥ śiṣṭāḥ sarve viśiṣṭā ca śiva śāsana yantritāḥ śaivāḥ siddhānta mārga sthāḥ śaivāḥ pāśupatāḥ tathā śaivāḥ mahāvrata dharāḥ śaivāḥ kāpālikāḥ pare śiva ājñā pālakāḥ pūjyāḥ mama api śiva śāsanāt sarve mama anugṛhṇantu śaṃsantu sa phala kriyām dakṣiṇa jñāna niṣṭhāḥ ca dakṣiṇa uttara mārga gāḥ nāstikāḥ ca śaṭhāḥ ca eva kṛtaghnāḥ ca eva tāmasāḥ pāṣaṃḍāḥ ca ati pāpāḥ ca vartantām dūratas mama sarve mām anugṛhṇantu santaḥ śaṃsantu maṃgalam namaḥ śivāya sa aṃbāya sa sutāya ādi hetave paṃca āvaraṇa rūpeṇa prapaṃcena āvṛtāya te iti uktvā daṃḍa vat bhūmau praṇipatya śivam śivām japet paṃcākṣarīm vidyām aṣṭottaraśata avarām kṛtvā tam kṣamayitvā īśam pūjā śeṣam samāpayet etat puṇyatamam stotram śivayoḥ hṛdayaṃgamam sarva abhīṣṭa pradam sākṣāt bhukti muktyā eka sādhanam yaḥ idam kīrtayet nityam śṛṇuyāt vā samāhitaḥ sa vidhūya āśu pāpāni śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt go ghnaḥ ca eva kṛtaghnaḥ ca vīra hā bhrūṇa hā api vā śaraṇa āgata ghātī ca mitra viśraṃbha ghātakaḥ duṣṭa pāpa samācāraḥ mātṛ hā pitṛ hā api vā duḥsvapna ādi mahā anartha sūcakeṣu bhayeṣu ca āyuḥ ārogyam aiśvaryam yat ca anyat api vāñchitam a saṃpūjya śiva stotram japāt phalam udāhṛtam āstām iyam phala avāptiḥ asmin saṃkīrtite sati sārddham aṃbikayā devaḥ śrutyā evam divi tiṣṭhati tasmāt nabhasi saṃpūjya devam devam saha umayā kṛta aṃjali puṭaḥ tiṣṭhan stotram etat udīrayet iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivamahāstotravarṇanam nāma ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha vakṣyāmi śaivānām iha eva phala dam nṛṇām dṛṣṭa siddhi karam karma na anyathā phala dam yatas parīkṣya śakuna ādyaiḥ tadā ādau niṣkṛtim ācaret sa khalu aśraddha dhānaḥ syāt na aśraddhaḥ phalam ṛcchati yathā ukta kāriṇām puṃsām iha eva phala darśanāt rātrau haviṣyam aśnīyāt pāyasam vā phalāni vā hiṃsā ādi yat niṣiddham syāt na kuryāt manasā api tat sadā bhasma anuliptām gaḥ su veṣaḥ ca śuciḥ bhavet ittham ācāravān bhūtvā sva anukūle śubhe ahani pūrva ukta lakṣaṇe deśe puṣpa dāma ādi alaṃkṛte ālipya śakṛtā bhūmim hasta māna avarām yathā tapta jāṃbūnada mayam aṣṭa patram sa kesaram tādṛśe svarṇa nirmāṇe kande samyak vidhānataḥ tatra aṇima ādikam sarvam saṃkalpya manasā punar ratna jam vā atha sauvarṇam sphaṭikam vā sa lakṣaṇam tatra āvāhya yajet devam sa aṃbam sa gaṇam avyayam tatra māheśvarī kalpyā mūrtiḥ mūrtimataḥ prabhoḥ catur bhujā catur vaktrā sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitā śārdūla carma vasanā kiṃcid vihasita ānanā vara dā abhaya hastā ca mṛga ṭaṃka dharā tathā atha vā aṣṭa bhujā ciṃtyā ciṃtakasya yathāruci tadā triśūla paraśu khaḍga vajrāṇi dakṣiṇe vāme pāśa aṃkuśau tadvat kheṭam nāgam ca bibhratī bāla arka sadṛśa prakhyā prativaktram tri locanā tasyāḥ pūrva mukham saumyam su ākāra sadṛśa prabham dakṣiṇam nīla jīmūta sadṛśam ghora darśanam uttaram vidruma prakhyam nīla alaka vibhūṣitam paścimam pūrṇa candra ābham saumyam indu kalā dharam tad aṃka maṃḍala ārūḍhā śaktiḥ māheśvarī parā mahālakṣmīḥ iti khyātā śyāmā sarva manoharā mūrtim kṛtvā evam ākārām sakalīkṛtya ca kramāt paṃcāmṛtam ca pūrṇāni bījāni ca viśeṣataḥ purastāt maṇḍalam kṛtvā ratna cūrṇa ādi alaṃkṛtam karṇikāyām pravinyasyet īśāna kalaśam punar tatas vidyeśa kalaśān aṣṭau pūrva ādi vat kramāt tīrtha ambu pūritān kṛtvā sūtreṇa āveṣṭya pūrvavat dukūla ādyena vastreṇa samācchādya samantataḥ tatas kuśa udaka ādyāni svarṇa ratna udakāni api gandham puṣpa ādi dīpān ca pūjā karma samācaret pala avaraḥ syāt ālepaḥ ekādaśa pala uttaraḥ suvarṇa ratna puṣpāṇi śubhāni surabhīṇi ca nīlotpala ādi utpalāni bilva patrāṇi anekaśas kamalāni ca raktāni śvetāni api ca śaṃbhave kṛṣṇa aguru udbhavaḥ dhūpaḥ sa karpūra ājya guggulaḥ kapilā ghṛta saṃsiddhāḥ dīpāḥ karpūra varti jāḥ paṃca brahma ṣaṣ aṃgāni pūjyāni āvaraṇāni ca naivedyaḥ payasā siddhaḥ sa guḍa ājyaḥ mahā caruḥ pāṭalā utpala padma ādyaiḥ pānīyam ca sugandhitam paṃca saugandhika upetam tāṃbūlam ca susaṃskṛtam suvarṇa ratna siddhāni bhūṣaṇāni viśeṣataḥ vāsāṃsi ca vicitrāṇi sūkṣmāṇi ca navāni ca darśanīyāni deyāni gāna vādya ādibhiḥ saha eka avarā tri uttarā ca pūjā phala vaśāt iha daśa saṃkhyā varaḥ homaḥ pratidravyam śata uttaraḥ ghora rūpaḥ śivaḥ ciṃtyaḥ māraṇa uccāṭana ādiṣu śiva liṃge śiva agnau ca hi anyāsu pratimāsu ca ciṃtyaḥ saumya tanuḥ śaṃbhuḥ kārye śāntika pauṣṭike āyasau sruc sruvau kāryau māraṇa ādiṣu karmasu tad anyatra tu sauvarṇau śāntika ādyeṣu kṛtsnaśas dūrvayā ghṛta go kṣīra miśrayā madhunā tathā caruṇā sa ghṛtena eva kevalam payasā api vā samṛddhi kāmaḥ juhuyāt mahā dāridrya śāntaye jātī puṣpeṇa vaśyā arthī juhuyāt sa ghṛtena tu ghṛtena karavīraiḥ ca kuryāt ākarṣaṇam dvijaḥ tailena uccāṭanam kuryāt staṃbhanam madhunā punar staṃbhanam sarṣapeṇa api laśunena tu pātanam tāḍanam rudhireṇa syāt kharasya uṣṭrasya ca ubhayoḥ māraṇa uccāṭane kuryāt rohi bījaiḥ tila anvitaiḥ vidveṣaṇam ca tailena kuryāt lāṃgalakasya tu kaṭukī tuṣa saṃyuktaiḥ kārpāsa asthibhiḥ eva ca jvara upaśānti dam kṣīram saubhāgya phala dam tathā kṣīreṇa tandulaiḥ ca eva caruṇā kevalena vā śāntikam pauṣṭikam vā api saptabhiḥ samidh ādibhiḥ dravyaiḥ viśeṣataḥ home vaśyam ākarṣaṇam tathā vaśyam ākarṣaṇam ca eva śrī padam ca viśeṣataḥ samidhaḥ śānti kāryeṣu pālāśa khadira ādikāḥ karavīra arka jāḥ kraurye kaṇṭakinyaḥ ca vigrahe praśāntaḥ śāntikam kuryāt pauṣṭikam ca viśeṣataḥ atīva duravasthāyām pratīkāra antaram na ced ātatāyinam uddiśya prakuryāt ābhicārikam sva rāṣṭra patim uddiśya na kuryāt ābhicārikam manasā karmmaṇā vācā yaḥ api kaḥ api śiva āśritaḥ sva rāṣṭra patim uddiśya śivā śritam atha api vā sva rāṣṭra pālakam tasmāt śiva bhaktam ca kañcana na hiṃsyāt abhicāra ādyaiḥ yadi icchet sukham ātmanaḥ anyam kam api ca uddiśya kṛtvā vai māraṇa ādikam paścāttāpena saṃyuktaḥ prāyaścittam samācaret bāṇaliṃge api vā kuryāt nirdhanaḥ dhanavān api svayaṃbhūte atha vā liṃge ārṣake vaidike api vā kvacid aṃśe tu yaḥ śaktaḥ tu aśaktaḥ kvacid aṃśake tat sarvam gurave dadyāt dakṣiṇām ca tatas pṛthak yaḥ svayam sādhayet śaktyā guru ādi nirapekṣayā saḥ api evam ācaret atra na gṛhṇīyāt svayam punar svayam gṛhṇāti yaḥ lobhāt pūjā aṃga dravyam uttamam kāṃkṣitam na labhet mūḍhaḥ na atra kāryā vicāraṇā arcitam yat tu tat liṃgam gṛhṇīyāt vā navā svayam gṛhṇīyāt yadi tat nityam svayam vā anyaḥ api vā arcayet api śatrubhiḥ ākrāntaḥ vyādhibhiḥ vā api anekaśas mṛtyoḥ āsya gataḥ ca api mucyate nirapāyataḥ pūjāyate ati kṛpaṇaḥ riktaḥ vaiśravaṇāyate kāmāyate virūpaḥ api vṛddhaḥ api taruṇāyate viṣāyate yat amṛtam viṣam api amṛtāyate mahīdharāyate śvabhram sa ca śvabhrāyate giriḥ padmākarāyate vahniḥ saraḥ vaiśvānarāyate siṃhāyate mṛgaḥ kṣudraḥ siṃhaḥ krīḍāmṛgāyate striyaḥ lakṣmīḥ sucaritāyate svairapreṣyāyate vāṇī kīrtiḥ tu gaṇikāyate svairācārāyate medhā vajrasūcīyate manaḥ mahāvātāyate śaktiḥ balam mattagajāyate śatru pakṣāyate arīṇām sarvaḥ eva suhṛd janaḥ śatravaḥ kuṇapāyante jīvantaḥ api sa bāndhavāḥ āpannaḥ gata ariṣṭaḥ svayam khalu amṛtāyate aniśam kriyamāṇā api ratiḥ tu abhinavāyate anāgata ādikam sarvam karasthāmalakāyate iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe aihikasiddhikarmavarṇanam nāma dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atas param pravakṣyāmi kevala āmuṣmikam vidhim puṇya atiśaya saṃyuktaḥ sarvaiḥ devaiḥ anuṣṭhitaḥ brahmaṇā viṣṇunā ca eva rudreṇa ca viśeṣataḥ śveta agastya dadhīca ādyaiḥ asmābhiḥ ca śiva āśritaiḥ nandīśvara mahākāla bhṛṃgīśa ādyaiḥ gaṇeśvaraiḥ pātāla vāsibhiḥ daityaiḥ śeṣa ādyaiḥ ca mahā uragaiḥ svam svam padam anuprāptam sarvaiḥ ayam anuṣṭhitaḥ brahmā brahmatvam āpannaḥ viṣṇuḥ viṣṇu tvam āgataḥ gaṇeśaḥ ca gaṇeśa tvam anena vidhinā gataḥ sitacandana toyena liṃgam snāpya śivam śivām tatra padmāsanam ramyam kṛtvā lakṣaṇa saṃyutam aṃguṣṭha pratimam ramyam sarva gandha mayam śubham agurum dakṣiṇe pārśve paścime tu manaḥśilām uttare candanam dadyāt haritālam tu pūrvatas dhūpam kṛṣṇa agurum dadyāt sarvatas ca sa guggulam vāsāṃsi ca ati sūkṣmāṇi vikāśāni nivedayet pāyasam ghṛta saṃmiśram ghṛta dīpān ca dāpayet praṇamya bhaktyā deveśam stutvā ca ante kṣamāpayet sarva upahāra saṃmiśram tatas liṃgam nivedayet śivāya śiva mantreṇa dakṣiṇāmūrtim āśritaḥ deyam ca śiva bhaktebhyaḥ śivena kathitam purā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe āmuṣmikakarmavidhivarṇanam nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sā sarvā labhyeta sadyas liṃgabera pratiṣṭhayā tasmāt pratiṣṭhite liṃge bhavet sarvam patiṣṭhitam brahmaṇā viṣṇunā vā api rudreṇa anyena kena vā kim anyat iha vaktavyam pratiṣṭhām prati kāraṇam partiṣṭhitam śivena api liṃgam vaiśveśvaram yatas sthāpayet parameśasya liṃgam beram atha api vā śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca kim idam liṃgam ākhyātam katham liṃgī maheśvaraḥ avyaktam liṃgam ākhyātam triguṇa prabhava apyayam anādi anantam viśvasya yat upādānakāraṇam tat eva mūlaprakṛtiḥ māyā ca gagana ātmikā aśuddham ca eva śuddham yat śuddha aśuddham ca tat tridhā tatas śivaḥ maheśaḥ ca rudraḥ viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ bhūtāni ca indriyaiḥ jātāḥ līyante atra śiva ājñayā atas eva śivaḥ liṃgaḥ liṃgam ājñāpayet yatas yatas na tat anājñātam kāryāya prabhavet svatas liṃgam ca śivayoḥ dehaḥ tābhyām yasmāt adhiṣṭhitam liṃga vedī mahādevī liṃgam sākṣāt maheśvaraḥ tat eva paramā śaktiḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ śaktiḥ rājñām yat ādatte prasūte tat carācaram yena ādau mohitau syātām brahma nārāyaṇau api vāri śayyā gataḥ viṣṇuḥ suṣvāpa an ākulaḥ sukham dadarśa puṇḍarīkākṣam svapantam tam an ākulam māyayā mohitaḥ śambhoḥ viṣṇum āha pitāmahaḥ sa tu hasta prahāreṇa tīvreṇa abhihataḥ kṣaṇāt iti viṣṇu vacaḥ śrutvā prabhu tva guṇa sūcakam vatsa iti mām kutas brūṣe guruḥ śiṣyam iva ātmanaḥ mām na jānāsi kim nātham prapaṃcaḥ yasya me kṛtiḥ tridhā ātmānam vibhajya idam sṛṣṭvā atha paripālyate saṃharāmi name kaścid sraṣṭā jagati vidyate iti ukte sati saḥ api āha brahmāṇam viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ bhavān api mama eva aṃgāt avatīrṇaḥ purā avyayāt mad niyogāt tvam ātmānam tridhā kṛtvā jagattrayam vismṛtaḥ asi jagannātham nārāyaṇam anāmayam tava api janakam sākṣāt mām evam avamanyase tava aparādhaḥ na asti atra bhrāntaḥ asi mama māyayā mad prasādāt iyam bhrāntiḥ apaiṣyati tava acirāt jvālā mālā sahasra āḍhyam aprameyam anaupamam tasya jvālā sahasreṇa brahma viṣṇū vimohitau visṛjya yuddham kim tu etat iti aciṃtayatām tadā tadā samudyatau syātām tasya ādi antam parīkṣitum tatra haṃsa ākṛtiḥ brahmā viśvatas pakṣa saṃyutaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ api viśvātmā līlāñjana caya upamam vārāham amitam rūpam asthāya gatavān adhas evam varṣa sahasram tu tvaran viṣṇuḥ adhas gataḥ na apaśyat alpam api asya mūlam liṃgasya sūkaraḥ tāvatkālam gataḥ ca ūrddhvam tasya antam jñātum icchayā śrānta utyantam a dṛṣṭvā antam pāpa tā adhas pitāmahaḥ tathā eva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śrāntaḥ saṃvigna locanaḥ samāgatau atha anyonyam vismaya smera vīkṣaṇau māyayā mohitau śaṃbhoḥ kṛtyākṛtyam na jagmatuḥ pṛṣṭhatas pārśvatas tasya ca agratas ca sthitau ubhau praṇipatya kim ātmā idam iti aciṃtayatām tadā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe harividhimohavarṇanam nāma catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha āvirabhavat tatra sa nādam śabda lakṣaṇam tat api aviditam tāvat brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā a u mā iti tri mātrābhiḥ parastāt ca arddha mātrayā tatra ākāraḥ śritaḥ bhāge jvalat liṃgasya dakṣiṇe arddha mātrā ātmakaḥ nādaḥ śrūyate liṃga mūrddhani veda ātmanā tadā avyaktaḥ praṇavaḥ vikṛtim gataḥ makāraḥ sāma saṃjātaḥ nādaḥ tu ātharvaṇī śrutiḥ ṛgayam sthāpayāmāsa samāsāt tu artham ātmanaḥ rajaḥ guṇeṣu brahmāṇam mūrtiṣu ādyam kriyāsu api sṛṣṭim lokeṣu pṛthivīm tattveṣu ātmānam avyayam liṃga bhāgeṣu adhobhāgam bīja ākhyam kāraṇa traye catuḥṣaṣṭi guṇa aiśvaryam bauddham yat aṇima ādiṣu atha upasthāpayāmāsa sva artham daśavidham yajuḥ sattvam guṇeṣu viṣṇum ca mūrtiṣu ādyam kriyāsu api sthitim lokeṣu antarikṣam vidyām tattveṣu ca triṣu kalā adhvasu pratiṣṭhām ca vāmam brahmasu paṃcasu madhyam tu liṃga bhāgeṣu yonim ca triṣu hetuṣu prākṛtam ca yathā aiśvaryam tasmāt viśvam yajuḥ mayam tatā upasthāpayāmāsa sāma artham daśadhā ātmanaḥ tamaḥ guṇeṣu atho rudram mūrtiṣu ādyam kriyāsu ca saṃhṛtim triṣu lokeṣu tattveṣu śivam uttamam liṃga bhāgeṣu pīṭha ūrddhvam bījinam kāraṇa traye pauruṣam ca tathā aiśvaryam ittham sāmnā tatam jagat tatas maheśvaram sākṣāt mūrtiṣu api sadāśivam kriyāsu niṣkriyasya api śivasya paramātmanaḥ śāntim ca śāntyatītām ca vyāpikām kalāsu api tatpūruṣam tathā īśānam brahma brahmasu paṃcasu yatra āvāhya samārādhyaḥ kevalaḥ niṣkalaḥ śivaḥ kāraṇeṣu traya atītāt māyā vikṣobha kāraṇāt anantāt śuddhavidyāyāḥ parastāt ca maheśvarāt sarva vidyā īśvara adhīśāt na parāt ca sadāśivāt paṃcavaktrāt daśa bhujāt sākṣāt sakala niṣkalāt tatas parāt niśādhīśān nāda ākhyāt ca tatas parāt tatas parāt suṣumnā īśāt brahmarandhra īśvarāt api paramam kāraṇam sākṣāt svayam niṣkāraṇam śivam kāraṇānām ca dhātāram dhyātārām dhyeyam avyayam sarva aiśvaryeṇa saṃpannam sarva īśvaram anīśvaram aiśvaryāt ca api māyā iyāt aśuddhāt mānuṣa ādikāt aparāt ca parāt tyājyāt adhiśuddha adhva gocarāt tad parāt śuddhavidyā ādyāt unmanā antāt parātparāt apāram apara adhīnam nirasta atiśayam sthiram yasmāt garīyasī tasmāt viśvam vyāptam atharvaṇāt ṛgvedaḥ punar āha idam jāgrat rūpam mayā ucyate bhogya ātmanā pariṇatāḥ vidyā vedyāḥ yatas mayi sāma ca āha suṣupti ākhyam evam sarvam mayā ucyate mama arthena śivena idam tāmasena abhidhīyate atharvā āha turāya ākhyam turīyātītam eva ca adhva ātmakam tu tritayam śiva vidyā ātma saṃjñitam tat traiguṇyam trayī sādhyam saṃśodhyam ca pada eṣiṇā adhva atītam turīya ākhyam nirvāṇam paramam padam dvayoḥ pramāpakaḥ nādaḥ nadāntaḥ ca mada ātmakaḥ tasmāt mama artha svātantryāt pradhānaḥ parameśvaraḥ śivaḥ hi praṇavaḥ hi eṣa praṇavaḥ hi śivaḥ smṛtaḥ eka akṣarāt akāra ākhyāt ātmā brahma abhidhīyate eka akṣarāt ukāra ākhyāt dvidhā viṣṇuḥ udīryate eka akṣarāt makāra ākhyāt śivaḥ rudraḥ udāhṛtaḥ dakṣiṇa aṃgāt maheśasya jātaḥ brahmā ātma mantraiḥ hṛdi tām san niyojayet kṛta ālayām parām āhuḥ pratiṣṭhām akṛta ālayāt śaktaḥ kṛta ālayaḥ paścāt pratiṣṭhā vidhim ācaret aśaktaḥ ced pratiṣṭhāpya liṃgam beram atha api vā śakteḥ anuguṇam paścāt prakurvīta śiva ālayam gṛha arcām ca punar vakṣye pratiṣṭhā vidhim uttamam kṛtvā liṃgam vā lakṣaṇa anvitam devīm kṛtvā śubhe deśe tatra abjam pūrvavat likhet paṃca brahmāṇi tad bījaiḥ teṣu paṃcasu paṃcabhiḥ viśodhya liṃgam beram vā mṛd toya ādyaiḥ yathā purā nidhāya puṣpam śirasi prokṣayet prokṣaṇī jalaiḥ kumbhaiḥ īśāna vidyā antaiḥ snāpayet mūlavidyayā tatas paṃcakalā nyāsam kṛtvā pūjām ca pūrvavat nyasya padma antare sarvam śeṣam pūrvavat ācaret liṃgāni bāṇa saṃjñāni sthāpanīyāni vā na vā tāni pūrvam śivena eva saṃskṛtāni yatas tatas śeṣāṇi sthāpanīyāni yāni dṛṣṭāni bāṇa vat a pīṭhe pīṭham āveśya kṛtvā saṃprokṣaṇam vidhim yajet tatra śivam teṣām pratiṣṭhā na vidhīyate dagdham ślatham kṣata aṃgam ca kṣipet liṃgam jalāśaye saṃdhāna yogyam saṃdhāya pratiṣṭhā vidhim ācaret berāt vā vikalāt liṃgāt deva pūjā purassaram udvāsya hṛdi saṃdhānam tyāgam vā yuktam ācaret dvi rātre ca mahā pūjām saṃprokṣaṇam atas param māsāt ūrdhvam aneka aham pūjā yadi vihanyate pratiṣṭhā procyate kaiścid kaiścid saṃprokṣaṇa kramaḥ saṃprokṣaṇe tu liṃga ādeḥ devam udvāsya pūrvavat aṣṭa pañca krameṇa eva snāpayitvā mṛd aṃbhasā prokṣayet prokṣaṇī toyaiḥ mūlena aṣṭa uttaram śatam sa puṣpam sa kuśam pāṇim nyasya liṃgasya mastake paṃca vāram japet mūlam aṣṭottaraśatam tatas tatas mūlena mūrddha ādi pīṭha antam saṃspṛśet api pūjām ca mahatīm kuryāt devam āvāhya pūrvavat iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe ptatiṣṭhāvidhivarṇanam nāma ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śīkṛṣṇaḥ uvāca jñāne kriyāyām caryāyām sāram uddhṛtya saṃgrahāt uktam bhagavatā sarvam śrutam śruti samam mayā idānīm śrotum icchāmi yogam parama durlabham sa adhikāram ca sa aṃgam ca sa vidhim sa prayojanam yadi asti maraṇam pūrvam yoga ādi anupamardataḥ sadyas sādhayitum śakyam yena syāt na ātma hā naraḥ tat ca tat kāraṇam ca eva tad kāla karaṇāni ca sthāne pṛṣṭam tvayā kṛṣṇa sarva praśna artha vedinā tatas krameṇa tat sarvam vakṣye śṛṇu samāhitaḥ yā vṛttiḥ sa samāsena yogaḥ sa khalu paṃcadhā avyākṣepā manaḥ vṛttiḥ mantra yogaḥ udāhṛtaḥ prāṇāyāma mukhā sā eva sparśe yogaḥ abhidhīyate vilīna avayavam viśvam rūpam saṃbhāvyate yatas abhāva yogaḥ saṃproktaḥ anābhāsāt vastunaḥ sataḥ śiva svabhāvaḥ eva ekaḥ ciṃtyate nirupādhikaḥ dṛṣṭe tathā ānuśravike viraktam viṣaye manaḥ viṣaya dvaya doṣāṇām guṇānām īśvarasya ca darśanāt eva satatam viraktam jāyate manaḥ aṣṭa aṃgaḥ vā ṣaṣ aṃgaḥ vā sarva yogaḥ samāsatas prāṇāyāmaḥ pratyāhāraḥ dhāraṇā dhyānam eva ca samādhiḥ iti yogāṃgāni aṣṭāv uktāni sūribhiḥ āsanam prāṇa saṃrodhaḥ pratyāhāraḥ utha dhāraṇā dhyānam samādhiḥ yogasya ṣaḍ aṃgāni samāsatas pṛthak lakṣaṇam eteṣām śivaśāstre samīritam śiva āgameṣu ca anyeṣu viśeṣāt kāmika ādiṣu yoga śāstreṣu api tathā purāṇeṣu api keṣu ca śaucam tuṣṭiḥ tapaḥ ca eva japaḥ praṇidhiḥ eva ca iti paṃca prabhedaḥ syāt niyamaḥ sva aṃśa bhedataḥ paryaṃkam ca yatheṣṭam ca proktam āsanam aṣṭadhā prāṇaḥ sva deha jaḥ vāyuḥ tasya āyāmaḥ nirodhanam nāsikā puṭam aṃgulyā pīḍya ekam apareṇa tu audaram recayet vāyum tathā ayam recakaḥ smṛtaḥ nāsāpuṭena apareṇa pūraṇāt pūrakam matam na muṃcati na gṛhṇāti vāyum antar bahis sthitam saṃpūrṇam kuṃbha vat tiṣṭhet acalaḥ sa tu kuṃbhaka recaka ādiṣu yaḥ bhyāsaḥ nāḍī śodhana pūrvakaḥ kanyakā ādi krama vaśāt prāṇāyāma nirodhanam tat caturddhā upadiṣṭam syāt mātrā guṇa vibhāgataḥ uttamaḥ tu tris uddhātaḥ ṣaḍviṃśat mātrakaḥ paraḥ sveda kaṃpa ādi janakaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ tad uttaraḥ ānanda udbhava romāṃca netra aśrūṇām vimocanam jānum pradakṣiṇīkṛtya na drutam na vilaṃbitam aṃgulī sphoṭanam kuryāt sā mātrā iti prakīrtitā mātrā krameṇa vijñeyāḥ ca udvāta krama yogataḥ nāḍī viśuddhi pūrvam tu prāṇāyāmam samācaret agarbhaḥ ca sagarbhaḥ ca prāṇāyāmaḥ dvidhā smṛtaḥ agarbhāt garbha saṃyuktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ śata adhikaḥ prāṇasya vijayāt eva jīyante deha vāyavaḥ prāṇaḥ samānaḥ ca hi udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca nāgaḥ kūrmaḥ ca kṛkalaḥ devadattaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ prayāṇam kurute yasmāt tasmāt prāṇaḥ abhidhīyate ava apāna ākhyaḥ yat āhāra ādi bhujyate vyānaḥ vyānaśayati aṃgāni aśeṣāṇi vivardhayan udvejayati marmāṇi iti udānaḥ vāyuḥ īritaḥ samam nayati sarva aṃgam samānaḥ tena gīyate udgāre nāgaḥ ākhyātaḥ kūrmaḥ unmīlane sthitaḥ kṛkalaḥ kṣavathau jñeyaḥ devadattaḥ vijṛṃbhaṇe na jahāti mṛtam ca api sarvavyāpī dhanaṃjayaḥ krameṇa abhyasyamānā iyam prāṇāyāma pramāṇavān viṣ mūtra śleṣmaṇām tāvat alpa bhāvaḥ prajāyate laghu tvam śīghra gāmi tvam utsāhaḥ svara sauṣṭhavam sarva roga kṣayaḥ ca eva balam tejaḥ surūpa tā tapāṃsi pāpa kṣaya tā yajña dāna vrata ādayaḥ prāṇāyāmasya tasya ete kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm indriyāṇi prasaktāni yathāsvam viṣayeṣu iha āhatya yat nigṛhṇāti sa pratyāhāraḥ ucyate namaḥ pūrvāṇi indriyāṇi svargam narakam eva ca nigṛhīta nisṛṣṭāni svargāya narakāya ca tasmāt sukha arthī matimān jñāna vairāgyam āsthitaḥ indriya aśvān nigṛhya āśu sva ātmanā ātmānam uddharet dhāraṇā nāma cittasya sthāna bandhaḥ samāsatas sthānam ca śivaḥ eva ekaḥ na anyat doṣa trayam yatas kālam kaṃca avadhīkṛtya sthāne avasthāpitam manaḥ na tu pracyavate lakṣyāt dhāraṇā syāt na ca anyathā manasaḥ prathamam sthairyam dhāraṇātaḥ prajāyate tasmāt dhīram manaḥ kuryāt dhāraṇa abhyāsa yogataḥ ciṃtāyām smṛtaḥ dhātuḥ śiva ciṃtā muhur muhur avyākṣiptena manasā dhyānam nāma tat ucyate paraḥ dhyeyaḥ samāpta ātharvaṇī śrutiḥ tathā śivā parā dhyeyā sarva bhūta gatau śivau vimuktiḥ pratyayaḥ pūrvaḥ pratyayaḥ ca aṇima ādikam dhyātā dhyānam tathā dhyeyam yat ca dhyāna prayojanam etat catuṣṭayam jñātvā yogam yuñjīta yoga vid jñāna vairāgya saṃpannaḥ śraddadhānaḥ kṣamā anvitaḥ nirmamaḥ ca sadā utsāhī dhyātā ittham puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ japāt śrāntaḥ punar dhyāyet dhyānāt śrāntaḥ punar japet dhāraṇā dvādaśa āyāmā dhyānam dvādaśa dhāraṇam dhyāna dvādaśakam yāvat samādhiḥ abhidhīyate samādhiḥ nāma yoga aṃgam antimam parikīrtitam svarūpa śūnya vat bhānam samādhiḥ abhidhīyate nirvāṇa anala vat yogī samādhi sthaḥ pragīyate na śṛṇoti na ca āghrāti na jalpati na paśyati na ca sparśam vijānāti na saṃkalpayate manaḥ evam śive vilīna ātmā samādhi sthaḥ iha ucyate tathā samādhi niṣṭhaḥ api tasmāt na vicalet sudhīḥ tad antarāyāḥ naśyanti vighnāḥ sarve śanais śanais iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīya saṃhitāyām vāyu naimiṣeya ṛṣi saṃvāde uttara khaṇḍe yogagativarṇanam nāma saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ālasyam vyādhayaḥ tīvrāḥ pramādaḥ sthāna saṃśayaḥ duḥkhāni daurmanasyam ca viṣayeṣu ca lola tā daśā ete yuñjatām puṃsām antarāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ dhātu vaiṣamya jāḥ doṣāḥ vyādhayaḥ karma doṣa jāḥ pramādaḥ nāma yogasya sādhanā nāma bhāvanā idam vijñānam sthāna saṃśayaḥ duḥkham ajñāna jam puṃsām cittasya ādhyātmikam viduḥ ādhibhautikam aṃga uttham yat ca duḥkham purā kṛtaiḥ ādhidaivikam ākhyātam aśani astra viṣa ādikam icchā vighāta jam mokṣam daurmanasyam pracakṣate śānteṣu eteṣu vighneṣu yoga āsaktasya yoginaḥ pratibhā śravaṇam vārtā darśana āsvāda vedanāḥ sūkṣme vyavahite atīte viprakṛṣṭe tu anāgate śravaṇam sarva śabdānām śravaṇe ca aprayatnataḥ vārttāḥ vārttāsu vijñānam sarveṣām eva dehinām darśanam nāma divyānām darśanam ca aprayatnataḥ tathā āsvādaḥ ca divyeṣu raseṣu āsvādaḥ ucyate sparśana adhigamaḥ tadvat vedanā nāma viśrutā gandha ādīnām ca divyānām ābrahma bhuvana adhipāḥ rasāyanāni sarvāṇi divyāḥ ca oṣadhayaḥ tathā kṛśa tā sthūla tā bālyam vārddhakyam ca eva yauvanam nānā cāti svarūpam ca caturṇām dehadhāraṇam pārthiva aṃśam vinā nityam surabhiḥ gandha saṃgrahaḥ evam aṣṭaguṇam prāhuḥ paiśācam pārthivam padam vinā kumbha ādikam pāṇau jala sañcaya dhāraṇam rasa ādikam bhavet ca anyat trayāṇām dehadhāraṇam tat idam ṣoḍaśaguṇam āpyam aiśvaryam adbhutam śarīrāt agni nirmāṇam tad tāpa bhaya varjjanam sthāpanam vā analasya ā apsu pāṇau pāvaka dhāraṇam dvābhyām deha vinirmāṇam āpya aiśvarya samanvitam manojava tvam bhūtānām kṣaṇāt antar praveśanam parvvata ādi mahā bhāra dhāraṇam ca aprayatnataḥ guru tvañca laghu tvañca pāṇau anila dhāraṇam dvātriṃśat guṇam aiśvaryyam mārutam kavayaḥ viduḥ chāyā hīna viniṣpattiḥ indriyāṇām adarśanam ākāśa laṃghanam ca eva sva dehe tad niveśanam ākāśa piṇḍīkaraṇam aśarīra tvam eva ca anila aiśvarya saṃyuktam catvāriṃśadguṇam mahat yathākāma upalabdhiḥ ca yathākāma vinirgamaḥ karma anurūpa nirmāṇam vaśi tvam priya darśanam chedanam tāḍanam ca eva bandhanam mocanam tathā grahaṇam sarva bhūtānām saṃsāra vaśa vartinām prasādaḥ ca api sarveṣām mṛtyu kāla jayaḥ tathā ābhimānikam aiśvaryam prājāpatyam pracakṣate etat cāndramasaiḥ bhogaiḥ ṣaṭpañcāśadguṇam mahat sargaḥ saṃkalpa mātreṇa trāṇam saṃharaṇam tathā sva adhikāraḥ ca sarveṣām bhūta citta pravartanam asādṛśyam ca sarvasya nirmāṇam jagataḥ pṛthak śubha aśubhasya karaṇam prājāpatyaiḥ ca saṃyutam catuṣṣaṣṭhi guṇam brāhmam aiśvaryam ca pracakṣate bauddhāt asmāt param gauṇam aiśvaryam prākṛtam viduḥ vaiṣṇavam tat samākhyātam tasya eva bhuvana sthitiḥ tat pauruṣam ca gauṇam ca gaṇeśam padam aiśvaram viṣṇunā tat padam kiṃcid jñātum anyaiḥ na śakyate vijñāna siddhayaḥ ca eva sarvāḥ eva aupasargikāḥ pratibhāseṣu aśuddheṣu guṇeṣu āsakta cetasaḥ tasmāt guṇān ca bhogān ca deva asura mahībhṛtām yathākāmam guṇān bhogān bhuktvā muktim prayāsyati atha prayogam yogasya vakṣye śṛṇu samāhitaḥ śubhe kāle śubhe deśe śiva kṣetra ādike punar mukta puṣpa samākīrṇe vitāna ādi vicitrite na agni abhyāśe jala abhyāśe śuṣka parṇa caye api vā na daṃśa maśaka ākīrṇe sarpa śvāpada saṃkule na ca duṣṭa mṛga ākīrṇe na bhaye durjana āvṛte śmaśāne caitya valmīke jīrṇāgāre catuṣpathe nadīnada samudrāṇām tīre rathyā antare api vā na jīrṇa udyāna goṣṭha ādau na aniṣṭe na ca nindite na ajīrṇa amla rasa udgāre na ca viṣ mūtra dūṣite na chardyām ātisāre vā na atibhuktau śrama anvite na ca ati ciṃtā ākulitaḥ na ca ati kṣudh pipāsitaḥ yukta āhāra vihāraḥ ca yukta ceṣṭaḥ ca karmasu āsanam mṛdulam ramyam vipulam su samam śuci ṛju grīva śiraḥ vakṣāḥ na ātiṣṭhet śiṣṭa locanaḥ kiṃcid unnāmita śirāḥ dantaiḥ dantān na saṃspṛśet danta agra saṃsthitāḥ jihvām acalām sanniveśya ca pārṣṇibhyām vṛṣaṇau rakṣan tathā prajananam punar ūrvoḥ upari saṃsthāpya bāhū tiryak ayatnataḥ dakṣiṇam kara pṛṣṭham tu nyasya vāma tala upari unnāmya śanakais pṛṣṭham uraḥ viṣṭabhya ca agratas saṃprekṣya nāsikā agram svam diśaḥ ca anavalokayān saṃbhṛta prāṇa saṃcāraḥ pāṣāṇaḥ iva niścalaḥ sva deha āyatanasya antar viciṃtya śivam aṃbayā hṛd padma pīṭhikā madhye dhyāna yajñena pūjayet mūle nāsā agratas nābhau kaṃṭhe vā tālu randhrayoḥ bhrū madhye dvāra deśe vā lalāṭe mūrdhni vā smaret parikalpya yathānyāyam śivayoḥ parama āsanam tatra sa āvaraṇam vā api nirāvaraṇam eva vā dvidaleṣoḍaśāre vā dvādaśāre yathāvidhi daśa are vā ṣaṣ asre vā catur asre śivam smaret vidyut samāna varṇe ca parṇe varṇa avasānake ṣoḍaśa arasya patrāṇi svarāḥ ṣoḍaśa tāni vai pūrva ādīni kramāt etat padmam kandasya mūlataḥ kakāra ādi ṭakāra antāḥ varṇāḥ parṇāni anukramāt go kṣīra dhavalasya uktāḥ ḍa ādi pha antāḥ yathākramam vidhūma aṃgāra varṇasya varṇāḥ vādyāḥ ca mūlādhāra aravindasya hema ābhasya yathākramam vakāra ādi sakāra antāḥ varṇāḥ parṇa mayāḥ sthitāḥ eteṣu atha aravindeṣu yatra eva abhiratam manaḥ tatra eva devam devīm ca ciṃtayet dhīrayā dhiyā aṃguṣṭha mātram amalam dīpyamānam samantataḥ śuddha dīpa śikhā ākāram sva śaktyā pūrṇa maṇḍitam indu rekhā sama ākāram tārā rūpam atha api vā nīvāra śūkaḥ sadṛśam bisa sutrābham eva vā kadamba golaka ākāram tuṣāra kaṇikā upamam kṣiti ādi tattva vijayam dhyātā yadi api vāñchati tad tad tattva adhipām eva mūrtim sthūlām viciṃtayet sadāśiva antāḥ brahma ādya bhava ādyāḥ ca aṣṭa mūrtayaḥ śivasya mūrtayaḥ sthūlāḥ śivaśāstre viniścitāḥ ghorā miśrā praśāntāḥ ca mūrtayaḥ tāḥ muni īśvaraiḥ phala abhilāṣa rahitaiḥ cintyāḥ cintā viśāradaiḥ ghorāḥ ced ciṃtitāḥ kuryuḥ pāpa roga parikṣayam saumye muktiḥ viśeṣeṇa śāntiḥ prajñā prasidhyati sidhyanti siddhayaḥ ca atra kramaśas na atra saṃśayaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe yogagatau vighnotpattivarṇanam nāma aṣṭatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrīkaṃṭhanātham smaratām sadyas sarva artha siddhayaḥ śive tu ciṃtite sākṣāt sarvāḥ sidhyanti siddhayaḥ mūrti antareṣu dhyāteṣu śiva rūpam viciṃtayet dhyānam ādau sa viṣayam tatas nirviṣayam jaguḥ tatra nirviṣayam dhyānam na asti iti eva satām matam tasmāt sa viṣayam dhyānam bāla arka kiraṇa āśrayam sūkṣma āśrayam nirviṣayam na aparam paramārthataḥ yat vā sa viṣayam dhyānam tat sa ākāra samāśrayam nirākāra ātma saṃvittiḥ dhyānam nirviṣayam matam nirākāra śraya tvena sa ākāra āśrayataḥ tathā tasmāt sa viṣayam dhyānam ādau kṛtvā sa bījakam prāṇāyāmena sidhyanti devyāḥ śānti ādayaḥ kramāt śāntiḥ praśāntiḥ dīptiḥ ca prasādaḥ ca tatas param śamaḥ sarva āpadām ca eva śāntiḥ iti abhidhīyate tamasaḥ anta bahis nāśaḥ praśāntiḥ parigīyate svastha tā yā tu sā buddhaḥ prasādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ kāraṇāni ca sarvāṇi sa bāhya abhyantarāṇi ca dhyātā dhyānam tathā dhyeyam yat vā dhyāna prayojanam etat catuṣṭayam jñātvā dhyātā dhyānam samācaret śraddadhānaḥ prasanna ātmā dhyātā sadbhiḥ udāhṛtaḥ ciṃtāyām smṛtaḥ dhātuḥ śiva ciṃtā muhur muhur yoga abhyāsaḥ tathā alpe api yathā pāpam vināśayet dhyāyataḥ kṣaṇa mātram vā śraddhayā parameśvaram vimukti pratyayam pūrṇam aiśvaryam ca aṇima ādikam śiva dhyānasya pūrṇasya sākṣāt uktam prayojanam yasmāt saukhyam ca mokṣam ca dhyānāt abhayam āpnuyāt na asti dhyānam vinā jñānam na asti dhyānam ayoginaḥ dhyānam jñānam ca yasya asti tīrṇaḥ tena bhava arṇavaḥ jñānam prasannam ekāgram aśeṣa upādhi varjjitam prakṣīṇa aśeṣa pāpānām jñāne dhyāne bhavet matiḥ pāpa upahata buddhīnām tad vārtā api su durlabhā yathā vahniḥ mahā dīptaḥ śuṣkam ārdram ca nirdahet tathā śubha aśubham karma dhyāna agniḥ dahate kṣaṇāt ati alpaḥ yathā dīpaḥ su mahat nāśayet tamaḥ yoga abhyāsaḥ tathā alpaḥ mahā pāpam vināśayet dhyāyataḥ kṣaṇa mātram vā śraddhayā parameśvaram na asti dhyāna samam tīrtham na asti dhyāna samam tapaḥ na asti dhyāna samaḥ yajñaḥ tasmāt dhyānam samācaret tīrthāni toya pūrṇāni devān pāṣāṇa mṛd mayān yoginām ca vapuḥ sūkṣmam bhavet pratyakṣam aiśvaram yathā sthūlam ayuktānām mṛd kāṣṭha ādyaiḥ prakalpitam yathā iha antar carāḥ rājñaḥ priyāḥ syuḥ na bahis carāḥ tathā antar dhyāna niratāḥ priyāḥ śaṃbhoḥ na karmiṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā narendra bhavane tadvat atra api karmiṇaḥ jijñāsuḥ api yogasya yām gatim labhate naraḥ dvijānām veda viduṣām koṭim saṃpūjya yat phalam bhikṣā mātra pradānena tat phalam śiva yogine ye ca apavādam kurvanti vimūḍhāḥ śiva yoginām śrotṛbhiḥ te prapadyante narakeṣu ā mahī kṣayāt tasmāt śrotā ca pāpīyān daṇḍyaḥ su mahatām mataḥ te vidanti mahā bhogān ante yogam ca śāṃkaram bhoga arthibhiḥ naraiḥ tasmāt saṃpūjyāḥ śiva yoginaḥ pratiśraya anna pāna ādyaiḥ śayyā prāvaraṇa ādibhiḥ deśaḥ bhavet pūtaḥ sa pūtaḥ iti kim punar sarva duḥkha prahāṇāya śiva yogam samabhyaset siddha yoga phalaḥ yogī lokānām hita kāmyayā bhogān bhuktvā yathākāmam viharet vā atra vartatām yaḥ tu āsannām mṛtim martyaḥ dṛṣṭa ariṣṭam ca bhūyasā sa yoga ārambha nirataḥ śiva kṣetram samāśrayet prāṇān vinā api roga ādyaiḥ svayam eva parityajet kṛtvā api anaśanam ca eva hutvā ca aṃgam śiva anale kṣiptvā vā śiva tīrtheṣu sva deham avagāhanāt sadyas eva vimucyeta na atra kāryā vicāraṇā roga ādyaiḥ vā atha vivaśaḥ śiva kṣetram samāśritaḥ yathā hi maraṇam śreṣṭham uśanti anaśana ādibhiḥ śāstra viśraṃbha dhīreṇa manasā kriyate yatas śiva nindā ratam hatvā pīḍitaḥ svayam eva vā yaḥ tyajet dustyajān prāṇān na sa bhūyas prajāyate śiva nindā ratam hantum aśaktaḥ yaḥ svayam mṛtaḥ śiva arthe yaḥ tyajet prāṇān śiva bhakta artham eva vā na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścid mukti mārga sthitaḥ naraḥ tasmāt śīghratarā muktiḥ tasya saṃsāra maṃḍalāt na eva āśaucam prapadyeta tad putra ādi viśeṣataḥ śiva cāra artham athavā śiva vidyā artham eva vā khanet vā bhuvi tad deham dahet vā śucinā agninā kṣipet vā apsu śivāsu eva tyajet vā kāṣṭha loṣṭa vat kalyāṇam eva kurvīta śaktyā bhaktān ca tarpayet iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śaivayogavarṇanam nāma ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī sūtaḥ uvāca tatas prabhāta samaye naimiṣīyāḥ tapodhanāḥ tadā brahma samādeśāt devī sākṣāt sarasvatī prasannā svādu salilā prāvartata nadī śubhā sarasvatīm nadīm dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ atha santarpya deva ādīn tadīyaiḥ salilaiḥ śivaiḥ smarantaḥ pūrva vṛttāntam yayuḥ vārāṇasīm prati tadā te himavat pādāt pantatīm dakṣiṇāmukhīm dṛṣṭvā bhāgīrathī tatra snātvā tad tīrataḥ yayuḥ tatas vārāṇasīm prāpya muditāḥ sarve eva te tadā uttara pravāhāyām gaṃgāyām avagāhya ca avimukteśvaram liṃgam dṛṣṭvā abhyarcya vidhānataḥ sūrya koṭi pratīkāśam tejaḥ divyam mahā adbhutam atha pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasma sañchanna vigrahāḥ tathā vilīyamāneṣu tapasviṣu mahātmasu tat dṛṣṭvā mahat āścaryam naimiṣīyāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ prāk eva eṣām tu gamanāt pavanaḥ loka pāvanaḥ darśanam naimiṣīyāṇām saṃvādaḥ taiḥ mahātmanaḥ śuddhām buddhim tatas teṣām sa ambe sa anucare śive samāptim ca api satrasya dīrghapūrvasya satriṇām tadā anavasarāt eva dvāḥsthaiḥ dvāri nivāritāḥ munayaḥ brahma bhavanāt bahis pārśvam upāviśan atha tumburuṇā gāne samatām prāpya nāradaḥ sāhacaryeṣu anujñātaḥ brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā tyaktvā paraspara sparddhām maitrīm ca paramām gataḥ upavīṇayitum devam nakuli īśvaram īśvaram bhavanāt niryayau dhātuḥ jaladāt aṃśumān iva tam dṛṣṭvā ṣaṭkulīyāḥ te nāradam muni go vṛṣam praṇamya avasaram śaṃbhoḥ papracchuḥ parama ādarāt tena te viviśuḥ veśma piṃḍībhūyāṃḍa janmanaḥ praviśya dūratas devam praṇamya bhuvi daṃḍa vat samīpe tad anujñātāḥ parivṛtya upatasthire tān tatra avasthitān pṛṣṭvā kuśalam kamalāsanaḥ vṛttāntam vaḥ mayā jñātam vāyuḥ eva āha naḥ yatas bhavadbhiḥ kim kṛtam paścāt māruta iṃtarhite sati gaṃgātīrtha isya gamanam yātrām vārāṇasīm prati darśanam tatra liṃgānām sthāpitānām sura īśvaraiḥ ākāśe mahataḥ tasya tejaḥ rāśeḥ ca darśanam munīnām vilayam tatra nirodham tejasaḥ tatas yāthātmya vedanam tasya ciṃtitasya api ca ātmabhiḥ munibhiḥ kathitam śrutvā viśvakarmā caturmukhaḥ kaṃpayitvā śiraḥ kiṃcid prāha gaṃbhīrayā girā pratyāsīdati yuṣmākam siddhiḥ āmuṣmikī parā prasāda abhimukhaḥ bhūtaḥ iti bhūtārtha sūcitam vārāṇasyām tu yuṣmābhiḥ yat dṛṣṭam divi dīptimat tat liṃga saṃjñitam sākṣāt tejaḥ māheśvaram param tatra līnāḥ ca munayaḥ śrauta pāśupata vratāḥ muktāḥ babhūvuḥ svasthāḥ ca naiṣṭhikāḥ dagdha kilbiṣāḥ sa ca ayam arthaḥ sūcyeta yuṣmad dṛṣṭena tejasā prayāta dakṣiṇam meroḥ śikharam deva sevitam pratīkṣya āgamanam sākṣāt bhūtanāthasya nandinaḥ purā sanatkumāraḥ api dṛṣṭvā api parameśvaram ajñānāt sarva yogi indra mānī vinaya dūṣitaḥ tatas aparādhāt kruddhena mahā uṣṭraḥ nandinā kṛtaḥ upāsya devam devīm ca nandinam ca anunīya vai kathaṃcid uṣṭra tā tasya prayatnena nivāritā prāpitaḥ hi yathāpūrvam sanat pūrvām kumāra tām avajñāya hi mām eva tathā aham kṛtavān muniḥ brahmaṇaḥ pūrvajaḥ putraḥ mām mūḍhaḥ iva saṃsmaran saḥ evam vyāhṛtaḥ bhūyas sarva bhūta gaṇāgraṇīḥ yat parājñāpanam mūrdhnā prātar pratigṛhītavān prasāda artham gaṇasya asya tapaḥ carati duścaram draṣṭavyaḥ ca iti yuṣmābhiḥ prāk gaṇeśa samāgamāt tad prasāda artham acirāt nandī tatra āgamiṣyati iti satvaram ādiśya preṣitā viśvayoginā kumāraśikharam meroḥ dakṣiṇam munayaḥ yayuḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe naimiṣarṣiyātrāvarṇanam nāma catvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca amṛta svādu śiśira svacchāḥ gādha laghu udakam samantataḥ saṃghaṭitam pala saṃcayaiḥ taraṃgaiḥ abhra saṃkāśaiḥ ākāśam iva bhūmi gam sukha avataraṇa ārohaiḥ sthalaiḥ nīla śilā mayaiḥ sopāna mārgau ruciraiḥ śobhamāna aṣṭa diś mukham tatra avatīrṇaiḥ ca yathā tatra uttīrṇaḥ ca bhūyasā snātaiḥ sita upavītaiḥ ca śukla a kaupīna valkalaiḥ jaṭā śikhāyanaiḥ muṃḍaiḥ tripuṃḍra kṛta maṃḍanaiḥ ghaṭaiḥ kamalinī patra puṭaiḥ ca kalaśaiḥ śivaiḥ kamaṇḍalubhiḥ anyaiḥ ca tādṛśaiḥ karaka ādibhiḥ ātma artham ca para artham ca devatā artham viśeṣataḥ ānīyamāna salilam ātta puṣpam ca nityaśas antar jala śilā ārūḍhaiḥ nīcānām sparśa śaṃkayā ācāravadbhiḥ munibhiḥ kṛta bhasma aṃga dhūsaraiḥ itas tatas majjadbhiḥ iṣṭa śiṣṭaiḥ śilā gataiḥ sthāne sthāne kṛta aneka bali puṣpa samīraṇaiḥ kvacid ca tṛṣayā āyāta mṛgī mṛga turaṃgamam kvacid pīta jana uttīrṇa mayūra vara vāraṇam kvacid kṛta taṭa āghāta vṛṣa prativṛṣa ujjvalam kvacid kāraṃḍava ravaiḥ kvacid sārasa kūjitaiḥ snāna pāna ādi karaṇaiḥ sva saṃpad druma jīvibhiḥ praṇayāt prāṇibhiḥ taiḥ taiḥ bhāṣamāṇam iva asakṛt kūla śākhi śikhā ālīna kokila ākula kūjitaiḥ ātapa upahatān sarvān na amantrayat ivāniśam vedyām vajra śilā mayyām mṛdule mṛga carmaṇi sanatkumāram āsīnam śaśvat bāla vapurddharam tad kāla mātra uparatam samādheḥ acala ātmanaḥ dadṛśuḥ naimiṣeyāḥ te praṇatāḥ ca upatasthire yāvat pṛṣṭavate tasmai procuḥ svāgata kāraṇam dadṛśe tad kṣaṇe tasmin vimānam bhānu sannibham gaṇeśvaraiḥ asaṃkhyeyaiḥ saṃvṛtam ca samantataḥ apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃkīrṇam rudra kanyābhiḥ āvṛtam mṛdaṃga muraja udghuṣṭam veṇu vīṇā rava anvitam citra ratna vitāna āḍhyam muktā dāma virājitam nṛtyadbhiḥ ca eva gāyadbhiḥ vādayadbhiḥ ca saṃvṛtam vīra go vṛṣa cihnena vidrama druma yaṣṭinā kṛta gopura satkāram ketunā mānya hetunā divya siṃhāsana ārūḍham devyā suyaśayā saha śriyā ca vapuṣā ca eva tribhiḥ ca api vilocanaiḥ prākāraiḥ abhikṛtyānām pratyabhijñāpakam prabhoḥ sarva anugrahaṇam śaṃbhoḥ sākṣāt iva puras sthitam śilāda tanayam sākṣāt śrīmat śūla vara āyudham viśva īśvara gaṇa adhyakṣam viśveśvaram iva aparam viśvasya api vidhātR̥ṇām nigraha anugraha kṣamam catur bāhum udāra aṅgam candra rekhā vibhūṣitam kaṃṭhe nāgena maulau ca śaśāṃkena api alaṃkṛtam samāptam iva nirvāṇam sarvajñam iva saṃgatam dṛṣṭvā prahṛṣṭa vadanaḥ brahma putraḥ saha ṛṣibhiḥ praṇamya daṇḍa vat devam stutvā vyajñāpayat munīm ṣaṭkulīyāḥ ime dīrgham naimiṣe satram āsthitāḥ āgatāḥ brahmaṇā ādiṣṭāḥ pūrvam eva abhikāṃkṣayā śrutvā vākyam brahma putrasya nandī chittvā pāśān dṛṣṭipātena sadyas śaivam dharmam ca aiśvaram jñāna yogam dattvā bhūyas deva pārśvam jagāma sanatkumāreṇa ca tat samastam vyāsāya sākṣāt gurave mama uktam na a veda vidbhyaḥ kathanīyam etat purāṇa ratnam puraśāsanasya na abhakta śiṣyāya ca nāstikebhyaḥ dattam hi mohāt nirayam dadāti mārgeṇa sevā anugatena yaiḥ tat dattam gṛhītam paṭhitam śrutam vā atas gamiṣye samastam eva astu śivam sadā naḥ sūte kṛta āśiṣi gate munayaḥ su vṛttāḥ yāge ca paryavasite mahati prayoge kāle kalau ca viṣayaiḥ kaluṣāyamāṇe vārāṇasī parisare vasatim vinetuḥ atha ca te paśu pāśa mumukṣayā akhila tayā kṛta pāśupata vratāḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca etat śiva purāṇam hi samāptam hitam ādarāt nāstikāya na vaktavyam aśraddhāya śaṭhāya ca tasmāt punar punar ca eva śrotavyam hi mumukṣubhiḥ pañcāvṛttiḥ prakartavyā purāṇasya asya sat dhiyā param phalam samuddiśya tat prāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ purātanāḥ ca rājānaḥ viprāḥ vaiśyāḥ ca sattamāḥ śroṣyati atha api yaḥ ca idam mānavaḥ bhakti tatparaḥ etat śiva purāṇam hi śivasya ati priyam param etat śiva purāṇasya vaktuḥ śrotuḥ ca sarvadā sa gaṇaḥ sa sutaḥ sa ambaḥ śam karotu sa śaṃkaraḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe vyāsopadeśaśrīśivamahāpurāṇamāhātmyavarṇanam nāma ekacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ayam granthaḥ
